Qala anthirnee ila yawmi yub'athoona

# 969

Qala innaka mina almunthareena

# 970

Qala fabima aghwaytanee laaq'udanna lahum sirataka almustaqeema

# 971

Thumma laatiyannahum min bayni aydeehim wamin khalfihim wa'an aymanihim wa'an shamailihim wala tajidu aktharahum shakireena

# 972

Qala okhruj minha mathooman madhooran laman tabi'aka minhum laamlaanna jahannama minkum ajma'eena

# 973

Waya adamu oskun anta wazawjuka aljannata fakula min haythu shituma wala taqraba hathihi ashshajarata fatakoona mina aththalimeena

# 974

Fawaswasa lahuma ashshaytanu liyubdiya lahuma ma wooriya 'anhuma min sawatihima waqala ma nahakuma rabbukuma 'an hathihi ashshajarati illa an takoona malakayni aw takoona mina alkhalideena

# 975

Waqasamahuma innee lakuma lamina annasiheena

# 976

Fadallahuma bighuroorin falamma thaqa ashshajarata badat lahuma sawatuhuma watafiqa yakhsifani 'alayhima min waraqi aljannati wanadahuma rabbuhuma alam anhakuma 'an tilkuma ashshajarati waaqul lakuma inna ashshaytana lakuma 'aduwwun mubeenun

# 977

Qala rabbana thalamna anfusana wain lam taghfir lana watarhamna lanakoonanna mina alkhasireena

# 978

Qala ihbitoo ba'dukum liba'din 'aduwwun walakum fee alardi mustaqarrun wamata'un ila heenin

# 979

Qala feeha tahyawna wafeeha tamootoona waminha tukhrajoona

# 980

Ya banee adama qad anzana 'alaykum libasan yuwaree sawatikum wareeshan walibasu attaqwa thalika khayrun thalika min ayati Allahi la'allahum yaththakkaroona

# 981

Ya banee adama la yaftinannakumu ashshaytanu kama akhraja abawaykum mina aljannati yanzi'u 'anhuma libasahuma liyuriyahuma sawatihima innahu yarakum huwa waqabeeluhu min haythu la tarawnahum inna ja'ana ashshayateena awliyaa lillatheena la yuminoona

# 982

Waitha fa'aloo fahishatan qaloo wajadna 'alayha abaana waAllahu amarana biha qul inna Allaha la yamuru bialfahshai ataqooloona 'ala Allahi ma la ta'lamoona

# 983

Qul amara rabbee bialqisti waaqeemoo wujoohakum 'inda kulli masjidin waod'oohu mukhliseena lahu addeena kama badaakum ta'oodoona

# 984

Fareeqan hada wafareeqan haqqa 'alayhimu addalalatu innahumu ittakhathoo ashshayateena awliyaa min dooni Allahi wayahsaboona annahum muhtadoona

# 985

Ya banee adama khuthoo zeenatakum 'inda kulli masjidin wakuloo waishraboo wala tusrifoo innahu la yuhibbu almusrifeena

# 986

Qul man harrama zeenata Allahi allatee akhraja li'ibadihi waattayyibati mina arrizqi qul hiya lillatheena amanoo fee alhayati addunya khalisatan yawma alqiyamati kathalika nufassilu alayati liqawmin ya'lamoona

# 987

Qul innama harrama rabbiya alfawahisha ma thahara minha wama batana waalithma waalbaghya bighayri alhaqqi waan tushrikoo biAllahi ma lam yunazzil bihi sultanan waan taqooloo 'ala Allahi ma la ta'lamoona

# 988

Walikulli ommatin ajalun faitha jaa ajaluhum la yastakhiroona sa'atan wala yastaqdimoona

# 989

Ya banee adama imma yatiyannakum rusulun minkum yaqussoona 'alaykum ayatee famani ittaqa waaslaha fala khawfun 'alayhim wala hum yahzanoona

# 990

Waallatheena kaththaboo biayatina waistakbaroo 'anha olaika ashabu annari hum feeha khalidoona

# 991

Faman athlamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban aw kaththaba biayatihi olaika yanaluhum naseebuhum mina alkitabi hatta itha jaathum rusuluna yatawaffawnahum qaloo ayna ma kuntum tad'oona min dooni Allahi qaloo dalloo 'anna washahidoo 'ala anfusihim annahum kanoo kafireena

# 992

Qala odkhuloo fee omamin qad khalat min qablikum mina aljinni waalinsi fee annari kullama dakhalat ommatun la'anat okhtaha hatta itha iddarakoo feeha jamee'an qalat okhrahum lioolahum rabbana haolai adalloona faatihim 'athaban di'fan mina annari qala likullin di'fun walakin la ta'lamoona

# 993

Waqalat oolahum liokhrahum fama kana lakum 'alayna min fadlin fathooqoo al'athaba bima kuntum taksiboona

# 994

Inna allatheena kaththaboo biayatina waistakbaroo 'anha la tufattahu lahum abwabu assamai wala yadkhuloona aljannata hatta yalija aljamalu fee sammi alkhiyati wakathalika najzee almujrimeena

# 995

Lahum min jahannama mihadun wamin fawqihim ghawashin wakathalika najzee aththalimeena

# 996

Waallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati la nukallifu nafsan illa wus'aha olaika ashabu aljannati hum feeha khalidoona

# 997

Wanaza'na ma fee sudoorihim min ghillin tajree min tahtihimu alanharu waqaloo alhamdu lillahi allathee hadana lihatha wama kunna linahtadiya lawla an hadana Allahu laqad jaat rusulu rabbina bialhaqqi wanoodoo an tilkumu aljannatu oorithtumooha bima kuntum ta'maloona

# 998

Wanada ashabu aljannati ashaba annari an qad wajadna ma wa'adana rabbuna haqqan fahal wajadtum ma wa'ada rabbukum haqqan qaloo na'am faaththana muaththinun baynahum an la'natu Allahi 'ala aththalimeena

# 999

Allatheena yasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi wayabghoonaha 'iwajan wahum bialakhirati kafiroona

# 1000

Wabaynahuma hijabun wa'ala ala'rafi rijalun ya'rifoona kullan biseemahum wanadaw ashaba aljannati an salamun 'alaykum lam yadkhulooha wahum yatma'oona

# 1001

Waitha surifat absaruhum tilqaa ashabi annari qaloo rabbana la taj'ana ma'a alqawmi aththalimeena

# 1002

Wanada ashabu ala'rafi rijalan ya'rifoonahum biseemahum qaloo ma aghna 'ankum jam'ukum wama kuntum tastakbiroona

# 1003

Ahaolai allatheena aqsamtum la yanaluhumu Allahu birahmatin odkhuloo aljannata la khawfun 'alaykum wala antum tahzanoona

# 1004

Wanada ashabu anari ashaba aljannati an afeedoo 'alayna mina almai aw mimma razaqakumu Allahu qaloo inna Allaha harramahuma 'ala alkafireena

# 1005

Allatheena ittakhathoo deenahum lahwan wala'iban wagharrathumu alhayatu addunya faalyawma nansahum kama nasoo liqaa yawmihim hatha wama kanoo biayatina yajhadoona

# 1006

Walaqad jinahum bikitabin fassanahu 'ala 'ilmin hudan warahmatan liqawmin yuminoona

# 1007

Hal yanthuroona illa taweelahu yawma yatee taweeluhu yaqoolu allatheena nasoohu min qablu qad jaat rusulu rabbina bialhaqqi fahal lana min shufa'aa fayashfa'oo lana aw nuraddu fana'mala ghayra allathee kunna na'malu qad khasiroo anfusahum wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yaftaroona

# 1008

Inna rabbakumu Allahu allathee khalaqa assamawati waalarda fee sittati ayyamin thumma istawa 'ala al'arshi yughshee allayla annahara yatlubuhu hatheethan waashshamsa waalqamara waannujooma musakhkharatin biamrihi ala lahu alkhalqu waalamru tabaraka Allahu rabbu al'alameena

# 1009

Od'oo rabbakum tadarru'an wakhufyatan innahu la yuhibbu almu'tadeena

# 1010

Wala tufsidoo fee alardi ba'da islahiha waod'oohu khawfan watama'an inna rahmata Allahi qareebun mina almuhsineena

# 1011

Wahuwa allathee yursilu arriyaha bushran bayna yaday rahmatihi hatta itha aqallat sahaban thiqalan suqnahu libaladin mayyitin faanzana bihi almaa faakhrajna bihi min kulli aththamarati kathalika nukhriju almawta la'allakum tathakkaroona

# 1012

Waalbaladu attayyibu yakhruju nabatuhu biithni rabbihi waallathee khabutha la yakhruju illa nakidan kathalika nusarrifu alayati liqawmin yashkuroona

# 1013

Laqad arsana noohan ila qawmihi faqala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu innee akhafu 'alaykum 'athaba yawmin 'atheemin

# 1014

Qala almalao min qawmihi inna lanaraka fee dalalin mubeenin

# 1015

Qala ya qawmi laysa bee dalalatun walakinnee rasoolun min rabbi al'alameena

# 1016

Oballighukum risalati rabbee waansahu lakum waa'lamu mina Allahi ma la ta'lamoona

# 1017

Awa'ajibtum an jaakum thikrun min rabbikum 'ala rajulin minkum liyunthirakum walitattaqoo wala'allakum turhamoona

# 1018

Fakaththaboohu faanjaynahu waallatheena ma'ahu fee alfulki waaghraqna allatheena kaththaboo biayatina innahum kanoo qawman 'ameena

# 1019

Waila 'adin akhahum hoodan qala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu afala tattaqoona

# 1020

Qala almalao allatheena kafaroo min qawmihi inna lanaraka fee safahatin wainna lanathunnuka mina alkathibeena

# 1021

Qala ya qawmi laysa bee safahatun walakinnee rasoolun min rabbi al'alameena

# 1022

Oballighukum risalati rabbee waana lakum nasihun ameenun

# 1023

Awa'ajibtum an jaakum thikrun min rabbikum 'ala rajulin minkum liyunthirakum waothkuroo ith ja'alakum khulafaa min ba'di qawmi noohin wazadakum fee alkhalqi bastatan faothkuroo alaa Allahi la'allakum tuflihoona

# 1024

Qaloo ajitana lina'buda Allaha wahdahu wanathara ma kana ya'budu abaona fatina bima ta'iduna in kunta mina assadiqeena

# 1025

Qala qad waqa'a 'alaykum min rabbikum rijsun waghadabun atujadiloonanee fee asmain sammaytumooha antum waabaokum ma nazzala Allahu biha min sultanin faintathiroo innee ma'akum mina almuntathireena

# 1026

Faanjaynahu waallatheena ma'ahu birahmatin minna waqata'na dabira allatheena kaththaboo biayatina wama kanoo mumineena

# 1027

Waila thamooda akhahum salihan qala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu qad jaatkum bayyinatun min rabbikum hathihi naqatu Allahi lakum ayatan fatharooha takul fee ardi Allahi wala tamassooha bisooin fayakhuthakum 'athabun aleemun

# 1028

Waothkuroo ith ja'alakum khulafaa min ba'di 'adin wabawwaakum fee alardi tattakhithoona min suhooliha qusooran watanhitoona aljibala buyootan faothkuroo alaa Allahi wala ta'thaw fee alardi mufsideena

# 1029

Qala almalao allatheena istakbaroo min qawmihi lillatheena istud'ifoo liman amana minhum ata'lamoona anna salihan mursalun min rabbihi qaloo inna bima orsila bihi muminoona

# 1030

Qala allatheena istakbaroo inna biallathee amantum bihi kafiroona

# 1031

Fa'aqaroo annaqata wa'ataw 'an amri rabbihim waqaloo ya salihu itina bima ta'iduna in kunta mina almursaleena

# 1032

Faakhathathumu arrajfatu faasbahoo fee darihim jathimeena

# 1033

Fatawalla 'anhum waqala ya qawmi laqad ablaghtukum risalata rabbee wanasahtu lakum walakin la tuhibboona annasiheena

# 1034

Walootan ith qala liqawmihi atatoona alfahishata ma sabaqakum biha min ahadin mina al'alameena

# 1035

Innakum latatoona arrijala shahwatan min dooni annisai bal antum qawmun musrifoona

# 1036

Wama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qaloo akhrijoohum min qaryatikum innahum onasun yatatahharoona

# 1037

Faanjaynahu waahlahu illa imraatahu kanat mina alghabireena

# 1038

Waamtarna 'alayhim mataran faonthur kayfa kana 'aqibatu almujrimeena

# 1039

Waila madyana akhahum shu'ayban qala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu qad jaatkum bayyinatun min rabbikum faawfoo alkayla waalmeezana wala tabkhasoo annasa ashyaahum wala tufsidoo fee alardi ba'da islahiha thalikum khayrun lakum in kuntum mumineena

# 1040

Wala taq'udoo bikulli siratin too'idoona watasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi man amana bihi watabghoonaha 'iwajan waothkuroo ith kuntum qaleelan fakaththarakum waonthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu almufsideena

# 1041

Wain kana taifatun minkum amanoo biallathee orsiltu bihi wataifatun lam yuminoo faisbiroo hatta yahkuma Allahu baynana wahuwa khayru alhakimeena

# 1042

Qala almalao allatheena istakbaroo min qawmihi lanukhrijannaka ya shu'aybu waallatheena amanoo ma'aka min qaryatina aw lata'oodunna fee millatina qala awalaw kunna kariheena

# 1043

Qadi iftarayna 'ala Allahi kathiban in 'udna fee millatikum ba'da ith najjana Allahu minha wama yakoonu lana an na'ooda feeha illa an yashaa Allahu rabbuna wasi'a rabbuna kulla shayin 'ilman 'ala Allahi tawakkana rabbana iftah baynana wabayna qawmina bialhaqqi waanta khayru alfatiheena

# 1044

Waqala almalao allatheena kafaroo min qawmihi laini ittaba'tum shu'ayban innakum ithan lakhasiroona

# 1045

Faakhathathumu arrajfatu faasbahoo fee darihim jathimeena

# 1046

Allatheena kaththaboo shu'ayban kaan lam yaghnaw feeha allatheena kaththaboo shu'ayban kanoo humu alkhasireena

# 1047

Fatawalla 'anhum waqala ya qawmi laqad ablaghtukum risalati rabbee wanasahtu lakum fakayfa asa 'ala qawmin kafireena

# 1048

Wama arsana fee qaryatin min nabiyyin illa akhathna ahlaha bialbasai waaddarrai la'allahum yaddarra'oona

# 1049

Thumma baddana makana assayyiati alhasanata hatta 'afaw waqaloo qad massa abaana addarrao waassarrao faakhathnahum baghtatan wahum la yash'uroona

# 1050

Walaw anna ahla alqura amanoo waittaqaw lafatahna 'alayhim barakatin mina assamai waalardi walakin kaththaboo faakhathnahum bima kanoo yaksiboona

# 1051

Afaamina ahlu alqura an yatiyahum basuna bayatan wahum naimoona

# 1052

Awa amina ahlu alqura an yatiyahum basuna duhan wahum yal'aboona

# 1053

Afaaminoo makra Allahi fala yamanu makra Allahi illa alqawmu alkhasiroona

# 1054

Awalam yahdi lillatheena yarithoona alarda min ba'di ahliha an law nashao asabnahum bithunoobihim wanatba'u 'ala quloobihim fahum la yasma'oona

# 1055

Tilka alqura naqussu 'alayka min anbaiha walaqad jaathum rusuluhum bialbayyinati fama kanoo liyuminoo bima kaththaboo min qablu kathalika yatba'u Allahu 'ala quloobi alkafireena

# 1056

Wama wajadna liaktharihim min 'ahdin wain wajadna aktharahum lafasiqeena

# 1057

Thumma ba'athna min ba'dihim moosa biayatina ila fir'awna wamalaihi fathalamoo biha faonuthur kayfa kana 'aqibatu almufsideena

# 1058

Waqala moosa ya fir'awnu innee rasoolun min rabbi al'alameena

# 1059

Haqeequn 'ala an la aqoola 'ala Allahi illa alhaqqa qad jitukum bibayyinatin min rabbikum faarsil ma'iya banee israeela

# 1060

Qala in kunta jita biayatin fati biha in kunta mina assadiqeena

# 1061

Faalqa 'asahu faitha hiya thu'banun mubeenun

# 1062

Wanaza'a yadahu faitha hiya baydao lilnnathireena

# 1063

Qala almalao min qawmi fir'awna inna hatha lasahirun 'aleemun

# 1064

Yureedu an yukhrijakum min ardikum famatha tamuroona

# 1065

Qaloo arjih waakhahu waarsil fee almadaini hashireena

# 1066

Yatooka bikulli sahirin 'aleemin

# 1067

Wajaa assaharatu fir'awna qaloo inna lana laajran in kunna nahnu alghalibeena

# 1068

Qala na'am wainnakum lamina almuqarrabeena

# 1069

Qaloo ya moosa imma an tulqiya waimma an nakoona nahnu almulqeena

# 1070

Qala alqoo falamma alqaw saharoo a'yuna annasi waistarhaboohum wajaoo bisihrin 'atheemin

# 1071

Waawhayna ila moosa an alqi 'asaka faitha hiya talqafu ma yafikoona

# 1072

Fawaqa'a alhaqqu wabatala ma kanoo ya'maloona

# 1073

Faghuliboo hunalika wainqalaboo saghireena

# 1074

Waolqiya assaharatu sajideena

# 1075

Qaloo amanna birabbi al'alameena

# 1076

Rabbi moosa waharoona

# 1077

Qala fir'awnu amantum bihi qabla an athana lakum inna hatha lamakrun makartumoohu fee almadeenati litukhrijoo minha ahlaha fasawfa ta'lamoona

# 1078

Laoqati'anna aydiyakum waarjulakum min khilafin thumma laosallibannakum ajma'eena

# 1079

Qaloo inna ila rabbina munqaliboona

# 1080

Wama tanqimu minna illa an amanna biayati rabbina lamma jaatna rabbana afrigh 'alayna sabran watawaffana muslimeena

# 1081

Waqala almalao min qawmi fir'awna atatharu moosa waqawmahu liyufsidoo fee alardi wayatharaka waalihataka qala sanuqattilu abnaahum wanastahyee nisaahum wainna fawqahum qahiroona

# 1082

Qala moosa liqawmihi ista'eenoo biAllahi waisbiroo inna alarda lillahi yoorithuha man yashao min 'ibadihi waal'aqibatu lilmuttaqeena

# 1083

Qaloo ootheena min qabli an tatiyana wamin ba'di ma jitana qala 'asa rabbukum an yuhlika 'aduwwakum wayastakhlifakum fee alardi fayanthura kayfa ta'maloona

# 1084

Walaqad akhathna ala fir'awna biassineena wanaqsin mina aththamarati la'allahum yaththakkaroona

# 1085

Faitha jaathumu alhasanatu qaloo lana hathihi wain tusibhum sayyiatun yattayyaroo bimoosa waman ma'ahu ala innama tairuhum 'inda Allahi walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoona

# 1086

Waqaloo mahma tatina bihi min ayatin litasharana biha fama nahnu laka bimumineena

# 1087

Faarsana 'alayhimu attoofana waaljarada waalqummala waaddafadi'a waaddama ayatin mufassalatin faistakbaroo wakanoo qawman mujrimeena

# 1088

Walamma waqa'a 'alayhimu arrijzu qaloo ya moosa od'u lana rabbaka bima 'ahida 'indaka lain kashafta 'anna arrijza lanuminanna laka walanursilanna ma'aka banee israeela

# 1089

Falamma kashafna 'anhumu arrijza ila ajalin hum balighoohu itha hum yankuthoona

# 1090

Faintaqamna minhum faaghraqnahum fee alyammi biannahum kaththaboo biayatina wakanoo 'anha ghafileena

# 1091

Waawrathna alqawma allatheena kanoo yustad'afoona mashariqa alardi wamagharibaha allatee barakna feeha watammat kalimatu rabbika alhusna 'ala banee israeela bima sabaroo wadammarna ma kana yasna'u fir'awnu waqawmuhu wama kanoo ya'rishoona

# 1092

Wajawazna bibanee israeela albahra faataw 'ala qawmin ya'kufoona 'ala asnamin lahum qaloo ya moosa ij'al lana ilahan kama lahum alihatun qala innakum qawmun tajhaloona

# 1093

Inna haolai mutabbarun ma hum feehi wabatilun ma kanoo ya'maloona

# 1094

Qala aghayra Allahi abgheekum ilahan wahuwa faddalakum 'ala al'alameena

# 1095

Waith anjaynakum min ali fir'awna yasoomoonakum sooa al'athabi yuqattiloona abnaakum wayastahyoona nisaakum wafee thalikum balaon min rabbikum 'atheemun

# 1096

Wawa'adna moosa thalatheena laylatan waatmamnaha bi'ashrin fatamma meeqatu rabbihi arba'eena laylatan waqala moosa liakheehi haroona okhlufnee fee qawmee waaslih wala tattabi' sabeela almufsideena

# 1097

Walamma jaa moosa limeeqatina wakallamahu rabbuhu qala rabbi arinee anthur ilayka qala lan taranee walakini onthur ila aljabali faini istaqarra makanahu fasawfa taranee falamma tajalla rabbuhu liljabali ja'alahu dakkan wakharra moosa sa'iqan falamma afaqa qala subhanaka tubtu ilayka waana awwalu almumineena

# 1098

Qala ya moosa innee istafaytuka 'ala annasi birisalatee wabikalamee fakhuth ma ataytuka wakun mina ashshakireena

# 1099

Wakatabna lahu fee alalwahi min kulli shayin maw'ithatan watafseelan likulli shayin fakhuthha biquwwatin wamur qawmaka yakhuthoo biahsaniha saoreekum dara alfasiqeena

# 1100

Saasrifu 'an ayatiya allatheena yatakabbaroona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi wain yaraw kulla ayatin la yuminoo biha wain yaraw sabeela arrushdi la yattakhithoohu sabeelan wain yaraw sabeela alghayyi yattakhithoohu sabeelan thalika biannahum kaththaboo biayatina wakanoo 'anha ghafileena

# 1101

Waallatheena kaththaboo biayatina waliqai alakhirati habitat a'maluhum hal yujzawna illa ma kanoo ya'maloona

# 1102

Waittakhatha qawmu moosa min ba'dihi min huliyyihim 'ijlan jasadan lahu khuwarun alam yaraw annahu la yukallimuhum wala yahdeehim sabeelan ittakhathoohu wakanoo thalimeena

# 1103

Walamma suqita fee aydeehim waraaw annahum qad dalloo qaloo lain lam yarhamna rabbuna wayaghfir lana lanakoonanna mina alkhasireena

# 1104

Walamma raja'a moosa ila qawmihi ghadbana asifan qala bisama khalaftumoonee min ba'dee a'ajiltum amra rabbikum waalqa alalwaha waakhatha birasi akheehi yajurruhu ilayhi qala ibna omma inna alqawma istad'afoonee wakadoo yaqtuloonanee fala tushmit biya ala'daa wala taj'anee ma'a alqawmi aththalimeena

# 1105

Qala rabbi ighfir lee waliakhee waadkhilna fee rahmatika waanta arhamu arrahimeena

# 1106

Inna allatheena ittakhathoo al'ijla sayanaluhum ghadabun min rabbihim wathillatun fee alhayati addunya wakathalika najzee almuftareena

# 1107

Waallatheena 'amiloo assayyiati thumma taboo min ba'diha waamanoo inna rabbaka min ba'diha laghafoorun raheemun

# 1108

Walamma sakata 'an moosa alghadabu akhatha alalwaha wafee nuskhatiha hudan warahmatun lillatheena hum lirabbihim yarhaboona

# 1109

Waikhtara moosa qawmahu sab'eena rajulan limeeqatina falamma akhathathumu arrajfatu qala rabbi law shita ahlaktahum min qablu waiyyaya atuhlikuna bima fa'ala assufahao minna in hiya illa fitnatuka tudillu biha man tashao watahdee man tashao anta waliyyuna faighfir lana wairhamna waanta khayru alghafireena

# 1110

Waoktub lana fee hathihi addunya hasanatan wafee alakhirati inna hudna ilayka qala 'athabee oseebu bihi man ashao warahmatee wasi'at kulla shayin fasaaktubuha lillatheena yattaqoona wayutoona azzakata waallatheena hum biayatina yuminoona

# 1111

Allatheena yattabi'oona arrasoola annabiyya alommiyya allathee yajidoonahu maktooban 'indahum fee attawrati waalinjeeli yamuruhum bialma'roofi wayanhahum 'ani almunkari wayuhillu lahumu attayyibati wayuharrimu 'alayhimu alkhabaitha wayada'u 'anhum israhum waalaghlala allatee kanat 'alayhim faallatheena amanoo bihi wa'azzaroohu wanasaroohu waittaba'oo annoora allathee onzila ma'ahu olaika humu almuflihoona

# 1112

Qul ya ayyuha annasu innee rasoolu Allahi ilaykum jamee'an allathee lahu mulku assamawati waalardi la ilaha illa huwa yuhyee wayumeetu faaminoo biAllahi warasoolihi annabiyyi alommiyyi allathee yuminu biAllahi wakalimatihi waittabi'oohu la'allakum tahtadoona

# 1113

Wamin qawmi moosa ommatun yahdoona bialhaqqi wabihi ya'diloona

# 1114

Waqatta'nahumu ithnatay 'ashrata asbatan omaman waawhayna ila moosa ithi istasqahu qawmuhu ani idrib bi'asaka alhajara fainbajasat minhu ithnata 'ashrata 'aynan qad 'alima kullu onasin mashrabahum wathallana 'alayhimu alghamama waanzana 'alayhimu almanna waassalwa kuloo min tayyibati ma razaqnakum wama thalamoona walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoona

# 1115

Waith qeela lahumu oskunoo hathihi alqaryata wakuloo minha haythu shitum waqooloo hittatun waodkhuloo albaba sujjadan naghfir lakum khateeatikum sanazeedu almuhsineena

# 1116

Fabaddala allatheena thalamoo minhum qawlan ghayra allathee qeela lahum faarsana 'alayhim rijzan mina assamai bima kanoo yathlimoona

# 1117

Waisalhum 'ani alqaryati allatee kanat hadirata albahri ith ya'doona fee assabti ith tateehim heetanuhum yawma sabtihim shurra'an wayawma la yasbitoona la tateehim kathalika nabloohum bima kanoo yafsuqoona

# 1118

Waith qalat ommatun minhum lima ta'ithoona qawman Allahu muhlikuhum aw mu'aththibuhum 'athaban shadeedan qaloo ma'thiratan ila rabbikum wala'allahum yattaqoona

# 1119

Falamma nasoo ma thukkiroo bihi anjayna allatheena yanhawna 'ani assooi waakhathna allatheena thalamoo bi'athabin baeesin bima kanoo yafsuqoona

# 1120

Falamma 'ataw 'an ma nuhoo 'anhu qulna lahum koonoo qiradatan khasieena

# 1121

Waith taaththana rabbuka layab'athanna 'alayhim ila yawmi alqiyamati man yasoomuhum sooa al'athabi inna rabbaka lasaree'u al'iqabi wainnahu laghafoorun raheemun

# 1122

Waqatta'nahum fee alardi omaman minhumu assalihoona waminhum doona thalika wabalawnahum bialhasanati waassayyiati la'allahum yarji'oona

# 1123

Fakhalafa min ba'dihim khalfun warithoo alkitaba yakhuthoona 'arada hatha aladna wayaqooloona sayughfaru lana wain yatihim 'aradun mithluhu yakhuthoohu alam yukhath 'alayhim meethaqu alkitabi an la yaqooloo 'ala Allahi illa alhaqqa wadarasoo ma feehi waaddaru alakhiratu khayrun lillatheena yattaqoona afala ta'qiloona

# 1124

Waallatheena yumassikoona bialkitabi waaqamoo assalata inna la nudee'u ajra almusliheena

# 1125

Waith nataqna aljabala fawqahum kaannahu thullatun wathannoo annahu waqi'un bihim khuthoo ma ataynakum biquwwatin waothkuroo ma feehi la'allakum tattaqoona

# 1126

Waith akhatha rabbuka min banee adama min thuhoorihim thurriyyatahum waashhadahum 'ala anfusihim alastu birabbikum qaloo bala shahidna an taqooloo yawma alqiyamati inna kunna 'an hatha ghafileena

# 1127

Aw taqooloo innama ashraka abaona min qablu wakunna thurriyyatan min ba'dihim afatuhlikuna bima fa'ala almubtiloona

# 1128

Wakathalika nufassilu alayati wala'allahum yarji'oona

# 1129

Waotlu 'alayhim nabaa allathee ataynahu ayatina fainsalakha minha faatba'ahu ashshaytanu fakana mina alghaweena

# 1130

Walaw shina larafa'nahu biha walakinnahu akhlada ila alardi waittaba'a hawahu famathaluhu kamathali alkalbi in tahmil 'alayhi yalhath aw tatrukhu yalhath thalika mathalu alqawmi allatheena kaththaboo biayatina faoqsusi alqasasa la'allahum yatafakkaroona

# 1131

Saa mathalan alqawmu allatheena kaththaboo biayatina waanfusahum kanoo yathlimoona

# 1132

Man yahdi Allahu fahuwa almuhtadee waman yudlil faolaika humu alkhasiroona

# 1133

Walaqad tharana lijahannama katheeran mina aljinni waalinsi lahum quloobun la yafqahoona biha walahum a'yunun la yubsiroona biha walahum athanun la yasma'oona biha olaika kaalan'ami bal hum adallu olaika humu alghafiloona

# 1134

Walillahi alasmao alhusna faod'oohu biha watharoo allatheena yulhidoona fee asmaihi sayujzawna ma kanoo ya'maloona

# 1135

Wamimman khalaqna ommatun yahdoona bialhaqqi wabihi ya'diloona

# 1136

Waallatheena kaththaboo biayatina sanastadrijuhum min haythu la ya'lamoona

# 1137

Waomlee lahum inna kaydee mateenun

# 1138

Awalam yatafakkaroo ma bisahibihim min jinnatin in huwa illa natheerun mubeenun

# 1139

Awalam yanthuroo fee malakooti assamawati waalardi wama khalaqa Allahu min shayin waan 'asa an yakoona qadi iqtaraba ajaluhum fabiayyi hadeethin ba'dahu yuminoona

# 1140

Man yudlili Allahu fala hadiya lahu wayatharuhum fee tughyanihim ya'mahoona

# 1141

Yasaloonaka 'ani assa'ati ayyana mursaha qul innama 'ilmuha 'inda rabbee la yujalleeha liwaqtiha illa huwa thaqulat fee assamawati waalardi la tateekum illa baghtatan yasaloonaka kaannaka hafiyyun 'anha qul innama 'ilmuha 'inda Allahi walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoona

# 1142

Qul la amliku linafsee naf'an wala darran illa ma shaa Allahu walaw kuntu a'lamu alghayba laistakthartu mina alkhayri wama massaniya assooo in ana illa natheerun wabasheerun liqawmin yuminoona

# 1143

Huwa allathee khalaqakum min nafsin wahidatin waja'ala minha zawjaha liyaskuna ilayha falamma taghashshaha hamalat hamlan khafeefan famarrat bihi falamma athqalat da'awa Allaha rabbahuma lain ataytana salihan lanakoonanna mina ashshakireena

# 1144

Falamma atahuma salihan ja'ala lahu shurakaa feema atahuma fata'ala Allahu 'amma yushrikoona

# 1145

Ayushrikoona ma la yakhluqu shayan wahum yukhlaqoona

# 1146

Wala yastatee'oona lahum nasran wala anfusahum yansuroona

# 1147

Wain tad'oohum ila alhuda la yattabi'ookum sawaon 'alaykum ada'awtumoohum am antum samitoona

# 1148

Inna allatheena tad'oona min dooni Allahi 'ibadun amthalukum faod'oohum falyastajeeboo lakum in kuntum sadiqeena

# 1149

Alahum arjulun yamshoona biha am lahum aydin yabtishoona biha am lahum a'yunun yubsiroona biha am lahum athanun yasma'oona biha quli od'oo shurakaakum thumma keedooni fala tunthirooni

# 1150

Inna waliyyiya Allahu allathee nazzala alkitaba wahuwa yatawalla assaliheena

# 1151

Waallatheena tad'oona min doonihi la yastatee'oona nasrakum wala anfusahum yansuroona

# 1152

Wain tad'oohum ila alhuda la yasma'oo watarahum yanthuroona ilayka wahum la yubsiroona

# 1153

Khuthi al'afwa wamur bial'urfi waa'rid 'ani aljahileena

# 1154

Waimma yanzaghannaka mina ashshaytani nazghun faista'ith biAllahi innahu samee'un 'aleemun

# 1155

Inna allatheena ittaqaw itha massahum taifun mina ashshaytani tathakkaroo faitha hum mubsiroona

# 1156

Waikhwanuhum yamuddoonahum fee alghayyi thumma la yuqsiroona

# 1157

Waitha lam tatihim biayatin qaloo lawla ijtabaytaha qul innama attabi'u ma yooha ilayya min rabbee hatha basairu min rabbikum wahudan warahmatun liqawmin yuminoona

# 1158

Waitha quria alquranu faistami'oo lahu waansitoo la'allakum turhamoona

# 1159

Waothkur rabbaka fee nafsika tadarru'an wakheefatan wadoona aljahri mina alqawli bialghuduwwi waalasali wala takun mina alghafileena

# 1160

Inna allatheena 'inda rabbika la yastakbiroona 'an 'ibadatihi wayusabbihoonahu walahu yasjudoona

# 1161

Yasaloonaka 'ani alanfali quli alanfalu lillahi waarrasooli faittaqoo Allaha waaslihoo thata baynikum waatee'oo Allaha warasoolahu in kuntum mumineena

# 1162

Innama almuminoona allatheena itha thukira Allahu wajilat quloobuhum waitha tuliyat 'alayhim ayatuhu zadathum eemanan wa'ala rabbihim yatawakkaloona

# 1163

Allatheena yuqeemoona assalata wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoona

# 1164

Olaika humu almuminoona haqqan lahum darajatun 'inda rabbihim wamaghfiratun warizqun kareemun

# 1165

Kama akhrajaka rabbuka min baytika bialhaqqi wainna fareeqan mina almumineena lakarihoona

# 1166

Yujadiloonaka fee alhaqqi ba'dama tabayyana kaannama yusaqoona ila almawti wahum yanthuroona

# 1167

Waith ya'idukumu Allahu ihda attaifatayni annaha lakum watawaddoona anna ghayra thati ashshawkati takoonu lakum wayureedu Allahu an yuhiqqa alhaqqa bikalimatihi wayaqta'a dabira alkafireena

# 1168

Liyuhiqqa alhaqqa wayubtila albatila walaw kariha almujrimoona

# 1169

Ith tastagheethoona rabbakum faistajaba lakum annee mumiddukum bialfin mina almalaikati murdifeena

# 1170

Wama ja'alahu Allahu illa bushra walitatmainna bihi quloobukum wama annasru illa min 'indi Allahi inna Allaha 'azeezun hakeemun

# 1171

Ith yughashsheekumu annu'asa amanatan minhu wayunazzilu 'alaykum mina assamai maan liyutahhirakum bihi wayuthhiba 'ankum rijza ashshaytani waliyarbita 'ala quloobikum wayuthabbita bihi alaqdama

# 1172

Ith yoohee rabbuka ila almalaikati annee ma'akum fathabbitoo allatheena amanoo saolqee fee quloobi allatheena kafaroo arru'ba faidriboo fawqa ala'naqi waidriboo minhum kulla bananin

# 1173

Thalika biannahum shaqqoo Allaha warasoolahu waman yushaqiqi Allaha warasoolahu fainna Allaha shadeedu al'iqabi

# 1174

Thalikum fathooqoohu waanna lilkafireena 'athaba annari

# 1175

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha laqeetumu allatheena kafaroo zahfan fala tuwalloohumu aladbara

# 1176

Waman yuwallihim yawmaithin duburahu illa mutaharrifan liqitalin aw mutahayyizan ila fiatin faqad baa bighadabin mina Allahi wamawahu jahannamu wabisa almaseeru

# 1177

Falam taqtuloohum walakinna Allaha qatalahum wama ramayta ith ramayta walakinna Allaha rama waliyubliya almumineena minhu balaan hasanan inna Allaha samee'un 'aleemun

# 1178

Thalikum waanna Allaha moohinu kaydi alkafireena

# 1179

In tastaftihoo faqad jaakumu alfathu wain tantahoo fahuwa khayrun lakum wain ta'oodoo na'ud walan tughniya 'ankum fiatukum shayan walaw kathurat waanna Allaha ma'a almumineena

# 1180

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo atee'oo Allaha warasoolahu wala tawallaw 'anhu waantum tasma'oona

# 1181

Wala takoonoo kaallatheena qaloo sami'na wahum la yasma'oona

# 1182

Inna sharra addawabbi 'inda Allahi assummu albukmu allatheena la ya'qiloona

# 1183

Walaw 'alima Allahu feehim khayran laasma'ahum walaw asma'ahum latawallaw wahum mu'ridoona

# 1184

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo istajeeboo lillahi walilrrasooli itha da'akum lima yuhyeekum wai'lamoo anna Allaha yahoolu bayna almari waqalbihi waannahu ilayhi tuhsharoona

# 1185

Waittaqoo fitnatan la tuseebanna allatheena thalamoo minkum khassatan wai'lamoo anna Allaha shadeedu al'iqabi

# 1186

Waothkuroo ith antum qaleelun mustad'afoona fee alardi takhafoona an yatakhattafakumu annasu faawakum waayyadakum binasrihi warazaqakum mina attayyibati la'allakum tashkuroona

# 1187

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la takhoonoo Allaha waarrasoola watakhoonoo amanatikum waantum ta'lamoona

# 1188

Wai'lamoo annama amwalukum waawladukum fitnatun waanna Allaha 'indahu ajrun 'atheemun

# 1189

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo in tattaqoo Allaha yaj'al lakum furqanan wayukaffir 'ankum sayyiatikum wayaghfir lakum waAllahu thoo alfadli al'atheemi

# 1190

Waith yamkuru bika allatheena kafaroo liyuthbitooka aw yaqtulooka aw yukhrijooka wayamkuroona wayamkuru Allahu waAllahu khayru almakireena

# 1191

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna qaloo qad sami'na law nashao laqulna mithla hatha in hatha illa asateeru alawwaleena

# 1192

Waith qaloo allahumma in kana hatha huwa alhaqqa min 'indika faamtir 'alayna hijaratan mina assamai awi itina bi'athabin aleemin

# 1193

Wama kana Allahu liyu'aththibahum waanta feehim wama kana Allahu mu'aththibahum wahum yastaghfiroona

# 1194

Wama lahum alla yu'aththibahumu Allahu wahum yasuddoona 'ani almasjidi alharami wama kanoo awliyaahu in awliyaohu illa almuttaqoona walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoona

# 1195

Wama kana salatuhum 'inda albayti illa mukaan watasdiyatan fathooqoo al'athaba bima kuntum takfuroona

# 1196

Inna allatheena kafaroo yunfiqoona amwalahum liyasuddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi fasayunfiqoonaha thumma takoonu 'alayhim hasratan thumma yughlaboona waallatheena kafaroo ila jahannama yuhsharoona

# 1197

Liyameeza Allahu alkhabeetha mina attayyibi wayaj'ala alkhabeetha ba'dahu 'ala ba'din fayarkumahu jamee'an fayaj'alahu fee jahannama olaika humu alkhasiroona

# 1198

Qul lillatheena kafaroo in yantahoo yughfar lahum ma qad salafa wain ya'oodoo faqad madat sunnatu alawwaleena

# 1199

Waqatiloohum hatta la takoona fitnatun wayakoona addeenu kulluhu lillahi faini intahaw fainna Allaha bima ya'maloona baseerun

# 1200

Wain tawallaw fai'lamoo anna Allaha mawlakum ni'ma almawla wani'ma annaseeru

# 1201

Wai'lamoo annama ghanimtum min shayin faanna lillahi khumusahu walilrrasooli walithee alqurba waalyatama waalmasakeeni waibni assabeeli in kuntum amantum biAllahi wama anzana 'ala 'abdina yawma alfurqani yawma iltaqa aljam'ani waAllahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 1202

Ith antum bial'udwati addunya wahum bial'udwati alquswa waarrakbu asfala minkum walaw tawa'adtum laikhtalaftum fee almee'adi walakin liyaqdiya Allahu amran kana maf'oolan liyahlika man halaka 'an bayyinatin wayahya man hayya 'an bayyinatin wainna Allaha lasamee'un 'aleemun

# 1203

Ith yureekahumu Allahu fee manamika qaleelan walaw arakahum katheeran lafashiltum walatanaza'tum fee alamri walakinna Allaha sallama innahu 'aleemun bithati assudoori

# 1204

Waith yureekumoohum ithi iltaqaytum fee a'yunikum qaleelan wayuqallilukum fee a'yunihim liyaqdiya Allahu amran kana maf'oolan waila Allahi turja'u alomooru

# 1205

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha laqeetum fiatan faothbutoo waothkuroo Allaha katheeran la'allakum tuflihoona

# 1206

Waatee'oo Allaha warasoolahu wala tanaza'oo fatafshaloo watathhaba reehukum waisbiroo inna Allaha ma'a assabireena

# 1207

Wala takoonoo kaallatheena kharajoo min diyarihim bataran wariaa annasi wayasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi waAllahu bima ya'maloona muheetun

# 1208

Waith zayyana lahumu ashshaytanu a'malahum waqala la ghaliba lakumu alyawma mina annasi wainnee jarun lakum falamma taraati alfiatani nakasa 'ala 'aqibayhi waqala innee bareeon minkum innee ara ma la tarawna innee akhafu Allaha waAllahu shadeedu al'iqabi

# 1209

Ith yaqoolu almunafiqoona waallatheena fee quloobihim maradun gharra haolai deenuhum waman yatawakkal 'ala Allahi fainna Allaha 'azeezun hakeemun

# 1210

Walaw tara ith yatawaffa allatheena kafaroo almalaikatu yadriboona wujoohahum waadbarahum wathooqoo 'athaba alhareeqi

# 1211

Thalika bima qaddamat aydeekum waanna Allaha laysa bithallamin lil'abeedi

# 1212

Kadabi ali fir'awna waallatheena min qablihim kafaroo biayati Allahi faakhathahumu Allahu bithunoobihim inna Allaha qawiyyun shadeedu al'iqabi

# 1213

Thalika bianna Allaha lam yaku mughayyiran ni'matan an'amaha 'ala qawmin hatta yughayyiroo ma bianfusihim waanna Allaha samee'un 'aleemun

# 1214

Kadabi ali fir'awna waallatheena min qablihim kaththaboo biayati rabbihim faahlaknahum bithunoobihim waaghraqna ala fir'awna wakullun kanoo thalimeena

# 1215

Inna sharra addawabbi 'inda Allahi allatheena kafaroo fahum la yuminoona

# 1216

Allatheena 'ahadta minhum thumma yanqudoona 'ahdahum fee kulli marratin wahum la yattaqoona

# 1217

Faimma tathqafannahum fee alharbi fasharrid bihim man khalfahum la'allahum yaththakkaroona

# 1218

Waimma takhafanna min qawmin khiyanatan fainbith ilayhim 'ala sawain inna Allaha la yuhibbu alkhaineena

# 1219

Wala yahsabanna allatheena kafaroo sabaqoo innahum la yu'jizoona

# 1220

Waa'iddoo lahum ma istata'tum min quwwatin wamin ribati alkhayli turhiboona bihi 'aduwwa Allahi wa'aduwwakum waakhareena min doonihim la ta'lamoonahumu Allahu ya'lamuhum wama tunfiqoo min shayin fee sabeeli Allahi yuwaffa ilaykum waantum la tuthlamoona

# 1221

Wain janahoo lilssalmi faijnah laha watawakkal 'ala Allahi innahu huwa assamee'u al'aleemu

# 1222

Wain yureedoo an yakhda'ooka fainna hasbaka Allahu huwa allathee ayyadaka binasrihi wabialmumineena

# 1223

Waallafa bayna quloobihim law anfaqta ma fee alardi jamee'an ma allafta bayna quloobihim walakinna Allaha allafa baynahum innahu 'azeezun hakeemun

# 1224

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu hasbuka Allahu wamani ittaba'aka mina almumineena

# 1225

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu harridi almumineena 'ala alqitali in yakun minkum 'ishroona sabiroona yaghliboo miatayni wain yakun minkum miatun yaghliboo alfan mina allatheena kafaroo biannahum qawmun la yafqahoona

# 1226

Alana khaffafa Allahu 'ankum wa'alima anna feekum da'fan fain yakun minkum miatun sabiratun yaghliboo miatayni wain yakun minkum alfun yaghliboo alfayni biithni Allahi waAllahu ma'a assabireena

# 1227

Ma kana linabiyyin an yakoona lahu asra hatta yuthkhina fee alardi tureedoona 'arada addunya waAllahu yureedu alakhirata waAllahu 'azeezun hakeemun

# 1228

Lawla kitabun mina Allahi sabaqa lamassakum feema akhathtum 'athabun 'atheemun

# 1229

Fakuloo mimma ghanimtum halalan tayyiban waittaqoo Allaha inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun

# 1230

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu qul liman fee aydeekum mina alasra in ya'lami Allahu fee quloobikum khayran yutikum khayran mimma okhitha minkum wayaghfir lakum waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun

# 1231

Wain yureedoo khiyanataka faqad khanoo Allaha min qablu faamkana minhum waAllahu 'aleemun hakeemun

# 1232

Inna allatheena amanoo wahajaroo wajahadoo biamwalihim waanfusihim fee sabeeli Allahi waallatheena awaw wanasaroo olaika ba'duhum awliyao ba'din waallatheena amanoo walam yuhajiroo ma lakum min walayatihim min shayin hatta yuhajiroo waini istansarookum fee addeeni fa'alaykumu annasru illa 'ala qawmin baynakum wabaynahum meethaqun waAllahu bima ta'maloona baseerun

# 1233

Waallatheena kafaroo ba'duhum awliyao ba'din illa taf'aloohu takun fitnatun fee alardi wafasadun kabeerun

# 1234

Waallatheena amanoo wahajaroo wajahadoo fee sabeeli Allahi waallatheena awaw wanasaroo olaika humu almuminoona haqqan lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareemun

# 1235

Waallatheena amanoo min ba'du wahajaroo wajahadoo ma'akum faolaika minkum waoloo alarhami ba'duhum awla biba'din fee kitabi Allahi inna Allaha bikulli shayin 'aleemun

# 1236

Baraatun mina Allahi warasoolihi ila allatheena 'ahadtum mina almushrikeena

# 1237

Faseehoo fee alardi arba'ata ashhurin wai'lamoo annakum ghayru mu'jizee Allahi waanna Allaha mukhzee alkafireena

# 1238

Waathanun mina Allahi warasoolihi ila annasi yawma alhajji alakbari anna Allaha bareeon mina almushrikeena warasooluhu fain tubtum fahuwa khayrun lakum wain tawallaytum fai'lamoo annakum ghayru mu'jizee Allahi wabashshiri allatheena kafaroo bi'athabin aleemin

# 1239

Illa allatheena 'ahadtum mina almushrikeena thumma lam yanqusookum shayan walam yuthahiroo 'alaykum ahadan faatimmoo ilayhim 'ahdahum ila muddatihim inna Allaha yuhibbu almuttaqeena

# 1240

Faitha insalakha alashhuru alhurumu faoqtuloo almushrikeena haythu wajadtumoohum wakhuthoohum waohsuroohum waoq'udoo lahum kulla marsadin fain taboo waaqamoo assalata waatawoo azzakata fakhalloo sabeelahum inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun

# 1241

Wain ahadun mina almushrikeena istajaraka faajirhu hatta yasma'a kalama Allahi thumma ablighhu mamanahu thalika biannahum qawmun la ya'lamoona

# 1242

Kayfa yakoonu lilmushrikeena 'ahdun 'inda Allahi wa'inda rasoolihi illa allatheena 'ahadtum 'inda almasjidi alharami fama istaqamoo lakum faistaqeemoo lahum inna Allaha yuhibbu almuttaqeena

# 1243

Kayfa wain yathharoo 'alaykum la yarquboo feekum illan wala thimmatan yurdoonakum biafwahihim wataba quloobuhum waaktharuhum fasiqoona

# 1244

Ishtaraw biayati Allahi thamanan qaleelan fasaddoo 'an sabeelihi innahum saa ma kanoo ya'maloona

# 1245

La yarquboona fee muminin illan wala thimmatan waolaika humu almu'tadoona

# 1246

Fain taboo waaqamoo assalata waatawoo azzakata faikhwanukum fee addeeni wanufassilu alayati liqawmin ya'lamoona

# 1247

Wain nakathoo aymanahum min ba'di 'ahdihim wata'anoo fee deenikum faqatiloo aimmata alkufri innahum la aymana lahum la'allahum yantahoona

# 1248

Ala tuqatiloona qawman nakathoo aymanahum wahammoo biikhraji arrasooli wahum badaookum awwala marratin atakhshawnahum faAllahu ahaqqu an takhshawhu in kuntum mumineena

# 1249

Qatiloohum yu'aththibhumu Allahu biaydeekum wayukhzihim wayansurkum 'alayhim wayashfi sudoora qawmin mumineena

# 1250

Wayuthhib ghaytha quloobihim wayatoobu Allahu 'ala man yashao waAllahu 'aleemun hakeemun

# 1251

Am hasibtum an tutrakoo walamma ya'lami Allahu allatheena jahadoo minkum walam yattakhithoo min dooni Allahi wala rasoolihi wala almumineena waleejatan waAllahu khabeerun bima ta'maloona

# 1252

Ma kana lilmushrikeena an ya'muroo masajida Allahi shahideena 'ala anfusihim bialkufri olaika habitat a'maluhum wafee annari hum khalidoona

# 1253

Innama ya'muru masajida Allahi man amana biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri waaqama assalata waata azzakata walam yakhsha illa Allaha fa'asa olaika an yakoonoo mina almuhtadeena

# 1254

Aja'atum siqayata alhajji wa'imarata almasjidi alharami kaman amana biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri wajahada fee sabeeli Allahi la yastawoona 'inda Allahi waAllahu la yahdee alqawma aththalimeena

# 1255

Allatheena amanoo wahajaroo wajahadoo fee sabeeli Allahi biamwalihim waanfusihim a'thamu darajatan 'inda Allahi waolaika humu alfaizoona

# 1256

Yubashshiruhum rabbuhum birahmatin minhu waridwanin wajannatin lahum feeha na'eemun muqeemun

# 1257

Khalideena feeha abadan inna Allaha 'indahu ajrun 'atheemun

# 1258

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattakhithoo abaakum waikhwanakum awliyaa ini istahabboo alkufra 'ala aleemani waman yatawallahum minkum faolaika humu aththalimoona

# 1259

Qul in kana abaokum waabnaokum waikhwanukum waazwajukum wa'asheeratukum waamwalun iqtaraftumooha watijaratun takhshawna kasadaha wamasakinu tardawnaha ahabba ilaykum mina Allahi warasoolihi wajihadin fee sabeelihi fatarabbasoo hatta yatiya Allahu biamrihi waAllahu la yahdee alqawma alfasiqeena

# 1260

Laqad nasarakumu Allahu fee mawatina katheeratin wayawma hunaynin ith a'jabatkum kathratukum falam tughni 'ankum shayan wadaqat 'alaykumu alardu bima rahubat thumma wallaytum mudbireena

# 1261

Thumma anzala Allahu sakeenatahu 'ala rasoolihi wa'ala almumineena waanzala junoodan lam tarawha wa'aththaba allatheena kafaroo wathalika jazao alkafireena

# 1262

Thumma yatoobu Allahu min ba'di thalika 'ala man yashao waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun

# 1263

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo innama almushrikoona najasun fala yaqraboo almasjida alharama ba'da 'amihim hatha wain khiftum 'aylatan fasawfa yughneekumu Allahu min fadlihi in shaa inna Allaha 'aleemun hakeemun

# 1264

Qatiloo allatheena la yuminoona biAllahi wala bialyawmi alakhiri wala yuharrimoona ma harrama Allahu warasooluhu wala yadeenoona deena alhaqqi mina allatheena ootoo alkitaba hatta yu'too aljizyata 'an yadin wahum saghiroona

# 1265

Waqalati alyahoodu 'uzayrun ibnu Allahi waqalati annasara almaseehu ibnu Allahi thalika qawluhum biafwahihim yudahioona qawla allatheena kafaroo min qablu qatalahumu Allahu anna yufakoona

# 1266

Ittakhathoo ahbarahum waruhbanahum arbaban min dooni Allahi waalmaseeha ibna maryama wama omiroo illa liya'budoo ilahan wahidan la ilaha illa huwa subhanahu 'amma yushrikoona

# 1267

Yureedoona an yutfioo noora Allahi biafwahihim wayaba Allahu illa an yutimma noorahu walaw kariha alkafiroona

# 1268

Huwa allathee arsala rasoolahu bialhuda wadeeni alhaqqi liyuthhirahu 'ala addeeni kullihi walaw kariha almushrikoona

# 1269

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo inna katheeran mina alahbari waarruhbani layakuloona amwala annasi bialbatili wayasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi waallatheena yaknizoona aththahaba waalfiddata wala yunfiqoonaha fee sabeeli Allahi fabashshirhum bi'athabin aleemin

# 1270

Yawma yuhma 'alayha fee nari jahannama fatukwa biha jibahuhum wajunoobuhum wathuhooruhum hatha ma kanaztum lianfusikum fathooqoo ma kuntum taknizoona

# 1271

Inna 'iddata ashshuhoori 'inda Allahi ithna 'ashara shahran fee kitabi Allahi yawma khalaqa assamawati waalarda minha arba'atun hurumun thalika addeenu alqayyimu fala tathlimoo feehinna anfusakum waqatiloo almushrikeena kaffatan kama yuqatiloonakum kaffatan wai'lamoo anna Allaha ma'a almuttaqeena

# 1272

Innama annaseeo ziyadatun fee alkufri yudallu bihi allatheena kafaroo yuhilloonahu 'aman wayuharrimoonahu 'aman liyuwatioo 'iddata ma harrama Allahu fayuhilloo ma harrama Allahu zuyyina lahum sooo a'malihim waAllahu la yahdee alqawma alkafireena

# 1273

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ma lakum itha qeela lakumu infiroo fee sabeeli Allahi iththaqatum ila alardi aradeetum bialhayati addunya mina alakhirati fama mata'u alhayati addunya fee alakhirati illa qaleelun

# 1274

Illa tanfiroo yu'aththibkum 'athaban aleeman wayastabdil qawman ghayrakum wala tadurroohu shayan waAllahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 1275

Illa tansuroohu faqad nasarahu Allahu ith akhrajahu allatheena kafaroo thaniya ithnayni ith huma fee alghari ith yaqoolu lisahibihi la tahzan inna Allaha ma'ana faanzala Allahu sakeenatahu 'alayhi waayyadahu bijunoodin lam tarawha waja'ala kalimata allatheena kafaroo assufla wakalimatu Allahi hiya al'ulya waAllahu 'azeezun hakeemun

# 1276

Infiroo khifafan wathiqalan wajahidoo biamwalikum waanfusikum fee sabeeli Allahi thalikum khayrun lakum in kuntum ta'lamoona

# 1277

Law kana 'aradan qareeban wasafaran qasidan laittaba'ooka walakin ba'udat 'alayhimu ashshuqqatu wasayahlifoona biAllahi lawi istata'na lakharajna ma'akum yuhlikoona anfusahum waAllahu ya'lamu innahum lakathiboona

# 1278

'afa Allahu 'anka lima athinta lahum hatta yatabayyana laka allatheena sadaqoo wata'lama alkathibeena

# 1279

La yastathinuka allatheena yuminoona biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri an yujahidoo biamwalihim waanfusihim waAllahu 'aleemun bialmuttaqeena

# 1280

Innama yastathinuka allatheena la yuminoona biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri wairtabat quloobuhum fahum fee raybihim yataraddadoona

# 1281

Walaw aradoo alkhurooja laa'addoo lahu 'uddatan walakin kariha Allahu inbi'athahum fathabbatahum waqeela oq'udoo ma'a alqa'ideena

# 1282

Law kharajoo feekum ma zadookum illa khabalan walaawda'oo khilalakum yabghoonakumu alfitnata wafeekum samma'oona lahum waAllahu 'aleemun biaththalimeena

# 1283

Laqadi ibtaghawoo alfitnata min qablu waqallaboo laka alomoora hatta jaa alhaqqu wathahara amru Allahi wahum karihoona

# 1284

Waminhum man yaqoolu ithan lee wala taftinnee ala fee alfitnati saqatoo wainna jahannama lamuheetatun bialkafireena

# 1285

In tusibka hasanatun tasuhum wain tusibka museebatun yaqooloo qad akhathna amrana min qablu wayatawallaw wahum farihoona

# 1286

Qul lan yuseebana illa ma kataba Allahu lana huwa mawlana wa'ala Allahi falyatawakkali almuminoona

# 1287

Qul hal tarabbasoona bina illa ihda alhusnayayni wanahnu natarabbasu bikum an yuseebakumu Allahu bi'athabin min 'indihi aw biaydeena fatarabbasoo inna ma'akum mutarabbisoona

# 1288

Qul anfiqoo taw'an aw karhan lan yutaqabbala minkum innakum kuntum qawman fasiqeena

# 1289

Wama mana'ahum an tuqbala minhum nafaqatuhum illa annahum kafaroo biAllahi wabirasoolihi wala yatoona assalata illa wahum kusala wala yunfiqoona illa wahum karihoona

# 1290

Fala tu'jibka amwaluhum wala awladuhum innama yureedu Allahu liyu'aththibahum biha fee alhayati addunya watazhaqa anfusuhum wahum kafiroona

# 1291

Wayahlifoona biAllahi innahum laminkum wama hum minkum walakinnahum qawmun yafraqoona

# 1292

Law yajidoona maljaan aw magharatin aw muddakhalan lawallaw ilayhi wahum yajmahoona

# 1293

Waminhum man yalmizuka fee assadaqati fain o'too minha radoo wain lam yu'taw minha itha hum yaskhatoona

# 1294

Walaw annahum radoo ma atahumu Allahu warasooluhu waqaloo hasbuna Allahu sayuteena Allahu min fadlihi warasooluhu inna ila Allahi raghiboona

# 1295

Innama assadaqatu lilfuqarai waalmasakeeni waal'amileena 'alayha waalmuallafati quloobuhum wafee arriqabi waalgharimeena wafee sabeeli Allahi waibni assabeeli fareedatan mina Allahi waAllahu 'aleemun hakeemun

# 1296

Waminhumu allatheena yuthoona annabiyya wayaqooloona huwa othunun qul othunu khayrin lakum yuminu biAllahi wayuminu lilmumineena warahmatun lillatheena amanoo minkum waallatheena yuthoona rasoola Allahi lahum 'athabun aleemun

# 1297

Yahlifoona biAllahi lakum liyurdookum waAllahu warasooluhu ahaqqu an yurdoohu in kanoo mumineena

# 1298

Alam ya'lamoo annahu man yuhadidi Allaha warasoolahu faanna lahu nara jahannama khalidan feeha thalika alkhizyu al'atheemu

# 1299

Yahtharu almunafiqoona an tunazzala 'alayhim sooratun tunabbiohum bima fee quloobihim quli istahzioo inna Allaha mukhrijun ma tahtharoona

# 1300

Walain saatahum layaqoolunna innama kunna nakhoodu wanal'abu qul abiAllahi waayatihi warasoolihi kuntum tastahzioona

# 1301

La ta'tathiroo qad kafartum ba'da eemanikum in na'fu 'an taifatin minkum nu'aththib taifatan biannahum kanoo mujrimeena

# 1302

Almunafiqoona waalmunafiqatu ba'duhum min ba'din yamuroona bialmunkari wayanhawna 'ani alma'roofi wayaqbidoona aydiyahum nasoo Allaha fanasiyahum inna almunafiqeena humu alfasiqoona

# 1303

Wa'ada Allahu almunafiqeena waalmunafiqati waalkuffara nara jahannama khalideena feeha hiya hasbuhum wala'anahumu Allahu walahum 'athabun muqeemun

# 1304

Kaallatheena min qablikum kanoo ashadda minkum quwwatan waakthara amwalan waawladan faistamta'oo bikhalaqihim faistamta'tum bikhalaqikum kama istamta'a allatheena min qablikum bikhalaqihim wakhudtum kaallathee khadoo olaika habitat a'maluhum fee addunya waalakhirati waolaika humu alkhasiroona

# 1305

Alam yatihim nabao allatheena min qablihim qawmi noohin wa'adin wathamooda waqawmi ibraheema waashabi madyana waalmutafikati atathum rusuluhum bialbayyinati fama kana Allahu liyathlimahum walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoona

# 1306

Waalmuminoona waalmuminatu ba'duhum awliyao ba'din yamuroona bialma'roofi wayanhawna 'ani almunkari wayuqeemoona assalata wayutoona azzakata wayutee'oona Allaha warasoolahu olaika sayarhamuhumu Allahu inna Allaha 'azeezun hakeemun

# 1307

Wa'ada Allahu almumineena waalmuminati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha wamasakina tayyibatan fee jannati 'adnin waridwanun mina Allahi akbaru thalika huwa alfawzu al'atheemu

# 1308

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu jahidi alkuffara waalmunafiqeena waoghluth 'alayhim wamawahum jahannamu wabisa almaseeru

# 1309

Yahlifoona biAllahi ma qaloo walaqad qaloo kalimata alkufri wakafaroo ba'da islamihim wahammoo bima lam yanaloo wama naqamoo illa an aghnahumu Allahu warasooluhu min fadlihi fain yatooboo yaku khayran lahum wain yatawallaw yu'aththibhumu Allahu 'athaban aleeman fee addunya waalakhirati wama lahum fee alardi min waliyyin wala naseerin

# 1310

Waminhum man 'ahada Allaha lain atana min fadlihi lanassaddaqanna walanakoonanna mina assaliheena

# 1311

Falamma atahum min fadlihi bakhiloo bihi watawallaw wahum mu'ridoona

# 1312

Faa'qabahum nifaqan fee quloobihim ila yawmi yalqawnahu bima akhlafoo Allaha ma wa'adoohu wabima kanoo yakthiboona

# 1313

Alam ya'lamoo anna Allaha ya'lamu sirrahum wanajwahum waanna Allaha 'allamu alghuyoobi

# 1314

Allatheena yalmizoona almuttawwi'eena mina almumineena fee assadaqati waallatheena la yajidoona illa juhdahum fayaskharoona minhum sakhira Allahu minhum walahum 'athabun aleemun

# 1315

Istaghfir lahum aw la tastaghfir lahum in tastaghfir lahum sab'eena marratan falan yaghfira Allahu lahum thalika biannahum kafaroo biAllahi warasoolihi waAllahu la yahdee alqawma alfasiqeena

# 1316

Fariha almukhallafoona bimaq'adihim khilafa rasooli Allahi wakarihoo an yujahidoo biamwalihim waanfusihim fee sabeeli Allahi waqaloo la tanfiroo fee alharri qul naru jahannama ashaddu harran law kanoo yafqahoona

# 1317

Falyadhakoo qaleelan walyabkoo katheeran jazaan bima kanoo yaksiboona

# 1318

Fain raja'aka Allahu ila taifatin minhum faistathanooka lilkhurooji faqul lan takhrujoo ma'iya abadan walan tuqatiloo ma'iya 'aduwwan innakum radeetum bialqu'oodi awwala marratin faoq'udoo ma'a alkhalifeena

# 1319

Wala tusalli 'ala ahadin minhum mata abadan wala taqum 'ala qabrihi innahum kafaroo biAllahi warasoolihi wamatoo wahum fasiqoona

# 1320

Wala tu'jibka amwaluhum waawladuhum innama yureedu Allahu an yu'aththibahum biha fee addunya watazhaqa anfusuhum wahum kafiroona

# 1321

Waitha onzilat sooratun an aminoo biAllahi wajahidoo ma'a rasoolihi istathanaka oloo attawli minhum waqaloo tharna nakun ma'a alqa'ideena

# 1322

Radoo bian yakoonoo ma'a alkhawalifi watubi'a 'ala quloobihim fahum la yafqahoona

# 1323

Lakini arrasoolu waallatheena amanoo ma'ahu jahadoo biamwalihim waanfusihim waolaika lahumu alkhayratu waolaika humu almuflihoona

# 1324

a'adda Allahu lahum jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha thalika alfawzu al'atheemu

# 1325

Wajaa almu'aththiroona mina ala'rabi liyuthana lahum waqa'ada allatheena kathaboo Allaha warasoolahu sayuseebu allatheena kafaroo minhum 'athabun aleemun

# 1326

Laysa 'ala addu'afai wala 'ala almarda wala 'ala allatheena la yajidoona ma yunfiqoona harajun itha nasahoo lillahi warasoolihi ma 'ala almuhsineena min sabeelin waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun

# 1327

Wala 'ala allatheena itha ma atawka litahmilahum qulta la ajidu ma ahmilukum 'alayhi tawallaw waa'yunuhum tafeedu mina addam'i hazanan alla yajidoo ma yunfiqoona

# 1328

Innama assabeelu 'ala allatheena yastathinoonaka wahum aghniyao radoo bian yakoonoo ma'a alkhawalifi wataba'a Allahu 'ala quloobihim fahum la ya'lamoona

# 1329

Ya'tathiroona ilaykum itha raja'tum ilayhim qul la ta'tathiroo lan numina lakum qad nabbaana Allahu min akhbarikum wasayara Allahu 'amalakum warasooluhu thumma turaddoona ila 'alimi alghaybi waashshahadati fayunabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloona

# 1330

Sayahlifoona biAllahi lakum itha inqalabtum ilayhim litu'ridoo 'anhum faa'ridoo 'anhum innahum rijsun wamawahum jahannamu jazaan bima kanoo yaksiboona

# 1331

Yahlifoona lakum litardaw 'anhum fain tardaw 'anhum fainna Allaha la yarda 'ani alqawmi alfasiqeena

# 1332

Ala'rabu ashaddu kufran wanifaqan waajdaru alla ya'lamoo hudooda ma anzala Allahu 'ala rasoolihi waAllahu 'aleemun hakeemun

# 1333

Wamina ala'rabi man yattakhithu ma yunfiqu maghraman wayatarabbasu bikumu addawaira 'alayhim dairatu assawi waAllahu samee'un 'aleemun

# 1334

Wamina ala'rabi man yuminu biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri wayattakhithu ma yunfiqu qurubatin 'inda Allahi wasalawati arrasooli ala innaha qurbatun lahum sayudkhiluhumu Allahu fee rahmatihi inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun

# 1335

Waassabiqoona alawwaloona mina almuhajireena waalansari waallatheena ittaba'oohum biihsanin radiya Allahu 'anhum waradoo 'anhu waa'adda lahum jannatin tajree tahtaha alanharu khalideena feeha abadan thalika alfawzu al'atheemu

# 1336

Wamimman hawlakum mina ala'rabi munafiqoona wamin ahli almadeenati maradoo 'ala annifaqi la ta'lamuhum nahnu na'lamuhum sanu'aththibuhum marratayni thumma yuraddoona ila 'athabin 'atheemin

# 1337

Waakharoona i'tarafoo bithunoobihim khalatoo 'amalan salihan waakhara sayyian 'asa Allahu an yatooba 'alayhim inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun

# 1338

Khuth min amwalihim sadaqatan tutahhiruhum watuzakkeehim biha wasalli 'alayhim inna salataka sakanun lahum waAllahu samee'un 'aleemun

# 1339

Alam ya'lamoo anna Allaha huwa yaqbalu attawbata 'an 'ibadihi wayakhuthu assadaqati waanna Allaha huwa attawwabu arraheemu

# 1340

Waquli i'maloo fasayara Allahu 'amalakum warasooluhu waalmuminoona wasaturaddoona ila 'alimi alghaybi waashshahadati fayunabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloona

# 1341

Waakharoona murjawna liamri Allahi imma yu'aththibuhum waimma yatoobu 'alayhim waAllahu 'aleemun hakeemun

# 1342

Waallatheena ittakhathoo masjidan diraran wakufran watafreeqan bayna almumineena wairsadan liman haraba Allaha warasoolahu min qablu walayahlifunna in aradna illa alhusna waAllahu yashhadu innahum lakathiboona

# 1343

La taqum feehi abadan lamasjidun ossisa 'ala attaqwa min awwali yawmin ahaqqu an taqooma feehi feehi rijalun yuhibboona an yatatahharoo waAllahu yuhibbu almuttahhireena

# 1344

Afaman assasa bunyanahu 'ala taqwa mina Allahi waridwanin khayrun am man assasa bunyanahu 'ala shafa jurufin harin fainhara bihi fee nari jahannama waAllahu la yahdee alqawma aththalimeena

# 1345

La yazalu bunyanuhumu allathee banaw reebatan fee quloobihim illa an taqatta'a quloobuhum waAllahu 'aleemun hakeemun

# 1346

Inna Allaha ishtara mina almumineena anfusahum waamwalahum bianna lahumu aljannata yuqatiloona fee sabeeli Allahi fayaqtuloona wayuqtaloona wa'dan 'alayhi haqqan fee attawrati waalinjeeli waalqurani waman awfa bi'ahdihi mina Allahi faistabshiroo bibay'ikumu allathee baya'tum bihi wathalika huwa alfawzu al'atheemu

# 1347

attaiboona al'abidoona alhamidoona assaihoona arraki'oona assajidoona alamiroona bialma'roofi waannahoona 'ani almunkari waalhafithoona lihudoodi Allahi wabashshiri almumineena

# 1348

Ma kana lilnnabiyyi waallatheena amanoo an yastaghfiroo lilmushrikeena walaw kanoo olee qurba min ba'di ma tabayyana lahum annahum ashabu aljaheemi

# 1349

Wama kana istighfaru ibraheema liabeehi illa 'an maw'idatin wa'adaha iyyahu falamma tabayyana lahu annahu 'aduwwun lillahi tabarraa minhu inna ibraheema laawwahun haleemun

# 1350

Wama kana Allahu liyudilla qawman ba'da ith hadahum hatta yubayyina lahum ma yattaqoona inna Allaha bikulli shayin 'aleemun

# 1351

Inna Allaha lahu mulku assamawati waalardi yuhyee wayumeetu wama lakum min dooni Allahi min waliyyin wala naseerin

# 1352

Laqad taba Allahu 'ala annabiyyi waalmuhajireena waalansari allatheena ittaba'oohu fee sa'ati al'usrati min ba'di ma kada yazeeghu quloobu fareeqin minhum thumma taba 'alayhim innahu bihim raoofun raheemun

# 1353

Wa'ala aththalathati allatheena khullifoo hatta itha daqat 'alayhimu alardu bima rahubat wadaqat 'alayhim anfusuhum wathannoo an la maljaa mina Allahi illa ilayhi thumma taba 'alayhim liyatooboo inna Allaha huwa attawwabu arraheemu

# 1354

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha wakoonoo ma'a assadiqeena

# 1355

Ma kana liahli almadeenati waman hawlahum mina ala'rabi an yatakhallafoo 'an rasooli Allahi wala yarghaboo bianfusihim 'an nafsihi thalika biannahum la yuseebuhum thamaon wala nasabun wala makhmasatun fee sabeeli Allahi wala yataoona mawtian yagheethu alkuffara wala yanaloona min 'aduwwin naylan illa kutiba lahum bihi 'amalun salihun inna Allaha la yudee'u ajra almuhsineena

# 1356

Wala yunfiqoona nafaqatan sagheeratan wala kabeeratan wala yaqta'oona wadiyan illa kutiba lahum liyajziyahumu Allahu ahsana ma kanoo ya'maloona

# 1357

Wama kana almuminoona liyanfiroo kaffatan falawla nafara min kulli firqatin minhum taifatun liyatafaqqahoo fee addeeni waliyunthiroo qawmahum itha raja'oo ilayhim la'allahum yahtharoona

# 1358

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo qatiloo allatheena yaloonakum mina alkuffari walyajidoo feekum ghilthatan wai'lamoo anna Allaha ma'a almuttaqeena

# 1359

Waitha ma onzilat sooratun faminhum man yaqoolu ayyukum zadathu hathihi eemanan faamma allatheena amanoo fazadathum eemanan wahum yastabshiroona

# 1360

Waamma allatheena fee quloobihim maradun fazadathum rijsan ila rijsihim wamatoo wahum kafiroona

# 1361

Awala yarawna annahum yuftanoona fee kulli 'amin marratan aw marratayni thumma la yatooboona wala hum yaththakkaroona

# 1362

Waitha ma onzilat sooratun nathara ba'duhum ila ba'din hal yarakum min ahadin thumma insarafoo sarafa Allahu quloobahum biannahum qawmun la yafqahoona

# 1363

Laqad jaakum rasoolun min anfusikum 'azeezun 'alayhi ma 'anittum hareesun 'alaykum bialmumineena raoofun raheemun

# 1364

Fain tawallaw faqul hasbiya Allahu la ilaha illa huwa 'alayhi tawakkatu wahuwa rabbu al'arshi al'atheemi

# 1365

Aliflamra tilka ayatu alkitabi alhakeemi

# 1366

Akana lilnnasi 'ajaban an awhayna ila rajulin minhum an anthiri annasa wabashshiri allatheena amanoo anna lahum qadama sidqin 'inda rabbihim qala alkafiroona inna hatha lasahirun mubeenun

# 1367

Inna rabbakumu Allahu allathee khalaqa assamawati waalarda fee sittati ayyamin thumma istawa 'ala al'arshi yudabbiru alamra ma min shafee'in illa min ba'di ithnihi thalikumu Allahu rabbukum fao'budoohu afala tathakkaroona

# 1368

Ilayhi marji'ukum jamee'an wa'da Allahi haqqan innahu yabdao alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu liyajziya allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati bialqisti waallatheena kafaroo lahum sharabun min hameemin wa'athabun aleemun bima kanoo yakfuroona

# 1369

Huwa allathee ja'ala ashshamsa diyaan waalqamara nooran waqaddarahu manazila lita'lamoo 'adada assineena waalhisaba ma khalaqa Allahu thalika illa bialhaqqi yufassilu alayati liqawmin ya'lamoona

# 1370

Inna fee ikhtilafi allayli waannahari wama khalaqa Allahu fee assamawati waalardi laayatin liqawmin yattaqoona

# 1371

Inna allatheena la yarjoona liqaana waradoo bialhayati addunya waitmaannoo biha waallatheena hum 'an ayatina ghafiloona

# 1372

Olaika mawahumu annaru bima kanoo yaksiboona

# 1373

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati yahdeehim rabbuhum bieemanihim tajree min tahtihimu alanharu fee jannati anna'eemi

# 1374

Da'wahum feeha subhanaka allahumma watahiyyatuhum feeha salamun waakhiru da'wahum ani alhamdu lillahi rabbi al'alameena

# 1375

Walaw yu'ajjilu Allahu lilnnasi ashsharra isti'jalahum bialkhayri laqudiya ilayhim ajaluhum fanatharu allatheena la yarjoona liqaana fee tughyanihim ya'mahoona

# 1376

Waitha massa alinsana addurru da'ana lijanbihi aw qa'idan aw qaiman falamma kashafna 'anhu durrahu marra kaan lam yad'una ila durrin massahu kathalika zuyyina lilmusrifeena ma kanoo ya'maloona

# 1377

Walaqad ahlakna alquroona min qablikum lamma thalamoo wajaathum rusuluhum bialbayyinati wama kanoo liyuminoo kathalika najzee alqawma almujrimeena

# 1378

Thumma ja'anakum khalaifa fee alardi min ba'dihim linanthura kayfa ta'maloona

# 1379

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna bayyinatin qala allatheena la yarjoona liqaana iti biquranin ghayri hatha aw baddilhu qul ma yakoonu lee an obaddilahu min tilqai nafsee in attabi'u illa ma yooha ilayya innee akhafu in 'asaytu rabbee 'athaba yawmin 'atheemin

# 1380

Qul law shaa Allahu ma talawtuhu 'alaykum wala adrakum bihi faqad labithtu feekum 'umuran min qablihi afala ta'qiloona

# 1381

Faman athlamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban aw kaththaba biayatihi innahu la yuflihu almujrimoona

# 1382

Waya'budoona min dooni Allahi ma la yadurruhum wala yanfa'uhum wayaqooloona haolai shufa'aona 'inda Allahi qul atunabbioona Allaha bima la ya'lamu fee assamawati wala fee alardi subhanahu wata'ala 'amma yushrikoona

# 1383

Wama kana annasu illa ommatan wahidatan faikhtalafoo walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika laqudiya baynahum feema feehi yakhtalifoona

# 1384

Wayaqooloona lawla onzila 'alayhi ayatun min rabbihi faqul innama alghaybu lillahi faintathiroo innee ma'akum mina almuntathireena

# 1385

Waitha athaqna annasa rahmatan min ba'di darraa massathum itha lahum makrun fee ayatina quli Allahu asra'u makran inna rusulana yaktuboona ma tamkuroona

# 1386

Huwa allathee yusayyirukum fee albarri waalbahri hatta itha kuntum fee alfulki wajarayna bihim bireehin tayyibatin wafarihoo biha jaatha reehun 'asifun wajaahumu almawju min kulli makanin wathannoo annahum oheeta bihim da'awoo Allaha mukhliseena lahu addeena lain anjaytana min hathihi lanakoonanna mina ashshakireena

# 1387

Falamma anjahum itha hum yabghoona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi ya ayyuha annasu innama baghyukum 'ala anfusikum mata'a alhayati addunya thumma ilayna marji'ukum fanunabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloona

# 1388

Innama mathalu alhayati addunya kamain anzanahu mina assamai faikhtalata bihi nabatu alardi mimma yakulu annasu waalan'amu hatta itha akhathati alardu zukhrufaha waizzayyanat wathanna ahluha annahum qadiroona 'alayha ataha amruna laylan aw naharan faja'anaha haseedan kaan lam taghna bialamsi kathalika nufassilu alayati liqawmin yatafakkaroona

# 1389

WaAllahu yad'oo ila dari assalami wayahdee man yashao ila siratin mustaqeemin

# 1390

Lillatheena ahsanoo alhusna waziyadatun wala yarhaqu wujoohahum qatarun wala thillatun olaika ashabu aljannati hum feeha khalidoona

# 1391

Waallatheena kasaboo assayyiati jazao sayyiatin bimithliha watarhaquhum thillatun ma lahum mina Allahi min 'asimin kaannama oghshiyat wujoohuhum qita'an mina allayli muthliman olaika ashabu annari hum feeha khalidoona

# 1392

Wayawma nahshuruhum jamee'an thumma naqoolu lillatheena ashrakoo makanakum antum washurakaokum fazayyana baynahum waqala shurakaohum ma kuntum iyyana ta'budoona

# 1393

Fakafa biAllahi shaheedan baynana wabaynakum in kunna 'an 'ibadatikum laghafileena

# 1394

Hunalika tabloo kullu nafsin ma aslafat waruddoo ila Allahi mawlahumu alhaqqi wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yaftaroona

# 1395

Qul man yarzuqukum mina assamai waalardi amman yamliku assam'a waalabsara waman yukhriju alhayya mina almayyiti wayukhriju almayyita mina alhayyi waman yudabbiru alamra fasayaqooloona Allahu faqul afala tattaqoona

# 1396

Fathalikumu Allahu rabbukumu alhaqqu famatha ba'da alhaqqi illa addalalu faanna tusrafoona

# 1397

Kathalika haqqat kalimatu rabbika 'ala allatheena fasaqoo annahum la yuminoona

# 1398

Qul hal min shurakaikum man yabdao alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu quli Allahu yabdao alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu faanna tufakoona

# 1399

Qul hal min shurakaikum man yahdee ila alhaqqi quli Allahu yahdee lilhaqqi afaman yahdee ila alhaqqi ahaqqu an yuttaba'a amman la yahiddee illa an yuhda fama lakum kayfa tahkumoona

# 1400

Wama yattabi'u aktharuhum illa thannan inna aththanna la yughnee mina alhaqqi shayan inna Allaha 'aleemun bima yaf'aloona

# 1401

Wama kana hatha alquranu an yuftara min dooni Allahi walakin tasdeeqa allathee bayna yadayhi watafseela alkitabi la rayba feehi min rabbi al'alameena

# 1402

Am yaqooloona iftarahu qul fatoo bisooratin mithlihi waod'oo mani istata'tum min dooni Allahi in kuntum sadiqeena

# 1403

Bal kaththaboo bima lam yuheetoo bi'ilmihi walamma yatihim taweeluhu kathalika kaththaba allatheena min qablihim faonthur kayfa kana 'aqibatu aththalimeena

# 1404

Waminhum man yuminu bihi waminhum man la yuminu bihi warabbuka a'lamu bialmufsideena

# 1405

Wain kaththabooka faqul lee 'amalee walakum 'amalukum antum bareeoona mimma a'malu waana bareeon mimma ta'maloona

# 1406

Waminhum man yastami'oona ilayka afaanta tusmi'u assumma walaw kanoo la ya'qiloona

# 1407

Waminhum man yanthuru ilayka afaanta tahdee al'umya walaw kanoo la yubsiroona

# 1408

Inna Allaha la yathlimu annasa shayan walakinna annasa anfusahum yathlimoona

# 1409

Wayawma yahshuruhum kaan lam yalbathoo illa sa'atan mina annahari yata'arafoona baynahum qad khasira allatheena kaththaboo biliqai Allahi wama kanoo muhtadeena

# 1410

Waimma nuriyannaka ba'da allathee na'iduhum aw natawaffayannaka failayna marji'uhum thumma Allahu shaheedun 'ala ma yaf'aloona

# 1411

Walikulli ommatin rasoolun faitha jaa rasooluhum qudiya baynahum bialqisti wahum la yuthlamoona

# 1412

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwa'du in kuntum sadiqeena

# 1413

Qul la amliku linafsee darran wala naf'an illa ma shaa Allahu likulli ommatin ajalun itha jaa ajaluhum fala yastakhiroona sa'atan wala yastaqdimoona

# 1414

Qul araaytum in atakum 'athabuhu bayatan aw naharan matha yasta'jilu minhu almujrimoona

# 1415

Athumma itha ma waqa'a amantum bihi alana waqad kuntum bihi tasta'jiloona

# 1416

Thumma qeela lillatheena thalamoo thooqoo 'athaba alkhuldi hal tujzawna illa bima kuntum taksiboona

# 1417

Wayastanbioonaka ahaqqun huwa qul ee warabbee innahu lahaqqun wama antum bimu'jizeena

# 1418

Walaw anna likulli nafsin thalamat ma fee alardi laiftadat bihi waasarroo annadamata lamma raawoo al'athaba waqudiya baynahum bialqisti wahum la yuthlamoona

# 1419

Ala inna lillahi ma fee assamawati waalardi ala inna wa'da Allahi haqqun walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoona

# 1420

Huwa yuhyee wayumeetu wailayhi turja'oona

# 1421

Ya ayyuha annasu qad jaatkum maw'ithatun min rabbikum washifaon lima fee assudoori wahudan warahmatun lilmumineena

# 1422

Qul bifadli Allahi wabirahmatihi fabithalika falyafrahoo huwa khayrun mimma yajma'oona

# 1423

Qul araaytum ma anzala Allahu lakum min rizqin faja'atum minhu haraman wahalalan qul allahu athina lakum am 'ala Allahi taftaroona

# 1424

Wama thannu allatheena yaftaroona 'ala Allahi alkathiba yawma alqiyamati inna Allaha lathoo fadlin 'ala annasi walakinna aktharahum la yashkuroona

# 1425

Wama takoonu fee shanin wama tatloo minhu min quranin wala ta'maloona min 'amalin illa kunna 'alaykum shuhoodan ith tufeedoona feehi wama ya'zubu 'an rabbika min mithqali tharratin fee alardi wala fee assamai wala asghara min thalika wala akbara illa fee kitabin mubeenun

# 1426

Ala inna awliyaa Allahi la khawfun 'alayhim wala hum yahzanoona

# 1427

Allatheena amanoo wakanoo yattaqoona

# 1428

Lahumu albushra fee alhayati addunya wafee alakhirati la tabdeela likalimati Allahi thalika huwa alfawzu al'atheemu

# 1429

Wala yahzunka qawluhum inna al'izzata lillahi jamee'an huwa assamee'u al'aleemu

# 1430

Ala inna lillahi man fee assamawati waman fee alardi wama yattabi'u allatheena yad'oona min dooni Allahi shurakaa in yattabi'oona illa aththanna wain hum illa yakhrusoona

# 1431

Huwa allathee ja'ala lakumu allayla litaskunoo feehi waannahara mubsiran inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yasma'oona

# 1432

Qaloo ittakhatha Allahu waladan subhanahu huwa alghaniyyu lahu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi in 'indakum min sultanin bihatha ataqooloona 'ala Allahi ma la ta'lamoona

# 1433

Qul inna allatheena yaftaroona 'ala Allahi alkathiba la yuflihoona

# 1434

Mata'un fee addunya thumma ilayna marji'uhum thumma nutheequhumu al'athaba ashshadeeda bima kanoo yakfuroona

# 1435

Waotlu 'alayhim nabaa noohin ith qala liqawmihi ya qawmi in kana kabura 'alaykum maqamee watathkeeree biayati Allahi fa'ala Allahi tawakkatu faajmi'oo amrakum washurakaakum thumma la yakun amrukum 'alaykum ghummatan thumma iqdoo ilayya wala tunthirooni

# 1436

Fain tawallaytum fama saatukum min ajrin in ajriya illa 'ala Allahi waomirtu an akoona mina almuslimeena

# 1437

Fakaththaboohu fanajjaynahu waman ma'ahu fee alfulki waja'anahum khalaifa waaghraqna allatheena kaththaboo biayatina faonthur kayfa kana 'aqibatu almunthareena

# 1438

Thumma ba'athna min ba'dihi rusulan ila qawmihim fajaoohum bialbayyinati fama kanoo liyuminoo bima kaththaboo bihi min qablu kathalika natba'u 'ala quloobi almu'tadeena

# 1439

Thumma ba'athna min ba'dihim moosa waharoona ila fir'awna wamalaihi biayatina faistakbaroo wakanoo qawman mujrimeena

# 1440

Falamma jaahumu alhaqqu min 'indina qaloo inna hatha lasihrun mubeenun

# 1441

Qala moosa ataqooloona lilhaqqi lamma jaakum asihrun hatha wala yuflihu assahiroona

# 1442

Qaloo ajitana litalfitana 'amma wajadna 'alayhi abaana watakoona lakuma alkibriyao fee alardi wama nahnu lakuma bimumineena

# 1443

Waqala fir'awnu itoonee bikulli sahirin 'aleemin

# 1444

Falamma jaa assaharatu qala lahum moosa alqoo ma antum mulqoona

# 1445

Falamma alqaw qala moosa ma jitum bihi assihru inna Allaha sayubtiluhu inna Allaha la yuslihu 'amala almufsideena

# 1446

Wayuhiqqu Allahu alhaqqa bikalimatihi walaw kariha almujrimoona

# 1447

Fama amana limoosa illa thurriyyatun min qawmihi 'ala khawfin min fir'awna wamalaihim an yaftinahum wainna fir'awna la'alin fee alardi wainnahu lamina almusrifeena

# 1448

Waqala moosa ya qawmi in kuntum amantum biAllahi fa'alayhi tawakkaloo in kuntum muslimeena

# 1449

Faqaloo 'ala Allahi tawakkana rabbana la taj'ana fitnatan lilqawmi aththalimeena

# 1450

Wanajjina birahmatika mina alqawmi alkafireena

# 1451

Waawhayna ila moosa waakheehi an tabawwaa liqawmikuma bimisra buyootan waij'aloo buyootakum qiblatan waaqeemoo assalata wabashshiri almumineena

# 1452

Waqala moosa rabbana innaka atayta fir'awna wamalaahu zeenatan waamwalan fee alhayati addunya rabbana liyudilloo 'an sabeelika rabbana itmis 'ala amwalihim waoshdud 'ala quloobihim fala yuminoo hatta yarawoo al'athaba alaleema

# 1453

Qala qad ojeebat da'watukuma faistaqeema wala tattabi'anni sabeela allatheena la ya'lamoona

# 1454

Wajawazna bibanee israeela albahra faatba'ahum fir'awnu wajunooduhu baghyan wa'adwan hatta itha adrakahu algharaqu qala amantu annahu la ilaha illa allathee amanat bihi banoo israeela waana mina almuslimeena

# 1455

Alana waqad 'asayta qablu wakunta mina almufsideena

# 1456

Faalyawma nunajjeeka bibadanika litakoona liman khalfaka ayatan wainna katheeran mina annasi 'an ayatina laghafiloona

# 1457

Walaqad bawwana banee israeela mubawwaa sidqin warazaqnahum mina attayyibati fama ikhtalafoo hatta jaahumu al'ilmu inna rabbaka yaqdee baynahum yawma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi yakhtalifoona

# 1458

Fain kunta fee shakkin mimma anzanna ilayka faisali allatheena yaqraoona alkitaba min qablika laqad jaaka alhaqqu min rabbika fala takoonanna mina almumtareena

# 1459

Wala takoonanna mina allatheena kaththaboo biayati Allahi fatakoona mina alkhasireena

# 1460

Inna allatheena haqqat 'alayhim kalimatu rabbika la yuminoona

# 1461

Walaw jaathum kullu ayatin hatta yarawoo al'athaba alaleema

# 1462

Falawla kanat qaryatun amanat fanafa'aha eemanuha illa qawma yoonusa lamma amanoo kashafna 'anhum 'athaba alkhizyi fee alhayati addunya wamatta'nahum ila heenin

# 1463

Walaw shaa rabbuka laamana man fee alardi kulluhum jamee'an afaanta tukrihu annasa hatta yakoonoo mumineena

# 1464

Wama kana linafsin an tumina illa biithni Allahi wayaj'alu arrijsa 'ala allatheena la ya'qiloona

# 1465

Quli onthuroo matha fee assamawati waalardi wama tughnee alayatu waannuthuru 'an qawmin la yuminoona

# 1466

Fahal yantathiroona illa mithla ayyami allatheena khalaw min qablihim qul faintathiroo innee ma'akum mina almuntathireena

# 1467

Thumma nunajjee rusulana waallatheena amanoo kathalika haqqan 'alayna nunjee almumineena

# 1468

Qul ya ayyuha annasu in kuntum fee shakkin min deenee fala a'budu allatheena ta'budoona min dooni Allahi walakin a'budu Allaha allathee yatawaffakum waomirtu an akoona mina almumineena

# 1469

Waan aqim wajhaka lilddeeni haneefan wala takoonanna mina almushrikeena

# 1470

Wala tad'u min dooni Allahi ma la yanfa'uka wala yadurruka fain fa'ata fainnaka ithan mina aththalimeena

# 1471

Wain yamsaska Allahu bidurrin fala kashifa lahu illa huwa wain yuridka bikhayrin fala radda lifadlihi yuseebu bihi man yashao min 'ibadihi wahuwa alghafooru arraheemu

# 1472

Qul ya ayyuha annasu qad jaakumu alhaqqu min rabbikum famani ihtada fainnama yahtadee linafsihi waman dalla fainnama yadillu 'alayha wama ana 'alaykum biwakeelin

# 1473

Waittabi' ma yooha ilayka waisbir hatta yahkuma Allahu wahuwa khayru alhakimeena

# 1474

Aliflamra kitabun ohkimat ayatuhu thumma fussilat min ladun hakeemin khabeerin

# 1475

Alla ta'budoo illa Allaha innanee lakum minhu natheerun wabasheerun

# 1476

Waani istaghfiroo rabbakum thumma tooboo ilayhi yumatti'kum mata'an hasanan ila ajalin musamman wayuti kulla thee fadlin fadlahu wain tawallaw fainee akhafu 'alaykum 'athaba yawmin kabeerin

# 1477

Ila Allahi marji'ukum wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 1478

Ala innahum yathnoona sudoorahum liyastakhfoo minhu ala heena yastaghshoona thiyabahum ya'lamu ma yusirroona wama yu'linoona innahu 'aleemun bithati assudoori

# 1479

Wama min dabbatin fee alardi illa 'ala Allahi rizquha waya'lamu mustaqarraha wamustawda'aha kullun fee kitabin mubeenin

# 1480

Wahuwa allathee khalaqa assamawati waalarda fee sittati ayyamin wakana 'arshuhu 'ala almai liyabluwakum ayyukum ahsanu 'amalan walain qulta innakum mab'oothoona min ba'di almawti layaqoolanna allatheena kafaroo in hatha illa sihrun mubeenun

# 1481

Walain akhkharna 'anhumu al'athaba ila ommatin ma'doodatin layaqoolunna ma yahbisuhu ala yawma yateehim laysa masroofan 'anhum wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioona

# 1482

Walain athaqna alinsana minna rahmatan thumma naza'naha minhu innahu layaoosun kafoorun

# 1483

Walain athaqnahu na'maa ba'da darraa massathu layaqoolanna thahaba assayyiatu 'annee innahu lafarihun fakhoorun

# 1484

Illa allatheena sabaroo wa'amiloo assalihati olaika lahum maghfiratun waajrun kabeerun

# 1485

Fala'allaka tarikun ba'da ma yooha ilayka wadaiqun bihi sadruka an yaqooloo lawla onzila 'alayhi kanzun aw jaa ma'ahu malakun innama anta natheerun waAllahu 'ala kulli shayin wakeelun

# 1486

Am yaqooloona iftarahu qul fatoo bi'ashri suwarin mithlihi muftarayatin waod'oo mani istata'tum min dooni Allahi in kuntum sadiqeena

# 1487

Fai llam yastajeeboo lakum fai'lamoo annama onzila bi'ilmi Allahi waan la ilaha illa huwa fahal antum muslimoona

# 1488

Man kana yureedu alhayata addunya wazeenataha nuwaffi ilayhim a'malahum feeha wahum feeha la yubkhasoona

# 1489

Olaika allatheena laysa lahum fee alakhirati illa annaru wahabita ma sana'oo feeha wabatilun ma kanoo ya'maloona

# 1490

Afaman kana 'ala bayyinatin min rabbihi wayatloohu shahidun minhu wamin qablihi kitabu moosa imaman warahmatan olaika yuminoona bihi waman yakfur bihi mina alahzabi faannaru maw'iduhu fala taku fee miryatin minhu innahu alhaqqu min rabbika walakinna akthara annasi la yuminoona

# 1491

Waman athlamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban olaika yu'radoona 'ala rabbihim wayaqoolu alashhadu haolai allatheena kathaboo 'ala rabbihim ala la'natu Allahi 'ala aththalimeena

# 1492

Allatheena yasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi wayabghoonaha 'iwajan wahum bialakhirati hum kafiroona

# 1493

Olaika lam yakoonoo mu'jizeena fee alardi wama kana lahum min dooni Allahi min awliyaa yuda'afu lahumu al'athabu ma kanoo yastatee'oona assam'a wama kanoo yubsiroona

# 1494

Olaika allatheena khasiroo anfusahum wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yaftaroona

# 1495

La jarama annahum fee alakhirati humu alakhsaroona

# 1496

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo asalihati waakhbatoo ila rabbihim olaika ashabu aljannati hum feeha khalidoona

# 1497

Mathalu alfareeqayni kaala'ma waalasammi waalbaseeri waassamee'i hal yastawiyani mathalan afala tathakkaroona

# 1498

Walaqad arsana noohan ila qawmihi innee lakum natheerun mubeenun

# 1499

An la ta'budoo illa Allaha innee akhafu 'alaykum 'athaba yawmin aleemin

# 1500

Faqala almalao allatheena kafaroo min qawmihi ma naraka illa basharan mithlana wama naraka ittaba'aka illa allatheena hum arathiluna badiya arrayi wama nara lakum 'alayna min fadlin bal nathunnukum kathibeena

# 1501

Qala ya qawmi araaytum in kuntu 'ala bayyinatin min rabbee waatanee rahmatan min 'indihi fa'ummiyat 'alaykum anulzimukumooha waantum laha karihoona

# 1502

Waya qawmi la asalukum 'alayhi malan in ajriya illa 'ala Allahi wama ana bitaridi allatheena amanoo innahum mulaqoo rabbihim walakinnee arakum qawman tajhaloona

# 1503

Waya qawmi man yansurunee mina Allahi in taradtuhum afala tathakkaroona

# 1504

Wala aqoolu lakum 'indee khazainu Allahi wala a'lamu alghayba wala aqoolu innee malakun wala aqoolu lillatheena tazdaree a'yunukum lan yutiyahumu Allahu khayran Allahu a'lamu bima fee anfusihim innee ithan lamina aththalimeena

# 1505

Qaloo ya noohu qad jadatana faaktharta jidalana fatina bima ta'iduna in kunta mina assadiqeena

# 1506

Qala innama yateekum bihi Allahu in shaa wama antum bimu'jizeena

# 1507

Wala yanfa'ukum nushee in aradtu an ansaha lakum in kana Allahu yureedu an yughwiyakum huwa rabbukum wailayhi turja'oona

# 1508

Am yaqooloona iftarahu qul ini iftaraytuhu fa'alayya ijramee waana bareeon mimma tujrimoona

# 1509

Waoohiya ila noohin annahu lan yumina min qawmika illa man qad amana fala tabtais bima kanoo yaf'aloona

# 1510

Waisna'i alfulka bia'yunina wawahyina wala tukhatibnee fee allatheena thalamoo innahum mughraqoona

# 1511

Wayasna'u alfulka wakullama marra 'alayhi malaon min qawmihi sakhiroo minhu qala in taskharoo minna fainna naskharu minkum kama taskharoona

# 1512

Fasawfa ta'lamoona man yateehi 'athabun yukhzeehi wayahillu 'alayhi 'athabun muqeemun

# 1513

Hatta itha jaa amruna wafara attannooru qulna ihmil feeha min kullin zawjayni ithnayni waahlaka illa man sabaqa 'alayhi alqawlu waman amana wama amana ma'ahu illa qaleelun

# 1514

Waqala irkaboo feeha bismi Allahi majraha wamursaha inna rabbee laghafoorun raheemun

# 1515

Wahiya tajree bihim fee mawjin kaaljibali wanada noohunu ibnahu wakana fee ma'zilin ya bunayya irkab ma'ana wala takun ma'a alkafireena

# 1516

Qala saawee ila jabalin ya'simunee mina almai qala la 'asima alyawma min amri Allahi illa man rahima wahala baynahuma almawju fakana mina almughraqeena

# 1517

Waqeela ya ardu ibla'ee maaki waya samao aqli'ee wagheeda almao waqudiya alamru waistawat 'ala aljoodiyyi waqeela bu'dan lilqawmi aththalimeena

# 1518

Wanada noohun rabbahu faqala rabbi inna ibnee min ahlee wainna wa'daka alhaqqu waanta ahkamu alhakimeena

# 1519
