Qala ya noohu innahu laysa min ahlika innahu 'amalun ghayru salihin fala tasani ma laysa laka bihi 'ilmun innee a'ithuka an takoona mina aljahileena

# 1520

Qala rabbi innee a'oothu bika an asalaka ma laysa lee bihi 'ilmun wailla taghfir lee watarhamnee akun mina alkhasireena

# 1521

Qeela ya noohu ihbit bisalamin minna wabarakatin 'alayka wa'ala omamin mimman ma'aka waomamun sanumatti'uhum thumma yamassuhum minna 'athabun aleemun

# 1522

Tilka min anbai alghaybi nooheeha ilayka ma kunta ta'lamuha anta wala qawmuka min qabli hatha faisbir inna al'aqibata lilmuttaqeena

# 1523

Waila 'adin akhahum hoodan qala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu in antum illa muftaroona

# 1524

Ya qawmi la asalukum 'alayhi ajran in ajriya illa 'ala allathee fataranee afala ta'qiloona

# 1525

Waya qawmi istaghfiroo rabbakum thumma tooboo ilayhi yursili assamaa 'alaykum midraran wayazidkum quwwatan ila quwwatikum wala tatawallaw mujrimeena

# 1526

Qaloo ya hoodu ma jitana bibayyinatin wama nahnu bitarikee alihatina 'an qawlika wama nahnu laka bimumineena

# 1527

In naqoolu illa i'taraka ba'du alihatina bisooin qala innee oshhidu Allaha waishhadoo annee bareeon mimma tushrikoona

# 1528

Min doonihi fakeedoonee jamee'an thumma la tunthirooni

# 1529

Innee tawakkatu 'ala Allahi rabbee warabbikum ma min dabbatin illa huwa akhithun binasiyatiha inna rabbee 'ala siratin mustaqeemin

# 1530

Fain tawallaw faqad ablaghtukum ma orsiltu bihi ilaykum wayastakhlifu rabbee qawman ghayrakum wala tadurroonahu shayan inna rabbee 'ala kulli shayin hafeethun

# 1531

Walamma jaa amruna najjayna hoodan waallatheena amanoo ma'ahu birahmatin minna wanajjaynahum min 'athabin ghaleethin

# 1532

Watilka 'adun jahadoo biayati rabbihim wa'asaw rusulahu waittaba'oo amra kulli jabbarin 'aneedin

# 1533

Waotbi'oo fee hathihi addunya la'natan wayawma alqiyamati ala inna 'adan kafaroo rabbahum ala bu'dan li'adin qawmi hoodin

# 1534

Waila thamooda akhahum salihan qala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu huwa anshaakum mina alardi waista'marakum feeha faistaghfiroohu thumma tooboo ilayhi inna rabbee qareebun mujeebun

# 1535

Qaloo ya salihu qad kunta feena marjuwwan qabla hatha atanhana an na'buda ma ya'budu abaona wainnana lafee shakkin mimma tad'oona ilayhi mureebun

# 1536

Qala ya qawmi araaytum in kuntu 'ala bayyinatin min rabbee waatanee minhu rahmatan faman yansurunee mina Allahi in 'asaytuhu fama tazeedoonanee ghayra takhseerin

# 1537

Waya qawmi hathihi naqatu Allahi lakum ayatan fatharooha takul fee ardi Allahi wala tamassooha bisooin fayakhuthakum 'athabun qareebun

# 1538

Fa'aqarooha faqala tamatta'oo fee darikum thalathata ayyamin thalika wa'dun ghayru makthoobin

# 1539

Falamma jaa amruna najjayna salihan waallatheena amanoo ma'ahu birahmatin minna wamin khizyi yawmiithin inna rabbaka huwa alqawiyyu al'azeezu

# 1540

Waakhatha allatheena thalamoo assayhatu faasbahoo fee diyarihim jathimeena

# 1541

Kaan lam yaghnaw feeha ala inna thamooda kafaroo rabbahum ala bu'dan lithamooda

# 1542

Walaqad jaat rusuluna ibraheema bialbushra qaloo salaman qala salamun fama labitha an jaa bi'ijlin haneethin

# 1543

Falamma raa aydiyahum la tasilu ilayhi nakirahum waawjasa minhum kheefatan qaloo la takhaf inna orsilna ila qawmi lootin

# 1544

Waimraatuhu qaimatun fadahikat fabashsharnaha biishaqa wamin warai ishaqa ya'qooba

# 1545

Qalat ya waylata aalidu waana 'ajoozun wahatha ba'lee shaykhan inna hatha lashayon 'ajeebun

# 1546

Qaloo ata'jabeena min amri Allahi rahmatu Allahi wabarakatuhu 'alaykum ahla albayti innahu hameedun majeedun

# 1547

Falamma thahaba 'an ibraheema arraw'u wajaathu albushra yujadiluna fee qawmi lootin

# 1548

Inna ibraheema lahaleemun awwahun muneebun

# 1549

Ya ibraheemu a'rid 'an hatha innahu qad jaa amru rabbika wainnahum ateehim 'athabun ghayru mardoodin

# 1550

Walamma jaat rusuluna lootan seea bihim wadaqa bihim thar'an waqala hatha yawmun 'aseebun

# 1551

Wajaahu qawmuhu yuhra'oona ilayhi wamin qablu kanoo ya'maloona assayyiati qala ya qawmi haolai banatee hunna atharu lakum faittaqoo Allaha wala tukhzooni fee dayfee alaysa minkum rajulun rasheedun

# 1552

Qaloo laqad 'alimta ma lana fee banatika min haqqin wainnaka lata'lamu ma nureedu

# 1553

Qala law anna lee bikum quwwatan aw awee ila ruknin shadeedin

# 1554

Qaloo ya lootu inna rusulu rabbika lan yasiloo ilayka faasri biahlika biqit'in mina allayli wala yatafit minkum ahadun illa imraataka innahu museebuha ma asabahum inna maw'idahumu assubhu alaysa assubhu biqareebin

# 1555

Falamma jaa amruna ja'ana 'aliyaha safilaha waamtarna 'alayha hijaratan min sijjeelin mandoodin

# 1556

Musawwamatan 'inda rabbika wama hiya mina aththalimeena biba'eedin

# 1557

Waila madyana akhahum shu'ayban qala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu wala tanqusoo almikyala waalmeezana innee arakum bikhayrin wainnee akhafu 'alaykum 'athaba yawmin muheetin

# 1558

Waya qawmi awfoo almikyala waalmeezana bialqisti wala tabkhasoo annasa ashyaahum wala ta'thaw fee alardi mufsideena

# 1559

Baqiyyatu Allahi khayrun lakum in kuntum mumineena wama ana 'alaykum bihafeethin

# 1560

Qaloo ya shu'aybu asalatuka tamuruka an natruka ma ya'budu abaona aw an naf'ala fee amwalina ma nashao innaka laanta alhaleemu arrasheedu

# 1561

Qala ya qawmi araaytum in kuntu 'ala bayyinatin min rabbee warazaqanee minhu rizqan hasanan wama oreedu an okhalifakum ila ma anhakum 'anhu in oreedu illa alislaha ma istata'tu wama tawfeeqee illa biAllahi 'alayhi tawakkatu wailayhi oneebu

# 1562

Waya qawmi la yajrimannakum shiqaqee an yuseebakum mithlu ma asaba qawma noohin aw qawma hoodin aw qawma salihin wama qawmu lootin minkum biba'eedin

# 1563

Waistaghfiroo rabbakum thumma tooboo ilayhi inna rabbee raheemun wadoodun

# 1564

Qaloo ya shu'aybu ma nafqahu katheeran mimma taqoolu wainna lanaraka feena da'eefan walawla rahtuka larajamnaka wama anta 'alayna bi'azeezin

# 1565

Qala ya qawmi arahtee a'azzu 'alaykum mina Allahi waittakhathtumoohu waraakum thihriyyan inna rabbee bima ta'maloona muheetun

# 1566

Waya qawmi i'maloo 'ala makanatikum innee 'amilun sawfa ta'lamoona man yateehi 'athabun yukhzeehi waman huwa kathibun wairtaqiboo inne ma'akum raqeebun

# 1567

Walamma jaa amruna najjayna shu'ayban waallatheena amanoo ma'ahu birahmatin minna waakhathati allatheena thalamoo assayhatu faasbahoo fee diyarihim jathimeena

# 1568

Kaan lam yaghnaw feeha ala bu'dan limadyana kama ba'idat thamoodu

# 1569

Walaqad arsana moosa biayatina wasultanin mubeenin

# 1570

Ila fir'awna wamalaihi faittaba'oo amra fir'awna wama amru fir'awna birasheedin

# 1571

Yaqdumu qawmahu yawma alqiyamati faawradahumu annara wabisa alwirdu almawroodu

# 1572

Waotbi'oo fee hathihi la'natan wayawma alqiyamati bisa arrifdu almarfoodu

# 1573

Thalika min anbai alqura naqussuhu 'alayka minha qaimun wahaseedun

# 1574

Wama thalamnahum walakin thalamoo anfusahum fama aghnat 'anhum alihatuhumu allatee yad'oona min dooni Allahi min shayin lamma jaa amru rabbika wama zadoohum ghayra tatbeebin

# 1575

Wakathalika akhthu rabbika itha akhatha alqura wahiya thalimatun inna akhthahu aleemun shadeedun

# 1576

Inna fee thalika laayatan liman khafa 'athaba alakhirati thalika yawmun majmoo'un lahu annasu wathalika yawmun mashhoodun

# 1577

Wama nuakhkhiruhu illa liajalin ma'doodin

# 1578

Yawma yati la takallamu nafsun illa biithnihi faminhum shaqiyyun wasa'eedin

# 1579

Faamma allatheena shaqoo fafee annari lahum feeha zafeerun washaheequn

# 1580

Khalideena feeha ma damati assamawatu waalardu illa ma shaa rabbuka inna rabbaka fa''alun lima yureedu

# 1581

Waamma allatheena su'idoo fafee aljannati khalideena feeha ma damati assamawatu waalardu illa ma shaa rabbuka 'ataan ghayra majthoothin

# 1582

Fala taku fee miryatin mimma ya'budu haolai ma ya'budoona illa kama ya'budu abaohum min qablu wainna lamuwaffoohum naseebahum ghayra manqoosin

# 1583

Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba faikhtulifa feehi walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika laqudiya baynahum wainnahum lafee shakkin minhu mureebun

# 1584

Wainna kullan lamma layuwaffiyannahum rabbuka a'malahum innahu bima ya'maloona khabeerun

# 1585

Faistaqim kama omirta waman taba ma'aka wala tatghaw innahu bima ta'maloona baseerun

# 1586

Wala tarkanoo ila allatheena thalamoo fatamassakumu annaru wama lakum min dooni Allahi min awliyaa thumma la tunsaroona

# 1587

Waaqimi assalata tarafayi annahari wazulafan mina allayli inna alhasanati yuthhibna assayyiati thalika thikra lilththakireena

# 1588

Waisbir fainna Allaha la yudee'u ajra almuhsineena

# 1589

Falawla kana mina alqurooni min qablikum oloo baqiyyatin yanhawna 'ani alfasadi fee alardi illa qaleelan mimman anjayna minhum waittaba'a allatheena thalamoo ma otrifoo feehi wakanoo mujrimeena

# 1590

Wama kana rabbuka liyuhlika alqura bithulmin waahluha muslihoona

# 1591

Walaw shaa rabbuka laja'ala annasa ommatan wahidatan wala yazaloona mukhtalifeena

# 1592

Illa man rahima rabbuka walithalika khalaqahum watammat kalimatu rabbika laamlaanna jahannama mina aljinnati waannasi ajma'eena

# 1593

Wakullan naqussu 'alayka min anbai arrusuli ma nuthabbitu bihi fuadaka wajaaka fee hathihi alhaqqu wamaw'ithatun wathikra lilmumineena

# 1594

Waqul lillatheena la yuminoona i'maloo 'ala makanatikum inna 'amiloona

# 1595

Waintathiroo inna muntathiroona

# 1596

Walillahi ghaybu assamawati waalardi wailayhi yurja'u alamru kulluhu fao'budhu watawakkal 'alayhi wama rabbuka bighafilin 'amma ta'maloona

# 1597

Aliflamra tilka ayatu alkitabi almubeenu

# 1598

Inna anzanahu quranan 'arabiyyan la'allakum ta'qiloona

# 1599

Nahnu naqussu 'alayka ahsana alqasasi bima awhayna ilayka hatha alqurana wain kunta min qablihi lamina alghafileena

# 1600

Ith qala yoosufu liabeehi ya abati innee raaytu ahada 'ashara kawkaban waashshamsa waalqamara raaytuhum lee sajideena

# 1601

Qala ya bunayya la taqsus ruyaka 'ala ikhwatika fayakeedoo laka kaydan inna ashshaytana lilinsani 'aduwwun mubeenun

# 1602

Wakathalika yajtabeeka rabbuka wayu'allimuka min taweeli alahadeethi wayutimmu ni'matahu 'alayka wa'ala ali ya'qooba kama atammaha 'ala abawayka min qablu ibraheema waishaqa inna rabbaka 'aleemun hakeemun

# 1603

Laqad kana fee yoosufa waikhwatihi ayatun lilssaileena

# 1604

Ith qaloo layoosufu waakhoohu ahabbu ila abeena minna wanahnu 'usbatun inna abana lafee dalalin mubeenin

# 1605

Oqtuloo yoosufa awi itrahoohu ardan yakhlu lakum wajhu abeekum watakoonoo min ba'dihi qawman saliheena

# 1606

Qala qailun minhum la taqtuloo yoosufa waalqoohu fee ghayabati aljubbi yataqithu ba'du assayyarati in kuntum fa'ileena

# 1607

Qaloo ya abana ma laka la tamanna 'ala yoosufa wainna lahu lanasihoona

# 1608

Arsilhu ma'ana ghadan yarta' wayal'ab wainna lahu lahafithoona

# 1609

Qala innee layahzununee an thathhaboo bihi waakhafu an yakulahu aththibu waantum 'anhu ghafiloona

# 1610

Qaloo lain akalahu aththibu wanahnu 'usbatun inna ithan lakhasiroona

# 1611

Falamma thahaboo bihi waajma'oo an yaj'aloohu fee ghayabati aljubbi waawhayna ilayhi latunabiannahum biamrihim hatha wahum la yash'uroona

# 1612

Wajaoo abahum 'ishaan yabkoona

# 1613

Qaloo ya abana inna thahabna nastabiqu watarakna yoosufa 'inda mata'ina faakalahu aththibu wama anta bimuminin lana walaw kunna sadiqeena

# 1614

Wajaoo 'ala qameesihi bidamin kathibin qala bal sawwalat lakum anfusukum amran fasabrun jameelun waAllahu almusta'anu 'ala ma tasifoona

# 1615

Wajaat sayyaratun faarsaloo waridahum faadla dalwahu qala ya bushra hatha ghulamun waasarroohu bida'atan waAllahu 'aleemun bima ya'maloona

# 1616

Washarawhu bithamanin bakhsin darahima ma'doodatin wakanoo feehi mina azzahideena

# 1617

Waqala allathee ishtarahu min misra liimraatihi akrimee mathwahu 'asa an yanfa'ana aw nattakhithahu waladan wakathalika makkanna liyoosufa fee alardi walinu'allimahu min taweeli alahadeethi waAllahu ghalibun 'ala amrihi walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoona

# 1618

Walamma balagha ashuddahu ataynahu hukman wa'ilman wakathalika najzee almuhsineena

# 1619

Warawadathu allatee huwa fee baytiha 'an nafsihi waghallaqati alabwaba waqalat hayta laka qala ma'atha Allahi innahu rabbee ahsana mathwaya innahu la yuflihu aththalimoona

# 1620

Walaqad hammat bihi wahamma biha lawla an raa burhana rabbihi kathalika linasrifa 'anhu assooa waalfahshaa innahu min 'ibadina almukhlaseena

# 1621

Waistabaqa albaba waqaddat qameesahu min duburin waalfaya sayyidaha lada albabi qalat ma jazao man arada biahlika sooan illa an yusjana aw 'athabun aleemun

# 1622

Qala hiya rawadatnee 'an nafsee washahida shahidun min ahliha in kana qameesuhu qudda min qubulin fasadaqat wahuwa mina alkathibeena

# 1623

Wain kana qameesuhu qudda min duburin fakathabat wahuwa mina assadiqeena

# 1624

Falamma raa qameesahu qudda min duburin qala innahu min kaydikunna inna kaydakunna 'atheemun

# 1625

Yoosufu a'rid 'an hatha waistaghfiree lithanbiki innaki kunti mina alkhatieena

# 1626

Waqala niswatun fee almadeenati imraatu al'azeezi turawidu fataha 'an nafsihi qad shaghafaha hubban inna lanaraha fee dalalin mubeenin

# 1627

Falamma sami'at bimakrihinna arsalat ilayhinna waa'tadat lahunna muttakaan waatat kulla wahidatin minhunna sikkeenan waqalati okhruj 'alayhinna falamma raaynahu akbarnahu waqatta'na aydiyahunna waqulna hasha lillahi ma hatha basharan in hatha illa malakun kareemun

# 1628

Qalat fathalikunna allathee lumtunnanee feehi walaqad rawadtuhu 'an nafsihi faist'sama walain lam yaf'al ma amuruhu layusjananna walayakoonan mina assaghireena

# 1629

Qala rabbi assijnu ahabbu ilayya mimma yad'oonanee ilayhi wailla tasrif 'annee kaydahunna asbu ilayhinna waakun mina aljahileena

# 1630

Faistajaba lahu rabbuhu fasarafa 'anhu kaydahunna innahu huwa assamee'u al'aleemu

# 1631

Thumma bada lahum min ba'di ma raawoo alayati layasjununnahu hatta heenin

# 1632

Wadakhala ma'ahu assijna fatayani qala ahaduhuma innee aranee a'siru khamran waqala alakharu innee aranee ahmilu fawqa rasee khubzan takulu attayru minhu nabbina bitaweelihi inna naraka mina almuhsineena

# 1633

Qala la yateekuma ta'amun turzaqanihi illa nabbatukuma bitaweelihi qabla an yatiyakuma thalikuma mimma 'allamanee rabbee innee taraktu millata qawmin la yuminoona biAllahi wahum bialakhirati hum kafiroona

# 1634

Waittaba'tu millata abaee ibraheema waishaqa waya'qooba ma kana lana an nushrika biAllahi min shayin thalika min fadli Allahi 'alayna wa'ala annasi walakinna akthara annasi la yashkuroona

# 1635

Ya sahibayi assijni aarbabun mutafarriqoona khayrun ami Allahu alwahidu alqahharu

# 1636

Ma ta'budoona min doonihi illa asmaan sammaytumooha antum waabaokum ma anzala Allahu biha min sultanin ini alhukmu illa lillahi amara alla ta'budoo illa iyyahu thalika addeenu alqayyimu walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoona

# 1637

Ya sahibayi assijni amma ahadukuma fayasqee rabbahu khamran waamma alakharu fayuslabu fatakulu attayru min rasihi qudiya alamru allathee feehi tastaftiyani

# 1638

Waqala lillathee thanna annahu najin minhuma othkurnee 'inda rabbika faansahu ashshaytanu thikra rabbihi falabitha fee assijni bid'a sineena

# 1639

Waqala almaliku innee ara sab'a baqaratin simanin yakuluhunna sab'un 'ijafun wasab'a sunbulatin khudrin waokhara yabisatin ya ayyuha almalao aftoonee fee ruyaya in kuntum lilrruya ta'buroona

# 1640

Qaloo adghathu ahlamin wama nahnu bitaweeli alahlami bi'alimeena

# 1641

Waqala allathee naja minhuma waiddakara ba'da ommatin ana onabbiokum bitaweelihi faarsilooni

# 1642

Yoosufu ayyuha assiddeequ aftina fee sab'i baqaratin simanin yakuluhunna sab'un 'ijafun wasab'i sunbulatin khudrin waokhara yabisatin la'allee arji'u ila annasi la'allahum ya'lamoona

# 1643

Qala tazra'oona sab'a sineena daaban fama hasadtum fatharoohu fee sunbulihi illa qaleelan mimma takuloona

# 1644

Thumma yatee min ba'di thalika sab'un shidadun yakulna ma qaddamtum lahunna illa qaleelan mimma tuhsinoona

# 1645

Thumma yatee min ba'di thalika 'amun feehi yughathu annasu wafeehi ya'siroona

# 1646

Waqala almaliku itoonee bihi falamma jaahu arrasoolu qala irji' ila rabbika faisalhu ma balu anniswati allatee qatta'na aydiyahunna inna rabbee bikaydihinna 'aleemun

# 1647

Qala ma khatbukunna ith rawadtunna yoosufa 'an nafsihi qulna hasha lillahi ma 'alimna 'alayhi min sooin qalati imraatu al'azeezi alana hashasa alhaqqu ana rawadtuhu 'an nafsihi wainnahu lamina assadiqeena

# 1648

Thalika liya'lama annee lam akhunhu bialghaybi waanna Allaha la yahdee kayda alkhaineena

# 1649

Wama obarrio nafsee inna annafsa laammaratun biassooi illa ma rahima rabbee inna rabbee ghafoorun raheemun

# 1650

Waqala almaliku itoonee bihi astakhlishu linafsee falamma kallamahu qala innaka alyawma ladayna makeenun ameenun

# 1651

Qala ij'anee 'ala khazaini alardi innee hafeethun 'aleemun

# 1652

Wakathalika makanna liyoosufa fee alardi yatabawwao minha haythu yashao nuseebu birahmatina man nashao wala nudee'u ajra almuhsineena

# 1653

Walaajru alakhirati khayrun lillatheena amanoo wakanoo yattaqoona

# 1654

Wajaa ikhwatu yoosufa fadakhaloo 'alayhi fa'arafahum wahum lahu munkiroona

# 1655

Walamma jahhazahum bijahazihim qala itoonee biakhin lakum min abeekum ala tarawna annee oofee alkayla waana khayru almunzileena

# 1656

Fain lam tatoonee bihi fala kayla lakum 'indee wala taqrabooni

# 1657

Qaloo sanurawidu 'anhu abahu wainna lafa'iloona

# 1658

Waqala lifityanihi ij'aloo bida'atahum fee rihalihim la'allahum ya'rifoonaha itha inqalaboo ila ahlihim la'allahum yarji'oona

# 1659

Falamma raja'oo ila abeehim qaloo ya abana muni'a minna alkaylu faarsil ma'ana akhana naktal wainna lahu lahafithoona

# 1660

Qala hal amanukum 'alayhi illa kama amintukum 'ala akheehi min qablu faAllahu khayrun hafithan wahuwa arhamu arrahimeena

# 1661

Walamma fatahoo mata'ahum wajadoo bida'atahum ruddat ilayhim qaloo ya abana ma nabghee hathihi bida'atuna ruddat ilayna wanameeru ahlana wanahfathu akhana wanazdadu kayla ba'eerin thalika kaylun yaseerun

# 1662

Qala lan orsilahu ma'akum hatta tutooni mawthiqan mina Allahi latatunnanee bihi illa an yuhata bikum falamma atawhu mawthiqahum qala Allahu 'ala ma naqoolu wakeelun

# 1663

Waqala ya baniyya la tadkhuloo min babin wahidin waodkhuloo min abwabin mutafarriqatin wama oghnee 'ankum mina Allahi min shayin ini alhukmu illa lillahi 'alayhi tawakkatu wa'alayhi falyatawakkali almutawakkiloona

# 1664

Walamma dakhaloo min haythu amarahum aboohum ma kana yughnee 'anhum mina Allahi min shayin illa hajatan fee nafsi ya'qooba qadaha wainnahu lathoo 'ilmin lima 'allamnahu walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoona

# 1665

Walamma dakhaloo 'ala yoosufa awa ilayhi akhahu qala innee ana akhooka fala tabtais bima kanoo ya'maloona

# 1666

Falamma jahhazahum bijahazihim ja'ala assiqayata fee rahli akheehi thumma aththana muaththinun ayyatuha al'eeru innakum lasariqoona

# 1667

Qaloo waaqbaloo 'alayhim matha tafqidoona

# 1668

Qaloo nafqidu suwa'a almaliki waliman jaa bihi himlu ba'eerin waana bihi za'eemun

# 1669

Qaloo taAllahi laqad 'alimtum ma jina linufsida fee alardi wama kunna sariqeena

# 1670

Qaloo fama jazaohu in kuntum kathibeena

# 1671

Qaloo jazaohu man wujida fee rahlihi fahuwa jazaohu kathalika najzee aththalimeena

# 1672

Fabadaa biaw'iyatihim qabla wi'ai akheehi thumma istakhrajaha min wi'ai akheehi kathalika kidna liyoosufa ma kana liyakhutha akhahu fee deeni almaliki illa an yashaa Allahu narfa'u darajatin man nashao wafawqa kulli thee 'ilmin 'aleemun

# 1673

Qaloo in yasriq faqad saraqa akhun lahu min qablu faasarraha yoosufu fee nafsihi walam yubdiha lahum qala antum sharrun makanan waAllahu a'lamu bima tasifoona

# 1674

Qaloo ya ayyuha al'azeezu inna lahu aban shaykhan kabeeran fakhuth ahadana makanahu inna naraka mina almuhsineena

# 1675

Qala ma'atha Allahi an nakhutha illa man wajadna mata'ana 'indahu inna ithan lathalimoona

# 1676

Falamma istayasoo minhu khalasoo najiyyan qala kabeeruhum alam ta'lamoo anna abakum qad akhatha 'alaykum mawthiqan mina Allahi wamin qablu ma farrattum fee yoosufa falan abraha alarda hatta yathana lee abee aw yahkuma Allahu lee wahuwa khayru alhakimeena

# 1677

Irji'oo ila abeekum faqooloo ya abana inna ibnaka saraqa wama shahidna illa bima 'alimna wama kunna lilghaybi hafitheena

# 1678

Waisali alqaryata allatee kunna feeha waal'eera allatee aqbana feeha wainna lasadiqoona

# 1679

Qala bal sawwalat lakum anfusukum amran fasabrun jameelun 'asa Allahu an yatiyanee bihim jamee'an innahu huwa al'aleemu alhakeemu

# 1680

Watawalla 'anhum waqala ya asafa 'ala yoosufa waibyaddat 'aynahu mina alhuzni fahuwa katheemun

# 1681

Qaloo taAllahi taftao tathkuru yoosufa hatta takoona haradan aw takoona mina alhalikeena

# 1682

Qala innama ashkoo baththee wahuznee ila Allahi waa'lamu mina Allahi ma la ta'lamoona

# 1683

Ya baniyya ithhaboo fatahassasoo min yoosufa waakheehi wala tayasoo min rawhi Allahi innahu la yayasu min rawhi Allahi illa alqawmu alkafiroona

# 1684

Falamma dakhaloo 'alayhi qaloo ya ayyuha al'azeezu massana waahlana addurru wajina bibida'atin muzjatin faawfi lana alkayla watasaddaq 'alayna inna Allaha yajzee almutasaddiqeena

# 1685

Qala hal 'alimtum ma fa'atum biyoosufa waakheehi ith antum jahiloona

# 1686

Qaloo ainnaka laanta yoosufa qala ana yoosufu wahatha akhee qad manna Allahu 'alayna innahu man yattaqi wayasbir fainna Allaha la yudee'u ajra almuhsineena

# 1687

Qaloo taAllahi laqad atharaka Allahu 'alayna wain kunna lakhatieena

# 1688

Qala la tathreeba 'alaykumu alyawma yaghfiru Allahu lakum wahuwa arhamu arrahimeena

# 1689

Ithhaboo biqameesee hatha faalqoohu 'ala wajhi abee yati baseeran watoonee biahlikum ajma'eena

# 1690

Walamma fasalati al'eeru qala aboohum innee laajidu reeha yoosufa lawla an tufannidooni

# 1691

Qaloo taAllahi innaka lafee dalalika alqadeemi

# 1692

Falamma an jaa albasheeru alqahu 'ala wajhihi fairtadda baseeran qala alam aqul lakum innee a'lamu mina Allahi ma la ta'lamoona

# 1693

Qaloo ya abana istaghfir lana thunoobana inna kunna khatieena

# 1694

Qala sawfa astaghfiru lakum rabbee innahu huwa alghafooru arraheemu

# 1695

Falamma dakhaloo 'ala yoosufa awa ilayhi abawayhi waqala odkhuloo misra in shaa Allahu amineena

# 1696

Warafa'a abawayhi 'ala al'arshi wakharroo lahu sujjadan waqala ya abati hatha taweelu ruyaya min qablu qad ja'alaha rabbee haqqan waqad ahsana bee ith akhrajanee mina assijni wajaa bikum mina albadwi min ba'di an nazagha ashshaytanu baynee wabayna ikhwatee inna rabbee lateefun lima yashao innahu huwa al'aleemu alhakeemu

# 1697

Rabbi qad ataytanee mina almulki wa'allamtanee min taweeli alahadeethi fatira assamawati waalardi anta waliyyee fee addunya waalakhirati tawaffanee musliman waalhiqnee biassaliheena

# 1698

Thalika min anbai alghaybi nooheehi ilayka wama kunta ladayhim ith ajma'oo amrahum wahum yamkuroona

# 1699

Wama aktharu annasi walaw harasta bimumineena

# 1700

Wama tasaluhum 'alayhi min ajrin in huwa illa thikrun lil'alameena

# 1701

Wakaayyin min ayatin fee assamawati waalardi yamurroona 'alayha wahum 'anha mu'ridoona

# 1702

Wama yuminu aktharuhum biAllahi illa wahum mushrikoona

# 1703

Afaaminoo an tatiyahum ghashiyatun min 'athabi Allahi aw tatiyahumu assa'atu baghtatan wahum la yash'uroona

# 1704

Qul hathihi sabeelee ad'oo ila Allahi 'ala baseeratin ana wamani ittaba'anee wasubhana Allahi wama ana mina almushrikeena

# 1705

Wama arsana min qablika illa rijalan noohee ilayhim min ahli alqura afalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena min qablihim waladaru alakhirati khayrun lillatheena ittaqaw afala ta'qiloona

# 1706

Hatta itha istayasa arrusulu wathannoo annahum qad kuthiboo jaahum nasruna fanujjiya man nashao wala yuraddu basuna 'ani alqawmi almujrimeena

# 1707

Laqad kana fee qasasihim 'ibratun liolee alalbabi ma kana hadeethan yuftara walakin tasdeeqa allathee bayna yadayhi watafseela kulli shayin wahudan warahmatan liqawmin yuminoona

# 1708

Aliflammeemra tilka ayatu alkitabi waallathee onzila ilayka min rabbika alhaqqu walakinna akthara annasi la yuminoona

# 1709

Allahu allathee rafa'a assamawati bighayri 'amadin tarawnaha thumma istawa 'ala al'arshi wasakhkhara ashshamsa waalqamara kullun yajree liajalin musamman yudabbiru alamra yufassilu alayati la'allakum biliqai rabbikum tooqinoona

# 1710

Wahuwa allathee madda alarda waja'ala feeha rawasiya waanharan wamin kulli aththamarati ja'ala feeha zawjayni ithnayni yughshee allayla annahara inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaroona

# 1711

Wafee alardi qita'un mutajawiratun wajannatun min a'nabin wazar'un wanakheelun sinwanun waghayru sinwanin yusqa bimain wahidin wanufaddilu ba'daha 'ala ba'din fee alokuli inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin ya'qiloona

# 1712

Wain ta'jab fa'ajabun qawluhum aitha kunna turaban ainna lafee khalqin jadeedin olaika allatheena kafaroo birabbihim waolaika alaghlalu fee a'naqihim waolaika ashabu annari hum feeha khalidoona

# 1713

Wayasta'jiloonaka biassayyiati qabla alhasanati waqad khalat min qablihimu almathulatu wainna rabbaka lathoo maghfiratin lilnnasi 'ala thulmihim wainna rabbaka lashadeedu al'iqabi

# 1714

Wayaqoolu allatheena kafaroo lawla onzila 'alayhi ayatun min rabbihi innama anta munthirun walikulli qawmin hadin

# 1715

Allahu ya'lamu ma tahmilu kullu ontha wama tagheedu alarhamu wama tazdadu wakullu shayin 'indahu bimiqdarin

# 1716

'alimu alghaybi waashshahadati alkabeeru almuta'ali

# 1717

Sawaon minkum man asarra alqawla waman jahara bihi waman huwa mustakhfin biallayli wasaribun biannahari

# 1718

Lahu mu'aqqibatun min bayni yadayhi wamin khalfihi yahfathoonahu min amri Allahi inna Allaha la yughayyiru ma biqawmin hatta yughayyiroo ma bianfusihim waitha arada Allahu biqawmin sooan fala maradda lahu wama lahum min doonihi min walin

# 1719

Huwa allathee yureekumu albarqa khawfan watama'an wayunshio assahaba aththiqala

# 1720

Wayusabbihu arra'du bihamdihi waalmalaikatu min kheefatihi wayursilu assawa'iqa fayuseebu biha man yashao wahum yujadiloona fee Allahi wahuwa shadeedu almihali

# 1721

Lahu da'watu alhaqqi waallatheena yad'oona min doonihi la yastajeeboona lahum bishayin illa kabasiti kaffayhi ila almai liyablugha fahu wama huwa bibalighihi wama du'ao alkafireena illa fee dalalin

# 1722

Walillahi yasjudu man fee assamawati waalardi taw'an wakarhan wathilaluhum bialghuduwwi waalasali

# 1723

Qul man rabbu assamawati waalardi quli Allahu qul afaittakhathtum min doonihi awliyaa la yamlikoona lianfusihim naf'an wala darran qul hal yastawee ala'ma waalbaseeru am hal tastawee aththulumatu waannooru am ja'aloo lillahi shurakaa khalaqoo kakhalqihi fatashabaha alkhalqu 'alayhim quli Allahu khaliqu kulli shayin wahuwa alwahidu alqahharu

# 1724

Anzala mina assamai maan fasalat awdiyatun biqadariha faihtamala assaylu zabadan rabiyan wamimma yooqidoona 'alayhi fee annari ibtighaa hilyatin aw mata'in zabadun mithluhu kathalika yadribu Allahu alhaqqa waalbatila faamma azzabadu fayathhabu jufaan waamma ma yanfa'u annasa fayamkuthu fee alardi kathalika yadribu Allahu alamthala

# 1725

Lillatheena istajaboo lirabbihimu alhusna waallatheena lam yastajeeboo lahu law anna lahum ma fee alardi jamee'an wamithlahu ma'ahu laiftadaw bihi olaika lahum sooo alhisabi wamawahum jahannamu wabisa almihadu

# 1726

Afaman ya'lamu annama onzila ilayka min rabbika alhaqqu kaman huwa a'ma innama yatathakkaru oloo alalbabi

# 1727

Allatheena yoofoona bi'ahdi Allahi wala yanqudoona almeethaqa

# 1728

Waallatheena yasiloona ma amara Allahu bihi an yoosala wayakhshawna rabbahum wayakhafoona sooa alhisabi

# 1729

Waallatheena sabaroo ibtighaa wajhi rabbihim waaqamoo assalata waanfaqoo mimma razaqnahum sirran wa'alaniyatan wayadraoona bialhasanati assayyiata olaika lahum 'uqba addari

# 1730

Jannatu 'adnin yadkhuloonaha waman salaha min abaihim waazwajihim wathurriyyatihim waalmalaikatu yadkhuloona 'alayhim min kulli babin

# 1731

Salamun 'alaykum bima sabartum fani'ma 'uqba addari

# 1732

Waallatheena yanqudoona 'ahda Allahi min ba'di meethaqihi wayaqta'oona ma amara Allahu bihi an yoosala wayufsidoona fee alardi olaika lahumu alla'natu walahum sooo addari

# 1733

Allahu yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru wafarihoo bialhayati addunya wama alhayatu addunya fee alakhirati illa mata'un

# 1734

Wayaqoolu allatheena kafaroo lawla onzila 'alayhi ayatun min rabbihi qul inna Allaha yudillu man yashao wayahdee ilayhi man anaba

# 1735

Allatheena amanoo watatmainnu quloobuhum bithikri Allahi ala bithikri Allahi tatmainnu alquloobu

# 1736

Allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati tooba lahum wahusnu maabin

# 1737

Kathalika arsanaka fee ommatin qad khalat min qabliha omamun litatluwa 'alayhimu allathee awhayna ilayka wahum yakfuroona biarrahmani qul huwa rabbee la ilaha illa huwa 'alayhi tawakkatu wailayhi matabi

# 1738

Walaw anna quranan suyyirat bihi aljibalu aw qutti'at bihi alardu aw kullima bihi almawta bal lillahi alamru jamee'an afalam yayasi allatheena amanoo an law yashao Allahu lahada annasa jamee'an wala yazalu allatheena kafaroo tuseebuhum bima sana'oo qari'atun aw tahullu qareeban min darihim hatta yatiya wa'du Allahi inna Allaha la yukhlifu almee'ada

# 1739

Walaqadi istuhzia birusulin min qablika faamlaytu lillatheena kafaroo thumma akhathtuhum fakayfa kana 'iqabi

# 1740

Afaman huwa qaimun 'ala kulli nafsin bima kasabat waja'aloo lillahi shurakaa qul sammoohum am tunabbioonahu bima la ya'lamu fee alardi am bithahirin mina alqawli bal zuyyina lillatheena kafaroo makruhum wasuddoo 'ani assabeeli waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min hadin

# 1741

Lahum 'athabun fee alhayati addunya wala'athabu alakhirati ashaqqu wama lahum mina Allahi min waqin

# 1742

Mathalu aljannati allatee wu'ida almuttaqoona tajree min tahtiha alanharu okuluha daimun wathilluha tilka 'uqba allatheena ittaqaw wa'uqba alkafireena annaru

# 1743

Waallatheena ataynahumu alkitaba yafrahoona bima onzila ilayka wamina alahzabi man yunkiru ba'dahu qul innama omirtu an a'buda Allaha wala oshrika bihi ilayhi ad'oo wailayhi maabi

# 1744

Wakathalika anzanahu hukman 'arabiyyan walaini ittaba'ta ahwaahum ba'da ma jaaka mina al'ilmi ma laka mina Allahi min waliyyin wala waqin

# 1745

Walaqad arsana rusulan min qablika waja'ana lahum azwajan wathurriyyatan wama kana lirasoolin an yatiya biayatin illa biithni Allahi likulli ajalin kitabun

# 1746

Yamhoo Allahu ma yashao wayuthbitu wa'indahu ommu alkitabi

# 1747

Wain ma nuriyannaka ba'da allathee na'iduhum aw natawaffayannaka fainnama 'alayka albalaghu wa'alayna alhisabu

# 1748

Awalam yaraw anna natee alarda nanqusuha min atrafiha waAllahu yahkumu la mu'aqqiba lihukmihi wahuwa saree'u alhisabi

# 1749

Waqad makara allatheena min qablihim falillahi almakru jamee'an ya'lamu ma taksibu kullu nafsin wasaya'lamu alkuffaru liman 'uqba addari

# 1750

Wayaqoolu allatheena kafaroo lasta mursalan qul kafa biAllahi shaheedan baynee wabaynakum waman 'indahu 'ilmu alkitabi

# 1751

Aliflamra kitabun anzanahu ilayka litukhrija annasa mina aththulumati ila annoori biithni rabbihim ila sirati al'azeezi alhameedi

# 1752

Allahi allathee lahu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi wawaylun lilkafireena min 'athabin shadeedin

# 1753

Allatheena yastahibboona alhayata addunya 'ala alakhirati wayasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi wayabghoonaha 'iwajan olaika fee dalalin ba'eedin

# 1754

Wama arsana min rasoolin illa bilisani qawmihi liyubayyina lahum fayudillu Allahu man yashao wayahdee man yashao wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 1755

Walaqad arsana moosa biayatina an akhrij qawmaka mina aththulumati ila annoori wathakkirhum biayyami Allahi inna fee thalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakoorin

# 1756

Waith qala moosa liqawmihi othkuroo ni'mata Allahi 'alaykum ith anjakum min ali fir'awna yasoomoonakum sooa al'athabi wayuthabbihoona abnaakum wayastahyoona nisaakum wafee thalikum balaon min rabbikum 'atheemun

# 1757

Waith taaththana rabbukum lain shakartum laazeedannakum walain kafartum inna 'athabee lashadeedun

# 1758

Waqala moosa in takfuroo antum waman fee alardi jamee'an fainna Allaha laghaniyyun hameedun

# 1759

Alam yatikum nabao allatheena min qablikum qawmi noohin wa'adin wathamooda waallatheena min ba'dihim la ya'lamuhum illa Allahu jaathum rusuluhum bialbayyinati faraddoo aydiyahum fee afwahihim waqaloo inna kafarna bima orsiltum bihi wainna lafee shakkin mimma tad'oonana ilayhi mureebun

# 1760

Qalat rusuluhum afee Allahi shakkun fatiri assamawati waalardi yad'ookum liyaghfira lakum min thunoobikum wayuakhkhirakum ila ajalin musamman qaloo in antum illa basharun mithluna tureedoona an tasuddoona 'amma kana ya'budu abaona fatoona bisultanin mubeenin

# 1761

Qalat lahum rusuluhum in nahnu illa basharun mithlukum walakinna Allaha yamunnu 'ala man yashao min 'ibadihi wama kana lana an natiyakum bisultanin illa biithni Allahi wa'ala Allahi falyatawakkali almuminoona

# 1762

Wama lana alla natawakkala 'ala Allahi waqad hadana subulana walanasbiranna 'ala ma athaytumoona wa'ala Allahi falyatawakkali almutawakkiloona

# 1763

Waqala allatheena kafaroo lirusulihim lanukhrijannakum min ardina aw lata'oodunna fee millatina faawha ilayhim rabbuhum lanuhlikanna aththalimeena

# 1764

Walanuskinannakumu alarda min ba'dihim thalika liman khafa maqamee wakhafa wa'eedi

# 1765

Waistaftahoo wakhaba kullu jabbarin 'aneedin

# 1766

Min waraihi jahannamu wayusqa min main sadeedin

# 1767

Yatajarra'uhu wala yakadu yuseeghuhu wayateehi almawtu min kulli makanin wama huwa bimayyitin wamin waraihi 'athabun ghaleethun

# 1768

Mathalu allatheena kafaroo birabbihim a'maluhum karamadin ishtaddat bihi arreehu fee yawmin 'asifin la yaqdiroona mimma kasaboo 'ala shayin thalika huwa addalalu alba'eedu

# 1769

Alam tara anna Allaha khalaqa assamawati waalarda bialhaqqi in yasha yuthhibkum wayati bikhalqin jadeedin

# 1770

Wama thalika 'ala Allahi bi'azeezin

# 1771

Wabarazoo lillahi jamee'an faqala addu'afao lillatheena istakbaroo inna kunna lakum taba'an fahal antum mughnoona 'anna min 'athabi Allahi min shayin qaloo law hadana Allahu lahadaynakum sawaon 'alayna ajazi'na am sabarna ma lana min maheesin

# 1772

Waqala ashshaytanu lamma qudiya alamru inna Allaha wa'adakum wa'da alhaqqi wawa'adtukum faakhlaftukum wama kana liya 'alaykum min sultanin illa an da'awtukum faistajabtum lee fala taloomoonee waloomoo anfusakum ma ana bimusrikhikum wama antum bimusrikhiyya innee kafartu bima ashraktumooni min qablu inna aththalimeena lahum 'athabun aleemun

# 1773

Waodkhila allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha biithni rabbihim tahiyyatuhum feeha salamun

# 1774

Alam tara kayfa daraba Allahu mathalan kalimatan tayyibatan kashajaratin tayyibatin asluha thabitun wafar'uha fee assamai

# 1775

Tutee okulaha kulla heenin biithni rabbiha wayadribu Allahu alamthala lilnnasi la'allahum yatathakkaroona

# 1776

Wamathalu kalimatin khabeethatin kashajaratin khabeethatin ijtuththat min fawqi alardi ma laha min qararin

# 1777

Yuthabbitu Allahu allatheena amanoo bialqawli aththabiti fee alhayati addunya wafee alakhirati wayudillu Allahu aththalimeena wayaf'alu Allahu ma yashao

# 1778

Alam tara ila allatheena baddaloo ni'mata Allahi kufran waahalloo qawmahum dara albawari

# 1779

Jahannama yaslawnaha wabisa alqararu

# 1780

Waja'aloo lillahi andadan liyudilloo 'an sabeelihi qul tamatta'oo fainna maseerakum ila annari

# 1781

Qul li'ibadiya allatheena amanoo yuqeemoo assalata wayunfiqoo mimma razaqnahum sirran wa'alaniyatan min qabli an yatiya yawmun la bay'un feehi wala khilalun

# 1782

Allahu allathee khalaqa assamawati waalarda waanzala mina assamai maan faakhraja bihi mina aththamarati rizqan lakum wasakhkhara lakumu alfulka litajriya fee albahri biamrihi wasakhkhara lakumu alanhara

# 1783

Wasakhkhara lakumu ashshamsa waalqamara daibayni wasakhkhara lakumu allayla waannahara

# 1784

Waatakum min kulli ma saatumoohu wain ta'uddoo ni'mata Allahi la tuhsooha inna alinsana lathaloomun kaffarun

# 1785

Waith qala ibraheemu rabbi ij'al hatha albalada aminan waojnubnee wabaniyya an na'buda alasnama

# 1786

Rabbi innahunna adlana katheeran mina annasi faman tabi'anee fainnahu minnee waman 'asanee fainnaka ghafoorun raheemun

# 1787

Rabbana innee askantu min thurriyyatee biwadin ghayri thee zar'in 'inda baytika almuharrami rabbana liyuqeemoo assalata faij'al afidatan mina annasi tahwee ilayhim waorzuqhum mina aththamarati la'allahum yashkuroona

# 1788

Rabbana innaka ta'lamu ma nukhfee wama nu'linu wama yakhfa 'ala Allahi min shayin fee alardi wala fee assamai

# 1789

Alhamdu lillahi allathee wahaba lee 'ala alkibari isma'eela waishaqa inna rabbee lasamee'u addu'ai

# 1790

Rabbi ij'anee muqeema assalati wamin thurriyyatee rabbana wtaqabbal du'ai

# 1791

Rabbana ighfir lee waliwalidayya walilmumineena yawma yaqoomu alhisabu

# 1792

Wala tahsabanna Allaha ghafilan 'amma ya'malu aththalimoona innama yuakhkhiruhum liyawmin tashkhasu feehi alabsaru

# 1793

Muhti'eena muqni'ee ruoosihim la yartaddu ilayhim tarfuhum waafidatuhum hawaon

# 1794

Waanthiri annasa yawma yateehimu al'athabu fayaqoolu allatheena thalamoo rabbana akhkhirna ila ajalin qareebin nujib da'wataka wanattabi'i arrusula awalam takoonoo aqsamtum min qablu ma lakum min zawalin

# 1795

Wasakantum fee masakini allatheena thalamoo anfusahum watabayyana lakum kayfa fa'ana bihim wadarabna lakumu alamthala

# 1796

Waqad makaroo makrahum wa'inda Allahi makruhum wain kana makruhum litazoola minhu aljibalu

# 1797

Fala tahsabanna Allaha mukhlifa wa'dihi rusulahu inna Allaha 'azeezun thoo intiqamin

# 1798

Yawma tubaddalu alardu ghayra alardi waassamawatu wabarazoo lillahi alwahidi alqahhari

# 1799

Watara almujrimeena yawmaithin muqarraneena fee alasfadi

# 1800

Sarabeeluhum min qatranin wataghsha wujoohahumu annaru

# 1801

Liyajziya Allahu kulla nafsin ma kasabat inna Allaha saree'u alhisabi

# 1802

Hatha balaghun lilnnasi waliyuntharoo bihi waliya'lamoo annama huwa ilahun wahidun waliyaththakkara oloo alalbabi

# 1803

Aliflamra tilka ayatu alkitabi waquranin mubeenin

# 1804

Rubama yawaddu allatheena kafaroo law kanoo muslimeena

# 1805

Tharhum yakuloo wayatamatta'oo wayulhihimu alamalu fasawfa ya'lamoona

# 1806

Wama ahlakna min qaryatin illa walaha kitabun ma'loomun

# 1807

Ma tasbiqu min ommatin ajalaha wama yastakhiroona

# 1808

Waqaloo ya ayyuha allathee nuzzila 'alayhi aththikru innaka lamajnoonun

# 1809

Law ma tateena bialmalaikati in kunta mina assadiqeena

# 1810

Ma nunazzilu almalaikata illa bialhaqqi wama kanoo ithan munthareena

# 1811

Inna nahnu nazzana aththikra wainna lahu lahafithoona

# 1812

Walaqad arsana min qablika fee shiya'i alawwaleena

# 1813

Wama yateehim min rasoolin illa kanoo bihi yastahzioona

# 1814

Kathalika naslukuhu fee quloobi almujrimeena

# 1815

La yuminoona bihi waqad khalat sunnatu alawwaleena

# 1816

Walaw fatahna 'alayhim baban mina assamai fathalloo feehi ya'rujoona

# 1817

Laqaloo innama sukkirat absaruna bal nahnu qawmun mashooroona

# 1818

Walaqad ja'ana fee assamai buroojan wazayyannaha lilnnathireena

# 1819

Wahafithnaha min kulli shaytanin rajeemin

# 1820

Illa mani istaraqa assam'a faatba'ahu shihabun mubeenun

# 1821

Waalarda madadnaha waalqayna feeha rawasiya waanbatna feeha min kulli shayin mawzoonin

# 1822

Waja'ana lakum feeha ma'ayisha waman lastum lahu biraziqeena

# 1823

Wain min shayin illa 'indana khazainuhu wama nunazziluhu illa biqadarin ma'loomin

# 1824

Waarsana arriyaha lawaqiha faanzana mina assamai maan faasqaynakumoohu wama antum lahu bikhazineena

# 1825

Wainna lanahnu nuhyee wanumeetu wanahnu alwarithoona

# 1826

Walaqad 'alimna almustaqdimeena minkum walaqad 'alimna almustakhireena

# 1827

Wainna rabbaka huwa yahshuruhum innahu hakeemun 'aleemun

# 1828

Walaqad khalaqna alinsana min sasalin min hamain masnoonin

# 1829

Waaljanna khalaqnahu min qablu min nari assamoomi

# 1830

Waith qala rabbuka lilmalaikati innee khaliqun basharan min sasalin min hamain masnoonin

# 1831

Faitha sawwaytuhu wanafakhtu feehi min roohee faqa'oo lahu sajideena

# 1832

Fasajada almalaikatu kulluhum ajma'oona

# 1833

Illa ibleesa aba an yakoona ma'a assajideena

# 1834

Qala ya ibleesu ma laka alla takoona ma'a assajideena

# 1835

Qala lam akun liasjuda libasharin khalaqtahu min sasalin min hamain masnoonin

# 1836

Qala faokhruj minha fainnaka rajeemun

# 1837

Wainna 'alayka alla'nata ila yawmi addeeni

# 1838

Qala rabbi faanthirnee ila yawmi yub'athoona

# 1839

Qala fainnaka mina almunthareena

# 1840

Ila yawmi alwaqti alma'loomi

# 1841

Qala rabbi bima aghwaytanee laozayyinanna lahum fee alardi walaoghwiyannahum ajma'eena

# 1842

Illa 'ibadaka minhumu almukhlaseena

# 1843

Qala hatha siratun 'alayya mustaqeemun

# 1844

Inna 'ibadee laysa laka 'alayhim sultanun illa mani ittaba'aka mina alghaweena

# 1845

Wainna jahannama lamaw'iduhum ajma'eena

# 1846

Laha sab'atu abwabin likulli babin minhum juzon maqsoomun

# 1847

Inna almuttaqeena fee jannatin wa'uyoonin

# 1848

Odkhulooha bisalamin amineena

# 1849

Wanaza'na ma fee sudoorihim min ghillin ikhwanan 'ala sururin mutaqabileena

# 1850

La yamassuhum feeha nasabun wama hum minha bimukhrajeena

# 1851

Nabbi 'ibadee annee ana alghafooru arraheemu

# 1852

Wa anna 'athabee huwa al'athabu alaleemu

# 1853

Wanabbihum 'an dayfi ibraheema

# 1854

Ith dakhaloo 'alayhi faqaloo salaman qala inna minkum wajiloona

# 1855

Qaloo la tawjal inna nubashshiruka bighulamin 'aleemin

# 1856

Qala abashshartumoonee 'ala an massaniya alkibaru fabima tubashshirooni

# 1857

Qaloo bashsharnaka bialhaqqi fala takun mina alqaniteena

# 1858

Qala waman yaqnatu min rahmati rabbihi illa addalloona

# 1859

Qala fama khatbukum ayyuha almursaloona

# 1860

Qaloo inna orsilna ila qawmin mujrimeena

# 1861

Illa ala lootin inna lamunajjoohum ajma'eena

# 1862

Illa imraatahu qaddarna innaha lamina alghabireena

# 1863

Falamma jaa ala lootin almursaloona

# 1864

Qala innakum qawmun munkaroona

# 1865

Qaloo bal jinaka bima kanoo feehi yamtaroona

# 1866

Waataynaka bialhaqqi wainna lasadiqoona

# 1867

Faasri biahlika biqit'in mina allayli waittabi' adbarahum wala yatafit minkum ahadun waimdoo haythu tumaroona

# 1868

Waqadayna ilayhi thalika alamra anna dabira haolai maqtoo'un musbiheena

# 1869

Wajaa ahlu almadeenati yastabshiroona

# 1870

Qala inna haolai dayfee fala tafdahooni

# 1871

Waittaqoo Allaha wala tukhzooni

# 1872

Qaloo awalam nanhaka 'ani al'alameena

# 1873

Qala haolai banatee in kuntum fa'ileena

# 1874

La'amruka innahum lafee sakratihim ya'mahoona

# 1875

Faakhathathumu assayhatu mushriqeena

# 1876

Faja'ana 'aliyaha safilaha waamtarna 'alayhim hijaratan min sijjeelin

# 1877

Inna fee thalika laayatin lilmutawassimeena

# 1878

Wainnaha labisabeelin muqeemin

# 1879

Inna fee thalika laayatan lilmumineena

# 1880

Wain kana ashabu alaykati lathalimeena

# 1881

Faintaqamna minhum wainnahuma labiimamin mubeenin

# 1882

Walaqad kaththaba ashabu alhijri almursaleena

# 1883

Waataynahum ayatina fakanoo 'anha mu'rideena

# 1884

Wakanoo yanhitoona mina aljibali buyootan amineena

# 1885

Faakhathathumu assayhatu musbiheena

# 1886

Fama aghna 'anhum ma kanoo yaksiboona

# 1887

Wama khalaqna assamawati waalarda wama baynahuma illa bialhaqqi wainna assa'ata laatiyatun faisfahi assafha aljameela

# 1888

Inna rabbaka huwa alkhallaqu al'aleemu

# 1889

Walaqad ataynaka sab'an mina almathanee waalqurana al'atheema

# 1890

La tamuddanna 'aynayka ila ma matta'na bihi azwajan minhum wala tahzan 'alayhim waikhfid janahaka lilmumineena

# 1891

Waqul innee ana annatheeru almubeenu

# 1892

Kama anzana 'ala almuqtasimeena

# 1893

Allatheena ja'aloo alqurana 'ideena

# 1894

Fawarabbika lanasalannahum ajma'eena

# 1895

'amma kanoo ya'maloona

# 1896

Faisda' bima tumaru waa'rid 'ani almushrikeena

# 1897

Inna kafaynaka almustahzieena

# 1898

Allatheena yaj'aloona ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara fasawfa ya'lamoona

# 1899

Walaqad na'lamu annaka yadeequ sadruka bima yaqooloona

# 1900

Fasabbih bihamdi rabbika wakun mina assajideena

# 1901

Wao'bud rabbaka hatta yatiyaka alyaqeenu

# 1902

Ata amru Allahi fala tasta'jiloohu subhanahu wata'ala 'amma yushrikoona

# 1903

Yunazzilu almalaikata biarroohi min amrihi 'ala man yashao min 'ibadihi an anthiroo annahu la ilaha illa ana faittaqooni

# 1904

Khalaqa assamawati waalarda bialhaqqi ta'ala 'amma yushrikoona

# 1905

Khalaqa alinsana min nutfatin faitha huwa khaseemun mubeenun

# 1906

Waalan'ama khalaqaha lakum feeha difon wamanafi'u waminha takuloona

# 1907

Walakum feeha jamalun heena tureehoona waheena tasrahoona

# 1908

Watahmilu athqalakum ila baladin lam takoonoo baligheehi illa bishiqqi alanfusi inna rabbakum laraoofun raheemun

# 1909

Waalkhayla waalbighala waalhameera litarkabooha wazeenatan wayakhluqu ma la ta'lamoona

# 1910

Wa'ala Allahi qasdu assabeeli waminha jairun walaw shaa lahadakum ajma'eena

# 1911

Huwa allathee anzala mina assamai maan lakum minhu sharabun waminhu shajarun feehi tuseemoona

# 1912

Yunbitu lakum bihi azzar'a waazzaytoona waannakheela waala'naba wamin kulli aththamarati inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin yatafakkaroona

# 1913

Wasakhkhara lakumu allayla waannahara waashshamsa waalqamara waannujoomu musakhkharatun biamrihi inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin ya'qiloona

# 1914

Wama tharaa lakum fee alardi mukhtalifan alwanuhu inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin yaththakkaroona

# 1915

Wahuwa allathee sakhkhara albahra litakuloo minhu lahman tariyyan watastakhrijoo minhu hilyatan talbasoonaha watara alfulka mawakhira feehi walitabtaghoo min fadlihi wala'allakum tashkuroona

# 1916

Waalqa fee alardi rawasiya an tameeda bikum waanharan wasubulan la'allakum tahtadoona

# 1917

Wa'alamatin wabiannajmi hum yahtadoona

# 1918

Afaman yakhluqu kaman la yakhluqu afala tathakkaroona

# 1919

Wain ta'uddoo ni'mata Allahi la tuhsooha inna Allaha laghafoorun raheemun

# 1920

WaAllahu ya'lamu ma tusirroona wama tu'linoona

# 1921

Waallatheena yad'oona min dooni Allahi la yakhluqoona shayan wahum yukhlaqoona

# 1922

Amwatun ghayru ahyain wama yash'uroona ayyana yub'athoona

# 1923

Ilahukum ilahun wahidun faallatheena la yuminoona bialakhirati quloobuhum munkiratun wahum mustakbiroona

# 1924

La jarama anna Allaha ya'lamu ma yusirroona wama yu'linoona innahu la yuhibbu almustakbireena

# 1925

Waitha qeela lahum matha anzala rabbukum qaloo asateeru alawwaleena

# 1926

Liyahmiloo awzarahum kamilatan yawma alqiyamati wamin awzari allatheena yudilloonahum bighayri 'ilmin ala saa ma yaziroona

# 1927

Qad makara allatheena min qablihim faata Allahu bunyanahum mina alqawa'idi fakharra 'alayhimu assaqfu min fawqihim waatahumu al'athabu min haythu la yash'uroona

# 1928

Thumma yawma alqiyamati yukhzeehim wayaqoolu ayna shurakaiya allatheena kuntum tushaqqoona feehim qala allatheena ootoo al'ilma inna alkhizya alyawma waassooa 'ala alkafireena

# 1929

Allatheena tatawaffahumu almalaikatu thalimee anfusihim faalqawoo assalama ma kunna na'malu min sooin bala inna Allaha 'aleemun bima kuntum ta'maloona

# 1930

Faodkhuloo abwaba jahannama khalideena feeha falabisa mathwa almutakabbireena

# 1931

Waqeela lillatheena ittaqaw matha anzala rabbukum qaloo khayran lillatheena ahsanoo fee hathihi addunya hasanatun waladaru alakhirati khayrun walani'ma daru almuttaqeena

# 1932

Jannatu 'adnin yadkhuloonaha tajree min tahtiha alanharu lahum feeha ma yashaoona kathalika yajzee Allahu almuttaqeena

# 1933

Allatheena tatawaffahumu almalaikatu tayyibeena yaqooloona salamun 'alaykumu odkhuloo aljannata bima kuntum ta'maloona

# 1934

Hal yanthuroona illa an tatiyahumu almalaikatu aw yatiya amru rabbika kathalika fa'ala allatheena min qablihim wama thalamahumu Allahu walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoona

# 1935

Faasabahum sayyiatu ma 'amiloo wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioona

# 1936

Waqala allatheena ashrakoo law shaa Allahu ma 'abadna min doonihi min shayin nahnu wala abaona wala harramna min doonihi min shayin kathalika fa'ala allatheena min qablihim fahal 'ala arrusuli illa albalaghu almubeenu

# 1937

Walaqad ba'athna fee kulli ommatin rasoolan ani o'budoo Allaha waijtaniboo attaghoota faminhum man hada Allahu waminhum man haqqat 'alayhi addalalatu faseeroo fee alardi faonthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu almukaththibeena

# 1938

In tahris 'ala hudahum fainna Allaha la yahdee man yudillu wama lahum min nasireena

# 1939

Waaqsamoo biAllahi jahda aymanihim la yab'athu Allahu man yamootu bala wa'dan 'alayhi haqqan walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoona

# 1940

Liyubayyina lahumu allathee yakhtalifoona feehi waliya'lama allatheena kafaroo annahum kanoo kathibeena

# 1941

Innama qawluna lishayin itha aradnahu an naqoola lahu kun fayakoonu

# 1942

Waallatheena hajaroo fee Allahi min ba'di ma thulimoo lanubawwiannahum fee addunya hasanatan walaajru alakhirati akbaru law kanoo ya'lamoona

# 1943

Allatheena sabaroo wa'ala rabbihim yatawakkaloona

# 1944

Wama arsana min qablika illa rijalan noohee ilayhim faisaloo ahla aththikri in kuntum la ta'lamoona

# 1945

Bialbayyinati waazzuburi waanzana ilayka aththikra litubayyina lilnnasi ma nuzzila ilayhim wala'allahum yatafakkaroona

# 1946

Afaamina allatheena makaroo assayyiati an yakhsifa Allahu bihimu alarda aw yatiyahumu al'athabu min haythu la yash'uroona

# 1947

Aw yakhuthahum fee taqallubihim fama hum bimu'jizeena

# 1948

Aw yakhuthahum 'ala takhawwufin fainna rabbakum laraoofun raheemun

# 1949

Awa lam yaraw ila ma khalaqa Allahu min shayin yatafayyao thilaluhu 'ani alyameeni waashshamaili sujjadan lillahi wahum dakhiroona

# 1950

Walillahi yasjudu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi min dabbatin waalmalaikatu wahum la yastakbiroona

# 1951

Yakhafoona rabbahum min fawqihim wayaf'aloona ma yumaroona

# 1952

Waqala Allahu la tattakhithoo ilahayni ithnayni innama huwa ilahun wahidun faiyyaya fairhabooni

# 1953

Walahu ma fee assamawati waalardi walahu addeenu wasiban afaghayra Allahi tattaqoona

# 1954

Wama bikum min ni'matin famina Allahi thumma itha massakumu addurru failayhi tajaroona

# 1955

Thumma itha kashafa addurra 'ankum itha fareequn minkum birabbihim yushrikoona

# 1956

Liyakfuroo bima ataynahum fatamatta'oo fasawfa ta'lamoona

# 1957

Wayaj'aloona lima la ya'lamoona naseeban mimma razaqnahum taAllahi latusalunna 'amma kuntum taftaroona

# 1958

Wayaj'aloona lillahi albanati subhanahu walahum ma yashtahoona

# 1959

Waitha bushshira ahaduhum bialontha thalla wajhuhu muswaddan wahuwa katheemun

# 1960

Yatawara mina alqawmi min sooi ma bushshira bihi ayumsikuhu 'ala hoonin am yadussuhu fee atturabi ala saa ma yahkumoona

# 1961

Lillatheena la yuminoona bialakhirati mathalu assawi walillahi almathalu ala'la wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 1962

Walaw yuakhithu Allahu annasa bithulmihim ma taraka 'alayha min dabbatin walakin yuakhkhiruhum ila ajalin musamman faitha jaa ajaluhum la yastakhiroona sa'atan wala yastaqdimoona

# 1963

Wayaj'aloona lillahi ma yakrahoona watasifu asinatuhumu alkathiba anna lahumu alhusna la jarama anna lahumu annara waannahum mufratoona

# 1964

TaAllahi laqad arsana ila omamin min qablika fazayyana lahumu ashshaytanu a'malahum fahuwa waliyyuhumu alyawma walahum 'athabun aleemun

# 1965

Wama anzana 'alayka alkitaba illa litubayyina lahumu allathee ikhtalafoo feehi wahudan warahmatan liqawmin yuminoona

# 1966

WaAllahu anzala mina assamai maan faahya bihi alarda ba'da mawtiha inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin yasma'oona

# 1967

Wainna lakum fee alan'ami la'ibratan nusqeekum mimma fee butoonihi min bayni farthin wadamin labanan khalisan saighan lilshsharibeena

# 1968

Wamin thamarati annakheeli waala'nabi tattakhithoona minhu sakaran warizqan hasanan inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin ya'qiloona

# 1969

Waawha rabbuka ila annahli ani ittakhithee mina aljibali buyootan wamina ashshajari wamimma ya'rishoona

# 1970

Thumma kulee min kulli aththamarati faoslukee subula rabbiki thululan yakhruju min butooniha sharabun mukhtalifun alwanuhu feehi shifaon lilnnasi inna fee thalika laayatan liqawmin yatafakkaroona

# 1971

WaAllahu khalaqakum thumma yatawaffakum waminkum man yuraddu ila arthali al'umuri likay la ya'lama ba'da 'ilmin shayan inna Allaha 'aleemun qadeerun

# 1972

WaAllahu faddala ba'dakum 'ala ba'din fee arrizqi fama allatheena fuddiloo biraddee rizqihim 'ala ma malakat aymanuhum fahum feehi sawaon afabini'mati Allahi yajhadoona

# 1973

WaAllahu ja'ala lakum min anfusikum azwajan waja'ala lakum min azwajikum baneena wahafadatan warazaqakum mina attayyibati afabialbatili yuminoona wabini'mati Allahi hum yakfuroona

# 1974

Waya'budoona min dooni Allahi ma la yamliku lahum rizqan mina assamawati waalardi shayan wala yastatee'oona

# 1975

Fala tadriboo lillahi alamthala inna Allaha ya'lamu waantum la ta'lamoona

# 1976

Daraba Allahu mathalan 'abdan mamlookan la yaqdiru 'ala shayin waman razaqnahu minna rizqan hasanan fahuwa yunfiqu minhu sirran wajahran hal yastawoona alhamdu lillahi bal aktharuhum la ya'lamoona

# 1977

Wadaraba Allahu mathalan rajulayni ahaduhuma abkamu la yaqdiru 'ala shayin wahuwa kallun 'ala mawlahu aynama yuwajjihhu la yati bikhayrin hal yastawee huwa waman yamuru bial'adli wahuwa 'ala siratin mustaqeemin

# 1978

Walillahi ghaybu assamawati waalardi wama amru assa'ati illa kalamhi albasari aw huwa aqrabu inna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 1979

WaAllahu akhrajakum min butooni ommahatikum la ta'lamoona shayan waja'ala lakumu assam'a waalabsara waalafidata la'allakum tashkuroona

# 1980

Alam yaraw ila attayri musakhkharatin fee jawwi assamai ma yumsikuhunna illa Allahu inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoona

# 1981

WaAllahu ja'ala lakum min buyootikum sakanan waja'ala lakum min juloodi alan'ami buyootan tastakhiffoonaha yawma tha'nikum wayawma iqamatikum wamin aswafiha waawbariha waash'ariha athathan wamata'an ila heenin

# 1982

WaAllahu ja'ala lakum mimma khalaqa thilalan waja'ala lakum mina aljibali aknanan waja'ala lakum sarabeela taqeekumu alharra wasarabeela taqeekum basakum kathalika yutimmu ni'matahu 'alaykum la'allakum tuslimoona

# 1983

Fain tawallaw fainnama 'alayka albalaghu almubeenu

# 1984

Ya'rifoona ni'mata Allahi thumma yunkiroonaha waaktharuhumu alkafiroona

# 1985

Wayawma nab'athu min kulli ommatin shaheedan thumma la yuthanu lillatheena kafaroo wala hum yusta'taboona

# 1986

Waitha raa allatheena thalamoo al'athaba fala yukhaffafu 'anhum wala hum yuntharoona

# 1987

Waitha raa allatheena ashrakoo shurakaahum qaloo rabbana haolai shurakaona allatheena kunna nad'oo min doonika faalqaw ilayhimu alqawla innakum lakathiboona

# 1988

Waalqaw ila Allahi yawmaithin assalama wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yaftaroona

# 1989

Allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi zidnahum 'athaban fawqa al'athabi bima kanoo yufsidoona

# 1990

Wayawma nab'athu fee kulli ommatin shaheedan 'alayhim min anfusihim wajina bika shaheedan 'ala haolai wanazzana 'alayka alkitaba tibyanan likulli shayin wahudan warahmatan wabushra lilmuslimeena

# 1991

Inna Allaha yamuru bial'adli waalihsani waeetai thee alqurba wayanha 'ani alfahshai waalmunkari waalbaghyi ya'ithukum la'allakum tathakkaroona

# 1992

Waawfoo bi'ahdi Allahi itha 'ahadtum wala tanqudoo alaymana ba'da tawkeediha waqad ja'atumu Allaha 'alaykum kafeelan inna Allaha ya'lamu ma taf'aloona

# 1993

Wala takoonoo kaallatee naqadat ghazlaha min ba'di quwwatin ankathan tattakhithoona aymanakum dakhalan baynakum an takoona ommatun hiya arba min ommatin innama yablookumu Allahu bihi walayubayyinanna lakum yawma alqiyamati ma kuntum feehi takhtalifoona

# 1994

Walaw shaa Allahu laja'alakum ommatan wahidatan walakin yudillu man yashao wayahdee man yashao walatusalunna 'amma kuntum ta'maloona

# 1995

Wala tattakhithoo aymanakum dakhalan baynakum fatazilla qadamun ba'da thubootiha watathooqoo assooa bima sadadtum 'an sabeeli Allahi walakum 'athabun 'atheemun

# 1996

Wala tashtaroo bi'ahdi Allahi thamanan qaleelan innama 'inda Allahi huwa khayrun lakum in kuntum ta'lamoona

# 1997

Ma 'indakum yanfadu wama 'inda Allahi baqin walanajziyanna allatheena sabaroo ajrahum biahsani ma kanoo ya'maloona

# 1998

Man 'amila salihan min thakarin aw ontha wahuwa muminun falanuhyiyannahu hayatan tayyibatan walanajziyannahum ajrahum biahsani ma kanoo ya'maloona

# 1999

Faitha qarata alqurana faista'ith biAllahi mina ashshaytani arrajeemi

# 2000

Innahu laysa lahu sultanun 'ala allatheena amanoo wa'ala rabbihim yatawakkaloona

# 2001

Innama sultanuhu 'ala allatheena yatawallawnahu waallatheena hum bihi mushrikoona

# 2002

Waitha baddana ayatan makana ayatin waAllahu a'lamu bima yunazzilu qaloo innama anta muftarin bal aktharuhum la ya'lamoona

# 2003

Qul nazzalahu roohu alqudusi min rabbika bialhaqqi liyuthabbita allatheena amanoo wahudan wabushra lilmuslimeena

# 2004

Walaqad na'lamu annahum yaqooloona innama yu'allimuhu basharun lisanu allathee yulhidoona ilayhi a'jamiyyun wahatha lisanun 'arabiyyun mubeenun

# 2005

Inna allatheena la yuminoona biayati Allahi la yahdeehimu Allahu walahum 'athabun aleemun

# 2006

Innama yaftaree alkathiba allatheena la yuminoona biayati Allahi waolaika humu alkathiboona

# 2007

Man kafara biAllahi min ba'di eemanihi illa man okriha waqalbuhu mutmainnun bialeemani walakin man sharaha bialkufri sadran fa'alayhim ghadabun mina Allahi walahum 'athabun 'atheemun

# 2008

Thalika biannahumu istahabboo alhayata addunya 'ala alakhirati waanna Allaha la yahdee alqawma alkafireena

# 2009

Olaika allatheena taba'a Allahu 'ala quloobihim wasam'ihim waabsarihim waolaika humu alghafiloona

# 2010

La jarama annahum fee alakhirati humu alkhasiroona

# 2011

Thumma inna rabbaka lillatheena hajaroo min ba'di ma futinoo thumma jahadoo wasabaroo inna rabbaka min ba'diha laghafoorun raheemun

# 2012

Yawma tatee kullu nafsin tujadilu 'an nafsiha watuwaffa kullu nafsin ma 'amilat wahum la yuthlamoona

# 2013

Wadaraba Allahu mathalan qaryatan kanat aminatan mutmainnatan yateeha rizquha raghadan min kulli makanin fakafarat bian'umi Allahi faathaqaha Allahu libasa aljoo'i waalkhawfi bima kanoo yasna'oona

# 2014

Walaqad jaahum rasoolun minhum fakaththaboohu faakhathahumu al'athabu wahum thalimoona

# 2015

Fakuloo mimma razaqakumu Allahu halalan tayyiban waoshkuroo ni'mata Allahi in kuntum iyyahu ta'budoona

# 2016

Innama harrama 'alaykumu almaytata waaddama walahma alkhinzeeri wama ohilla lighayri Allahi bihi famani idturra ghayra baghin wala 'adin fainna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun

# 2017

Wala taqooloo lima tasifu asinatukumu alkathiba hatha halalun wahatha haramun litaftaroo 'ala Allahi alkathiba inna allatheena yaftaroona 'ala Allahi alkathiba la yuflihoona

# 2018

Mata'un qaleelun walahum 'athabun aleemun

# 2019

Wa'ala allatheena hadoo harramna ma qasasna 'alayka min qablu wama thalamnahum walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoona

# 2020

Thumma inna rabbaka lillatheena 'amiloo assooa bijahalatin thumma taboo min ba'di thalika waaslahoo inna rabbaka min ba'diha laghafoorun raheemun

# 2021

Inna ibraheema kana ommatan qanitan lillahi haneefan walam yaku mina almushrikeena

# 2022

Shakiran lian'umihi ijtabahu wahadahu ila siratin mustaqeemin

# 2023

Waataynahu fee addunya hasanatan wainnahu fee alakhirati lamina assaliheena

# 2024

Thumma awhayna ilayka ani ittabi' millata ibraheema haneefan wama kana mina almushrikeena

# 2025

Innama ju'ila assabtu 'ala allatheena ikhtalafoo feehi wainna rabbaka layahkumu baynahum yawma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi yakhtalifoona

# 2026

Od'u ila sabeeli rabbika bialhikmati waalmaw'ithati alhasanati wajadilhum biallatee hiya ahsanu inna rabbaka huwa a'lamu biman dalla 'an sabeelihi wahuwa a'lamu bialmuhtadeena

# 2027

Wain 'aqabtum fa'aqiboo bimithli ma 'ooqibtum bihi walain sabartum lahuwa khayrun lilssabireena

# 2028

Waisbir wama sabruka illa biAllahi wala tahzan 'alayhim wala taku fee dayqin mimma yamkuroona

# 2029

Inna Allaha ma'a allatheena ittaqaw waallatheena hum muhsinoona

# 2030

Subhana allathee asra bi'abdihi laylan mina almasjidi alharami ila almasjidi alaqsa allathee barakna hawlahu linuriyahu min ayatina innahu huwa assamee'u albaseeru

# 2031

Waatayna moosa alkitaba waja'anahu hudan libanee israeela alla tattakhithoo min doonee wakeelan

# 2032

Thurriyyata man hamana ma'a noohin innahu kana 'abdan shakooran

# 2033

Waqadayna ila banee israeela fee alkitabi latufsidunna fee alardi marratayni walata'lunna 'uluwwan kabeeran

# 2034

Faitha jaa wa'du oolahuma ba'athna 'alaykum 'ibadan lana olee basin shadeedin fajasoo khilala addiyari wakana wa'dan maf'oolan

# 2035

Thumma radadna lakumu alkarrata 'alayhim waamdadnakum biamwalin wabaneena waja'anakum akthara nafeeran

# 2036

In ahsantum ahsantum lianfusikum wain asatum falaha faitha jaa wa'du alakhirati liyasoooo wujoohakum waliyadkhuloo almasjida kama dakhaloohu awwala marratin waliyutabbiroo ma 'alaw tatbeeran

# 2037

'asa rabbukum an yarhamakum wain 'udtum 'udna waja'ana jahannama lilkafireena haseeran

# 2038

Inna hatha alqurana yahdee lillatee hiya aqwamu wayubashshiru almumineena allatheena ya'maloona assalihati anna lahum ajran kabeeran

# 2039

Waanna allatheena la yuminoona bialakhirati a'tadna lahum 'athaban aleeman

# 2040

Wayad'u alinsanu biashsharri du'aahu bialkhayri wakana alinsanu 'ajoolan

# 2041

Waja'ana allayla waannahara ayatayni famahawna ayata allayli waja'ana ayata annahari mubsiratan litabtaghoo fadlan min rabbikum walita'lamoo 'adada assineena waalhisaba wakulla shayin fassanahu tafseelan

# 2042

Wakulla insanin azamnahu tairahu fee 'unuqihi wanukhriju lahu yawma alqiyamati kitaban yalqahu manshooran

# 2043

Iqra kitabaka kafa binafsika alyawma 'alayka haseeban

# 2044

Mani ihtada fainnama yahtadee linafsihi waman dalla fainnama yadillu 'alayha wala taziru waziratun wizra okhra wama kunna mu'aththibeena hatta nab'atha rasoolan

# 2045

Waitha aradna an nuhlika qaryatan amarna mutrafeeha fafasaqoo feeha fahaqqa 'alayha alqawlu fadammarnaha tadmeeran

# 2046

Wakam ahlakna mina alqurooni min ba'di noohin wakafa birabbika bithunoobi 'ibadihi khabeeran baseeran

# 2047

Man kana yureedu al'ajilata 'ajjana lahu feeha ma nashao liman nureedu thumma ja'ana lahu jahannama yaslaha mathmooman madhooran

# 2048

Waman arada alakhirata wasa'a laha sa'yaha wahuwa muminun faolaika kana sa'yuhum mashkooran

# 2049

Kullan numiddu haolai wahaolai min 'atai rabbika wama kana 'atao rabbika mahthooran

# 2050

Onthur kayfa faddana ba'dahum 'ala ba'din walalakhiratu akbaru darajatin waakbaru tafdeelan

# 2051

La taj'al ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara fataq'uda mathmooman makhthoolan

# 2052

Waqada rabbuka alla ta'budoo illa iyyahu wabialwalidayni ihsanan imma yablughanna 'indaka alkibara ahaduhuma aw kilahuma fala taqul lahuma offin wala tanharhuma waqul lahuma qawlan kareeman

# 2053

Waikhfid lahuma janaha aththulli mina arrahmati waqul rabbi irhamhuma kama rabbayanee sagheeran

# 2054

Rabbukum a'lamu bima fee nufoosikum in takoonoo saliheena fainnahu kana lilawwabeena ghafooran

# 2055

Waati tha alqurba haqqahu waalmiskeena waibna assabeeli wala tubaththir tabtheeran

# 2056

Inna almubaththireena kanoo ikhwana ashshayateeni wakana ashshaytanu lirabbihi kafooran

# 2057

Waimma tu'ridanna 'anhumu ibtighaa rahmatin min rabbika tarjooha faqul lahum qawlan maysooran

# 2058

Wala taj'al yadaka maghloolatan ila 'unuqika wala tabsutha kulla albasti fataq'uda malooman mahsooran

# 2059

Inna rabbaka yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru innahu kana bi'ibadihi khabeeran baseeran

# 2060

Wala taqtuloo awladakum khashyata imlaqin nahnu narzuquhum waiyyakum inna qatlahum kana khitan kabeeran

# 2061

Wala taqraboo azzina innahu kana fahishatan wasaa sabeelan

# 2062

Wala taqtuloo annafsa allatee harrama Allahu illa bialhaqqi waman qutila mathlooman faqad ja'ana liwaliyyihi sultanan fala yusrif fee alqatli innahu kana mansooran

# 2063

Wala taqraboo mala alyateemi illa biallatee hiya ahsanu hatta yablugha ashuddahu waawfoo bial'ahdi inna al'ahda kana masoolan

# 2064

Waawfoo alkayla itha kiltum wazinoo bialqistasi almustaqeemi thalika khayrun waahsanu taweelan

# 2065

Wala taqfu ma laysa laka bihi 'ilmun inna assam'a waalbasara waalfuada kullu olaika kana 'anhu masoolan

# 2066

Wala tamshi fee alardi marahan innaka lan takhriqa alarda walan tablugha aljibala toolan

# 2067

Kullu thalika kana sayyiohu 'inda rabbika makroohan

# 2068

Thalika mimma awha ilayka rabbuka mina alhikmati wala taj'al ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara fatulqa fee jahannama malooman madhooran

# 2069

Afaasfakum rabbukum bialbaneena waittakhatha mina almalaikati inathan innakum lataqooloona qawlan 'atheeman

# 2070

Walaqad sarrafna fee hatha alqurani liyaththakkaroo wama yazeeduhum illa nufooran

# 2071

Qul law kana ma'ahu alihatun kama yaqooloona ithan laibtaghaw ila thee al'arshi sabeelan

# 2072

Subhanahu wata'ala 'amma yaqooloona 'uluwwan kabeeran

# 2073

Tusabbihu lahu assamawatu assab'u waalardu waman feehinna wain min shayin illa yusabbihu bihamdihi walakin la tafqahoona tasbeehahum innahu kana haleeman ghafooran

# 2074

Waitha qarata alqurana ja'ana baynaka wabayna allatheena la yuminoona bialakhirati hijaban mastooran

# 2075

Waja'ana 'ala quloobihim akinnatan an yafqahoohu wafee athanihim waqran waitha thakarta rabbaka fee alqurani wahdahu wallaw 'ala adbarihim nufooran

# 2076

Nahnu a'lamu bima yastami'oona bihi ith yastami'oona ilayka waith hum najwa ith yaqoolu aththalimoona in tattabi'oona illa rajulan mashooran

# 2077

Onthur kayfa daraboo laka alamthala fadalloo fala yastatee'oona sabeelan

# 2078

Waqaloo aitha kunna 'ithaman warufatan ainna lamab'oothoona khalqan jadeedan

# 2079

Qul koonoo hijaratan aw hadeedan

# 2080

Aw khalqan mimma yakburu fee sudoorikum fasayaqooloona man yu'eeduna quli allathee fatarakum awwala marratin fasayunghidoona ilayka ruoosahum wayaqooloona mata huwa qul 'asa an yakoona qareeban

# 2081

Yawma yad'ookum fatastajeeboona bihamdihi watathunnoona in labithtum illa qaleelan

# 2082

Waqul li'ibadee yaqooloo allatee hiya ahsanu inna ashshaytana yanzaghu baynahum inna ashshaytana kana lilinsani 'aduwwan mubeenan

# 2083

Rabbukum a'lamu bikum in yasha yarhamkum aw in yasha yu'aththibkum wama arsanaka 'alayhim wakeelan

# 2084

Warabbuka a'lamu biman fee assamawati waalardi walaqad faddana ba'da annabiyyeena 'ala ba'din waatayna dawooda zabooran

# 2085

Quli od'u allatheena za'amtum min doonihi fala yamlikoona kashfa addurri 'ankum wala tahweelan

# 2086

Olaika allatheena yad'oona yabtaghoona ila rabbihimu alwaseelata ayyuhum aqrabu wayarjoona rahmatahu wayakhafoona 'athabahu inna 'athaba rabbika kana mahthooran

# 2087

Wain min qaryatin illa nahnu muhlikooha qabla yawmi alqiyamati aw mu'aththibooha 'athaban shadeedan kana thalika fee alkitabi mastooran

# 2088

Wama mana'ana an nursila bialayati illa an kaththaba biha alawwaloona waatayna thamooda annaqata mubsiratan fathalamoo biha wama nursilu bialayati illa takhweefan

# 2089

Waith qulna laka inna rabbaka ahata biannasi wama ja'ana arruya allatee araynaka illa fitnatan lilnnasi waashshajarata almal'oonata fee alqurani wanukhawwifuhum fama yazeeduhum illa tughyanan kabeeran

# 2090

Waith qulna lilmalaikati osjudoo liadama fasajadoo illa ibleesa qala aasjudu liman khalaqta teenan

# 2091

Qala araaytaka hatha allathee karramta 'alayya lain akhkhartani ila yawmi alqiyamati laahtanikanna thurriyyatahu illa qaleelan

# 2092

Qala ithhab faman tabi'aka minhum fainna jahannama jazaokum jazaan mawfooran

# 2093

Waistafziz mani istata'ta minhum bisawtika waajlib 'alayhim bikhaylika warajlika washarikhum fee alamwali waalawladi wa'idhum wama ya'iduhumu ashshaytanu illa ghurooran

# 2094

Inna 'ibadee laysa laka 'alayhim sultanun wakafa birabbika wakeelan

# 2095

Rabbukumu allathee yuzjee lakumu alfulka fee albahri litabtaghoo min fadlihi innahu kana bikum raheeman

# 2096

Waitha massakumu addurru fee albahri dalla man tad'oona illa iyyahu falamma najjakum ila albarri a'radtum wakana alinsanu kafooran

# 2097

Afaamintum an yakhsifa bikum janiba albarri aw yursila 'alaykum hasiban thumma la tajidoo lakum wakeelan

# 2098

Am amintum an yu'eedakum feehi taratan okhra fayursila 'alaykum qasifan mina arreehi fayughriqakum bima kafartum thumma la tajidoo lakum 'alayna bihi tabee'an

# 2099

Walaqad karramna banee adama wahamanahum fee albarri waalbahri warazaqnahum mina attayyibati wafaddanahum 'ala katheerin mimman khalaqna tafdeelan

# 2100

Yawma nad'oo kulla onasin biimamihim faman ootiya kitabahu biyameenihi faolaika yaqraoona kitabahum wala yuthlamoona fateelan

# 2101

Waman kana fee hathihi a'ma fahuwa fee alakhirati a'ma waadallu sabeelan

# 2102

Wain kadoo layaftinoonaka 'ani allathee awhayna ilayka litaftariya 'alayna ghayrahu waithan laittakhathooka khaleelan

# 2103

Walawla an thabbatnaka laqad kidta tarkanu ilayhim shayan qaleelan

# 2104

Ithan laathaqnaka di'fa alhayati wadi'fa almamati thumma la tajidu laka 'alayna naseeran

# 2105

Wain kadoo layastafizzoonaka mina alardi liyukhrijooka minha waithan la yalbathoona khilafaka illa qaleelan

# 2106

Sunnata man qad arsana qablaka min rusulina wala tajidu lisunnatina tahweelan

# 2107

Aqimi assalata lidulooki ashshamsi ila ghasaqi allayli waqurana alfajri inna qurana alfajri kana mashhoodan

# 2108

Wamina allayli fatahajjad bihi nafilatan laka 'asa an yab'athaka rabbuka maqaman mahmoodan

# 2109

Waqul rabbi adkhilnee mudkhala sidqin waakhrijnee mukhraja sidqin waij'al lee min ladunka sultanan naseeran

# 2110

Waqul jaa alhaqqu wazahaqa albatilu inna albatila kana zahooqan

# 2111

Wanunazzilu mina alqurani ma huwa shifaon warahmatun lilmumineena wala yazeedu aththalimeena illa khasaran

# 2112

Waitha an'amna 'ala alinsani a'rada wanaa bijanibihi waitha massahu ashsharru kana yaoosan

# 2113

Qul kullun ya'malu 'ala shakilatihi farabbukum a'lamu biman huwa ahda sabeelan

# 2114

Wayasaloonaka 'ani arroohi quli arroohu min amri rabbee wama ooteetum mina al'ilmi illa qaleelan

# 2115

Walain shina lanathhabanna biallathee awhayna ilayka thumma la tajidu laka bihi 'alayna wakeelan

# 2116

Illa rahmatan min rabbika inna fadlahu kana 'alayka kabeeran

# 2117

Qul laini ijtama'ati alinsu waaljinnu 'ala an yatoo bimithli hatha alqurani la yatoona bimithlihi walaw kana ba'duhum liba'din thaheeran

# 2118

Walaqad sarrafna lilnnasi fee hatha alqurani min kulli mathalin faaba aktharu annasi illa kufooran

# 2119

Waqaloo lan numina laka hatta tafjura lana mina alardi yanboo'an

# 2120

Aw takoona laka jannatun min nakheelin wa'inabin fatufajjira alanhara khilalaha tafjeeran

# 2121

Aw tusqita assamaa kama za'amta 'alayna kisafan aw tatiya biAllahi waalmalaikati qabeelan

# 2122

Aw yakoona laka baytun min zukhrufin aw tarqa fee assamai walan numina liruqiyyika hatta tunazzila 'alayna kitaban naqraohu qul subhana rabbee hal kuntu illa basharan rasoolan

# 2123

Wama mana'a annasa an yuminoo ith jaahumu alhuda illa an qaloo aba'atha Allahu basharan rasoolan

# 2124

Qul law kana fee alardi malaikatun yamshoona mutmainneena lanazzana 'alayhim mina assamai malakan rasoolan

# 2125

Qul kafa biAllahi shaheedan baynee wabaynakum innahu kana bi'ibadihi khabeeran baseeran

# 2126

Waman yahdi Allahu fahuwa almuhtadi waman yudlil falan tajida lahum awliyaa min doonihi wanahshuruhum yawma alqiyamati 'ala wujoohihim 'umyan wabukman wasumman mawahum jahannamu kullama khabat zidnahum sa'eeran

# 2127

Thalika jazaohum biannahum kafaroo biayatina waqaloo aitha kunna 'ithaman warufatan ainna lamab'oothoona khalqan jadeedan

# 2128

Awalam yaraw anna Allaha allathee khalaqa assamawati waalarda qadirun 'ala an yakhluqa mithlahum waja'ala lahum ajalan la rayba feehi faaba aththalimoona illa kufooran

# 2129

Qul law antum tamlikoona khazaina rahmati rabbee ithan laamsaktum khashyata alinfaqi wakana alinsanu qatooran

# 2130

Walaqad atayna moosa tis'a ayatin bayyinatin faisal banee israeela ith jaahum faqala lahu fir'awnu innee laathunnuka ya moosa mashooran

# 2131

Qala laqad 'alimta ma anzala haolai illa rabbu assamawati waalardi basaira wainnee laathunnuka ya fir'awnu mathbooran

# 2132

Faarada an yastafizzahum mina alardi faaghraqnahu waman ma'ahu jamee'an

# 2133

Waqulna min ba'dihi libanee israeela oskunoo alarda faitha jaa wa'du alakhirati jina bikum lafeefan

# 2134

Wabialhaqqi anzanahu wabialhaqqi nazala wama arsanaka illa mubashshiran wanatheeran

# 2135

Waquranan faraqnahu litaqraahu 'ala annasi 'ala mukthin wanazzanahu tanzeelan

# 2136

Qul aminoo bihi aw la tuminoo inna allatheena ootoo al'ilma min qablihi itha yutla 'alayhim yakhirroona lilathqani sujjadan

# 2137

Wayaqooloona subhana rabbina in kana wa'du rabbina lamaf'oolan

# 2138

Wayakhirroona lilathqani yabkoona wayazeeduhum khushoo'an

# 2139

Quli od'oo Allaha awi od'oo arrahmana ayyan ma tad'oo falahu alasmao alhusna wala tajhar bisalatika wala tukhafit biha waibtaghi bayna thalika sabeelan

# 2140

Waquli alhamdu lillahi allathee lam yattakhith waladan walam yakun lahu shareekun fee almulki walam yakun lahu waliyyun mina aththulli wakabbirhu takbeeran

# 2141

Alhamdu lillahi allathee anzala 'ala 'abdihi alkitaba walam yaj'al lahu 'iwajan

# 2142

Qayyiman liyunthira basan shadeedan min ladunhu wayubashshira almumineena allatheena ya'maloona assalihati anna lahum ajran hasanan

# 2143

Makitheena feehi abadan

# 2144

Wayunthira allatheena qaloo ittakhatha Allahu waladan

# 2145

Ma lahum bihi min 'ilmin wala liabaihim kaburat kalimatan takhruju min afwahihim in yaqooloona illa kathiban

# 2146

Fala'allaka bakhi'un nafsaka 'ala atharihim in lam yuminoo bihatha alhadeethi asafan

# 2147

Inna ja'ana ma 'ala alardi zeenatan laha linabluwahum ayyuhum ahsanu 'amalan

# 2148

Wainna laja'iloona ma 'alayha sa'eedan juruzan

# 2149

Am hasibta anna ashaba alkahfi waarraqeemi kanoo min ayatina 'ajaban

# 2150

Ith awa alfityatu ila alkahfi faqaloo rabbana atina min ladunka rahmatan wahayyi lana min amrina rashadan

# 2151

Fadarabna 'ala athanihim fee alkahfi sineena 'adadan

# 2152

Thumma ba'athnahum lina'lama ayyu alhizbayni ahsa lima labithoo amadan

# 2153

Nahnu naqussu 'alayka nabaahum bialhaqqi innahum fityatun amanoo birabbihim wazidnahum hudan

# 2154

Warabatna 'ala quloobihim ith qamoo faqaloo rabbuna rabbu assamawati waalardi lan nad'uwa min doonihi ilahan laqad qulna ithan shatatan

# 2155

Haolai qawmuna ittakhathoo min doonihi alihatan lawla yatoona 'alayhim bisultanin bayyinin faman athlamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban

# 2156

Waithi i'tazatumoohum wama ya'budoona illa Allaha fawoo ila alkahfi yanshur lakum rabbukum min rahmatihi wayuhayyi lakum min amrikum mirfaqan

# 2157

Watara ashshamsa itha tala'at tazawaru 'an kahfihim thata alyameeni waitha gharabat taqriduhum thata ashshimali wahum fee fajwatin minhu thalika min ayati Allahi man yahdi Allahu fahuwa almuhtadi waman yudlil falan tajida lahu waliyyan murshidan

# 2158

Watahsabuhum ayqathan wahum ruqoodun wanuqallibuhum thata alyameeni wathata ashshimali wakalbuhum basitun thira'ayhi bialwaseedi lawi ittala'ta 'alayhim lawallayta minhum firaran walamulita minhum ru'ban

# 2159

Wakathalika ba'athnahum liyatasaaloo baynahum qala qailun minhum kam labithtum qaloo labithna yawman aw ba'da yawmin qaloo rabbukum a'lamu bima labithtum faib'athoo ahadakum biwariqikum hathihi ila almadeenati falyanthur ayyuha azka ta'aman falyatikum birizqin minhu walyatalattaf wala yush'iranna bikum ahadan

# 2160

Innahum in yathharoo 'alaykum yarjumookum aw yu'eedookum fee millatihim walan tuflihoo ithan abadan

# 2161

Wakathalika a'tharna 'alayhim liya'lamoo anna wa'da Allahi haqqun waanna asa'ata la rayba feeha ith yatanaza'oona baynahum amrahum faqaloo ibnoo 'alayhim bunyanan rabbuhum a'lamu bihim qala allatheena ghalaboo 'ala amrihim lanattakhithanna 'alayhim masjidan

# 2162

Sayaqooloona thalathatun rabi'uhum kalbuhum wayaqooloona khamsatun sadisuhum kalbuhum rajman bialghaybi wayaqooloona sab'atun wathaminuhum kalbuhum qul rabbee a'lamu bi'iddatihim ma ya'lamuhum illa qaleelun fala tumari feehim illa miraan thahiran wala tastafti feehim minhum ahadan

# 2163

Wala taqoolanna lishayin innee fa'ilun thalika ghadan

# 2164

Illa an yashaa Allahu waothkur rabbaka itha naseeta waqul 'asa an yahdiyani rabbee liaqraba min hatha rashadan

# 2165

Walabithoo fee kahfihim thalatha miatin sineena waizdadoo tis'an

# 2166

Quli Allahu a'lamu bima labithoo lahu ghaybu assamawati waalardi absir bihi waasmi' ma lahum min doonihi min waliyyin wala yushriku fee hukmihi ahadan

# 2167

Waotlu ma oohiya ilayka min kitabi rabbika la mubaddila likalimatihi walan tajida min doonihi multahadan

# 2168

Waisbir nafsaka ma'a allatheena yad'oona rabbahum bialghadati waal'ashiyyi yureedoona wajhahu wala ta'du 'aynaka 'anhum tureedu zeenata alhayati addunya wala tuti' man aghfana qalbahu 'an thikrina waittaba'a hawahu wakana amruhu furutan

# 2169

Waquli alhaqqu min rabbikum faman shaa falyumin waman shaa falyakfur inna a'tadna lilththalimeena naran ahata bihim suradiquha wain yastagheethoo yughathoo bimain kaalmuhli yashwee alwujooha bisa ashsharabu wasaat murtafaqan

# 2170

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati inna la nudee'u ajra man ahsana 'amalan

# 2171

Olaika lahum jannatu 'adnin tajree min tahtihimu alanharu yuhallawna feeha min asawira min thahabin wayalbasoona thiyaban khudran min sundusin waistabraqin muttakieena feeha 'ala alaraiki ni'ma aththawabu wahasunat murtafaqan

# 2172

Waidrib lahum mathalan rajulayni ja'ana liahadihima jannatayni min a'nabin wahafafnahuma binakhlin waja'ana baynahuma zar'an

# 2173

Kilta aljannatayni atat okulaha walam tathlim minhu shayan wafajjarna khilalahuma naharan

# 2174

Wakana lahu thamarun faqala lisahibihi wahuwa yuhawiruhu ana aktharu minka malan waa'azzu nafaran

# 2175

Wadakhala jannatahu wahuwa thalimun linafsihi qala ma athunnu an tabeeda hathihi abadan

# 2176

Wama athunnu assa'ata qaimatan walain rudidtu ila rabbee laajidanna khayran minha munqalaban

# 2177

Qala lahu sahibuhu wahuwa yuhawiruhu akafarta biallathee khalaqaka min turabin thumma min nutfatin thumma sawwaka rajulan

# 2178

Lakinna huwa Allahu rabbee wala oshriku birabbee ahadan

# 2179

Walawla ith dakhata jannataka qulta ma shaa Allahu la quwwata illa biAllahi in tarani ana aqalla minka malan wawaladan

# 2180

Fa'asa rabbee an yutiyani khayran min jannatika wayursila 'alayha husbanan mina assamai fatusbiha sa'eedan zalaqan

# 2181

Aw yusbiha maoha ghawran falan tastatee'a lahu talaban

# 2182

Waoheeta bithamarihi faasbaha yuqallibu kaffayhi 'ala ma anfaqa feeha wahiya khawiyatun 'ala 'urooshiha wayaqoolu ya laytanee lam oshrik birabbee ahadan

# 2183

Walam takun lahu fiatun yansuroonahu min dooni Allahi wama kana muntasiran

# 2184

Hunalika alwalayatu lillahi alhaqqi huwa khayrun thawaban wakhayrun 'uqban

# 2185

Waidrib lahum mathala alhayati addunya kamain anzanahu mina assamai faikhtalata bihi nabatu alardi faasbaha hasheeman tathroohu arriyahu wakana Allahu 'ala kulli shayin muqtadiran

# 2186

Almalu waalbanoona zeenatu alhayati addunya waalbaqiyatu assalihatu khayrun 'inda rabbika thawaban wakhayrun amalan

# 2187

Wayawma nusayyiru aljibala watara alarda barizatan wahasharnahum falam nughadir minhum ahadan

# 2188

Wa'uridoo 'ala rabbika saffan laqad jitumoona kama khalaqnakum awwala marratin bal za'amtum allan naj'ala lakum maw'idan

# 2189

Wawudi'a alkitabu fatara almujrimeena mushfiqeena mimma feehi wayaqooloona ya waylatana ma lihatha alkitabi la yughadiru sagheeratan wala kabeeratan illa ahsaha wawajadoo ma 'amiloo hadiran wala yathlimu rabbuka ahadan

# 2190

Waith qulna lilmalaikati osjudoo liadama fasajadoo illa ibleesa kana mina aljinni fafasaqa 'an amri rabbihi afatattakhithoonahu wathurriyyatahu awliyaa min doonee wahum lakum 'aduwwun bisa lilththalimeena badalan

# 2191

Ma ashhadtuhum khalqa assamawati waalardi wala khalqa anfusihim wama kuntu muttakhitha almudilleena 'adudan

# 2192

Wayawma yaqoolu nadoo shurakaiya allatheena za'amtum fada'awhum falam yastajeeboo lahum waja'ana baynahum mawbiqan

# 2193
