Waraa almujrimoona annara fathannoo annahum muwaqi'ooha walam yajidoo 'anha masrifan

# 2194

Walaqad sarrafna fee hatha alqurani lilnnasi min kulli mathalin wakana alinsanu akthara shayin jadalan

# 2195

Wama mana'a annasa an yuminoo ith jaahumu alhuda wayastaghfiroo rabbahum illa an tatiyahum sunnatu alawwaleena aw yatiyahumu al'athabu qubulan

# 2196

Wama nursilu almursaleena illa mubashshireena wamunthireena wayujadilu allatheena kafaroo bialbatili liyudhidoo bihi alhaqqa waittakhathoo ayatee wama onthiroo huzuwan

# 2197

Waman athlamu mimman thukkira biayati rabbihi faa'rada 'anha wanasiya ma qaddamat yadahu inna ja'ana 'ala quloobihim akinnatan an yafqahoohu wafee athanihim waqran wain tad'uhum ila alhuda falan yahtadoo ithan abadan

# 2198

Warabbuka alghafooru thoo arrahmati law yuakhithuhum bima kasaboo la'ajjala lahumu al'athaba bal lahum maw'idun lan yajidoo min doonihi mawilan

# 2199

Watilka alqura ahlaknahum lamma thalamoo waja'ana limahlikihim maw'idan

# 2200

Waith qala moosa lifatahu la abrahu hatta ablugha majma'a albahrayni aw amdiya huquban

# 2201

Falamma balagha majma'a baynihima nasiya hootahuma faittakhatha sabeelahu fee albahri saraban

# 2202

Falamma jawaza qala lifatahu atina ghadaana laqad laqeena min safarina hatha nasaban

# 2203

Qala araayta ith awayna ila assakhrati fainnee naseetu alhoota wama ansaneehu illa ashshaytanu an athkurahu waittakhatha sabeelahu fee albahri 'ajaban

# 2204

Qala thalika ma kunna nabghi fairtadda 'ala atharihima qasasan

# 2205

Fawajada 'abdan min 'ibadina ataynahu rahmatan min 'indina wa'allamnahu min ladunna 'ilman

# 2206

Qala lahu moosa hal attabi'uka 'ala an tu'allimani mimma 'ullimta rushdan

# 2207

Qala innaka lan tastatee'a ma'iya sabran

# 2208

Wakayfa tasbiru 'ala ma lam tuhit bihi khubran

# 2209

Qala satajidunee in shaa Allahu sabiran wala a'see laka amran

# 2210

Qala faini ittaba'tanee fala tasanee 'an shayin hatta ohditha laka minhu thikran

# 2211

Faintalaqa hatta itha rakiba fee assafeenati kharaqaha qala akharaqtaha litughriqa ahlaha laqad jita shayan imran

# 2212

Qala alam aqul innaka lan tastatee'a ma'iya sabran

# 2213

Qala la tuakhithnee bima naseetu wala turhiqnee min amree 'usran

# 2214

Faintalaqa hatta itha laqiya ghulaman faqatalahu qala aqatata nafsan zakiyyatan bighayri nafsin laqad jita shayan nukran

# 2215

Qala alam aqul laka innaka lan tastatee'a ma'iya sabran

# 2216

Qala in saatuka 'an shayin ba'daha fala tusahibnee qad balaghta min ladunnee 'uthran

# 2217

Faintalaqa hatta itha ataya ahla qaryatin istat'ama ahlaha faabaw an yudayyifoohuma fawajada feeha jidaran yureedu an yanqadda faaqamahu qala law shita laittakhathta 'alayhi ajran

# 2218

Qala hatha firaqu baynee wabaynika saonabbioka bitaweeli ma lam tastati' 'alayhi sabran

# 2219

Amma assafeenatu fakanat limasakeena ya'maloona fee albahri faaradtu an a'eebaha wakana waraahum malikun yakhuthu kulla safeenatin ghasban

# 2220

Waamma alghulamu fakana abawahu muminayni fakhasheena an yurhiqahuma tughyanan wakufran

# 2221

Faaradna an yubdilahuma rabbuhuma khayran minhu zakatan waaqraba ruhman

# 2222

Waamma aljidaru fakana lighulamayni yateemayni fee almadeenati wakana tahtahu kanzun lahuma wakana aboohuma salihan faarada rabbuka an yablugha ashuddahuma wayastakhrija kanzahuma rahmatan min rabbika wama fa'atuhu 'an amree thalika taweelu ma lam tasti' 'alayhi sabran

# 2223

Wayasaloonaka 'an thee alqarnayni qul saatloo 'alaykum minhu thikran

# 2224

Inna makkanna lahu fee alardi waataynahu min kulli shayin sababan

# 2225

Faatba'a sababan

# 2226

Hatta itha balagha maghriba ashshamsi wajadaha taghrubu fee 'aynin hamiatin wawajada 'indaha qawman qulna ya tha alqarnayni imma an tu'aththiba waimma an tattakhitha feehim husnan

# 2227

Qala amma man thalama fasawfa nu'aththibuhu thumma yuraddu ila rabbihi fayu'aththibuhu 'athaban nukran

# 2228

Waamma man amana wa'amila salihan falahu jazaan alhusna wasanaqoolu lahu min amrina yusran

# 2229

Thumma atba'a sababan

# 2230

Hatta itha balagha matli'a ashshamsi wajadaha tatlu'u 'ala qawmin lam naj'al lahum min dooniha sitran

# 2231

Kathalika waqad ahatna bima ladayhi khubran

# 2232

Thumma atba'a sababan

# 2233

Hatta itha balagha bayna assaddayni wajada min doonihima qawman la yakadoona yafqahoona qawlan

# 2234

Qaloo ya tha alqarnayni inna yajooja wamajooja mufsidoona fee alardi fahal naj'alu laka kharjan 'ala an taj'ala baynana wabaynahum saddan

# 2235

Qala ma makkannee feehi rabbee khayrun faa'eenoonee biquwwatin aj'al baynakum wabaynahum radman

# 2236

Atoonee zubara alhadeedi hatta itha sawa bayna asadafayni qala onfukhoo hatta itha ja'alahu naran qala atoonee ofrigh 'alayhi qitran

# 2237

Fama ista'oo an yathharoohu wama istata'oo lahu naqban

# 2238

Qala hatha rahmatun min rabbee faitha jaa wa'du rabbee ja'alahu dakkaa wakana wa'du rabbee haqqan

# 2239

Watarakna ba'dahum yawmaithin yamooju fee ba'din wanufikha fee assoori fajama'nahum jam'an

# 2240

Wa'aradna jahannama yawmaithin lilkafireena 'ardan

# 2241

Allatheena kanat a'yunuhum fee ghitain 'an thikree wakanoo la yastatee'oona sam'an

# 2242

Afahasiba allatheena kafaroo an yattakhithoo 'ibadee min doonee awliyaa inna a'tadna jahannama lilkafireena nuzulan

# 2243

Qul hal nunabbiokum bialakhsareena a'malan

# 2244

Allatheena dalla sa'yuhum fee alhayati addunya wahum yahsaboona annahum yuhsinoona sun'an

# 2245

Olaika allatheena kafaroo biayati rabbihim waliqaihi fahabitat a'maluhum fala nuqeemu lahum yawma alqiyamati waznan

# 2246

Thalika jazaohum jahannamu bima kafaroo waittakhathoo ayatee warusulee huzuwan

# 2247

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati kanat lahum jannatu alfirdawsi nuzulan

# 2248

Khalideena feeha la yabghoona 'anha hiwalan

# 2249

Qul law kana albahru midadan likalimati rabbee lanafida albahru qabla an tanfada kalimatu rabbee walaw jina bimithlihi madadan

Qala ihbita minha jamee'an ba'dukum liba'din 'aduwwun faimma yatiyannakum minnee hudan famani ittaba'a hudaya fala yadillu wala yashqa

# 2472

Waman a'rada 'an thikree fainna lahu ma'eeshatan dankan wanahshuruhu yawma alqiyamati a'man

# 2473

Qala rabbi lima hashartanee a'ma waqad kuntu baseeran

# 2474

Qala kathalika atatka ayatuna fanaseetaha wakathalika alyawma tunsa

# 2475

Wakathalika najzee man asrafa walam yumin biayati rabbihi wala'athabu alakhirati ashaddu waabqa

# 2476

Afalam yahdi lahum kam ahlakna qablahum mina alqurooni yamshoona fee masakinihim inna fee thalika laayatin liolee annuha

# 2477

Walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika lakana lizaman waajalun musamman

# 2478

Faisbir 'ala ma yaqooloona wasabbih bihamdi rabbika qabla tuloo'i ashshamsi waqabla ghuroobiha wamin anai allayli fasabbih waatrafa annahari la'allaka tarda

# 2479

Wala tamuddanna 'aynayka ila ma matta'na bihi azwajan minhum zahrata alhayati addunya linaftinahum feehi warizqu rabbika khayrun waabqa

# 2480

Wamur ahlaka biassalati waistabir 'alayha la nasaluka rizqan nahnu narzuquka waal'aqibatu lilttaqwa

# 2481

Waqaloo lawla yateena biayatin min rabbihi awalam tatihim bayyinatu ma fee assuhufi aloola

# 2482

Walaw anna ahlaknahum bi'athabin min qablihi laqaloo rabbana lawla arsata ilayna rasoolan fanattabi'a ayatika min qabli an nathilla wanakhza

# 2483

Qul kullun mutarabbisun fatarabbasoo fasata'lamoona man ashabu assirati assawiyyi wamani ihtada

# 2484

Iqtaraba lilnnasi hisabuhum wahum fee ghaflatin mu'ridoona

# 2485

Ma yateehim min thikrin min rabbihim muhdathin illa istama'oohu wahum yal'aboona

# 2486

Lahiyatan quloobuhum waasarroo annajwa allatheena thalamoo hal hatha illa basharun mithlukum afatatoona assihra waantum tubsiroona

# 2487

Qala rabbee ya'lamu alqawla fee assamai waalardi wahuwa assamee'u al'aleemu

# 2488

Bal qaloo adghathu ahlamin bali iftarahu bal huwa sha'irun falyatina biayatin kama orsila alawwaloona

# 2489

Ma amanat qablahum min qaryatin ahlaknaha afahum yuminoona

# 2490

Wama arsana qablaka illa rijalan noohee ilayhim faisaloo ahla aththikri in kuntum la ta'lamoona

# 2491

Wama ja'anahum jasadan la yakuloona atta'ama wama kanoo khalideena

# 2492

Thumma sadaqnahumu alwa'da faanjaynahum waman nashao waahlakna almusrifeena

# 2493

Laqad anzana ilaykum kitaban feehi thikrukum afala ta'qiloona

# 2494

Wakam qasamna min qaryatin kanat thalimatan waanshana ba'daha qawman akhareena

# 2495

Falamma ahassoo basana itha hum minha yarkudoona

# 2496

La tarkudoo wairji'oo ila ma otriftum feehi wamasakinikum la'allakum tusaloona

# 2497

Qaloo ya waylana inna kunna thalimeena

# 2498

Fama zalat tilka da'wahum hatta ja'anahum haseedan khamideena

# 2499

Wama khalaqna assamaa waalarda wama baynahuma la'ibeena

# 2500

Law aradna an nattakhitha lahwan laittakhathnahu min ladunna in kunna fa'ileena

# 2501

Bal naqthifu bialhaqqi 'ala albatili fayadmaghuhu faitha huwa zahiqun walakumu alwaylu mimma tasifoona

# 2502

Walahu man fee assamawati waalardi waman 'indahu la yastakbiroona 'an 'ibadatihi wala yastahsiroona

# 2503

Yusabbihoona allayla waannahara la yafturoona

# 2504

Ami ittakhathoo alihatan mina alardi hum yunshiroona

# 2505

Law kana feehima alihatun illa Allahu lafasadata fasubhana Allahi rabbi al'arshi 'amma yasifoona

# 2506

La yusalu 'amma yaf'alu wahum yusaloona

# 2507

Ami ittakhathoo min doonihi alihatan qul hatoo burhanakum hatha thikru man ma'iya wathikru man qablee bal aktharuhum la ya'lamoona alhaqqa fahum mu'ridoona

# 2508

Wama arsana min qablika min rasoolin illa noohee ilayhi annahu la ilaha illa ana fao'budooni

# 2509

Waqaloo ittakhatha arrahmanu waladan subhanahu bal 'ibadun mukramoona

# 2510

La yasbiqoonahu bialqawli wahum biamrihi ya'maloona

# 2511

Ya'lamu ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum wala yashfa'oona illa limani irtada wahum min khashyatihi mushfiqoona

# 2512

Waman yaqul minhum innee ilahun min doonihi fathalika najzeehi jahannama kathalika najzee aththalimeena

# 2513

Awalam yara allatheena kafaroo anna assamawati waalarda kanata ratqan fafataqnahuma waja'ana mina almai kulla shayin hayyin afala yuminoona

# 2514

Waja'ana fee alardi rawasiya an tameeda bihim waja'ana feeha fijajan subulan la'allahum yahtadoona

# 2515

Waja'ana assamaa saqfan mahfoothan wahum 'an ayatiha mu'ridoona

# 2516

Wahuwa allathee khalaqa allayla waannahara waashshamsa waalqamara kullun fee falakin yasbahoona

# 2517

Wama ja'ana libasharin min qablika alkhulda afain mitta fahumu alkhalidoona

# 2518

Kullu nafsin thaiqatu almawti wanablookum biashsharri waalkhayri fitnatan wailayna turja'oona

# 2519

Waitha raaka allatheena kafaroo in yattakhithoonaka illa huzuwan ahatha allathee yathkuru alihatakum wahum bithikri arrahmani hum kafiroona

# 2520

Khuliqa alinsanu min 'ajalin saoreekum ayatee fala tasta'jiloona

# 2521

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwa'du in kuntum sadiqeena

# 2522

Law ya'lamu allatheena kafaroo heena la yakuffoona 'an wujoohihimu annara wala 'an thuhoorihim wala hum yunsaroona

# 2523

Bal tateehim baghtatan fatabhatuhum fala yastatee'oona raddaha wala hum yuntharoona

# 2524

Walaqadi istuhzia birusulin min qablika fahaqa biallatheena sakhiroo minhum ma kanoo bihi yastahzioona

# 2525

Qul man yaklaokum biallayli waannahari mina arrahmani bal hum 'an thikri rabbihim mu'ridoona

# 2526

Am lahum alihatun tamna'uhum min doonina la yastatee'oona nasra anfusihim wala hum minna yushaboona

# 2527

Bal matta'na haolai waabaahum hatta tala 'alayhimu al'umuru afala yarawna anna natee alarda nanqusuha min atrafiha afahumu alghaliboona

# 2528

Qul innama onthirukum bialwahyi wala yasma'u assummu addu'aa itha ma yuntharoona

# 2529

Walain massathum nafhatun min 'athabi rabbika layaqoolunna ya waylana inna kunna thalimeena

# 2530

Wanada'u almawazeena alqista liyawmi alqiyamati fala tuthlamu nafsun shayan wain kana mithqala habbatin min khardalin atayna biha wakafa bina hasibeena

# 2531

Walaqad atayna moosa waharoona alfurqana wadiyaan wathikran lilmuttaqeena

# 2532

Allatheena yakhshawna rabbahum bialghaybi wahum mina assa'ati mushfiqoona

# 2533

Wahatha thikrun mubarakun anzanahu afaantum lahu munkiroona

# 2534

Walaqad atayna ibraheema rushdahu min qablu wakunna bihi 'alimeena

# 2535

Ith qala liabeehi waqawmihi ma hathihi attamatheelu allatee antum laha 'akifoona

# 2536

Qaloo wajadna abaana laha 'abideena

# 2537

Qala laqad kuntum antum waabaokum fee dalalin mubeenin

# 2538

Qaloo ajitana bialhaqqi am anta mina alla'ibeena

# 2539

Qala bal rabbukum rabbu assamawati waalardi allathee fatarahunna waana 'ala thalikum mina ashshahideena

# 2540

WataAllahi laakeedanna asnamakum ba'da an tuwalloo mudbireena

# 2541

Faja'alahum juthathan illa kabeeran lahum la'allahum ilayhi yarji'oona

# 2542

Qaloo man fa'ala hatha bialihatina innahu lamina aththalimeena

# 2543

Qaloo sami'na fatan yathkuruhum yuqalu lahu ibraheemu

# 2544

Qaloo fatoo bihi 'ala a'yuni annasi la'allahum yashhadoona

# 2545

Qaloo aanta fa'ata hatha bialihatina ya ibraheemu

# 2546

Qala bal fa'alahu kabeeruhum hatha faisaloohum in kanoo yantiqoona

# 2547

Faraja'oo ila anfusihim faqaloo innakum antumu aththalimoona

# 2548

Thumma nukisoo 'ala ruoosihim laqad 'alimta ma haolai yantiqoona

# 2549

Qala afata'budoona min dooni Allahi ma la yanfa'ukum shayan wala yadurrukum

# 2550

Offin lakum walima ta'budoona min dooni Allahi afala ta'qiloona

# 2551

Qaloo harriqoohu waonsuroo alihatakum in kuntum fa'ileena

# 2552

Qulna ya naru koonee bardan wasalaman 'ala ibraheema

# 2553

Waaradoo bihi kaydan faja'anahumu alakhsareena

# 2554

Wanajjaynahu walootan ila alardi allatee barakna feeha lil'alameena

# 2555

Wawahabna lahu ishaqa waya'qooba nafilatan wakullan ja'ana saliheena

# 2556

Waja'anahum aimmatan yahdoona biamrina waawhayna ilayhim fi'la alkhayrati waiqama assalati waeetaa azzakati wakanoo lana 'abideena

# 2557

Walootan ataynahu hukman wa'ilman wanajjaynahu mina alqaryati allatee kanat ta'malu alkhabaitha innahum kanoo qawma sawin fasiqeena

# 2558

Waadkhanahu fee rahmatina innahu mina assaliheena

# 2559

Wanoohan ith nada min qablu faistajabna lahu fanajjaynahu waahlahu mina alkarbi al'atheemi

# 2560

Wanasarnahu mina alqawmi allatheena kaththaboo biayatina innahum kanoo qawma sawin faaghraqnahum ajma'eena

# 2561

Wadawooda wasulaymana ith yahkumani fee alharthi ith nafashat feehi ghanamu alqawmi wakunna lihukmihim shahideena

# 2562

Fafahhamnaha sulaymana wakullan atayna hukman wa'ilman wasakhkharna ma'a dawooda aljibala yusabbihna waattayra wakunna fa'ileena

# 2563

Wa'allamnahu san'ata laboosin lakum lituhsinakum min basikum fahal antum shakiroona

# 2564

Walisulaymana arreeha 'asifatan tajree biamrihi ila alardi allatee barakna feeha wakunna bikulli shayin 'alimeena

# 2565

Wamina ashshayateeni man yaghoosoona lahu waya'maloona 'amalan doona thalika wakunna lahum hafitheena

# 2566

Waayyooba ith nada rabbahu annee massaniya addurru waanta arhamu arrahimeena

# 2567

Faistajabna lahu fakashafna ma bihi min durrin waataynahu ahlahu wamithlahum ma'ahum rahmatan min 'indina wathikra lil'abideena

# 2568

Waisma'eela waidreesa watha alkifli kullun mina assabireena

# 2569

Waadkhanahum fee rahmatina innahum mina assaliheena

# 2570

Watha annooni ith thahaba mughadiban fathanna an lan naqdira 'alayhi fanada fee aththulumati an la ilaha illa anta subhanaka innee kuntu mina aththalimeena

# 2571

Faistajabna lahu wanajjaynahu mina alghammi wakathalika nunjee almumineena

# 2572

Wazakariyya ith nada rabbahu rabbi la tatharnee fardan waanta khayru alwaritheena

# 2573

Faistajabna lahu wawahabna lahu yahya waaslahna lahu zawjahu innahum kanoo yusari'oona fee alkhayrati wayad'oonana raghaban warahaban wakanoo lana khashi'eena

# 2574

Waallatee ahsanat farjaha fanafakhna feeha min roohina waja'anaha waibnaha ayatan lil'alameena

# 2575

Inna hathihi ommatukum ommatan wahidatan waana rabbukum fao'budooni

# 2576

Wataqatta'oo amrahum baynahum kullun ilayna raji'oona

# 2577

Faman ya'mal mina assalihati wahuwa muminun fala kufrana lisa'yihi wainna lahu katiboona

# 2578

Waharamun 'ala qaryatin ahlaknaha annahum la yarji'oona

# 2579

Hatta itha futihat yajooju wamajooju wahum min kulli hadabin yansiloona

# 2580

Waiqtaraba alwa'du alhaqqu faitha hiya shakhisatun absaru allatheena kafaroo ya waylana qad kunna fee ghaflatin min hatha bal kunna thalimeena

# 2581

Innakum wama ta'budoona min dooni Allahi hasabu jahannama antum laha waridoona

# 2582

Law kana haolai alihatan ma waradooha wakullun feeha khalidoona

# 2583

Lahum feeha zafeerun wahum feeha la yasma'oona

# 2584

Inna allatheena sabaqat lahum minna alhusna olaika 'anha mub'adoona

# 2585

La yasma'oona haseesaha wahum fee ma ishtahat anfusuhum khalidoona

# 2586

La yahzunuhumu alfaza'u alakbaru watatalaqqahumu almalaikatu hatha yawmukumu allathee kuntum too'adoona

# 2587

Yawma natwee assamaa katayyi assijlli lilkutubi kama badana awwala khalqin nu'eeduhu wa'dan 'alayna inna kunna fa'ileena

# 2588

Walaqad katabna fee azzaboori min ba'di aththikri anna alarda yarithuha 'ibadiya assalihoona

# 2589

Inna fee hatha labalaghan liqawmin 'abideena

# 2590

Wama arsanaka illa rahmatan lil'alameena

# 2591

Qul innama yooha ilayya annama ilahukum ilahun wahidun fahal antum muslimoona

# 2592

Fain tawallaw faqul athantukum 'ala sawain wain adree aqareebun am ba'eedun ma too'adoona

# 2593

Innahu ya'lamu aljahra mina alqawli waya'lamu ma taktumoona

# 2594

Wain adree la'allahu fitnatun lakum wamata'un ila heenin

# 2595

Qala rabbi ohkum bialhaqqi warabbuna arrahmanu almusta'anu 'ala ma tasifoona

# 2596

Ya ayyuha annasu ittaqoo rabbakum inna zazalata assa'ati shayon 'atheemun

# 2597

Yawma tarawnaha tathhalu kullu murdi'atin 'amma arda'at watada'u kullu thati hamlin hamlaha watara annasa sukara wama hum bisukara walakinna 'athaba Allahi shadeedun

# 2598

Wamina annasi man yujadilu fee Allahi bighayri 'ilmin wayattabi'u kulla shaytanin mareedin

# 2599

Kutiba 'alayhi annahu man tawallahu faannahu yudilluhu wayahdeehi ila 'athabi assa'eeri

# 2600

Ya ayyuha annasu in kuntum fee raybin mina alba'thi fainna khalaqnakum min turabin thumma min nutfatin thumma min 'alaqatin thumma min mudghatin mukhallaqatin waghayri mukhallaqatin linubayyina lakum wanuqirru fee alarhami ma nashao ila ajalin musamman thumma nukhrijukum tiflan thumma litablughoo ashuddakum waminkum man yutawaffa waminkum man yuraddu ila arthali al'umuri likayla ya'lama min ba'di 'ilmin shayan watara alarda hamidatan faitha anzana 'alayha almaa ihtazzat warabat waanbatat min kulli zawjin baheejin

# 2601

Thalika bianna Allaha huwa alhaqqu waannahu yuhyee almawta waannahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 2602

Waanna assa'ata atiyatun la rayba feeha waanna Allaha yab'athu man fee alquboori

# 2603

Wamina annasi man yujadilu fee Allahi bighayri 'ilmin wala hudan wala kitabin muneerin

# 2604

Thaniya 'itfihi liyudilla 'an sabeeli Allahi lahu fee addunya khizyun wanutheequhu yawma alqiyamati 'athaba alhareeqi

# 2605

Thalika bima qaddamat yadaka waanna Allaha laysa bithallamin lil'abeedi

# 2606

Wamina annasi man ya'budu Allaha 'ala harfin fain asabahu khayrun itmaanna bihi wain asabathu fitnatun inqalaba 'ala wajhihi khasira addunya waalakhirata thalika huwa alkhusranu almubeenu

# 2607

Yad'oo min dooni Allahi ma la yadurruhu wama la yanfa'uhu thalika huwa addalalu alba'eedu

# 2608

Yad'oo laman darruhu aqrabu min naf'ihi labisa almawla walabisa al'asheeru

# 2609

Inna Allaha yudkhilu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu inna Allaha yaf'alu ma yureedu

# 2610

Man kana yathunnu an lan yansurahu Allahu fee addunya waalakhirati falyamdud bisababin ila assamai thumma liyaqta' falyanthur hal yuthhibanna kayduhu ma yagheethu

# 2611

Wakathalika anzanahu ayatin bayyinatin waanna Allaha yahdee man yureedu

# 2612

Inna allatheena amanoo waallatheena hadoo waassabieena waannasara waalmajoosa waallatheena ashrakoo inna Allaha yafsilu baynahum yawma alqiyamati inna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin shaheedun

# 2613

Alam tara anna Allaha yasjudu lahu man fee assamawati waman fee alardi waashshamsu waalqamaru waannujoomu waaljibalu waashshajaru waaddawabbu wakatheerun mina annasi wakatheerun haqqa 'alayhi al'athabu waman yuhini Allahu fama lahu min mukrimin inna Allaha yaf'alu ma yashao

# 2614

Hathani khasmani ikhtasamoo fee rabbihim faallatheena kafaroo qutti'at lahum thiyabun min narin yusabbu min fawqi ruoosihimu alhameemu

# 2615

Yusharu bihi ma fee butoonihim waaljuloodu

# 2616

Walahum maqami'u min hadeedin

# 2617

Kullama aradoo an yakhrujoo minha min ghammin o'eedoo feeha wathooqoo 'athaba alhareeqi

# 2618

Inna Allaha yudkhilu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu yuhallawna feeha min asawira min thahabin waluluan walibasuhum feeha hareerun

# 2619

Wahudoo ila attayyibi mina alqawli wahudoo ila sirati alhameedi

# 2620

Inna allatheena kafaroo wayasuddoona 'an sabeeli Allahi waalmasjidi alharami allathee ja'anahu lilnnasi sawaan al'akifu feehi waalbadi waman yurid feehi biilhadin bithulmin nuthiqhu min 'athabin aleemin

# 2621

Waith bawwana liibraheema makana albayti an la tushrik bee shayan watahhir baytiya lilttaifeena waalqaimeena waarrukka'i assujoodi

# 2622

Waaththin fee annasi bialhajji yatooka rijalan wa'ala kulli damirin yateena min kulli fajjin 'ameeqin

# 2623

Liyashhadoo manafi'a lahum wayathkuroo isma Allahi fee ayyamin ma'loomatin 'ala ma razaqahum min baheemati alan'ami fakuloo minha waat'imoo albaisa alfaqeera

# 2624

Thumma lyaqdoo tafathahum walyoofoo nuthoorahum walyattawwafoo bialbayti al'ateeqi

# 2625

Thalika waman yu'aththim hurumati Allahi fahuwa khayrun lahu 'inda rabbihi waohillat lakumu alan'amu illa ma yutla 'alaykum faijtaniboo arrijsa mina alawthani waijtaniboo qawla azzoori

# 2626

Hunafaa lillahi ghayra mushrikeena bihi waman yushrik biAllahi fakaannama kharra mina assamai fatakhtafuhu attayru aw tahwee bihi arreehu fee makanin saheeqin

# 2627

Thalika waman yu'aththim sha'aira Allahi fainnaha min taqwa alquloobi

# 2628

Lakum feeha manafi'u ila ajalin musamman thumma mahilluha ila albayti al'ateeqi

# 2629

Walikulli ommatin ja'ana mansakan liyathkuroo isma Allahi 'ala ma razaqahum min baheemati alan'ami failahukum ilahun wahidun falahu aslimoo wabashshiri almukhbiteena

# 2630

Allatheena itha thukira Allahu wajilat quloobuhum waassabireena 'ala ma asabahum waalmuqeemee assalati wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoona

# 2631

Waalbudna ja'anaha lakum min sha'airi Allahi lakum feeha khayrun faothkuroo isma Allahi 'alayha sawaffa faitha wajabat junoobuha fakuloo minha waat'imoo alqani'a waalmu'tarra kathalika sakhkharnaha lakum la'allakum tashkuroona

# 2632

Lan yanala Allaha luhoomuha wala dimaoha walakin yanaluhu attaqwa minkum kathalika sakhkharaha lakum litukabbiroo Allaha 'ala ma hadakum wabashshiri almuhsineena

# 2633

Inna Allaha yudafi'u 'ani allatheena amanoo inna Allaha la yuhibbu kulla khawwanin kafoorin

# 2634

Othina lillatheena yuqataloona biannahum thulimoo wainna Allaha 'ala nasrihim laqadeerun

# 2635

Allatheena okhrijoo min diyarihim bighayri haqqin illa an yaqooloo rabbuna Allahu walawla daf'u Allahi annasa ba'dahum biba'din lahuddimat sawami'u wabiya'un wasalawatun wamasajidu yuthkaru feeha ismu Allahi katheeran walayansuranna Allahu man yansuruhu inna Allaha laqawiyyun 'azeezun

# 2636

Allatheena in makkannahum fee alardi aqamoo assalata waatawoo azzakata waamaroo bialma'roofi wanahaw 'ani almunkari walillahi 'aqibatu alomoori

# 2637

Wain yukaththibooka faqad kaththabat qablahum qawmu noohin wa'adun wathamoodu

# 2638

Waqawmu ibraheema waqawmu lootin

# 2639

Waashabu madyana wakuththiba moosa faamlaytu lilkafireena thumma akhathtuhum fakayfa kana nakeeri

# 2640

Fakaayyin min qaryatin ahlaknaha wahiya thalimatun fahiya khawiyatun 'ala 'urooshiha wabirin mu'attalatin waqasrin masheedin

# 2641

Afalam yaseeroo fee alardi fatakoona lahum quloobun ya'qiloona biha aw athanun yasma'oona biha fainnaha la ta'ma alabsaru walakin ta'ma alquloobu allatee fee assudoori

# 2642

Wayasta'jiloonaka bial'athabi walan yukhlifa Allahu wa'dahu wainna yawman 'inda rabbika kaalfi sanatin mimma ta'uddoona

# 2643

Wakaayyin min qaryatin amlaytu laha wahiya thalimatun thumma akhathtuha wailayya almaseeru

# 2644

Qul ya ayyuha annasu innama ana lakum natheerun mubeenun

# 2645

Faallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareemun

# 2646

Waallatheena sa'aw fee ayatina mu'ajizeena olaika ashabu aljaheemi

# 2647

Wama arsana min qablika min rasoolin wala nabiyyin illa itha tamanna alqa ashshaytanu fee omniyyatihi fayansakhu Allahu ma yulqee ashshaytanu thumma yuhkimu Allahu ayatihi waAllahu 'aleemun hakeemun

# 2648

Liyaj'ala ma yulqee ashshaytanu fitnatan lillatheena fee quloobihim maradun waalqasiyati quloobuhum wainna aththalimeena lafee shiqaqin ba'eedin

# 2649

Waliya'lama allatheena ootoo al'ilma annahu alhaqqu min rabbika fayuminoo bihi fatukhbita lahu quloobuhum wainna Allaha lahadi allatheena amanoo ila siratin mustaqeemin

# 2650

Wala yazalu allatheena kafaroo fee miryatin minhu hatta tatiyahumu assa'atu baghtatan aw yatiyahum 'athabu yawmin 'aqeemin

# 2651

Almulku yawmaithin lillahi yahkumu baynahum faallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati fee jannati anna'eemi

# 2652

Waallatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina faolaika lahum 'athabun muheenun

# 2653

Waallatheena hajaroo fee sabeeli Allahi thumma qutiloo aw matoo layarzuqannahumu Allahu rizqan hasanan wainna Allaha lahuwa khayru arraziqeena

# 2654

Layudkhilannahum mudkhalan yardawnahu wainna Allaha la'aleemun haleemun

# 2655

Thalika waman 'aqaba bimithli ma 'ooqiba bihi thumma bughiya 'alayhi layansurannahu Allahu inna Allaha la'afuwwun ghafoorun

# 2656

Thalika bianna Allaha yooliju allayla fee annahari wayooliju annahara fee allayli waanna Allaha samee'un baseerun

# 2657

Thalika bianna Allaha huwa alhaqqu waanna ma yad'oona min doonihi huwa albatilu waanna Allaha huwa al'aliyyu alkabeeru

# 2658

Alam tara anna Allaha anzala mina assamai maan fatusbihu alardu mukhdarratan inna Allaha lateefun khabeerun

# 2659

Lahu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi wainna Allaha lahuwa alghaniyyu alhameedu

# 2660

Alam tara anna Allaha sakhkhara lakum ma fee alardi waalfulka tajree fee albahri biamrihi wayumsiku assamaa an taqa'a 'ala alardi illa biithnihi inna Allaha biannasi laraoofun raheemun

# 2661

Wahuwa allathee ahyakum thumma yumeetukum thumma yuhyeekum inna alinsana lakafoorun

# 2662

Likulli ommatin ja'ana mansakan hum nasikoohu fala yunazi'unnaka fee alamri waod'u ila rabbika innaka la'ala hudan mustaqeemin

# 2663

Wain jadalooka faquli Allahu a'lamu bima ta'maloona

# 2664

Allahu yahkumu baynakum yawma alqiyamati feema kuntum feehi takhtalifoona

# 2665

Alam ta'lam anna Allaha ya'lamu ma fee assamai waalardi inna thalika fee kitabin inna thalika 'ala Allahi yaseerun

# 2666

Waya'budoona min dooni Allahi ma lam yunazzil bihi sultanan wama laysa lahum bihi 'ilmun wama lilththalimeena min naseerin

# 2667

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna bayyinatin ta'rifu fee wujoohi allatheena kafaroo almunkara yakadoona yastoona biallatheena yatloona 'alayhim ayatina qul afaonabbiokum bisharrin min thalikum annaru wa'adaha Allahu allatheena kafaroo wabisa almaseeru

# 2668

Ya ayyuha annasu duriba mathalun faistami'oo lahu inna allatheena tad'oona min dooni Allahi lan yakhluqoo thubaban walawi ijtama'oo lahu wain yaslubuhumu aththubabu shayan la yastanqithoohu minhu da'ufa attalibu waalmatloobu

# 2669

Ma qadaroo Allaha haqqa qadrihi inna Allaha laqawiyyun 'azeezun

# 2670

Allahu yastafee mina almalaikati rusulan wamina annasi inna Allaha samee'un baseerun

# 2671

Ya'lamu ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum waila Allahi turja'u alomooru

# 2672

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo irka'oo waosjudoo wao'budoo rabbakum waif'aloo alkhayra la'allakum tuflihoona

# 2673

Wajahidoo fee Allahi haqqa jihadihi huwa ijtabakum wama ja'ala 'alaykum fee addeeni min harajin millata abeekum ibraheema huwa sammakumu almuslimeena min qablu wafee hatha liyakoona arrasoolu shaheedan 'alaykum watakoonoo shuhadaa 'ala annasi faaqeemoo assalata waatoo azzakata wai'tasimoo biAllahi huwa mawlakum fani'ma almawla wani'ma annaseeru

# 2674

Qad aflaha almuminoona

# 2675

# 2677

# 2678

# 2680

# 2681

# 2682

# 2684

# 2685

# 2686

# 2687

# 2688

# 2689

# 2690

# 2691

Waanzana mina assamai maan biqadarin faaskannahu fee alardi wainna 'ala thahabin bihi laqadiroona

# 2692

Faanshana lakum bihi jannatin min nakheelin waa'nabin lakum feeha fawakihu katheeratun waminha takuloona

# 2693

Washajaratan takhruju min toori saynaa tanbutu biadduhni wasibghin lilakileena

# 2694

Wainna lakum fee alan'ami la'ibratan nusqeekum mimma fee butooniha walakum feeha manafi'u katheeratun waminha takuloona

# 2695

# 2696

Walaqad arsana noohan ila qawmihi faqala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha ma lakum min ilahin ghayruhu afala tattaqoona

# 2697

Faqala almalao allatheena kafaroo min qawmihi ma hatha illa basharun mithlukum yureedu an yatafaddala 'alaykum walaw shaa Allahu laanzala malaikatan ma sami'na bihatha fee abaina alawwaleena

# 2698

In huwa illa rajulun bihi jinnatun fatarabbasoo bihi hatta heenin

# 2699

Qala rabbi onsurnee bima kaththabooni

# 2700

Faawhayna ilayhi ani isna'i alfulka bia'yunina wawahyina faitha jaa amruna wafara attannooru faosluk feeha min kullin zawjayni ithnayni waahlaka illa man sabaqa 'alayhi alqawlu minhum wala tukhatibnee fee allatheena thalamoo innahum mughraqoona

# 2701

Faitha istawayta anta waman ma'aka 'ala alfulki faquli alhamdu lillahi allathee najjana mina alqawmi aththalimeena

# 2702

Waqul rabbi anzilnee munzalan mubarakan waanta khayru almunzileena

# 2703

Inna fee thalika laayatin wain kunna lamubtaleena

# 2704

# 2705

# 2706

Waqala almalao min qawmihi allatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biliqai alakhirati waatrafnahum fee alhayati addunya ma hatha illa basharun mithlukum yakulu mimma takuloona minhu wayashrabu mimma tashraboona

# 2707

Walain ata'tum basharan mithlakum innakum ithan lakhasiroona

# 2708

# 2709

# 2710

# 2711

# 2712

Qala rabbi onsurnee bima kaththabooni

# 2713

# 2714

# 2715

# 2716

Ma tasbiqu min ommatin ajalaha wama yastakhiroona

# 2717

Thumma arsana rusulana tatra kulla ma jaa ommatan rasooluha kaththaboohu faatba'na ba'dahum ba'dan waja'anahum ahadeetha fabu'dan liqawmin la yuminoona

# 2718

# 2719

# 2723

# 2725

# 2726

# 2733

# 2734

# 2735

# 2736

# 2737

# 2738

# 2740

# 2741

# 2742

# 2743

# 2744

# 2746

# 2750

# 2751

# 2752

# 2763

# 2766

# 2774

# 2775

# 2781

# 2793

azzanee la yankihu illa zaniyatan aw mushrikatan waazzaniyatu la yankihuha illa zanin aw mushrikun wahurrima thalika 'ala almumineena

# 2795

Waallatheena yarmoona almuhsanati thumma lam yatoo biarba'ati shuhadaa faijlidoohum thamaneena jadatan wala taqbaloo lahum shahadatan abadan waolaika humu alfasiqoona

# 2796

# 2797

# 2798

Waalkhamisatu anna la'nata Allahi 'alayhi in kana mina alkathibeena

# 2799

# 2800

Waalkhamisata anna ghadaba Allahi 'alayha in kana mina assadiqeena

# 2801

Walawla fadlu Allahi 'alaykum warahmatuhu waanna Allaha tawwabun hakeemun

# 2802

Inna allatheena jaoo bialifki 'usbatun minkum la tahsaboohu sharran lakum bal huwa khayrun lakum likulli imriin minhum ma iktasaba mina alithmi waallathee tawalla kibrahu minhum lahu 'athabun 'atheemun

# 2803

Lawla ith sami'tumoohu thanna almuminoona waalmuminatu bianfusihim khayran waqaloo hatha ifkun mubeenun

# 2804

# 2805

Walawla fadlu Allahi 'alaykum warahmatuhu fee addunya waalakhirati lamassakum fee ma afadtum feehi 'athabun 'atheemun

# 2806

# 2807

Walawla ith sami'tumoohu qultum ma yakoonu lana an natakallama bihatha subhanaka hatha buhtanun 'atheemun

# 2808

# 2809

Wayubayyinu Allahu lakumu alayati waAllahu 'aleemun hakeemun

# 2810

Inna allatheena yuhibboona an tashee'a alfahishatu fee allatheena amanoo lahum 'athabun aleemun fee addunya waalakhirati waAllahu ya'lamu waantum la ta'lamoona

# 2811

Walawla fadlu Allahi 'alaykum warahmatuhu waanna Allaha raoofun raheemun

# 2812

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattabi'oo khutuwati ashshaytani waman yattabi' khutuwati ashshaytani fainnahu yamuru bialfahshai waalmunkari walawla fadlu Allahi 'alaykum warahmatuhu ma zaka minkum min ahadin abadan walakinna Allaha yuzakkee man yashao waAllahu samee'un 'aleemun

# 2813

Wala yatali oloo alfadli minkum waassa'ati an yutoo olee alqurba waalmasakeena waalmuhajireena fee sabeeli Allahi walya'foo walyasfahoo ala tuhibboona an yaghfira Allahu lakum waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun

# 2814

Inna allatheena yarmoona almuhsanati alghafilati almuminati lu'inoo fee addunya waalakhirati walahum 'athabun 'atheemun

# 2815

# 2816

# 2817

Alkhabeethatu lilkhabeetheena waalkhabeethoona lilkhabeethati waattayyibatu lilttayyibeena waattayyiboona lilttayyibati olaika mubarraoona mimma yaqooloona lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareemun

# 2818

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tadkhuloo buyootan ghayra buyootikum hatta tastanisoo watusallimoo 'ala ahliha thalikum khayrun lakum la'allakum tathakkaroona

# 2819

Fain lam tajidoo feeha ahadan fala tadkhulooha hatta yuthana lakum wain qeela lakumu irji'oo fairji'oo huwa azka lakum waAllahu bima ta'maloona 'aleemun

# 2820

Laysa 'alaykum junahun an tadkhuloo buyootan ghayra maskoonatin feeha mata'un lakum waAllahu ya'lamu ma tubdoona wama taktumoona

# 2821

Qul lilmumineena yaghuddoo min absarihum wayahfathoo furoojahum thalika azka lahum inna Allaha khabeerun bima yasna'oona

# 2822

Waqul lilmuminati yaghdudna min absarihinna wayahfathna furoojahunna wala yubdeena zeenatahunna illa ma thahara minha walyadribna bikhumurihinna 'ala juyoobihinna wala yubdeena zeenatahunna illa libu'oolatihinna aw abaihinna aw abai bu'oolatihinna aw abnaihinna aw abnai bu'oolatihinna aw ikhwanihinna aw banee ikhwanihinna aw banee akhawatihinna aw nisaihinna aw ma malakat aymanuhunna awi attabi'eena ghayri olee alirbati mina arrijali awi attifli allatheena lam yathharoo 'ala 'awrati annisai wala yadribna biarjulihinna liyu'lama ma yukhfeena min zeenatihinna watooboo ila Allahi jamee'an ayyuha almuminoona la'allakum tuflihoona

# 2823

Waankihoo alayama minkum waassaliheena min 'ibadikum waimaikum in yakoonoo fuqaraa yughnihimu Allahu min fadlihi waAllahu wasi'un 'aleemun

# 2824

Walyasta'fifi allatheena la yajidoona nikahan hatta yughniyahumu Allahu min fadlihi waallatheena yabtaghoona alkitaba mimma malakat aymanukum fakatiboohum in 'alimtum feehim khayran waatoohum min mali Allahi allathee atakum wala tukrihoo fatayatikum 'ala albighai in aradna tahassunan litabtaghoo 'arada alhayati addunya waman yukrihhunna fainna Allaha min ba'di ikrahihinna ghafoorun raheemun

# 2825

Walaqad anzana ilaykum ayatin mubayyinatin wamathalan mina allatheena khalaw min qablikum wamaw'ithatan lilmuttaqeena

# 2826

Allahu nooru assamawati waalardi mathalu noorihi kamishkatin feeha misbahun almisbahu fee zujajatin azzujajatu kaannaha kawkabun durriyyun yooqadu min shajaratin mubarakatin zaytoonatin la sharqiyyatin wala gharbiyyatin yakadu zaytuha yudeeo walaw lam tamsashu narun noorun 'ala noorin yahdee Allahu linoorihi man yashao wayadribu Allahu alamthala lilnnasi waAllahu bikulli shayin 'aleemun

# 2827

Fee buyootin athina Allahu an turfa'a wayuthkara feeha ismuhu yusabbihu lahu feeha bialghuduwwi waalasali

# 2828

Rijalun la tulheehim tijaratun wala bay'un 'an thikri Allahi waiqami assalati waeetai azzakati yakhafoona yawman tataqallabu feehi alquloobu waalabsaru

# 2829

Liyajziyahumu Allahu ahsana ma 'amiloo wayazeedahum min fadlihi waAllahu yarzuqu man yashao bighayri hisabin

# 2830

Waallatheena kafaroo a'maluhum kasarabin biqee'atin yahsabuhu aththamanu maan hatta itha jaahu lam yajidhu shayan wawajada Allaha 'indahu fawaffahu hisabahu waAllahu saree'u alhisabi

# 2831

Aw kathulumatin fee bahrin lujjiyyin yaghshahu mawjun min fawqihi mawjun min fawqihi sahabun thulumatun ba'duha fawqa ba'din itha akhraja yadahu lam yakad yaraha waman lam yaj'ali Allahu lahu nooran fama lahu min noorin

# 2832

Alam tara anna Allaha yusabbihu lahu man fee assamawati waalardi waattayru saffatin kullun qad 'alima salatahu watasbeehahu waAllahu 'aleemun bima yaf'aloona

# 2833

Walillahi mulku assamawati waalardi waila Allahi almaseeru

# 2834

Alam tara anna Allaha yuzjee sahaban thumma yuallifu baynahu thumma yaj'aluhu rukaman fatara alwadqa yakhruju min khilalihi wayunazzilu mina assamai min jibalin feeha min baradin fayuseebu bihi man yashao wayasrifuhu 'an man yashao yakadu sana barqihi yathhabu bialabsari

# 2835

Yuqallibu Allahu allayla waannahara inna fee thalika la'ibratan liolee alabsari

# 2836

WaAllahu khalaqa kulla dabbatin min main faminhum man yamshee 'ala batnihi waminhum man yamshee 'ala rijlayni waminhum man yamshee 'ala arba'in yakhluqu Allahu ma yashao inna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 2837

Laqad anzana ayatin mubayyinatin waAllahu yahdee man yashao ila siratin mustaqeemin

# 2838

Wayaqooloona amanna biAllahi wabiarrasooli waata'na thumma yatawalla fareequn minhum min ba'di thalika wama olaika bialmumineena

# 2839

Waitha du'oo ila Allahi warasoolihi liyahkuma baynahum itha fareequn minhum mu'ridoona

# 2840

Wain yakun lahumu alhaqqu yatoo ilayhi muth'ineena

# 2841

Afee quloobihim maradun ami irtaboo am yakhafoona an yaheefa Allahu 'alayhim warasooluhu bal olaika humu aththalimoona

# 2842

Innama kana qawla almumineena itha du'oo ila Allahi warasoolihi liyahkuma baynahum an yaqooloo sami'na waata'na waolaika humu almuflihoona

# 2843

Waman yuti'i Allaha warasoolahu wayakhsha Allaha wayattaqhi faolaika humu alfaizoona

# 2844

Waaqsamoo biAllahi jahda aymanihim lain amartahum layakhrujunna qul la tuqsimoo ta'atun ma'roofatun inna Allaha khabeerun bima ta'maloona

# 2845

Qul atee'oo Allaha waatee'oo arrasoola fain tawallaw fainnama 'alayhi ma hummila wa'alaykum ma hummiltum wain tutee'oohu tahtadoo wama 'ala arrasooli illa albalaghu almubeena

# 2846

Wa'ada Allahu allatheena amanoo minkum wa'amiloo assalihati layastakhlifannahum fee alardi kama istakhlafa allatheena min qablihim walayumakkinanna lahum deenahumu allathee irtada lahum walayubaddilannahum min ba'di khawfihim amnan ya'budoonanee la yushrikoona bee shayan waman kafara ba'da thalika faolaika humu alfasiqoona

# 2847

Waaqeemoo assalata waatoo azzakata waatee'oo arrasoola la'allakum turhamoona

# 2848

La tahsabanna allatheena kafaroo mu'jizeena fee alardi wamawahumu annaru walabisa almaseeru

# 2849

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo liyastathinkumu allatheena malakat aymanukum waallatheena lam yablughoo alhuluma minkum thalatha marratin min qabli salati alfajri waheena tada'oona thiyabakum mina aththaheerati wamin ba'di salati al'ishai thalathu 'awratin lakum laysa 'alaykum wala 'alayhim junahun ba'dahunna tawwafoona 'alaykum ba'dukum 'ala ba'din kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakumu alayati waAllahu 'aleemun hakeemun

# 2850

Waitha balagha alatfalu minkumu alhuluma falyastathinoo kama istathana allatheena min qablihim kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakum ayatihi waAllahu 'aleemun hakeemun

# 2851

Waalqawa'idu mina annisai allatee la yarjoona nikahan falaysa 'alayhinna junahun an yada'na thiyabahunna ghayra mutabarrijatin bizeenatin waan yasta'fifna khayrun lahunna waAllahu samee'un 'aleemun

# 2852

Laysa 'ala ala'ma harajun wala 'ala ala'raji harajun wala 'ala almareedi harajun wala 'ala anfusikum an takuloo min buyootikum aw buyooti abaikum aw buyooti ommahatikum aw buyooti ikhwanikum aw buyooti akhawatikum aw buyooti a'mamikum aw buyooti 'ammatikum aw buyooti akhwalikum aw buyooti khalatikum aw ma malaktum mafatihahu aw sadeeqikum laysa 'alaykum junahun an takuloo jamee'an aw ashtatan faitha dakhatum buyootan fasallimoo 'ala anfusikum tahiyyatan min 'indi Allahi mubarakatan tayyibatan kathalika yubayyinu Allahu lakumu alayati la'allakum ta'qiloona

# 2853

Innama almuminoona allatheena amanoo biAllahi warasoolihi waitha kanoo ma'ahu 'ala amrin jami'in lam yathhaboo hatta yastathinoohu inna allatheena yastathinoonaka olaika allatheena yuminoona biAllahi warasoolihi faitha istathanooka liba'di shanihim fathan liman shita minhum waistaghfir lahumu Allaha inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun

# 2854

La taj'aloo du'aa arrasooli baynakum kadu'ai ba'dikum ba'dan qad ya'lamu Allahu allatheena yatasallaloona minkum liwathan falyahthari allatheena yukhalifoona 'an amrihi an tuseebahum fitnatun aw yuseebahum 'athabun aleemun

# 2855

Ala inna lillahi ma fee assamawati waalardi qad ya'lamu ma antum 'alayhi wayawma yurja'oona ilayhi fayunabbiohum bima 'amiloo waAllahu bikulli shayin 'aleemun

# 2856

Tabaraka allathee nazzala alfurqana 'ala 'abdihi liyakoona lil'alameena natheeran

# 2857

# 2858

# 2859

# 2860

Waqaloo asateeru alawwaleena iktatabaha fahiya tumla 'alayhi bukratan waaseelan

# 2861

# 2862

# 2863

# 2864

# 2865

# 2866

# 2867

# 2868

# 2869

# 2870

# 2871

Lahum feeha ma yashaoona khalideena kana 'ala rabbika wa'dan masoolan

# 2872

# 2873

# 2874

# 2875

# 2876

# 2879

# 2880

# 2883

# 2891

# 2898

# 2899

# 2901

# 2911

# 2912

# 2924

# 3159

Illa allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati wathakaroo Allaha katheeran waintasaroo min ba'di ma thulimoo wasaya'lamu allatheena thalamoo ayya munqalabin yanqaliboona

# 3161

Hudan wabushra lilmumineena

# 3168

# 3169

# 3170

Illa man thalama thumma baddala husnan ba'da sooin fainnee ghafoorun raheemun

# 3171

# 3172

Falamma jaathum ayatuna mubsiratan qaloo hatha sihrun mubeenun

# 3173

# 3174

# 3175

# 3176

Wahushira lisulaymana junooduhu mina aljinni waalinsi waattayri fahum yooza'oona

# 3177

Hatta itha ataw 'ala wadi annamli qalat namlatun ya ayyuha annamlu odkhuloo masakinakum la yahtimannakum sulaymanu wajunooduhu wahum la yash'uroona

# 3178

Fatabassama dahikan min qawliha waqala rabbi awzi'nee an ashkura ni'mataka allatee an'amta 'alayya wa'ala walidayya waan a'mala salihan tardahu waadkhilnee birahmatika fee 'ibadika assaliheena

# 3179

Watafaqqada attayra faqala ma liya la ara alhudhuda am kana mina alghaibeena

# 3197

# 3198

# 3199

Qala allathee 'indahu 'ilmun mina alkitabi ana ateeka bihi qabla an yartadda ilayka tarfuka falamma raahu mustaqirran 'indahu qala hatha min fadli rabbee liyabluwanee aashkuru am akfuru waman shakara fainnama yashkuru linafsihi waman kafara fainna rabbee ghaniyyun kareemun

# 3200

# 3201

# 3202

# 3203

Qeela laha odkhulee assarha falamma raathu hasibathu lujjatan wakashafat 'an saqayha qala innahu sarhun mumarradun min qawareera qalat rabbi innee thalamtu nafsee waaslamtu ma'a sulaymana lillahi rabbi al'alameena

# 3204

# 3205

# 3209

# 3215

# 3217

Waamtarna 'alayhim mataran fasaa mataru almunthareena

# 3218

Quli alhamdu lillahi wasalamun 'ala 'ibadihi allatheena istafa allahu khayrun amma yushrikoona

# 3219

Amman khalaqa assamawati waalarda waanzala lakum mina assamai maan faanbatna bihi hadaiqa thata bahjatin ma kana lakum an tunbitoo shajaraha ailahun ma'a Allahi bal hum qawmun ya'diloona

# 3220

Amman ja'ala alarda qararan waja'ala khilalaha anharan waja'ala laha rawasiya waja'ala bayna albahrayni hajizan ailahun ma'a Allahi bal aktharuhum la ya'lamoona

# 3221

Amman yujeebu almudtarra itha da'ahu wayakshifu assooa wayaj'alukum khulafaa alardi ailahun ma'a Allahi qaleelan ma tathakkaroona

# 3222

Amman yahdeekum fee thulumati albarri waalbahri waman yursilu arriyaha bushran bayna yaday rahmatihi ailahun ma'a Allahi ta'ala Allahu 'amma yushrikoona

# 3223

Amman yabdao alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu waman yarzuqukum mina assamai waalardi ailahun ma'a Allahi qul hatoo burhanakum in kuntum sadiqeena

# 3224

Qul la ya'lamu man fee assamawati waalardi alghayba illa Allahu wama yash'uroona ayyana yub'athoona

# 3225

Bali iddaraka 'ilmuhum fee alakhirati bal hum fee shakkin minha bal hum minha 'amoona

# 3226

Waqala allatheena kafaroo aitha kunna turaban waabaona ainna lamukhrajoona

# 3227

# 3228

# 3229

Wala tahzan 'alayhim wala takun fee dayqin mimma yamkuroona

# 3230

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwa'du in kuntum sadiqeena

# 3231

Qul 'asa an yakoona radifa lakum ba'du allathee tasta'jiloona

# 3232

# 3233

# 3234

Wama min ghaibatin fee assamai waalardi illa fee kitabin mubeenin

# 3235
