# 3236

Wainnahu lahudan warahmatun lilmumineena

# 3237

Inna rabbaka yaqdee baynahum bihukmihi wahuwa al'azeezu al'aleemu

# 3238

Fatawakkal 'ala Allahi innaka 'ala alhaqqi almubeeni

# 3239

Innaka la tusmi'u almawta wala tusmi'u assumma addu'aa itha wallaw mudbireena

# 3240

Wama anta bihadee al'umyi 'an dalalatihim in tusmi'u illa man yuminu biayatina fahum muslimoona

# 3241

Waitha waqa'a alqawlu 'alayhim akhrajna lahum dabbatan mina alardi tukallimuhum anna annasa kanoo biayatina la yooqinoona

# 3242

Wayawma nahshuru min kulli ommatin fawjan mimman yukaththibu biayatina fahum yooza'oona

# 3243

Hatta itha jaoo qala akaththabtum biayatee walam tuheetoo biha 'ilman ammatha kuntum ta'maloona

# 3244

Wawaqa'a alqawlu 'alayhim bima thalamoo fahum la yantiqoona

# 3245

Alam yaraw anna ja'ana allayla liyaskunoo feehi waannahara mubsiran inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoona

# 3246

Wayawma yunfakhu fee assoori fafazi'a man fee assamawati waman fee alardi illa man shaa Allahu wakullun atawhu dakhireena

# 3247

Watara aljibala tahsabuha jamidatan wahiya tamurru marra assahabi sun'a Allahi allathee atqana kulla shayin innahu khabeerun bima taf'aloona

# 3248

Man jaa bialhasanati falahu khayrun minha wahum min faza'in yawmaithin aminoona

# 3249

Waman jaa biassayyiati fakubbat wujoohuhum fee annari hal tujzawna illa ma kuntum ta'maloona

# 3250

Innama omirtu an a'buda rabba hathihi albadati allathee harramaha walahu kullu shayin waomirtu an akoona mina almuslimeena

# 3251

Waan atluwa alqurana famani ihtada fainnama yahtadee linafsihi waman dalla faqul innama ana mina almunthireena

# 3252

Waquli alhamdu lillahi sayureekum ayatihi fata'rifoonaha wama rabbuka bighafilin 'amma ta'maloona

# 3253

Taseenmeem

# 3254

Tilka ayatu alkitabi almubeeni

# 3255

Natloo 'alayka min nabai moosa wafir'awna bialhaqqi liqawmin yuminoona

# 3256

Inna fir'awna 'ala fee alardi waja'ala ahlaha shiya'an yastad'ifu taifatan minhum yuthabbihu abnaahum wayastahyee nisaahum innahu kana mina almufsideena

# 3257

Wanureedu an namunna 'ala allatheena istud'ifoo fee alardi wanaj'alahum aimmatan wanaj'alahumu alwaritheena

# 3258

Wanumakkina lahum fee alardi wanuriya fir'awna wahamana wajunoodahuma minhum ma kanoo yahtharoona

# 3259

Waawhayna ila ommi moosa an ardi'eehi faitha khifti 'alayhi faalqeehi fee alyammi wala takhafee wala tahzanee inna raddoohu ilayki waja'iloohu mina almursaleena

# 3260

Failtaqatahu alu fir'awna liyakoona lahum 'aduwwan wahazanan inna fir'awna wahamana wajunoodahuma kanoo khatieena

# 3261

Waqalati imraatu fir'awna qurratu 'aynin lee walaka la taqtuloohu 'asa an yanfa'ana aw nattakhithahu waladan wahum la yash'uroona

# 3262

Waasbaha fuadu ommi moosa farighan in kadat latubdee bihi lawla an rabatna 'ala qalbiha litakoona mina almumineena

# 3263

Waqalat liokhtihi qusseehi fabasurat bihi 'an junubin wahum la yash'uroona

# 3264

Waharramna 'alayhi almaradi'a min qablu faqalat hal adullukum 'ala ahli baytin yakfuloonahu lakum wahum lahu nasihoona

# 3265

Faradadnahu ila ommihi kay taqarra 'aynuha wala tahzana walita'lama anna wa'da Allahi haqqun walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoona

# 3266

Walamma balagha ashuddahu waistawa ataynahu hukman wa'ilman wakathalika najzee almuhsineena

# 3267

Wadakhala almadeenata 'ala heeni ghaflatin min ahliha fawajada feeha rajulayni yaqtatilani hatha min shee'atihi wahatha min 'aduwwihi faistaghathahu allathee min shee'atihi 'ala allathee min 'aduwwihi fawakazahu moosa faqada 'alayhi qala hatha min 'amali ashshaytani innahu 'aduwwun mudillun mubeenun

# 3268

Qala rabbi innee thalamtu nafsee faighfir lee faghafara lahu innahu huwa alghafooru arraheemu

# 3269

Qala rabbi bima an'amta 'alayya falan akoona thaheeran lilmujrimeena

# 3270

Faasbaha fee almadeenati khaifan yataraqqabu faitha allathee istansarahu bialamsi yastasrikhuhu qala lahu moosa innaka laghawiyyun mubeenun

# 3271

Falamma an arada an yabtisha biallathee huwa 'aduwwun lahuma qala ya moosa atureedu an taqtulanee kama qatata nafsan bialamsi in tureedu illa an takoona jabbaran fee alardi wama tureedu an takoona mina almusliheena

# 3272

Wajaa rajulun min aqsa almadeenati yas'a qala ya moosa inna almalaa yatamiroona bika liyaqtulooka faokhruj innee laka mina annasiheena

# 3273

Fakharaja minha khaifan yataraqqabu qala rabbi najjinee mina alqawmi aththalimeena

# 3274

Walamma tawajjaha tilqaa madyana qala 'asa rabbee an yahdiyanee sawaa assabeeli

# 3275

Walamma warada maa madyana wajada 'alayhi ommatan mina annasi yasqoona wawajada min doonihimu imraatayni tathoodani qala ma khatbukuma qalata la nasqee hatta yusdira arri'ao waaboona shaykhun kabeerun

# 3276

Fasaqa lahuma thumma tawalla ila aththilli faqala rabbi innee lima anzata ilayya min khayrin faqeerun

# 3277

Fajaathu ihdahuma tamshee 'ala istihyain qalat inna abee yad'ooka liyajziyaka ajra ma saqayta lana falamma jaahu waqassa 'alayhi alqasasa qala la takhaf najawta mina alqawmi aththalimeena

# 3278

Qalat ihdahuma ya abati istajirhu inna khayra mani istajarta alqawiyyu alameenu

# 3279

Qala innee oreedu an onkihaka ihda ibnatayya hatayni 'ala an tajuranee thamaniya hijajin fain atmamta 'ashran famin 'indika wama oreedu an ashuqqa 'alayka satajidunee in shaa Allahu mina assaliheena

# 3280

Qala thalika baynee wabaynaka ayyama alajalayni qadaytu fala 'udwana 'alayya waAllahu 'ala ma naqoolu wakeelun

# 3281

Falamma qada moosaalajala wasara biahlihi anasa min janibi attoori naran qala liahlihi omkuthoo innee anastu naran la'allee ateekum minha bikhabarin aw jathwatin mina annari la'allakum tastaloona

# 3282

Falamma ataha noodiya min shatii alwadi alaymani fee albuq'ati almubarakati mina ashshajarati an ya moosa innee ana Allahu rabbu al'alameena

# 3283

Waan alqi 'asaka falamma raaha tahtazzu kaannaha jannun walla mudbiran walam yu'aqqib ya moosa aqbil wala takhaf innaka mina alamineena

# 3284

Osluk yadaka fee jaybika takhruj baydaa min ghayri sooin waodmum ilayka janahaka mina arrahbi fathanika burhanani min rabbika ila fir'awna wamalaihi innahum kanoo qawman fasiqeena

# 3285

Qala rabbi innee qatatu minhum nafsan faakhafu an yaqtulooni

# 3286

Waakhee haroonu huwa afsahu minnee lisanan faarsilhu ma'iya ridan yusaddiqunee innee akhafu an yukaththibooni

# 3287

Qala sanashuddu 'adudaka biakheeka wanaj'alu lakuma sultanan fala yasiloona ilaykuma biayatina antuma wamani ittaba'akuma alghaliboona

# 3288

Falamma jaahum moosa biayatina bayyinatin qaloo ma hatha illa sihrun muftaran wama sami'na bihatha fee abaina alawwaleena

# 3289

Waqala moosa rabbee a'lamu biman jaa bialhuda min 'indihi waman takoonu lahu 'aqibatu addari innahu la yuflihu aththalimoona

# 3290

Waqala fir'awnu ya ayyuha almalao ma 'alimtu lakum min ilahin ghayree faawqid lee ya hamanu 'ala atteeni faij'al lee sarhan la'allee attali'u ila ilahi moosa wainnee laathunnuhu mina alkathibeena

# 3291

Waistakbara huwa wajunooduhu fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi wathannoo annahum ilayna la yurja'oona

# 3292

Faakhathnahu wajunoodahu fanabathnahum fee alyammi faonthur kayfa kana 'aqibatu aththalimeena

# 3293

Waja'anahum aimmatan yad'oona ila annari wayawma alqiyamati la yunsaroona

# 3294

Waatba'nahum fee hathihi addunya la'natan wayawma alqiyamati hum mina almaqbooheena

# 3295

Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba min ba'di ma ahlakna alquroona aloola basaira lilnnasi wahudan warahmatan la'allahum yatathakkaroona

# 3296

Wama kunta bijanibi algharbiyyi ith qadayna ila moosa alamra wama kunta mina ashshahideena

# 3297

Walakinna anshana quroonan fatatawala 'alayhimu al'umuru wama kunta thawiyan fee ahli madyana tatloo 'alayhim ayatina walakinna kunna mursileena

# 3298

Wama kunta bijanibi attoori ith nadayna walakin rahmatan min rabbika litunthira qawman ma atahum min natheerin min qablika la'allahum yatathakkaroona

# 3299

Walawla an tuseebahum museebatun bima qaddamat aydeehim fayaqooloo rabbana lawla arsata ilayna rasoolan fanattabi'a ayatika wanakoona mina almumineena

# 3300

Falamma jaahumu alhaqqu min 'indina qaloo lawla ootiya mithla ma ootiya moosa awalam yakfuroo bima ootiya moosa min qablu qaloo sihrani tathahara waqaloo inna bikullin kafiroona

# 3301

Qul fatoo bikitabin min 'indi Allahi huwa ahda minhuma attabi'hu in kuntum sadiqeena

# 3302

Fain lam yastajeeboo laka fai'lam annama yattabi'oona ahwaahum waman adallu mimmani ittaba'a hawahu bighayri hudan mina Allahi inna Allaha la yahdee alqawma aththalimeena

# 3303

Walaqad wassana lahumu alqawla la'allahum yatathakkaroona

# 3304

Allatheena ataynahumu alkitaba min qablihi hum bihi yuminoona

# 3305

Waitha yutla 'alayhim qaloo amanna bihi innahu alhaqqu min rabbina inna kunna min qablihi muslimeena

# 3306

Olaika yutawna ajrahum marratayni bima sabaroo wayadraoona bialhasanati assayyiata wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoona

# 3307

Waitha sami'oo allaghwa a'radoo 'anhu waqaloo lana a'maluna walakum a'malukum salamun 'alaykum la nabtaghee aljahileena

# 3308

Innaka la tahdee man ahbabta walakinna Allaha yahdee man yashao wahuwa a'lamu bialmuhtadeena

# 3309

Waqaloo in nattabi'i alhuda ma'aka nutakhattaf min ardina awalam numakkin lahum haraman aminan yujba ilayhi thamaratu kulli shayin rizqan min ladunna walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoona

# 3310

Wakam ahlakna min qaryatin batirat ma'eeshataha fatilka masakinuhum lam tuskan min ba'dihim illa qaleelan wakunna nahnu alwaritheena

# 3311

Wama kana rabbuka muhlika alqura hatta yab'atha fee ommiha rasoolan yatloo 'alayhim ayatina wama kunna muhlikee alqura illa waahluha thalimoona

# 3312

Wama ooteetum min shayin famata'u alhayati addunya wazeenatuha wama 'inda Allahi khayrun waabqa afala ta'qiloona

# 3313

Afaman wa'adnahu wa'dan hasanan fahuwa laqeehi kaman matta'nahu mata'a alhayati addunya thumma huwa yawma alqiyamati mina almuhdareena

# 3314

Wayawma yunadeehim fayaqoolu ayna shurakaiya allatheena kuntum taz'umoona

# 3315

Qala allatheena haqqa 'alayhimu alqawlu rabbana haolai allatheena aghwayna aghwaynahum kama ghawayna tabarrana ilayka ma kanoo iyyana ya'budoona

# 3316

Waqeela od'oo shurakaakum fada'awhum falam yastajeeboo lahum waraawoo al'athaba law annahum kanoo yahtadoona

# 3317

Wayawma yunadeehim fayaqoolu matha ajabtumu almursaleena

# 3318

Fa'amiyat 'alayhimu alanbao yawmaithin fahum la yatasaaloona

# 3319

Faamma man taba waamana wa'amila salihan fa'asa an yakoona mina almufliheena

# 3320

Warabbuka yakhluqu ma yashao wayakhtaru ma kana lahumu alkhiyaratu subhana Allahi wata'ala 'amma yushrikoona

# 3321

Warabbuka ya'lamu ma tukinnu sudooruhum wama yu'linoona

# 3322

Wahuwa Allahu la ilaha illa huwa lahu alhamdu fee aloola waalakhirati walahu alhukmu wailayhi turja'oona

# 3323

Qul araaytum in ja'ala Allahu 'alaykumu allayla sarmadan ila yawmi alqiyamati man ilahun ghayru Allahi yateekum bidiyain afala tasma'oona

# 3324

Qul araaytum in ja'ala Allahu 'alaykumu annahara sarmadan ila yawmi alqiyamati man ilahun ghayru Allahi yateekum bilaylin taskunoona feehi afala tubsiroona

# 3325

Wamin rahmatihi ja'ala lakumu allayla waannahara litaskunoo feehi walitabtaghoo min fadlihi wala'allakum tashkuroona

# 3326

Wayawma yunadeehim fayaqoolu ayna shurakaiya allatheena kuntum taz'umoona

# 3327

Wanaza'na min kulli ommatin shaheedan faqulna hatoo burhanakum fa'alimoo anna alhaqqa lillahi wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yaftaroona

# 3328

Inna qaroona kana min qawmi moosa fabagha 'alayhim waataynahu mina alkunoozi ma inna mafatihahu latanooo bial'usbati olee alquwwati ith qala lahu qawmuhu la tafrah inna Allaha la yuhibbu alfariheena

# 3329

Waibtaghi feema ataka Allahu addara alakhirata wala tansa naseebaka mina addunya waahsin kama ahsana Allahu ilayka wala tabghi alfasada fee alardi inna Allaha la yuhibbu almufsideena

# 3330

Qala innama ooteetuhu 'ala 'ilmin 'indee awalam ya'lam anna Allaha qad ahlaka min qablihi mina alqurooni man huwa ashaddu minhu quwwatan waaktharu jam'an wala yusalu 'an thunoobihimu almujrimoona

# 3331

Fakharaja 'ala qawmihi fee zeenatihi qala allatheena yureedoona alhayata addunya ya layta lana mithla ma ootiya qaroonu innahu lathoo haththin 'atheemin

# 3332

Waqala allatheena ootoo al'ilma waylakum thawabu Allahi khayrun liman amana wa'amila salihan wala yulaqqaha illa assabiroona

# 3333

Fakhasafna bihi wabidarihi alarda fama kana lahu min fiatin yansuroonahu min dooni Allahi wama kana mina almuntasireena

# 3334

Waasbaha allatheena tamannaw makanahu bialamsi yaqooloona waykaanna Allaha yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao min 'ibadihi wayaqdiru lawla an manna Allahu 'alayna lakhasafa bina waykaannahu la yuflihu alkafiroona

# 3335

Tilka addaru alakhiratu naj'aluha lillatheena la yureedoona 'uluwwan fee alardi wala fasadan waal'aqibatu lilmuttaqeena

# 3336

Man jaa bialhasanati falahu khayrun minha waman jaa biassayyiati fala yujza allatheena 'amiloo assayyiati illa ma kanoo ya'maloona

# 3337

Inna allathee farada 'alayka alqurana laradduka ila ma'adin qul rabbee a'lamu man jaa bialhuda waman huwa fee dalalin mubeenin

# 3338

Wama kunta tarjoo an yulqa ilayka alkitabu illa rahmatan min rabbika fala takoonanna thaheeran lilkafireena

# 3339

Wala yasuddunnaka 'an ayati Allahi ba'da ith onzilat ilayka waod'u ila rabbika wala takoonanna mina almushrikeena

# 3340

Wala tad'u ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara la ilaha illa huwa kullu shayin halikun illa wajhahu lahu alhukmu wailayhi turja'oona

# 3341

Aliflammeem

# 3342

Ahasiba annasu an yutrakoo an yaqooloo amanna wahum la yuftanoona

# 3343

Walaqad fatanna allatheena min qablihim falaya'lamanna Allahu allatheena sadaqoo walaya'lamanna alkathibeena

# 3344

Am hasiba allatheena ya'maloona assayyiati an yasbiqoona saa ma yahkumoona

# 3345

Man kana yarjoo liqaa Allahi fainna ajala Allahi laatin wahuwa assamee'u al'aleemu

# 3346

Waman jahada fainnama yujahidu linafsihi inna Allaha laghaniyyun 'ani al'alameena

# 3347

Waallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati lanukaffiranna 'anhum sayyiatihim walanajziyannahum ahsana allathee kanoo ya'maloona

# 3348

Wawassayna alinsana biwalidayhi husnan wain jahadaka litushrika bee ma laysa laka bihi 'ilmun fala tuti'huma ilayya marji'ukum faonabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloona

# 3349

Waallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati lanudkhilannahum fee assaliheena

# 3350

Wamina annasi man yaqoolu amanna biAllahi faitha oothiya fee Allahi ja'ala fitnata annasi ka'athabi Allahi walain jaa nasrun min rabbika layaqoolunna inna kunna ma'akum awalaysa Allahu bia'lama bima fee sudoori al'alameena

# 3351

Walaya'lamanna Allahu allatheena amanoo walaya'lamanna almunafiqeena

# 3352

Waqala allatheena kafaroo lillatheena amanoo ittabi'oo sabeelana wanahmil khatayakum wama hum bihamileena min khatayahum min shayin innahum lakathiboona

# 3353

Walayahmilunna athqalahum waathqalan ma'a athqalihim walayusalunna yawma alqiyamati 'amma kanoo yaftaroona

# 3354

Walaqad arsana noohan ila qawmihi falabitha feehim alfa sanatin illa khamseena 'aman faakhathahumu attoofanu wahum thalimoona

# 3355

Faanjaynahu waashaba assafeenati waja'anaha ayatan lil'alameena

# 3356

Waibraheema ith qala liqawmihi o'budoo Allaha waittaqoohu thalikum khayrun lakum in kuntum ta'lamoona

# 3357

Innama ta'budoona min dooni Allahi awthanan watakhluqoona ifkan inna allatheena ta'budoona min dooni Allahi la yamlikoona lakum rizqan faibtaghoo 'inda Allahi arrizqa wao'budoohu waoshkuroo lahu ilayhi turja'oona

# 3358

Wain tukaththiboo faqad kaththaba omamun min qablikum wama 'ala arrasooli illa albalaghu almubeenu

# 3359

Awalam yaraw kayfa yubdio Allahu alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu inna thalika 'ala Allahi yaseerun

# 3360

Qul seeroo fee alardi faonthuroo kayfa badaa alkhalqa thumma Allahu yunshio annashata alakhirata inna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 3361

Yu'aththibu man yashao wayarhamu man yashao wailayhi tuqlaboona

# 3362

Wama antum bimu'jizeena fee alardi wala fee assamai wama lakum min dooni Allahi min waliyyin wala naseerin

# 3363

Waallatheena kafaroo biayati Allahi waliqaihi olaika yaisoo min rahmatee waolaika lahum 'athabun aleemun

# 3364

Fama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qaloo oqtuloohu aw harriqoohu faanjahu Allahu mina annari inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoona

# 3365

Waqala innama ittakhathtum min dooni Allahi awthanan mawaddata baynikum fee alhayati addunya thumma yawma alqiyamati yakfuru ba'dukum biba'din wayal'anu ba'dukum ba'dan wamawakumu annaru wama lakum min nasireena

# 3366

Faamana lahu lootun waqala innee muhajirun ila rabbee innahu huwa al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 3367

Wawahabna lahu ishaqa waya'qooba waja'ana fee thurriyyatihi annubuwwata waalkitaba waataynahu ajrahu fee addunya wainnahu fee alakhirati lamina assaliheena

# 3368

Walootan ith qala liqawmihi innakum latatoona alfahishata ma sabaqakum biha min ahadin mina al'alameena

# 3369

Ainnakum latatoona arrijala wataqta'oona assabeela watatoona fee nadeekumu almunkara fama kana jawaba qawmihi illa an qaloo itina bi'athabi Allahi in kunta mina assadiqeena

# 3370

Qala rabbi onsurnee 'ala alqawmi almufsideena

# 3371

Walamma jaat rusuluna ibraheema bialbushra qaloo inna muhlikoo ahli hathihi alqaryati inna ahlaha kanoo thalimeena

# 3372

Qala inna feeha lootan qaloo nahnu a'lamu biman feeha lanunajjiyannahu waahlahu illa imraatahu kanat mina alghabireena

# 3373

Walamma an jaat rusuluna lootan seea bihim wadaqa bihim thar'an waqaloo la takhaf wala tahzan inna munajjooka waahlaka illa imraataka kanat mina alghabireena

# 3374

Inna munziloona 'ala ahli hathihi alqaryati rijzan mina assamai bima kanoo yafsuqoona

# 3375

Walaqad tarakna minha ayatan bayyinatan liqawmin ya'qiloona

# 3376

Waila madyana akhahum shu'ayban faqala ya qawmi o'budoo Allaha waorjoo alyawma alakhira wala ta'thaw fee alardi mufsideena

# 3377

Fakaththaboohu faakhathathumu arrajfatu faasbahoo fee darihim jathimeena

# 3378

Wa'adan wathamooda waqad tabayyana lakum min masakinihim wazayyana lahumu ashshaytanu a'malahum fasaddahum 'ani assabeeli wakanoo mustabsireena

# 3379

Waqaroona wafir'awna wahamana walaqad jaahum moosa bialbayyinati faistakbaroo fee alardi wama kanoo sabiqeena

# 3380

Fakullan akhathna bithanbihi faminhum man arsana 'alayhi hasiban waminhum man akhathathu assayhatu waminhum man khasafna bihi alarda waminhum man aghraqna wama kana Allahu liyathlimahum walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoona

# 3381

Mathalu allatheena ittakhathoo min dooni Allahi awliyaa kamathali al'ankabooti ittakhathat baytan wainna awhana albuyooti labaytu al'ankabooti law kanoo ya'lamoona

# 3382

Inna Allaha ya'lamu ma yad'oona min doonihi min shayin wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 3383

Watilka alamthalu nadribuha lilnnasi wama ya'qiluha illa al'alimoona

# 3384

Khalaqa Allahu assamawati waalarda bialhaqqi inna fee thalika laayatan lilmumineena

# 3385

Otlu ma oohiya ilayka mina alkitabi waaqimi assalata inna assalata tanha 'ani alfahshai waalmunkari walathikru Allahi akbaru waAllahu ya'lamu ma tasna'oona

# 3386

Wala tujadiloo ahla alkitabi illa biallatee hiya ahsanu illa allatheena thalamoo minhum waqooloo amanna biallathee onzila ilayna waonzila ilaykum wailahuna wailahukum wahidun wanahnu lahu muslimoona

# 3387

Wakathalika anzana ilayka alkitaba faallatheena ataynahumu alkitaba yuminoona bihi wamin haolai man yuminu bihi wama yajhadu biayatina illa alkafiroona

# 3388

Wama kunta tatloo min qablihi min kitabin wala takhuttuhu biyameenika ithan lairtaba almubtiloona

# 3389

Bal huwa ayatun bayyinatun fee sudoori allatheena ootoo al'ilma wama yajhadu biayatina illa aththalimoona

# 3390

Waqaloo lawla onzila 'alayhi ayatun min rabbihi qul innama alayatu 'inda Allahi wainnama ana natheerun mubeenun

# 3391

Awalam yakfihim anna anzana 'alayka alkitaba yutla 'alayhim inna fee thalika larahmatan wathikra liqawmin yuminoona

# 3392

Qul kafa biAllahi baynee wabaynakum shaheedan ya'lamu ma fee assamawati waalardi waallatheena amanoo bialbatili wakafaroo biAllahi olaika humu alkhasiroona

# 3393

Wayasta'jiloonaka bial'athabi walawla ajalun musamman lajaahumu al'athabu walayatiyannahum baghtatan wahum la yash'uroona

# 3394

Yasta'jiloonaka bial'athabi wainna jahannama lamuheetatun bialkafireena

# 3395

Yawma yaghshahumu al'athabu min fawqihim wamin tahti arjulihim wayaqoolu thooqoo ma kuntum ta'maloona

# 3396

Ya 'ibadiya allatheena amanoo inna ardee wasi'atun faiyyaya fao'budooni

# 3397

Kullu nafsin thaiqatu almawti thumma ilayna turja'oona

# 3398

Waallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati lanubawwiannahum mina aljannati ghurafan tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha ni'ma ajru al'amileena

# 3399

Allatheena sabaroo wa'ala rabbihim yatawakkaloona

# 3400

Wakaayyin min dabbatin la tahmilu rizqaha Allahu yarzuquha waiyyakum wahuwa assamee'u al'aleemu

# 3401

Walain saatahum man khalaqa assamawati waalarda wasakhkhara ashshamsa waalqamara layaqoolunna Allahu faanna yufakoona

# 3402

Allahu yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao min 'ibadihi wayaqdiru lahu inna Allaha bikulli shayin 'aleemun

# 3403

Walain saatahum man nazzala mina assamai maan faahya bihi alarda min ba'di mawtiha layaqoolunna Allahu quli alhamdu lillahi bal aktharuhum la ya'qiloona

# 3404

Wama hathihi alhayatu addunya illa lahwun wala'ibun wainna addara alakhirata lahiya alhayawanu law kanoo ya'lamoona

# 3405

Faitha rakiboo fee alfulki da'awoo Allaha mukhliseena lahu addeena falamma najjahum ila albarri itha hum yushrikoona

# 3406

Liyakfuroo bima ataynahum waliyatamatta'oo fasawfa ya'lamoona

# 3407

Awalam yaraw anna ja'ana haraman aminan wayutakhattafu annasu min hawlihim afabialbatili yuminoona wabini'mati Allahi yakfuroona

# 3408

Waman athlamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban aw kaththaba bialhaqqi lamma jaahu alaysa fee jahannama mathwan lilkafireena

# 3409

Waallatheena jahadoo feena lanahdiyannahum subulana wainna Allaha lama'a almuhsineena

# 3410

Aliflammeem

# 3411

Ghulibati arroomu

# 3412

Fee adna alardi wahum min ba'di ghalabihim sayaghliboona

# 3413

Fee bid'i sineena lillahi alamru min qablu wamin ba'du wayawmaithin yafrahu almuminoona

# 3414

Binasri Allahi yansuru man yashao wahuwa al'azeezu arraheemu

# 3415

Wa'da Allahi la yukhlifu Allahu wa'dahu walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoona

# 3416

Ya'lamoona thahiran mina alhayati addunya wahum 'ani alakhirati hum ghafiloona

# 3417

Awalam yatafakkaroo fee anfusihim ma khalaqa Allahu assamawati waalarda wama baynahuma illa bialhaqqi waajalin musamman wainna katheeran mina annasi biliqai rabbihim lakafiroona

# 3418

Awalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena min qablihim kanoo ashadda minhum quwwatan waatharoo alarda wa'amarooha akthara mimma 'amarooha wajaathum rusuluhum bialbayyinati fama kana Allahu liyathlimahum walakin kanoo anfusahum yathlimoona

# 3419

Thumma kana 'aqibata allatheena asaoo assooa an kaththaboo biayati Allahi wakanoo biha yastahzioona

# 3420

Allahu yabdao alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu thumma ilayhi turja'oona

# 3421

Wayawma taqoomu assa'atu yublisu almujrimoona

# 3422

Walam yakun lahum min shurakaihim shufa'ao wakanoo bishurakaihim kafireena

# 3423

Wayawma taqoomu assa'atu yawmaithin yatafarraqoona

# 3424

Faamma allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati fahum fee rawdatin yuhbaroona

# 3425

Waamma allatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina waliqai alakhirati faolaika fee al'athabi muhdaroona

# 3426

Fasubhana Allahi heena tumsoona waheena tusbihoona

# 3427

Walahu alhamdu fee assamawati waalardi wa'ashiyyan waheena tuthhiroona

# 3428

Yukhriju alhayya mina almayyiti wayukhriju almayyita mina alhayyi wayuhyee alarda ba'da mawtiha wakathalika tukhrajoona

# 3429

Wamin ayatihi an khalaqakum min turabin thumma itha antum basharun tantashiroona

# 3430

Wamin ayatihi an khalaqa lakum min anfusikum azwajan litaskunoo ilayha waja'ala baynakum mawaddatan warahmatan inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaroona

# 3431

Wamin ayatihi khalqu assamawati waalardi waikhtilafu asinatikum waalwanikum inna fee thalika laayatin lil'alimeena

# 3432

Wamin ayatihi manamukum biallayli waannahari waibtighaokum min fadlihi inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yasma'oona

# 3433

Wamin ayatihi yureekumu albarqa khawfan watama'an wayunazzilu mina assamai maan fayuhyee bihi alarda ba'da mawtiha inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin ya'qiloona

# 3434

Wamin ayatihi an taqooma assamao waalardu biamrihi thumma itha da'akum da'watan mina alardi itha antum takhrujoona

# 3435

Walahu man fee assamawati waalardi kullun lahu qanitoona

# 3436

Wahuwa allathee yabdao alkhalqa thumma yu'eeduhu wahuwa ahwanu 'alayhi walahu almathalu ala'la fee assamawati waalardi wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 3437

Daraba lakum mathalan min anfusikum hal lakum mi mma malakat aymanukum min shurakaa fee ma razaqnakum faantum feehi sawaon takhafoonahum kakheefatikum anfusakum kathalika nufassilu alayati liqawmin ya'qiloona

# 3438

Bali ittaba'a allatheena thalamoo ahwaahum bighayri 'ilmin faman yahdee man adalla Allahu wama lahum min nasireena

# 3439

Faaqim wajhaka lilddeeni haneefan fitrata Allahi allatee fatara annasa 'alayha la tabdeela likhalqi Allahi thalika addeenu alqayyimu walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoona

# 3440

Muneebeena ilayhi waittaqoohu waaqeemoo assalata wala takoonoo mina almushrikeena

# 3441

Mina allatheena farraqoo deenahum wakanoo shiya'an kullu hizbin bima ladayhim farihoona

# 3442

Waitha massa annasa durrun da'aw rabbahum muneebeena ilayhi thumma itha athaqahum minhu rahmatan itha fareequn minhum birabbihim yushrikoona

# 3443

Liyakfuroo bima ataynahum fatamatta'oo fasawfa ta'lamoona

# 3444

Am anzana 'alayhim sultanan fahuwa yatakallamu bima kanoo bihi yushrikoona

# 3445

Waitha athaqna annasa rahmatan farihoo biha wain tusibhum sayyiatun bima qaddamat aydeehim itha hum yaqnatoona

# 3446

Awalam yaraw anna Allaha yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoona

# 3447

Faati tha alqurba haqqahu waalmiskeena waibna assabeeli thalika khayrun lillatheena yureedoona wajha Allahi waolaika humu almuflihoona

# 3448

Wama ataytum min riban liyarbuwa fee amwali annasi fala yarboo 'inda Allahi wama ataytum min zakatin tureedoona wajha Allahi faolaika humu almud'ifoona

# 3449

Allahu allathee khalaqakum thumma razaqakum thumma yumeetukum thumma yuhyeekum hal min shurakaikum man yaf'alu min thalikum min shayin subhanahu wata'ala 'amma yushrikoona

# 3450

Thahara alfasadu fee albarri waalbahri bima kasabat aydee annasi liyutheeqahum ba'da allathee 'amiloo la'allahum yarji'oona

# 3451

Qul seeroo fee alardi faonthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena min qablu kana aktharuhum mushrikeena

# 3452

Faaqim wajhaka lilddeeni alqayyimi min qabli an yatiya yawmun la maradda lahu mina Allahi yawmaithin yassadda'oona

# 3453

Man kafara fa'alayhi kufruhu waman 'amila salihan falianfusihim yamhadoona

# 3454

Liyajziya allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati min fadlihi innahu la yuhibbu alkafireena

# 3455

Wamin ayatihi an yursila arriyaha mubashshiratin waliyutheeqakum min rahmatihi walitajriya alfulku biamrihi walitabtaghoo min fadlihi wala'allakum tashkuroona

# 3456

Walaqad arsana min qablika rusulan ila qawmihim fajaoohum bialbayyinati faintaqamna mina allatheena ajramoo wakana haqqan 'alayna nasru almumineena

# 3457

Allahu allathee yursilu arriyaha fatutheeru sahaban fayabsutuhu fee assamai kayfa yashao wayaj'aluhu kisafan fatara alwadqa yakhruju min khilalihi faitha asaba bihi man yashao min 'ibadihi itha hum yastabshiroona

# 3458

Wain kanoo min qabli an yunazzala 'alayhim min qablihi lamubliseena

# 3459

Faonthur ila athari rahmati Allahi kayfa yuhyee alarda ba'da mawtiha inna thalika lamuhyee almawta wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 3460

Walain arsana reehan faraawhu musfarran lathalloo min ba'dihi yakfuroona

# 3461

Fainnaka la tusmi'u almawta wala tusmi'u assumma addu'aa itha wallaw mudbireena

# 3462

Wama anta bihadi al'umyi 'an dalalatihim in tusmi'u illa man yuminu biayatina fahum muslimoona

# 3463

Allahu allathee khalaqakum min da'fin thumma ja'ala min ba'di da'fin quwwatan thumma ja'ala min ba'di quwwatin da'fan washaybatan yakhluqu ma yashao wahuwa al'aleemu alqadeeru

# 3464

Wayawma taqoomu assa'atu yuqsimu almujrimoona ma labithoo ghayra sa'atin kathalika kanoo yufakoona

# 3465

Waqala allatheena ootoo al'ilma waaleemana laqad labithtum fee kitabi Allahi ila yawmi alba'thi fahatha yawmu alba'thi walakinnakum kuntum la ta'lamoona

# 3466

Fayawmaithin la yanfa'u allatheena thalamoo ma'thiratuhum wala hum yusta'taboona

# 3467

Walaqad darabna lilnnasi fee hatha alqurani min kulli mathalin walain jitahum biayatin layaqoolanna allatheena kafaroo in antum illa mubtiloona

# 3468

Kathalika yatba'u Allahu 'ala quloobi allatheena la ya'lamoona

# 3469

Faisbir inna wa'da Allahi haqqun wala yastakhiffannaka allatheena la yooqinoona

# 3470

Aliflammeem

# 3471

Tilka ayatu alkitabi alhakeemi

# 3472

Hudan warahmatan lilmuhsineena

# 3473

Allatheena yuqeemoona assalata wayutoona azzakata wahum bialakhirati hum yooqinoona

# 3474

Olaika 'ala hudan min rabbihim waolaika humu almuflihoona

# 3475

Wamina annasi man yashtaree lahwa alhadeethi liyudilla 'an sabeeli Allahi bighayri 'ilmin wayattakhithaha huzuwan olaika lahum 'athabun muheenun

# 3476

Waitha tutla 'alayhi ayatuna walla mustakbiran kaan lam yasma'ha kaanna fee othunayhi waqran fabashshirhu bi'athabin aleemin

# 3477

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati lahum jannatu anna'eemi

# 3478

Khalideena feeha wa'da Allahi haqqan wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 3479

Khalaqa assamawati bighayri 'amadin tarawnaha waalqa fee alardi rawasiya an tameeda bikum wabaththa feeha min kulli dabbatin waanzana mina assamai maan faanbatna feeha min kulli zawjin kareemin

# 3480

Hatha khalqu Allahi faaroonee matha khalaqa allatheena min doonihi bali aththalimoona fee dalalin mubeenin

# 3481

Walaqad atayna luqmana alhikmata ani oshkur lillahi waman yashkur fainnama yashkuru linafsihi waman kafara fainna Allaha ghaniyyun hameedun

# 3482

Waith qala luqmanu liibnihi wahuwa ya'ithuhu ya bunayya la tushrik biAllahi inna ashshirka lathulmun 'atheemun

# 3483

Wawassayna alinsana biwalidayhi hamalathu ommuhu wahnan 'ala wahnin wafisaluhu fee 'amayni ani oshkur lee waliwalidayka ilayya almaseeru

# 3484

Wain jahadaka 'ala an tushrika bee ma laysa laka bihi 'ilmun fala tuti'huma wasahibhuma fee addunya ma'roofan waittabi' sabeela man anaba ilayya thumma ilayya marji'ukum faonabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloona

# 3485

Ya bunayya innaha in taku mithqala habbatin min khardalin fatakun fee sakhratin aw fee assamawati aw fee alardi yati biha Allahu inna Allaha lateefun khabeerun

# 3486

Ya bunayya aqimi assalata wamur bialma'roofi wainha 'ani almunkari waisbir 'ala ma asabaka inna thalika min 'azmi alomoori

# 3487

Wala tusa''ir khaddaka lilnnasi wala tamshi fee alardi marahan inna Allaha la yuhibbu kulla mukhtalin fakhoorin

# 3488

Waiqsid fee mashyika waoghdud min sawtika inna ankara alaswati lasawtu alhameeri

# 3489

Alam taraw anna Allaha sakhkhara lakum ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi waasbagha 'alaykum ni'amahu thahiratan wabatinatan wamina annasi man yujadilu fee Allahi bighayri 'ilmin wala hudan wala kitabin muneerin

# 3490

Waitha qeela lahumu ittabi'oo ma anzala Allahu qaloo bal nattabi'u ma wajadna 'alayhi abaana awalaw kana ashshaytanu yad'oohum ila 'athabi assa'eeri

# 3491

Waman yuslim wajhahu ila Allahi wahuwa muhsinun faqadi istamsaka bial'urwati alwuthqa waila Allahi 'aqibatu alomoori

# 3492

Waman kafara fala yahzunka kufruhu ilayna marji'uhum fanunabbiohum bima 'amiloo inna Allaha 'aleemun bithati assudoori

# 3493

Numatti'uhum qaleelan thumma nadtarruhum ila 'athabin ghaleethin

# 3494

Walain saatahum man khalaqa assamawati waalarda layaqoolunna Allahu quli alhamdu lillahi bal aktharuhum la ya'lamoona

# 3495

Lillahi ma fee assamawati waalardi inna Allaha huwa alghaniyyu alhameedu

# 3496

Walaw annama fee alardi min shajaratin aqlamun waalbahru yamudduhu min ba'dihi sab'atu abhurin ma nafidat kalimatu Allahi inna Allaha 'azeezun hakeemun

# 3497

Ma khalqukum wala ba'thukum illa kanafsin wahidatin inna Allaha samee'un baseerun

# 3498

Alam tara anna Allaha yooliju allayla fee annahari wayooliju annahara fee allayli wasakhkhara ashshamsa waalqamara kullun yajree ila ajalin musamman waanna Allaha bima ta'maloona khabeerun

# 3499

Thalika bianna Allaha huwa alhaqqu waanna ma yad'oona min doonihi albatilu waanna Allaha huwa al'aliyyu alkabeeru

# 3500

Alam tara anna alfulka tajree fee albahri bini'mati Allahi liyuriyakum min ayatihi inna fee thalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakoorin

# 3501

Waitha ghashiyahum mawjun kaaththulali da'awoo Allaha mukhliseena lahu addeena falamma najjahum ila albarri faminhum muqtasidun wama yajhadu biayatina illa kullu khattarin kafoorin

# 3502

Ya ayyuha annasu ittaqoo rabbakum waikhshaw yawman la yajzee walidun 'an waladihi wala mawloodun huwa jazin 'an walidihi shayan inna wa'da Allahi haqqun fala taghurrannakumu alhayatu addunya wala yaghurrannakum biAllahi algharooru

# 3503

Inna Allaha 'indahu 'ilmu assa'ati wayunazzilu alghaytha waya'lamu ma fee alarhami wama tadree nafsun matha taksibu ghadan wama tadree nafsun biayyi ardin tamootu inna Allaha 'aleemun khabeerun

# 3504

Aliflammeem

# 3505

Tanzeelu alkitabi la rayba feehi min rabbi al'alameena

# 3506

Am yaqooloona iftarahu bal huwa alhaqqu min rabbika litunthira qawman ma atahum min natheerin min qablika la'allahum yahtadoona

# 3507

Allahu allathee khalaqa assamawati waalarda wama baynahuma fee sittati ayyamin thumma istawa 'ala al'arshi ma lakum min doonihi min waliyyin wala shafee'in afala tatathakkaroona

# 3508

Yudabbiru alamra mina assamai ila alardi thumma ya'ruju ilayhi fee yawmin kana miqdaruhu alfa sanatin mimma ta'uddoona

# 3509

Thalika 'alimu alghaybi waashshahadati al'azeezu arraheemu

# 3510

Allathee ahsana kulla shayin khalaqahu wabadaa khalqa alinsani min teenin

# 3511

Thumma ja'ala naslahu min sulalatin min main maheenin

# 3512

Thumma sawwahu wanafakha feehi min roohihi waja'ala lakumu assam'a waalabsara waalafidata qaleelan ma tashkuroona

# 3513

Waqaloo aitha dalana fee alardi ainna lafee khalqin jadeedin bal hum biliqai rabbihim kafiroona

# 3514

Qul yatawaffakum malaku almawti allathee wukkila bikum thumma ila rabbikum turja'oona

# 3515

Walaw tara ithi almujrimoona nakisoo ruoosihim 'inda rabbihim rabbana absarna wasami'na faarji'na na'mal salihan inna mooqinoona

# 3516

Walaw shina laatayna kulla nafsin hudaha walakin haqqa alqawlu minnee laamlaanna jahannama mina aljinnati waannasi ajma'eena

# 3517

Fathooqoo bima naseetum liqaa yawmikum hatha inna naseenakum wathooqoo 'athaba alkhuldi bima kuntum ta'maloona

# 3518

Innama yuminu biayatina allatheena itha thukkiroo biha kharroo sujjadan wasabbahoo bihamdi rabbihim wahum la yastakbiroona

# 3519

Tatajafa junoobuhum 'ani almadaji'i yad'oona rabbahum khawfan watama'an wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoona

# 3520

Fala ta'lamu nafsun ma okhfiya lahum min qurrati a'yunin jazaan bima kanoo ya'maloona

# 3521

Afaman kana muminan kaman kana fasiqan la yastawoona

# 3522

Amma allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati falahum jannatu almawa nuzulan bima kanoo ya'maloona

# 3523

Waamma allatheena fasaqoo famawahumu annaru kullama aradoo an yakhrujoo minha o'eedoo feeha waqeela lahum thooqoo 'athaba annari allathee kuntum bihi tukaththiboona

# 3524

Walanutheeqannahum mina al'athabi aladna doona al'athabi alakbari la'allahum yarji'oona

# 3525

Waman athlamu mimman thukkira biayati rabbihi thumma a'rada 'anha inna mina almujrimeena muntaqimoona

# 3526

Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba fala takun fee miryatin min liqaihi waja'anahu hudan libanee israeela

# 3527

Waja'ana minhum aimmatan yahdoona biamrina lamma sabaroo wakanoo biayatina yooqinoona

# 3528

Inna rabbaka huwa yafsilu baynahum yawma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi yakhtalifoona

# 3529

Awalam yahdi lahum kam ahlakna min qablihim mina alqurooni yamshoona fee masakinihim inna fee thalika laayatin afala yasma'oona

# 3530

Awalam yaraw anna nasooqu almaa ila alardi aljuruzi fanukhriju bihi zar'an takulu minhu an'amuhum waanfusuhum afala yubsiroona

# 3531

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alfathu in kuntum sadiqeena

# 3532

Qul yawma alfathi la yanfa'u allatheena kafaroo eemanuhum wala hum yuntharoona

# 3533

Faa'rid 'anhum waintathir innahum muntathiroona

# 3534

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu ittaqi Allaha wala tuti'i alkafireena waalmunafiqeena inna Allaha kana 'aleeman hakeeman

# 3535

Waittabi' ma yooha ilayka min rabbika inna Allaha kana bima ta'maloona khabeeran

# 3536

Watawakkal 'ala Allahi wakafa biAllahi wakeelan

# 3537

Ma ja'ala Allahu lirajulin min qalbayni fee jawfihi wama ja'ala azwajakumu allaee tuthahiroona minhunna ommahatikum wama ja'ala ad'iyaakum abnaakum thalikum qawlukum biafwahikum waAllahu yaqoolu alhaqqa wahuwa yahdee assabeela

# 3538

Od'oohum liabaihim huwa aqsatu 'inda Allahi fain lam ta'lamoo abaahum faikhwanukum fee addeeni wamawaleekum walaysa 'alaykum junahun feema akhtatum bihi walakin ma ta'ammadat quloobukum wakana Allahu ghafooran raheeman

# 3539

annabiyyu awla bialmumineena min anfusihim waazwajuhu ommahatuhum waoloo alarhami ba'duhum awla biba'din fee kitabi Allahi mina almumineena waalmuhajireena illa an taf'aloo ila awliyaikum ma'roofan kana thalika fee alkitabi mastooran

# 3540

Waith akhathna mina annabiyyeena meethaqahum waminka wamin noohin waibraheema wamoosa wa'eesa ibni maryama waakhathna minhum meethaqan ghaleethan

# 3541

Liyasala assadiqeena 'an sidqihim waa'adda lilkafireena 'athaban aleeman

# 3542

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo othkuroo ni'mata Allahi 'alaykum ith jaatkum junoodun faarsana 'alayhim reehan wajunoodan lam tarawha wakana Allahu bima ta'maloona baseeran

# 3543

Ith jaookum min fawqikum wamin asfala minkum waith zaghati alabsaru wabalaghati alquloobu alhanajira watathunnoona biAllahi aththunoona

# 3544

Hunalika ibtuliya almuminoona wazulziloo zilzalan shadeedan

# 3545

Waith yaqoolu almunafiqoona waallatheena fee quloobihim maradun ma wa'adana Allahu warasooluhu illa ghurooran

# 3546

Waith qalat taifatun minhum ya ahla yathriba la muqama lakum fairji'oo wayastathinu fareequn minhumu annabiyya yaqooloona inna buyootana 'awratun wama hiya bi'awratin in yureedoona illa firaran

# 3547

Walaw dukhilat 'alayhim min aqtariha thumma suiloo alfitnata laatawha wama talabbathoo biha illa yaseeran

# 3548

Walaqad kanoo 'ahadoo Allaha min qablu la yuwalloona aladbara wakana 'ahdu Allahi masoolan

# 3549

Qul lan yanfa'akumu alfiraru in farartum mina almawti awi alqatli waithan la tumatta'oona illa qaleelan

# 3550

Qul man tha allathee ya'simukum mina Allahi in arada bikum sooan aw arada bikum rahmatan wala yajidoona lahum min dooni Allahi waliyyan wala naseeran

# 3551

Qad ya'lamu Allahu almu'awwiqeena minkum waalqaileena liikhwanihim halumma ilayna wala yatoona albasa illa qaleelan

# 3552

Ashihhatan 'alaykum faitha jaa alkhawfu raaytahum yanthuroona ilayka tadooru a'yunuhum kaallathee yughsha 'alayhi mina almawti faitha thahaba alkhawfu salaqookum biasinatin hidadin ashihhatan 'ala alkhayri olaika lam yuminoo faahbata Allahu a'malahum wakana thalika 'ala Allahi yaseeran

# 3553

Yahsaboona alahzaba lam yathhaboo wain yati alahzabu yawaddoo law annahum badoona fee ala'rabi yasaloona 'an anbaikum walaw kanoo feekum ma qataloo illa qaleelan

# 3554

Laqad kana lakum fee rasooli Allahi oswatun hasanatun liman kana yarjoo Allaha waalyawma alakhira wathakara Allaha katheeran

# 3555

Walamma raa almuminoona alahzaba qaloo hatha ma wa'adana Allahu warasooluhu wasadaqa Allahu warasooluhu wama zadahum illa eemanan watasleeman

# 3556

Mina almumineena rijalun sadaqoo ma 'ahadoo Allaha 'alayhi faminhum man qada nahbahu waminhum man yantathiru wama baddaloo tabdeelan

# 3557

Liyajziya Allahu assadiqeena bisidqihim wayu'aththiba almunafiqeena in shaa aw yatooba 'alayhim inna Allaha kana ghafooran raheeman

# 3558

Waradda Allahu allatheena kafaroo bighaythihim lam yanaloo khayran wakafa Allahu almumineena alqitala wakana Allahu qawiyyan 'azeezan

# 3559

Waanzala allatheena thaharoohum min ahli alkitabi min sayaseehim waqathafa fee quloobihimu arru'ba fareeqan taqtuloona watasiroona fareeqan

# 3560

Waawrathakum ardahum wadiyarahum waamwalahum waardan lam tataooha wakana Allahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeeran

# 3561

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu qul liazwajika in kuntunna turidna alhayata addunya wazeenataha fata'alayna omatti'kunna waosarrihkunna sarahan jameelan

# 3562

Wain kuntunna turidna Allaha warasoolahu waaddara alakhirata fainna Allaha a'adda lilmuhsinati minkunna ajran 'atheeman

# 3563

Ya nisaa annabiyyi man yati minkunna bifahishatin mubayyinatin yuda'af laha al'athabu di'fayni wakana thalika 'ala Allahi yaseeran

# 3564

Waman yaqnut minkunna lillahi warasoolihi wata'mal salihan nutiha ajraha marratayni waa'tadna laha rizqan kareeman

# 3565

Ya nisaa annabiyyi lastunna kaahadin mina annisai ini ittaqaytunna fala takhda'na bialqawli fayatma'a allathee fee qalbihi maradun waqulna qawlan ma'roofan

# 3566

Waqarna fee buyootikunna wala tabarrajna tabarruja aljahiliyyati aloola waaqimna assalata waateena azzakata waati'na Allaha warasoolahu innama yureedu Allahu liyuthhiba 'ankumu arrijsa ahla albayti wayutahhirakum tatheeran

# 3567

Waothkurna ma yutla fee buyootikunna min ayati Allahi waalhikmati inna Allaha kana lateefan khabeeran

# 3568

Inna almuslimeena waalmuslimati waalmumineena waalmuminati waalqaniteena waalqanitati waassadiqeena waassadiqati waassabireena waassabirati waalkhashi'eena waalkhashi'ati waalmutasaddiqeena waalmutasaddiqati waassaimeena waassaimati waalhafitheena furoojahum waalhafithati waaththakireena Allaha katheeran waaththakirati a'adda Allahu lahum maghfiratan waajran 'atheeman

# 3569

Wama kana limuminin wala muminatin itha qada Allahu warasooluhu amran an yakoona lahumu alkhiyaratu min amrihim waman ya'si Allaha warasoolahu faqad dalla dalalan mubeenan

# 3570

Waith taqoolu lillathee an'ama Allahu 'alayhi waan'amta 'alayhi amsik 'alayka zawjaka waittaqi Allaha watukhfee fee nafsika ma Allahu mubdeehi watakhsha annasa waAllahu ahaqqu an takhshahu falamma qada zaydun minha wataran zawwajnakaha likay la yakoona 'ala almumineena harajun fee azwaji ad'iyaihim itha qadaw minhunna wataran wakana amru Allahi maf'oolan

# 3571

Ma kana 'ala annabiyyi min harajin feema farada Allahu lahu sunnata Allahi fee allatheena khalaw min qablu wakana amru Allahi qadaran maqdooran

# 3572

Allatheena yuballighoona risalati Allahi wayakhshawnahu wala yakhshawna ahadan illa Allaha wakafa biAllahi haseeban

# 3573

Ma kana muhammadun aba ahadin min rijalikum walakin rasoola Allahi wakhatama annabiyyeena wakana Allahu bikulli shayin 'aleeman

# 3574

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo othkuroo Allaha thikran katheeran

# 3575

Wasabbihoohu bukratan waaseelan

# 3576

Huwa allathee yusallee 'alaykum wamalaikatuhu liyukhrijakum mina aththulumati ila annoori wakana bialmumineena raheeman

# 3577

Tahiyyatuhum yawma yalqawnahu salamun waa'adda lahum ajran kareeman

# 3578

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu inna arsanaka shahidan wamubashshiran wanatheeran

# 3579

Wada'iyan ila Allahi biithnihi wasirajan muneeran

# 3580

Wabashshiri almumineena bianna lahum mina Allahi fadlan kabeeran

# 3581

Wala tuti'i alkafireena waalmunafiqeena wada' athahum watawakkal 'ala Allahi wakafa biAllahi wakeelan

# 3582

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha nakahtumu almuminati thumma tallaqtumoohunna min qabli an tamassoohunna fama lakum 'alayhinna min 'iddatin ta'taddoonaha famatti'oohunna wasarrihoohunna sarahan jameelan

# 3583

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu inna ahlana laka azwajaka allatee atayta ojoorahunna wama malakat yameenuka mimma afaa Allahu 'alayka wabanati 'ammika wabanati 'ammatika wabanati khalika wabanati khalatika allatee hajarna ma'aka waimraatan muminatan in wahabat nafsaha lilnnabiyyi in arada annabiyyu an yastankihaha khalisatan laka min dooni almumineena qad 'alimna ma faradna 'alayhim fee azwajihim wama malakat aymanuhum likayla yakoona 'alayka harajun wakana Allahu ghafooran raheeman

# 3584

Turjee man tashao minhunna watuwee ilayka man tashao wamani ibtaghayta mimman 'azata fala junaha 'alayka thalika adna an taqarra a'yunuhunna wala yahzanna wayardayna bima ataytahunna kulluhunna waAllahu ya'lamu ma fee quloobikum wakana Allahu 'aleeman haleeman

# 3585

La yahillu laka annisao min ba'du wala an tabaddala bihinna min azwajin walaw a'jabaka husnuhunna illa ma malakat yameenuka wakana Allahu 'ala kulli shayin raqeeban

# 3586

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tadkhuloo buyoota annabiyyi illa an yuthana lakum ila ta'amin ghayra nathireena inahu walakin itha du'eetum faodkhuloo faitha ta'imtum faintashiroo wala mustaniseena lihadeethin inna thalikum kana yuthee annabiyya fayastahyee minkum waAllahu la yastahyee mina alhaqqi waitha saatumoohunna mata'an faisaloohunna min warai hijabin thalikum atharu liquloobikum waquloobihinna wama kana lakum an tuthoo rasoola Allahi wala an tankihoo azwajahu min ba'dihi abadan inna thalikum kana 'inda Allahi 'atheeman

# 3587

In tubdoo shayan aw tukhfoohu fainna Allaha kana bikulli shayin 'aleeman

# 3588

La junaha 'alayhinna fee abaihinna wala abnaihinna wala ikhwanihinna wala abnai ikhwanihinna wala abnai akhawatihinna wala nisaihinna wala ma malakat aymanuhunna waittaqeena Allaha inna Allaha kana 'ala kulli shayin shaheedan

# 3589

Inna Allaha wamalaikatahu yusalloona 'ala annabiyyi ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo salloo 'alayhi wasallimoo tasleeman

# 3590

Inna allatheena yuthoona Allaha warasoolahu la'anahumu Allahu fee addunya waalakhirati waa'adda lahum 'athaban muheenan

# 3591

Waallatheena yuthoona almumineena waalmuminati bighayri ma iktasaboo faqadi ihtamaloo buhtanan waithman mubeenan

# 3592

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu qul liazwajika wabanatika wanisai almumineena yudneena 'alayhinna min jalabeebihinna thalika adna an yu'rafna fala yuthayna wakana Allahu ghafooran raheeman

# 3593

Lain lam yantahi almunafiqoona waallatheena fee quloobihim maradun waalmurjifoona fee almadeenati lanughriyannaka bihim thumma la yujawiroonaka feeha illa qaleelan

# 3594

Mal'ooneena aynama thuqifoo okhithoo waquttiloo taqteelan

# 3595

Sunnata Allahi fee allatheena khalaw min qablu walan tajida lisunnati Allahi tabdeelan

# 3596

Yasaluka annasu 'ani assa'ati qul innama 'ilmuha 'inda Allahi wama yudreeka la'alla assa'ata takoonu qareeban

# 3597

Inna Allaha la'ana alkafireena waa'adda lahum sa'eeran

# 3598

Khalideena feeha abadan la yajidoona waliyyan wala naseeran

# 3599

Yawma tuqallabu wujoohuhum fee annari yaqooloona ya laytana ata'na Allaha waata'na arrasoola

# 3600

Waqaloo rabbana inna ata'na sadatana wakubaraana faadalloona assabeela

# 3601

Rabbana atihim di'fayni mina al'athabi wail'anhum la'nan kabeeran

# 3602

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la takoonoo kaallatheena athaw moosa fabarraahu Allahu mimma qaloo wakana 'inda Allahi wajeehan

# 3603

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha waqooloo qawlan sadeedan

# 3604

Yuslih lakum a'malakum wayaghfir lakum thunoobakum waman yuti'i Allaha warasoolahu faqad faza fawzan 'atheeman

# 3605

Inna 'aradna alamanata 'ala assamawati waalardi waaljibali faabayna an yahmilnaha waashfaqna minha wahamalaha alinsanu innahu kana thalooman jahoolan

# 3606

Liyu'aththiba Allahu almunafiqeena waalmunafiqati waalmushrikeena waalmushrikati wayatooba Allahu 'ala almumineena waalmuminati wakana Allahu ghafooran raheeman

# 3607

Alhamdu lillahi allathee lahu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi walahu alhamdu fee alakhirati wahuwa alhakeemu alkhabeeru

# 3608

Ya'lamu ma yaliju fee alardi wama yakhruju minha wama yanzilu mina assamai wama ya'ruju feeha wahuwa arraheemu alghafooru

# 3609

Waqala allatheena kafaroo la tateena assa'atu qul bala warabbee latatiyannakum 'alimi alghaybi la ya'zubu 'anhu mithqalu tharratin fee assamawati wala fee alardi wala asgharu min thalika wala akbaru illa fee kitabin mubeenin

# 3610

Liyajziya allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati olaika lahum maghfiratun warizqun kareemun

# 3611

Waallatheena sa'aw fee ayatina mu'ajizeena olaika lahum 'athabun min rijzin aleemin

# 3612

Wayara allatheena ootoo al'ilma allathee onzila ilayka min rabbika huwa alhaqqa wayahdee ila sirati al'azeezi alhameedi

# 3613

Waqala allatheena kafaroo hal nadullukum 'ala rajulin yunabbiokum itha muzziqtum kulla mumazzaqin innakum lafee khalqin jadeedin

# 3614

Aftara 'ala Allahi kathiban am bihi jinnatun bali allatheena la yuminoona bialakhirati fee al'athabi waaddalali alba'eedi

# 3615

Afalam yaraw ila ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum mina assamai waalardi in nasha nakhsif bihimu alarda aw nusqit 'alayhim kisafan mina assamai inna fee thalika laayatan likulli 'abdin muneebin

# 3616

Walaqad atayna dawooda minna fadlan ya jibalu awwibee ma'ahu waattayra waalanna lahu alhadeeda

# 3617

Ani i'mal sabighatin waqaddir fee assardi wai'maloo salihan innee bima ta'maloona baseerun

# 3618

Walisulaymana arreeha ghuduwwuha shahrun warawahuha shahrun waasana lahu 'ayna alqitri wamina aljinni man ya'malu bayna yadayhi biithni rabbihi waman yazigh minhum 'an amrina nuthiqhu min 'athabi assa'eeri

# 3619

Ya'maloona lahu ma yashao min mahareeba watamatheela wajifanin kaaljawabi waqudoorin rasiyatin i'maloo ala dawooda shukran waqaleelun min 'ibadiya ashshakooru

# 3620

Falamma qadayna 'alayhi almawta ma dallahum 'ala mawtihi illa dabbatu alardi takulu minsaatahu falamma kharra tabayyanati aljinnu an law kanoo ya'lamoona alghayba ma labithoo fee al'athabi almuheeni

# 3621

Laqad kana lisabain fee maskanihim ayatun jannatani 'an yameenin washimalin kuloo min rizqi rabbikum waoshkuroo lahu badatun tayyibatun warabbun ghafoorun

# 3622

Faa'radoo faarsana 'alayhim sayla al'arimi wabaddanahum bijannatayhim jannatayni thawatay okulin khamtin waathlin washayin min sidrin qaleelin

# 3623

Thalika jazaynahum bima kafaroo wahal nujazee illa alkafoora

# 3624

Waja'ana baynahum wabayna alqura allatee barakna feeha quran thahiratan waqaddarna feeha assayra seeroo feeha layaliya waayyaman amineena

# 3625

Faqaloo rabbana ba'id bayna asfarina wathalamoo anfusahum faja'anahum ahadeetha wamazzaqnahum kulla mumazzaqin inna fee thalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakoorin

# 3626

Walaqad saddaqa 'alayhim ibleesu thannahu faittaba'oohu illa fareeqan mina almumineena

# 3627

Wama kana lahu 'alayhim min sultanin illa lina'lama man yuminu bialakhirati mimman huwa minha fee shakkin warabbuka 'ala kulli shayin hafeethun

# 3628

Quli od'oo allatheena za'amtum min dooni Allahi la yamlikoona mithqala tharratin fee assamawati wala fee alardi wama lahum feehima min shirkin wama lahu minhum min thaheerin

# 3629

Wala tanfa'u ashshafa'atu 'indahu illa liman athina lahu hatta itha fuzzi'a 'an quloobihim qaloo matha qala rabbukum qaloo alhaqqa wahuwa al'aliyyu alkabeeru

# 3630

Qul man yarzuqukum mina assamawati waalardi quli Allahu wainna aw iyyakum la'ala hudan aw fee dalalin mubeenin

# 3631

Qul la tusaloona 'amma ajramna wala nusalu 'amma ta'maloona

# 3632

Qul yajma'u baynana rabbuna thumma yaftahu baynana bialhaqqi wahuwa alfattahu al'aleemu

# 3633

Qul arooniya allatheena alhaqtum bihi shurakaa kalla bal huwa Allahu al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 3634

Wama arsanaka illa kaffatan lilnnasi basheeran wanatheeran walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoona

# 3635

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwa'du in kuntum sadiqeena

# 3636

Qul lakum mee'adu yawmin la tastakhiroona 'anhu sa'atan wala tastaqdimoona

# 3637

Waqala allatheena kafaroo lan numina bihatha alqurani wala biallathee bayna yadayhi walaw tara ithi aththalimoona mawqoofoona 'inda rabbihim yarji'u ba'duhum ila ba'din alqawla yaqoolu allatheena istud'ifoo lillatheena istakbaroo lawla antum lakunna mumineena

# 3638

Qala allatheena istakbaroo lillatheena istud'ifoo anahnu sadadnakum 'ani alhuda ba'da ith jaakum bal kuntum mujrimeena

# 3639

Waqala allatheena istud'ifoo lillatheena istakbaroo bal makru allayli waannahari ith tamuroonana an nakfura biAllahi wanaj'ala lahu andadan waasarroo annadamata lamma raawoo al'athaba waja'ana alaghlala fee a'naqi allatheena kafaroo hal yujzawna illa ma kanoo ya'maloona

# 3640

Wama arsana fee qaryatin min natheerin illa qala mutrafooha inna bima orsiltum bihi kafiroona

# 3641

Waqaloo nahnu aktharu amwalan waawladan wama nahnu bimu'aththabeena

# 3642

Qul inna rabbee yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoona

# 3643

Wama amwalukum wala awladukum biallatee tuqarribukum 'indana zulfa illa man amana wa'amila salihan faolaika lahum jazao addi'fi bima 'amiloo wahum fee alghurufati aminoona

# 3644

Waallatheena yas'awna fee ayatina mu'ajizeena olaika fee al'athabi muhdaroona

# 3645

Qul inna rabbee yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao min 'ibadihi wayaqdiru lahu wama anfaqtum min shayin fahuwa yukhlifuhu wahuwa khayru arraziqeena

# 3646

Wayawma yahshuruhum jamee'an thumma yaqoolu lilmalaikati ahaolai iyyakum kanoo ya'budoona

# 3647

Qaloo subhanaka anta waliyyuna min doonihim bal kanoo ya'budoona aljinna aktharuhum bihim muminoona

# 3648

Faalyawma la yamliku ba'dukum liba'din naf'an wala darran wanaqoolu lillatheena thalamoo thooqoo 'athaba annari allatee kuntum biha tukaththiboona

# 3649

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna bayyinatin qaloo ma hatha illa rajulun yureedu an yasuddakum 'amma kana ya'budu abaokum waqaloo ma hatha illa ifkun muftaran waqala allatheena kafaroo lilhaqqi lamma jaahum in hatha illa sihrun mubeenun

# 3650

Wama ataynahum min kutubin yadrusoonaha wama arsana ilayhim qablaka min natheerin

# 3651

Wakaththaba allatheena min qablihim wama balaghoo mi'shara ma ataynahum fakaththaboo rusulee fakayfa kana nakeeri

# 3652

Qul innama a'ithukum biwahidatin an taqoomoo lillahi mathna wafurada thumma tatafakkaroo ma bisahibikum min jinnatin in huwa illa natheerun lakum bayna yaday 'athabin shadeedin

# 3653

Qul ma saatukum min ajrin fahuwa lakum in ajriya illa 'ala Allahi wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin shaheedun

# 3654

Qul inna rabbee yaqthifu bialhaqqi 'allamu alghuyoobi

# 3655

Qul jaa alhaqqu wama yubdio albatilu wama yu'eedu

# 3656

Qul in dalatu fainnama adillu 'ala nafsee waini ihtadaytu fabima yoohee ilayya rabbee innahu samee'un qareebun

# 3657

Walaw tara ith fazi'oo fala fawta waokhithoo min makanin qareebin

# 3658

Waqaloo amanna bihi waanna lahumu attanawushu min makanin ba'eedin

# 3659

Waqad kafaroo bihi min qablu wayaqthifoona bialghaybi min makanin ba'eedin

# 3660

Waheela baynahum wabayna ma yashtahoona kama fu'ila biashya'ihim min qablu innahum kanoo fee shakkin mureebin

# 3661

Alhamdu lillahi fatiri assamawati waalardi ja'ili almalaikati rusulan olee ajnihatin mathna wathulatha waruba'a yazeedu fee alkhalqi ma yashao inna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 3662

Ma yaftahi Allahu lilnnasi min rahmatin fala mumsika laha wama yumsik fala mursila lahu min ba'dihi wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 3663

Ya ayyuha annasu othkuroo ni'mata Allahi 'alaykum hal min khaliqin ghayru Allahi yarzuqukum mina assamai waalardi la ilaha illa huwa faanna tufakoona

# 3664

Wain yukaththibooka faqad kuththibat rusulun min qablika waila Allahi turja'u alomooru

# 3665

Ya ayyuha annasu inna wa'da Allahi haqqun fala taghurrannakumu alhayatu addunya wala yaghurrannakum biAllahi algharooru

# 3666

Inna ashshaytana lakum 'aduwwun faittakhithoohu 'aduwwan innama yad'oo hizbahu liyakoonoo min ashabi assa'eeri

# 3667

Allatheena kafaroo lahum 'athabun shadeedun waallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati lahum maghfiratun waajrun kabeerun

# 3668

Afaman zuyyina lahu sooo 'amalihi faraahu hasanan fainna Allaha yudillu man yashao wayahdee man yashao fala tathhab nafsuka 'alayhim hasaratin inna Allaha 'aleemun bima yasna'oona

# 3669

WaAllahu allathee arsala arriyaha fatutheeru sahaban fasuqnahu ila baladin mayyitin faahyayna bihi alarda ba'da mawtiha kathalika annushooru

# 3670

Man kana yureedu al'izzata falillahi al'izzatu jamee'an ilayhi yas'adu alkalimu attayyibu waal'amalu assalihu yarfa'uhu waallatheena yamkuroona assayyiati lahum 'athabun shadeedun wamakru olaika huwa yabooru

# 3671

WaAllahu khalaqakum min turabin thumma min nutfatin thumma ja'alakum azwajan wama tahmilu min ontha wala tada'u illa bi'ilmihi wama yu'ammaru min mu'ammarin wala yunqasu min 'umurihi illa fee kitabin inna thalika 'ala Allahi yaseerun

# 3672

Wama yastawee albahrani hatha 'athbun furatun saighun sharabuhu wahatha milhun ojajun wamin kullin takuloona lahman tariyyan watastakhrijoona hilyatan talbasoonaha watara alfulka feehi mawakhira litabtaghoo min fadlihi wala'allakum tashkuroona

# 3673

Yooliju allayla fee annahari wayooliju annahara fee allayli wasakhkhara ashshamsa waalqamara kullun yajree liajalin musamman thalikumu Allahu rabbukum lahu almulku waallatheena tad'oona min doonihi ma yamlikoona min qitmeerin

# 3674

In tad'oohum la yasma'oo du'aakum walaw sami'oo ma istajaboo lakum wayawma alqiyamati yakfuroona bishirkikum wala yunabbioka mithlu khabeerin

# 3675

Ya ayyuha annasu antumu alfuqarao ila Allahi waAllahu huwa alghaniyyu alhameedu

# 3676

In yasha yuthhibkum wayati bikhalqin jadeedin

# 3677

Wama thalika 'ala Allahi bi'azeezin

# 3678

Wala taziru waziratun wizra okhra wain tad'u muthqalatun ila himliha la yuhmal minhu shayon walaw kana tha qurba innama tunthiru allatheena yakhshawna rabbahum bialghaybi waaqamoo assalata waman tazakka fainnama yatazakka linafsihi waila Allahi almaseeru

# 3679

Wama yastawee ala'ma waalbaseeru

# 3680

Wala aththulumatu wala annooru

# 3681

Wala aththillu wala alharooru

# 3682

Wama yastawee alahyao wala alamwatu inna Allaha yusmi'u man yashao wama anta bimusmi'in man fee alquboori

# 3683

In anta illa natheerun

# 3684

Inna arsanaka bialhaqqi basheeran wanatheeran wain min ommatin illa khala feeha natheerun

# 3685

Wain yukaththibooka faqad kaththaba allatheena min qablihim jaathum rusuluhum bialbayyinati wabiazzuburi wabialkitabi almuneeri

# 3686

Thumma akhathtu allatheena kafaroo fakayfa kana nakeeri

# 3687

Alam tara anna Allaha anzala mina assamai maan faakhrajna bihi thamaratin mukhtalifan alwanuha wamina aljibali judadun beedun wahumrun mukhtalifun alwanuha wagharabeebu soodun

# 3688

Wamina annasi waaddawabbi waalan'ami mukhtalifun alwanuhu kathalika innama yakhsha Allaha min 'ibadihi al'ulamao inna Allaha 'azeezun ghafoorun

# 3689

Inna allatheena yatloona kitaba Allahi waaqamoo assalata waanfaqoo mimma razaqnahum sirran wa'alaniyatan yarjoona tijaratan lan taboora

# 3690

Liyuwaffiyahum ojoorahum wayazeedahum min fadlihi innahu ghafoorun shakoorun

# 3691

Waallathee awhayna ilayka mina alkitabi huwa alhaqqu musaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi inna Allaha bi'ibadihi lakhabeerun baseerun

# 3692

Thumma awrathna alkitaba allatheena istafayna min 'ibadina faminhum thalimun linafsihi waminhum muqtasidun waminhum sabiqun bialkhayrati biithni Allahi thalika huwa alfadlu alkabeeru

# 3693

Jannatu 'adnin yadkhuloonaha yuhallawna feeha min asawira min thahabin waluluan walibasuhum feeha hareerun

# 3694

Waqaloo alhamdu lillahi allathee athhaba 'anna alhazana inna rabbana laghafoorun shakoorun

# 3695

Allathee ahallana dara almuqamati min fadlihi la yamassuna feeha nasabun wala yamassuna feeha lughoobun

# 3696

Waallatheena kafaroo lahum naru jahannama la yuqda 'alayhim fayamootoo wala yukhaffafu 'anhum min 'athabiha kathalika najzee kulla kafoorin

# 3697

Wahum yastarikhoona feeha rabbana akhrijna na'mal salihan ghayra allathee kunna na'malu awalam nu'ammirkum ma yatathakkaru feehi man tathakkara wajaakumu annatheeru fathooqoo fama lilththalimeena min naseerin

# 3698

Inna Allaha 'alimu ghaybi assamawati waalardi innahu 'aleemun bithati assudoori

# 3699

Huwa allathee ja'alakum khalaifa fee alardi faman kafara fa'alayhi kufruhu wala yazeedu alkafireena kufruhum 'inda rabbihim illa maqtan wala yazeedu alkafireena kufruhum illa khasaran

# 3700

Qul araaytum shurakaakumu allatheena tad'oona min dooni Allahi aroonee matha khalaqoo mina alardi am lahum shirkun fee assamawati am ataynahum kitaban fahum 'ala bayyinatin minhu bal in ya'idu aththalimoona ba'duhum ba'dan illa ghurooran

# 3701

Inna Allaha yumsiku assamawati waalarda an tazoola walain zalata in amsakahuma min ahadin min ba'dihi innahu kana haleeman ghafooran

# 3702

# 3703

# 3704
