Inna hatha akhee lahu tis'un watis'oona na'jatan waliya na'jatun wahidatun faqala akfilneeha wa'azzanee fee alkhitabi

# 3994

Qala laqad thalamaka bisuali na'jatika ila ni'ajihi wainna katheeran mina alkhulatai layabghee ba'duhum 'ala ba'din illa allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati waqaleelun ma hum wathanna dawoodu annama fatannahu faistaghfara rabbahu wakharra raki'an waanaba

# 3995

Faghafarna lahu thalika wainna lahu 'indana lazulfa wahusna maabin

# 3996

Ya dawoodu inna ja'anaka khaleefatan fee alardi faohkum bayna annasi bialhaqqi wala tattabi'i alhawa fayudillaka 'an sabeeli Allahi inna allatheena yadilloona 'an sabeeli Allahi lahum 'athabun shadeedun bima nasoo yawma alhisabi

# 3997

Wama khalaqna assamaa waalarda wama baynahuma batilan thalika thannu allatheena kafaroo fawaylun lillatheena kafaroo mina annari

# 3998

Am naj'alu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati kaalmufsideena fee alardi am naj'alu almuttaqeena kaalfujjari

# 3999

Kitabun anzanahu ilayka mubarakun liyaddabbaroo ayatihi waliyatathakkara oloo alalbabi

# 4000

Wawahabna lidawooda sulaymana ni'ma al'abdu innahu awwabun

# 4001

Ith 'urida 'alayhi bial'ashiyyi assafinatu aljiyadu

# 4002

Faqala innee ahbabtu hubba alkhayri 'an thikri rabbee hatta tawarat bialhijabi

# 4003

Ruddooha 'alayya fatafiqa mashan biassooqi waala'naqi

# 4004

Walaqad fatanna sulaymana waalqayna 'ala kursiyyihi jasadan thumma anaba

# 4005

Qala rabbi ighfir lee wahab lee mulkan la yanbaghee liahadin min ba'dee innaka anta alwahhabu

# 4006

Fasakhkharna lahu arreeha tajree biamrihi rukhaan haythu asaba

# 4007

Waashshayateena kulla bannain waghawwasin

# 4008

Waakhareena muqarraneena fee alasfadi

# 4009

Hatha 'ataona faomnun aw amsik bighayri hisabin

# 4010

Wainna lahu 'indana lazulfa wahusna maabin

# 4011

Waothkur 'abdana ayyooba ith nada rabbahu annee massaniya ashshaytanu binusbin wa'athabin

# 4012

Orkud birijlika hatha mughtasalun baridun washarabun

# 4013

Wawahabna lahu ahlahu wamithlahum ma'ahum rahmatan minna wathikra liolee alalbabi

# 4014

Wakhuth biyadika dighthan faidrib bihi wala tahnath inna wajadnahu sabiran ni'ma al'abdu innahu awwabun

# 4015

Waothkur 'ibadana ibraheema waishaqa waya'qooba olee alaydee waalabsari

# 4016

Inna akhlasnahum bikhalisatin thikra addari

# 4017

Wainnahum 'indana lamina almustafayna alakhyari

# 4018

Waothkur isma'eela wailyasa'a watha alkifli wakullun mina alakhyari

# 4019

Hatha thikrun wainna lilmuttaqeena lahusna maabin

# 4020

Jannati 'adnin mufattahatan lahumu alabwabu

# 4021

Muttakieena feeha yad'oona feeha bifakihatin katheeratin washarabin

# 4022

Wa'indahum qasiratu attarfi atrabun

# 4023

Hatha ma too'adoona liyawmi alhisabi

# 4024

Inna hatha larizquna ma lahu min nafadin

# 4025

Hatha wainna lilttagheena lasharra maabin

# 4026

Jahannama yaslawnaha fabisa almihadu

# 4027

Hatha falyathooqoohu hameemun waghassaqun

# 4028

Waakharu min shaklihi azwajun

# 4029

Hatha fawjun muqtahimun ma'akum la marhaban bihim innahum saloo annari

# 4030

Qaloo bal antum la marhaban bikum antum qaddamtumoohu lana fabisa alqararu

# 4031

Qaloo rabbana man qaddama lana hatha fazidhu 'athaban di'fan fee annari

# 4032

Waqaloo ma lana la nara rijalan kunna na'udduhum mina alashrari

# 4033

Attakhathnahum sikhriyyan am zaghat 'anhumu alabsaru

# 4034

Inna thalika lahaqqun takhasumu ahli annari

# 4035

Qul innama ana munthirun wama min ilahin illa Allahu alwahidu alqahharu

# 4036

Rabbu assamawati waalardi wama baynahuma al'azeezu alghaffaru

# 4037

Qul huwa nabaon 'atheemun

# 4038

Antum 'anhu mu'ridoona

# 4039

Ma kana liya min 'ilmin bialmalai ala'la ith yakhtasimoona

# 4040

In yooha ilayya illa annama ana natheerun mubeenun

# 4041

Ith qala rabbuka lilmalaikati innee khaliqun basharan min teenin

# 4042

Faitha sawwaytuhu wanafakhtu feehi min roohee faqa'oo lahu sajideena

# 4043

Fasajada almalaikatu kulluhum ajma'oona

# 4044

Illa ibleesa istakbara wakana mina alkafireena

# 4045

Qala ya ibleesu ma mana'aka an tasjuda lima khalaqtu biyadayya astakbarta am kunta mina al'aleena

# 4046

Qala ana khayrun minhu khalaqtanee min narin wakhalaqtahu min teenin

# 4047

Qala faokhruj minha fainnaka rajeemun

# 4048

Wainna 'alayka la'natee ila yawmi addeeni

# 4049

Qala rabbi faanthirnee ila yawmi yub'athoona

# 4050

Qala fainnaka mina almunthareena

# 4051

Ila yawmi alwaqti alma'loomi

# 4052

Qala fabi'izzatika laoghwiyannahum ajma'eena

# 4053

Illa 'ibadaka minhumu almukhlaseena

# 4054

Qala faalhaqqu waalhaqqa aqoolu

# 4055

Laamlaanna jahannama minka wamimman tabi'aka minhum ajma'eena

# 4056

Qul ma asalukum 'alayhi min ajrin wama ana mina almutakallifeena

# 4057

In huwa illa thikrun lil'alameena

# 4058

Walata'lamunna nabaahu ba'da heenin

# 4059

Tanzeelu alkitabi mina Allahi al'azeezi alhakeemi

# 4060

Inna anzana ilayka alkitaba bialhaqqi fao'budi Allaha mukhlisan lahu addeena

# 4061

Ala lillahi addeenu alkhalisu waallatheena ittakhathoo min doonihi awliyaa ma na'buduhum illa liyuqarriboona ila Allahi zulfa inna Allaha yahkumu baynahum fee ma hum feehi yakhtalifoona inna Allaha la yahdee man huwa kathibun kaffarun

# 4062

Law arada Allahu an yattakhitha waladan laistafa mimma yakhluqu ma yashao subhanahu huwa Allahu alwahidu alqahharu

# 4063

Khalaqa assamawati waalarda bialhaqqi yukawwiru allayla 'ala annahari wayukawwiru annahara 'ala allayli wasakhkhara ashshamsa waalqamara kullun yajree liajalin musamman ala huwa al'azeezu alghaffaru

# 4064

Khalaqakum min nafsin wahidatin thumma ja'ala minha zawjaha waanzala lakum mina alan'ami thamaniyata azwajin yakhluqukum fee butooni ommahatikum khalqan min ba'di khalqin fee thulumatin thalathin thalikumu Allahu rabbukum lahu almulku la ilaha illa huwa faanna tusrafoona

# 4065

In takfuroo fainna Allaha ghaniyyun 'ankum wala yarda li'ibadihi alkufra wain tashkuroo yardahu lakum wala taziru waziratun wizra okhra thumma ila rabbikum marji'ukum fayunabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloona innahu 'aleemun bithati assudoori

# 4066

Waitha massa alinsana durrun da'a rabbahu muneeban ilayhi thumma itha khawwalahu ni'matan minhu nasiya ma kana yad'oo ilayhi min qablu waja'ala lillahi andadan liyudilla 'an sabeelihi qul tamatta' bikufrika qaleelan innaka min ashabi annari

# 4067

Amman huwa qanitun anaa allayli sajidan waqaiman yahtharu alakhirata wayarjoo rahmata rabbihi qul hal yastawee allatheena ya'lamoona waallatheena la ya'lamoona innama yatathakkaru oloo alalbabi

# 4068

Qul ya 'ibadi allatheena amanoo ittaqoo rabbakum lillatheena ahsanoo fee hathihi addunya hasanatun waardu Allahi wasi'atun innama yuwaffa assabiroona ajrahum bighayri hisabin

# 4069

Qul innee omirtu an a'buda Allaha mukhlisan lahu addeena

# 4070

Waomirtu lian akoona awwala almuslimeena

# 4071

Qul innee akhafu in 'asaytu rabbee 'athaba yawmin 'atheemin

# 4072

Quli Allaha a'budu mukhlisan lahu deenee

# 4073

Fao'budoo ma shitum min doonihi qul inna alkhasireena allatheena khasiroo anfusahum waahleehim yawma alqiyamati ala thalika huwa alkhusranu almubeenu

# 4074

Lahum min fawqihim thulalun mina annari wamin tahtihim thulalun thalika yukhawwifu Allahu bihi 'ibadahu ya 'ibadi faittaqooni

# 4075

Waallatheena ijtanaboo attaghoota an ya'budooha waanaboo ila Allahi lahumu albushra fabashshir 'ibadi

# 4076

Allatheena yastami'oona alqawla fayattabi'oona ahsanahu olaika allatheena hadahumu Allahu waolaika hum oloo alalbabi

# 4077

Afaman haqqa 'alayhi kalimatu al'athabi afaanta tunqithu man fee annari

# 4078

Lakini allatheena ittaqaw rabbahum lahum ghurafun min fawqiha ghurafun mabniyyatun tajree min tahtiha alanharu wa'da Allahi la yukhlifu Allahu almee'ada

# 4079

Alam tara anna Allaha anzala mina assamai maan fasalakahu yanabee'a fee alardi thumma yukhriju bihi zar'an mukhtalifan alwanuhu thumma yaheeju fatarahu musfarran thumma yaj'aluhu hutaman inna fee thalika lathikra liolee alalbabi

# 4080

Afaman sharaha Allahu sadrahu lilislami fahuwa 'ala noorin min rabbihi fawaylun lilqasiyati quloobuhum min thikri Allahi olaika fee dalalin mubeenin

# 4081

Allahu nazzala ahsana alhadeethi kitaban mutashabihan mathaniya taqsha'irru minhu juloodu allatheena yakhshawna rabbahum thumma taleenu julooduhum waquloobuhum ila thikri Allahi thalika huda Allahi yahdee bihi man yashao waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min hadin

# 4082

Afaman yattaqee biwajhihi sooa al'athabi yawma alqiyamati waqeela lilththalimeena thooqoo ma kuntum taksiboona

# 4083

Kaththaba allatheena min qablihim faatahumu al'athabu min haythu la yash'uroona

# 4084

Faathaqahumu Allahu alkhizya fee alhayati addunya wala'athabu alakhirati akbaru law kanoo ya'lamoona

# 4085

Walaqad darabna lilnnasi fee hatha alqurani min kulli mathalin la'allahum yatathakkaroona

# 4086

Quranan 'arabiyyan ghayra thee 'iwajin la'allahum yattaqoona

# 4087

Daraba Allahu mathalan rajulan feehi shurakao mutashakisoona warajulan salaman lirajulin hal yastawiyani mathalan alhamdu lillahi bal aktharuhum la ya'lamoona

# 4088

Innaka mayyitun wainnahum mayyitoona

# 4089

Thumma innakum yawma alqiyamati 'inda rabbikum takhtasimoona

# 4090

Faman athlamu mimman kathaba 'ala Allahi wakaththaba biassidqi ith jaahu alaysa fee jahannama mathwan lilkafireena

# 4091

Waallathee jaa biassidqi wasaddaqa bihi olaika humu almuttaqoona

# 4092

Lahum ma yashaoona 'inda rabbihim thalika jazao almuhsineena

# 4093

Liyukaffira Allahu 'anhum aswaa allathee 'amiloo wayajziyahum ajrahum biahsani allathee kanoo ya'maloona

# 4094

Alaysa Allahu bikafin 'abdahu wayukhawwifoonaka biallatheena min doonihi waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min hadin

# 4095

Waman yahdi Allahu fama lahu min mudillin alaysa Allahu bi'azeezin thee intiqamin

# 4096

Walain saatahum man khalaqa assamawati waalarda layaqoolunna Allahu qul afaraaytum ma tad'oona min dooni Allahi in aradaniya Allahu bidurrin hal hunna kashifatu durrihi aw aradanee birahmatin hal hunna mumsikatu rahmatihi qul hasbiya Allahu 'alayhi yatawakkalu almutawakkiloona

# 4097

Qul ya qawmi i'maloo 'ala makanatikum innee 'amilun fasawfa ta'lamoona

# 4098

Man yateehi 'athabun yukhzeehi wayahillu 'alayhi 'athabun muqeemun

# 4099

Inna anzana 'alayka alkitaba lilnnasi bialhaqqi famani ihtada falinafsihi waman dalla fainnama yadillu 'alayha wama anta 'alayhim biwakeelin

# 4100

Allahu yatawaffa alanfusa heena mawtiha waallatee lam tamut fee manamiha fayumsiku allatee qada 'alayha almawta wayursilu alokhra ila ajalin musamman inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaroona

# 4101

Ami ittakhathoo min dooni Allahi shufa'aa qul awalaw kanoo la yamlikoona shayan wala ya'qiloona

# 4102

Qul lillahi ashshafa'atu jamee'an lahu mulku assamawati waalardi thumma ilayhi turja'oona

# 4103

Waitha thukira Allahu wahdahu ishmaazzat quloobu allatheena la yuminoona bialakhirati waitha thukira allatheena min doonihi itha hum yastabshiroona

# 4104

Quli allahumma fatira assamawati waalardi 'alima alghaybi waashshahadati anta tahkumu bayna 'ibadika fee ma kanoo feehi yakhtalifoona

# 4105

Walaw anna lillatheena thalamoo ma fee alardi jamee'an wamithlahu ma'ahu laiftadaw bihi min sooi al'athabi yawma alqiyamati wabada lahum mina Allahi ma lam yakoonoo yahtasiboona

# 4106

Wabada lahum sayyiatu ma kasaboo wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioona

# 4107

Faitha massa alinsana durrun da'ana thumma itha khawwanahu ni'matan minna qala innama ooteetuhu 'ala 'ilmin bal hiya fitnatun walakinna aktharahum la ya'lamoona

# 4108

Qad qalaha allatheena min qablihim fama aghna 'anhum ma kanoo yaksiboona

# 4109

Faasabahum sayyiatu ma kasaboo waallatheena thalamoo min haolai sayuseebuhum sayyiatu ma kasaboo wama hum bimu'jizeena

# 4110

Awalam ya'lamoo anna Allaha yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yuminoona

# 4111

Qul ya 'ibadiya allatheena asrafoo 'ala anfusihim la taqnatoo min rahmati Allahi inna Allaha yaghfiru aththunooba jamee'an innahu huwa alghafooru arraheemu

# 4112

Waaneeboo ila rabbikum waaslimoo lahu min qabli an yatiyakumu al'athabu thumma la tunsaroona

# 4113

Waittabi'oo ahsana ma onzila ilaykum min rabbikum min qabli an yatiyakumu al'athabu baghtatan waantum la tash'uroona

# 4114

An taqoola nafsun ya hasrata 'ala ma farrattu fee janbi Allahi wain kuntu lamina assakhireena

# 4115

Aw taqoola law anna Allaha hadanee lakuntu mina almuttaqeena

# 4116

Aw taqoola heena tara al'athaba law anna lee karratan faakoona mina almuhsineena

# 4117

Bala qad jaatka ayatee fakaththabta biha waistakbarta wakunta mina alkafireena

# 4118

Wayawma alqiyamati tara allatheena kathaboo 'ala Allahi wujoohuhum muswaddatun alaysa fee jahannama mathwan lilmutakabbireena

# 4119

Wayunajjee Allahu allatheena ittaqaw bimafazatihim la yamassuhumu assooo wala hum yahzanoona

# 4120

Allahu khaliqu kulli shayin wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin wakeelun

# 4121

Lahu maqaleedu assamawati waalardi waallatheena kafaroo biayati Allahi olaika humu alkhasiroona

# 4122

Qul afaghayra Allahi tamuroonnee a'budu ayyuha aljahiloona

# 4123

Walaqad oohiya ilayka waila allatheena min qablika lain ashrakta layahbatanna 'amaluka walatakoonanna mina alkhasireena

# 4124

Bali Allaha fao'bud wakun mina ashshakireena

# 4125

Wama qadaroo Allaha haqqa qadrihi waalardu jamee'an qabdatuhu yawma alqiyamati waassamawatu matwiyyatun biyameenihi subhanahu wata'ala 'amma yushrikoona

# 4126

Wanufikha fee assoori fasa'iqa man fee assamawati waman fee alardi illa man shaa Allahu thumma nufikha feehi okhra faitha hum qiyamun yanthuroona

# 4127

Waashraqati alardu binoori rabbiha wawudi'a alkitabu wajeea biannabiyyeena waashshuhadai waqudiya baynahum bialhaqqi wahum la yuthlamoona

# 4128

Wawuffiyat kullu nafsin ma 'amilat wahuwa a'lamu bima yaf'aloona

# 4129

Waseeqa allatheena kafaroo ila jahannama zumaran hatta itha jaooha futihat abwabuha waqala lahum khazanatuha alam yatikum rusulun minkum yatloona 'alaykum ayati rabbikum wayunthiroonakum liqaa yawmikum hatha qaloo bala walakin haqqat kalimatu al'athabi 'ala alkafireena

# 4130

Qeela odkhuloo abwaba jahannama khalideena feeha fabisa mathwa almutakabbireena

# 4131

Waseeqa allatheena ittaqaw rabbahum ila aljannati zumaran hatta itha jaooha wafutihat abwabuha waqala lahum khazanatuha salamun 'alaykum tibtum faodkhulooha khalideena

# 4132

Waqaloo alhamdu lillahi allathee sadaqana wa'dahu waawrathana alarda natabawwao mina aljannati haythu nashao fani'ma ajru al'amileena

# 4133

Watara almalaikata haffeena min hawli al'arshi yusabbihoona bihamdi rabbihim waqudiya baynahum bialhaqqi waqeela alhamdu lillahi rabbi al'alameena

# 4134

Hameem

# 4135

Tanzeelu alkitabi mina Allahi al'azeezi al'aleemi

# 4136

Ghafiri aththanbi waqabili attawbi shadeedi al'iqabi thee attawli la ilaha illa huwa ilayhi almaseeru

# 4137

Ma yujadilu fee ayati Allahi illa allatheena kafaroo fala yaghrurka taqallubuhum fee albiladi

# 4138

Kaththabat qablahum qawmu noohin waalahzabu min ba'dihim wahammat kullu ommatin birasoolihim liyakhuthoohu wajadaloo bialbatili liyudhidoo bihi alhaqqa faakhathtuhum fakayfa kana 'iqabi

# 4139

Wakathalika haqqat kalimatu rabbika 'ala allatheena kafaroo annahum ashabu annari

# 4140

Allatheena yahmiloona al'arsha waman hawlahu yusabbihoona bihamdi rabbihim wayuminoona bihi wayastaghfiroona lillatheena amanoo rabbana wasi'ta kulla shayin rahmatan wa'ilman faighfir lillatheena taboo waittaba'oo sabeelaka waqihim 'athaba aljaheemi

# 4141

Rabbana waadkhilhum jannati 'adnin allatee wa'adtahum waman salaha min abaihim waazwajihim wathurriyyatihim innaka anta al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 4142

Waqihimu assayyiati waman taqi assayyiati yawmaithin faqad rahimtahu wathalika huwa alfawzu al'atheemu

# 4143

Inna allatheena kafaroo yunadawna lamaqtu Allahi akbaru min maqtikum anfusakum ith tud'awna ila aleemani fatakfuroona

# 4144

Qaloo rabbana amattana ithnatayni waahyaytana ithnatayni fai'tarafna bithunoobina fahal ila khuroojin min sabeelin

# 4145

Thalikum biannahu itha du'iya Allahu wahdahu kafartum wain yushrak bihi tuminoo faalhukmu lillahi al'aliyyi alkabeeri

# 4146

Huwa allathee yureekum ayatihi wayunazzilu lakum mina assamai rizqan wama yatathakkaru illa man yuneebu

# 4147

Faod'oo Allaha mukhliseena lahu addeena walaw kariha alkafiroona

# 4148

Rafee'u addarajati thoo al'arshi yulqee arrooha min amrihi 'ala man yashao min 'ibadihi liyunthira yawma attalaqi

# 4149

Yawma hum barizoona la yakhfa 'ala Allahi minhum shayon limani almulku alyawma lillahi alwahidi alqahhari

# 4150

Alyawma tujza kullu nafsin bima kasabat la thulma alyawma inna Allaha saree'u alhisabi

# 4151

Waanthirhum yawma alazifati ithi alquloobu lada alhanajiri kathimeena ma lilththalimeena min hameemin wala shafee'in yuta'u

# 4152

Ya'lamu khainata ala'yuni wama tukhfee assudooru

# 4153

WaAllahu yaqdee bialhaqqi waallatheena yad'oona min doonihi la yaqdoona bishayin inna Allaha huwa assamee'u albaseeru

# 4154

Awa lam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena kanoo min qablihim kanoo hum ashadda minhum quwwatan waatharan fee alardi faakhathahumu Allahu bithunoobihim wama kana lahum mina Allahi min waqin

# 4155

Thalika biannahum kanat tateehim rusuluhum bialbayyinati fakafaroo faakhathahumu Allahu innahu qawiyyun shadeedu al'iqabi

# 4156

Walaqad arsana moosa biayatina wasultanin mubeenin

# 4157

Ila fir'awna wahamana waqaroona faqaloo sahirun kaththabun

# 4158

Falamma jaahum bialhaqqi min 'indina qaloo oqtuloo abnaa allatheena amanoo ma'ahu waistahyoo nisaahum wama kaydu alkafireena illa fee dalalin

# 4159

Waqala fir'awnu tharoonee aqtul moosa walyad'u rabbahu innee akhafu an yubaddila deenakum aw an yuthhira fee alardi alfasada

# 4160

Waqala moosa innee 'uthtu birabbee warabbikum min kulli mutakabbirin la yuminu biyawmi alhisabi

# 4161

Waqala rajulun muminun min ali fir'awna yaktumu eemanahu ataqtuloona rajulan an yaqoola rabbiyya Allahu waqad jaakum bialbayyinati min rabbikum wain yaku kathiban fa'alayhi kathibuhu wain yaku sadiqan yusibkum ba'du allathee ya'idukum inna Allaha la yahdee man huwa musrifun kaththabun

# 4162

Ya qawmi lakumu almulku alyawma thahireena fee alardi faman yansuruna min basi Allahi in jaana qala fir'awnu ma oreekum illa ma ara wama ahdeekum illa sabeela arrashadi

# 4163

Waqala allathee amana ya qawmi innee akhafu 'alaykum mithla yawmi alahzabi

# 4164

Mithla dabi qawmi noohin wa'adin wathamooda waallatheena min ba'dihim wama Allahu yureedu thulman lil'ibadi

# 4165

Waya qawmi innee akhafu 'alaykum yawma attanadi

# 4166

Yawma tuwalloona mudbireena ma lakum mina Allahi min 'asimin waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min hadin

# 4167

Walaqad jaakum yoosufu min qablu bialbayyinati fama ziltum fee shakkin mimma jaakum bihi hatta itha halaka qultum lan yab'atha Allahu min ba'dihi rasoolan kathalika yudillu Allahu man huwa musrifun murtabun

# 4168

Allatheena yujadiloona fee ayati Allahi bighayri sultanin atahum kabura maqtan 'inda Allahi wa'inda allatheena amanoo kathalika yatba'u Allahu 'ala kulli qalbi mutakabbirin jabbarin

# 4169

Waqala fir'awnu ya hamanu ibni lee sarhan la'allee ablughu alasbaba

# 4170

Asbaba assamawati faattali'a ila ilahi moosa wainnee laathunnuhu kathiban wakathalika zuyyina lifir'awna sooo 'amalihi wasudda 'ani assabeeli wama kaydu fir'awna illa fee tababin

# 4171

Waqala allathee amana ya qawmi ittabi'ooni ahdikum sabeela arrashadi

# 4172

Ya qawmi innama hathihi alhayatu addunya mata'un wainna alakhirata hiya daru alqarari

# 4173

Man 'amila sayyiatan fala yujza illa mithlaha waman 'amila salihan min thakarin aw ontha wahuwa muminun faolaika yadkhuloona aljannata yurzaqoona feeha bighayri hisabin

# 4174

Waya qawmi ma lee ad'ookum ila annajati watad'oonanee ila annari

# 4175

Tad'oonanee liakfura biAllahi waoshrika bihi ma laysa lee bihi 'ilmun waana ad'ookum ila al'azeezi alghaffari

# 4176

La jarama annama tad'oonanee ilayhi laysa lahu da'watun fee addunya wala fee alakhirati waanna maraddana ila Allahi waanna almusrifeena hum ashabu annari

# 4177

Fasatathkuroona ma aqoolu lakum waofawwidu amree ila Allahi inna Allaha baseerun bial'ibadi

# 4178

Fawaqahu Allahu sayyiati ma makaroo wahaqa biali fir'awna sooo al'athabi

# 4179

annaru yu'radoona 'alayha ghuduwwan wa'ashiyyan wayawma taqoomu assa'atu adkhiloo ala fir'awna ashadda al'athabi

# 4180

Waith yatahajjoona fee annari fayaqoolu addu'afao lillatheena istakbaroo inna kunna lakum taba'an fahal antum mughnoona 'anna naseeban mina annari

# 4181

Qala allatheena istakbaroo inna kullun feeha inna Allaha qad hakama bayna al'ibadi

# 4182

Waqala allatheena fee annari likhazanati jahannama od'oo rabbakum yukhaffif 'anna yawman mina al'athabi

# 4183

Qaloo awalam taku tateekum rusulukum bialbayyinati qaloo bala qaloo faod'oo wama du'ao alkafireena illa fee dalalin

# 4184

Inna lanansuru rusulana waallatheena amanoo fee alhayati addunya wayawma yaqoomu alashhadu

# 4185

Yawma la yanfa'u aththalimeena ma'thiratuhum walahumu alla'natu walahum sooo addari

# 4186

Walaqad atayna moosa alhuda waawrathna banee israeela alkitaba

# 4187

Hudan wathikra liolee alalbabi

# 4188

Faisbir inna wa'da Allahi haqqun waistaghfir lithanbika wasabbih bihamdi rabbika bial'ashiyyi waalibkari

# 4189

Inna allatheena yujadiloona fee ayati Allahi bighayri sultanin atahum in fee sudoorihim illa kibrun ma hum bibaligheehi faista'ith biAllahi innahu huwa assamee'u albaseeru

# 4190

Lakhalqu assamawati waalardi akbaru min khalqi annasi walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoona

# 4191

Wama yastawee ala'ma waalbaseeru waallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati wala almuseeo qaleelan ma tatathakkaroona

# 4192

Inna assa'ata laatiyatun la rayba feeha walakinna akthara annasi la yuminoona

# 4193

Waqala rabbukumu od'oonee astajib lakum inna allatheena yastakbiroona 'an 'ibadatee sayadkhuloona jahannama dakhireena

# 4194

Allahu allathee ja'ala lakumu allayla litaskunoo feehi waannahara mubsiran inna Allaha lathoo fadlin 'ala annasi walakinna akthara annasi la yashkuroona

# 4195

Thalikumu Allahu rabbukum khaliqu kulli shayin la ilaha illa huwa faanna tufakoona

# 4196

Kathalika yufaku allatheena kanoo biayati Allahi yajhadoona

# 4197

Allahu allathee ja'ala lakumu alarda qararan waassamaa binaan wasawwarakum faahsana suwarakum warazaqakum mina attayyibati thalikumu Allahu rabbukum fatabaraka Allahu rabbu al'alameena

# 4198

Huwa alhayyu la ilaha illa huwa faod'oohu mukhliseena lahu addeena alhamdu lillahi rabbi al'alameena

# 4199

Qul innee nuheetu an a'buda allatheena tad'oona min dooni Allahi lamma jaaniya albayyinatu min rabbee waomirtu an oslima lirabbi al'alameena

# 4200

Huwa allathee khalaqakum min turabin thumma min nutfatin thumma min 'alaqatin thumma yukhrijukum tiflan thumma litablughoo ashuddakum thumma litakoonoo shuyookhan waminkum man yutawaffa min qablu walitablughoo ajalan musamman wala'allakum ta'qiloona

# 4201

Huwa allathee yuhyee wayumeetu faitha qada amran fainnama yaqoolu lahu kun fayakoonu

# 4202

Alam tara ila allatheena yujadiloona fee ayati Allahi anna yusrafoona

# 4203

Allatheena kaththaboo bialkitabi wabima arsana bihi rusulana fasawfa ya'lamoona

# 4204

Ithi alaghlalu fee a'naqihim waassalasilu yushaboona

# 4205

Fee alhameemi thumma fee annari yusjaroona

# 4206

Thumma qeela lahum ayna ma kuntum tushrikoona

# 4207

Min dooni Allahi qaloo dalloo 'anna bal lam nakun nad'oo min qablu shayan kathalika yudillu Allahu alkafireena

# 4208

Thalikum bima kuntum tafrahoona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi wabima kuntum tamrahoona

# 4209

Odkhuloo abwaba jahannama khalideena feeha fabisa mathwa almutakabbireena

# 4210

Faisbir inna wa'da Allahi haqqun faimma nuriyannaka ba'da allathee na'iduhum aw natawaffayannaka failayna yurja'oona

# 4211

Walaqad arsana rusulan min qablika minhum man qasasna 'alayka waminhum man lam naqsus 'alayka wama kana lirasoolin an yatiya biayatin illa biithni Allahi faitha jaa amru Allahi qudiya bialhaqqi wakhasira hunalika almubtiloona

# 4212

Allahu allathee ja'ala lakumu alan'ama litarkaboo minha waminha takuloona

# 4213

Walakum feeha manafi'u walitablughoo 'alayha hajatan fee sudoorikum wa'alayha wa'ala alfulki tuhmaloona

# 4214

Wayureekum ayatihi faayya ayati Allahi tunkiroona

# 4215

Afalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena min qablihim kanoo akthara minhum waashadda quwwatan waatharan fee alardi fama aghna 'anhum ma kanoo yaksiboona

# 4216

Falamma jaathum rusuluhum bialbayyinati farihoo bima 'indahum mina al'ilmi wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioona

# 4217

Falamma raaw basana qaloo amanna biAllahi wahdahu wakafarna bima kunna bihi mushrikeena

# 4218

Falam yaku yanfa'uhum eemanuhum lamma raaw basana sunnata Allahi allatee qad khalat fee 'ibadihi wakhasira hunalika alkafiroona

# 4219

Hameem

# 4220

Tanzeelun mina arrahmani arraheemi

# 4221

Kitabun fussilat ayatuhu quranan 'arabiyyan liqawmin ya'lamoona

# 4222

Basheeran wanatheeran faa'rada aktharuhum fahum la yasma'oona

# 4223

Waqaloo quloobuna fee akinnatin mimma tad'oona ilayhi wafee athanina waqrun wamin baynina wabaynika hijabun fai'mal innana 'amiloona

# 4224

Qul innama ana basharun mithlukum yooha ilayya annama ilahukum ilahun wahidun faistaqeemoo ilayhi waistaghfiroohu wawaylun lilmushrikeena

# 4225

Allatheena la yutoona azzakata wahum bialakhirati hum kafiroona

# 4226

Inna allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati lahum ajrun ghayru mamnoonin

# 4227

Qul ainnakum latakfuroona biallathee khalaqa alarda fee yawmayni wataj'aloona lahu andadan thalika rabbu al'alameena

# 4228

Waja'ala feeha rawasiya min fawqiha wabaraka feeha waqaddara feeha aqwataha fee arba'ati ayyamin sawaan lilssaileena

# 4229

Thumma istawa ila assamai wahiya dukhanun faqala laha walilardi itiya taw'an aw karhan qalata atayna tai'eena

# 4230

Faqadahunna sab'a samawatin fee yawmayni waawha fee kulli samain amraha wazayyanna assamaa addunya bimasabeeha wahifthan thalika taqdeeru al'azeezi al'aleemi

# 4231

Fain a'radoo fuqul anthartukum sa'iqatan mithla sa'iqati 'adin wathamooda

# 4232

Ith jaathumu arrusulu min bayni aydeehim wamin khalfihim alla ta'budoo illa Allaha qaloo law shaa rabbuna laanzala malaikatan fainna bima orsiltum bihi kafiroona

# 4233

Faamma 'adun faistakbaroo fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi waqaloo man ashaddu minna quwwatan awalam yaraw anna Allaha allathee khalaqahum huwa ashaddu minhum quwwatan wakanoo biayatina yajhadoona

# 4234

Faarsana 'alayhim reehan sarsaran fee ayyamin nahisatin linutheeqahum 'athaba alkhizyi fee alhayati addunya wala'athabu alakhirati akhza wahum la yunsaroona

# 4235

Waamma thamoodu fahadaynahum faistahabboo al'ama 'ala alhuda faakhathathum sa'iqatu al'athabi alhooni bima kanoo yaksiboona

# 4236

Wanajjayna allatheena amanoo wakanoo yattaqoona

# 4237

Wayawma yuhsharu a'dao Allahi ila annari fahum yooza'oona

# 4238

Hatta itha ma jaooha shahida 'alayhim sam'uhum waabsaruhum wajulooduhum bima kanoo ya'maloona

# 4239

Waqaloo lijuloodihim lima shahidtum 'alayna qaloo antaqana Allahu allathee antaqa kulla shayin wahuwa khalaqakum awwala marratin wailayhi turja'oona

# 4240

Wama kuntum tastatiroona an yashhada 'alaykum sam'ukum wala absarukum wala juloodukum walakin thanantum anna Allaha la ya'lamu katheeran mimma ta'maloona

# 4241

Wathalikum thannukumu allathee thanantum birabbikum ardakum faasbahtum mina alkhasireena

# 4242

Fain yasbiroo faannaru mathwan lahum wain yasta'tiboo fama hum mina almu'tabeena

# 4243

Waqayyadna lahum quranaa fazayyanoo lahum ma bayna aydeehim wama khalfahum wahaqqa 'alayhimu alqawlu fee omamin qad khalat min qablihim mina aljinni waalinsi innahum kanoo khasireena

# 4244

Waqala allatheena kafaroo la tasma'oo lihatha alqurani wailghaw feehi la'allakum taghliboona

# 4245

Falanutheeqanna allatheena kafaroo 'athaban shadeedan walanajziyannahum aswaa allathee kanoo ya'maloona

# 4246

Thalika jazao a'dai Allahi annaru lahum feeha daru alkhuldi jazaan bima kanoo biayatina yajhadoona

# 4247

Waqala allatheena kafaroo rabbana arina allathayni adallana mina aljinni waalinsi naj'alhuma tahta aqdamina liyakoona mina alasfaleena

# 4248

Inna allatheena qaloo rabbuna Allahu thumma istaqamoo tatanazzalu 'alayhimu almalaikatu alla takhafoo wala tahzanoo waabshiroo bialjannati allatee kuntum too'adoona

# 4249

Nahnu awliyaokum fee alhayati addunya wafee alakhirati walakum feeha ma tashtahee anfusukum walakum feeha ma tadda'oona

# 4250

Nuzulan min ghafoorin raheemin

# 4251

Waman ahsanu qawlan mimman da'a ila Allahi wa'amila salihan waqala innanee mina almuslimeena

# 4252

Wala tastawee alhasanatu wala assayyiatu idfa' biallatee hiya ahsanu faitha allathee baynaka wabaynahu 'adawatun kaannahu waliyyun hameemun

# 4253

Wama yulaqqaha illa allatheena sabaroo wama yulaqqaha illa thoo haththin 'atheemin

# 4254

Waimma yanzaghannaka mina ashshaytani nazghun faista'ith biAllahi innahu huwa assamee'u al'aleemu

# 4255

Wamin ayatihi allaylu waannaharu waashshamsu waalqamaru la tasjudoo lilshshamsi wala lilqamari waosjudoo lillahi alathee khalaqahunna in kuntum iyyahu ta'budoona

# 4256

Faini istakbaroo faallatheena 'inda rabbika yusabbihoona lahu biallayli waannahari wahum la yasamoona

# 4257

Wamin ayatihi annaka tara alarda khashi'atan faitha anzana 'alayha almaa ihtazzat warabat inna allathee ahyaha lamuhyee almawta innahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 4258

Inna allatheena yulhidoona fee ayatina la yakhfawna 'alayna afaman yulqa fee annari khayrun am man yatee aminan yawma alqiyamati i'maloo ma shitum innahu bima ta'maloona baseerun

# 4259

Inna allatheena kafaroo biaththikri lamma jaahum wainnahu lakitabun 'azeezun

# 4260

La yateehi albatilu min bayni yadayhi wala min khalfihi tanzeelun min hakeemin hameedin

# 4261

Ma yuqalu laka illa ma qad qeela lilrrusuli min qablika inna rabbaka lathoo maghfiratin wathoo 'iqabin aleemin

# 4262

Walaw ja'anahu quranan a'jamiyyan laqaloo lawla fussilat ayatuhu aa'jamiyyun wa'arabiyyun qul huwa lillatheena amanoo hudan washifaon waallatheena la yuminoona fee athanihim waqrun wahuwa 'alayhim 'aman olaika yunadawna min makanin ba'eedin

# 4263

Walaqad atayna moosa alkitaba faikhtulifa feehi walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika laqudiya baynahum wainnahum lafee shakkin minhu mureebin

# 4264

Man 'amila salihan falinafsihi waman asaa fa'alayha wama rabbuka bithallamin lil'abeedi

# 4265

Ilayhi yuraddu 'ilmu assa'ati wama takhruju min thamaratin min akmamiha wama tahmilu min ontha wala tada'u illa bi'ilmihi wayawma yunadeehim ayna shurakaee qaloo athannaka ma minna min shaheedin

# 4266

Wadalla 'anhum ma kanoo yad'oona min qablu wathannoo ma lahum min maheesin

# 4267

La yasamu alinsanu min du'ai alkhayri wain massahu ashsharru fayaoosun qanootun

# 4268

Walain athaqnahu rahmatan minna min ba'di darraa massathu layaqoolanna hatha lee wama athunnu assa'ata qaimatan walain ruji'tu ila rabbee inna lee 'indahu lalhusna falanunabbianna allatheena kafaroo bima 'amiloo walanutheeqannahum min 'athabin ghaleethin

# 4269

Waitha an'amna 'ala alinsani a'rada wanaa bijanibihi waitha massahu ashsharru fathoo du'ain 'areedin

# 4270

Qul araaytum in kana min 'indi Allahi thumma kafartum bihi man adallu mimman huwa fee shiqaqin ba'eedin

# 4271

Sanureehim ayatina fee alafaqi wafee anfusihim hatta yatabayyana lahum annahu alhaqqu awalam yakfi birabbika annahu 'ala kulli shayin shaheedun

# 4272

Ala innahum fee miryatin min liqai rabbihim ala innahu bikulli shayin muheetun

# 4273

Hameem

# 4274

'aynseenqaf

# 4275

Kathalika yoohee ilayka waila allatheena min qablika Allahu al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 4276

Lahu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi wahuwa al'aliyyu al'atheemu

# 4277

Takadu assamawatu yatafattarna min fawqihinna waalmalaikatu yusabbihoona bihamdi rabbihim wayastaghfiroona liman fee alardi ala inna Allaha huwa alghafooru arraheemu

# 4278

Waallatheena ittakhathoo min doonihi awliyaa Allahu hafeethun 'alayhim wama anta 'alayhim biwakeelin

# 4279

Wakathalika awhayna ilayka quranan 'arabiyyan litunthira omma alqura waman hawlaha watunthira yawma aljam'i la rayba feehi fareequn fee aljannati wafareequn fee assa'eeri

# 4280

Walaw shaa Allahu laja'alahum ommatan wahidatan walakin yudkhilu man yashao fee rahmatihi waaththalimoona ma lahum min waliyyin wala naseerin

# 4281

Ami ittakhathoo min doonihi awliyaa faAllahu huwa alwaliyyu wahuwa yuhyee almawta wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 4282

Wama ikhtalaftum feehi min shayin fahukmuhu ila Allahi thalikumu Allahu rabbee 'alayhi tawakkatu wailayhi oneebu

# 4283

Fatiru assamawati waalardi ja'ala lakum min anfusikum azwajan wamina alan'ami azwajan yathraokum feehi laysa kamithlihi shayon wahuwa assamee'u albaseeru

# 4284

Lahu maqaleedu assamawati waalardi yabsutu arrizqa liman yashao wayaqdiru innahu bikulli shayin 'aleemun

# 4285

Shara'a lakum mina addeeni ma wassa bihi noohan waallathee awhayna ilayka wama wassayna bihi ibraheema wamoosa wa'eesa an aqeemoo addeena wala tatafarraqoo feehi kabura 'ala almushrikeena ma tad'oohum ilayhi Allahu yajtabee ilayhi man yashao wayahdee ilayhi man yuneebu

# 4286

Wama tafarraqoo illa min ba'di ma jaahumu al'ilmu baghyan baynahum walawla kalimatun sabaqat min rabbika ila ajalin musamman laqudiya baynahum wainna allatheena oorithoo alkitaba min ba'dihim lafee shakkin minhu mureebin

# 4287

Falithalika faod'u waistaqim kama omirta wala tattabi' ahwaahum waqul amantu bima anzala Allahu min kitabin waomirtu lia'dila baynakum Allahu rabbuna warabbukum lana a'maluna walakum a'malukum la hujjata baynana wabaynakumu Allahu yajma'u baynana wailayhi almaseeru

# 4288

Waallatheena yuhajjoona fee Allahi min ba'di ma istujeeba lahu hujjatuhum dahidatun 'inda rabbihim wa'alayhim ghadabun walahum 'athabun shadeedun

# 4289

Allahu allathee anzala alkitaba bialhaqqi waalmeezani wama yudreeka la'alla assa'ata qareebun

# 4290

Yasta'jilu biha allatheena la yuminoona biha waallatheena amanoo mushfiqoona minha waya'lamoona annaha alhaqqu ala inna allatheena yumaroona fee assa'ati lafee dalalin ba'eedin

# 4291

Allahu lateefun bi'ibadihi yarzuqu man yashao wahuwa alqawiyyu al'azeezu

# 4292

Man kana yureedu hartha alakhirati nazid lahu fee harthihi waman kana yureedu hartha addunya nutihi minha wama lahu fee alakhirati min naseebin

# 4293

Am lahum shurakao shara'oo lahum mina addeeni ma lam yathan bihi Allahu walawla kalimatu alfasli laqudiya baynahum wainna aththalimeena lahum 'athabun aleemun

# 4294

Tara aththalimeena mushfiqeena mimma kasaboo wahuwa waqi'un bihim waallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati fee rawdati aljannati lahum ma yashaoona 'inda rabbihim thalika huwa alfadlu alkabeeru

# 4295

Thalika allathee yubashshiru Allahu 'ibadahu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati qul la asalukum 'alayhi ajran illa almawaddata fee alqurba waman yaqtarif hasanatan nazid lahu feeha husnan inna Allaha ghafoorun shakoorun

# 4296

Am yaqooloona iftara 'ala Allahi kathiban fain yashai Allahu yakhtim 'ala qalbika wayamhu Allahu albatila wayuhiqqu alhaqqa bikalimatihi innahu 'aleemun bithati assudoori

# 4297

Wahuwa allathee yaqbalu attawbata 'an 'ibadihi waya'foo 'ani assayyiati waya'lamu ma taf'aloona

# 4298

Wayastajeebu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati wayazeeduhum min fadlihi waalkafiroona lahum 'athabun shadeedun

# 4299

Walaw basata Allahu arrizqa li'ibadihi labaghaw fee alardi walakin yunazzilu biqadarin ma yashao innahu bi'ibadihi khabeerun baseerun

# 4300

Wahuwa allathee yunazzilu alghaytha min ba'di ma qanatoo wayanshuru rahmatahu wahuwa alwaliyyu alhameedu

# 4301

Wamin ayatihi khalqu assamawati waalardi wama baththa feehima min dabbatin wahuwa 'ala jam'ihim itha yashao qadeerun

# 4302

Wama asabakum min museebatin fabima kasabat aydeekum waya'foo 'an katheerin

# 4303

Wama antum bimu'jizeena fee alardi wama lakum min dooni Allahi min waliyyin wala naseerin

# 4304

Wamin ayatihi aljawari fee albahri kaala'lami

# 4305

In yasha yuskini arreeha fayathlana rawakida 'ala thahrihi inna fee thalika laayatin likulli sabbarin shakoorin

# 4306

Aw yoobiqhunna bima kasaboo waya'fu 'an katheerin

# 4307

Waya'lama allatheena yujadiloona fee ayatina ma lahum min maheesin

# 4308

Fama ooteetum min shayin famata'u alhayati addunya wama 'inda Allahi khayrun waabqa lillatheena amanoo wa'ala rabbihim yatawakkaloona

# 4309

Waallatheena yajtaniboona kabaira alithmi waalfawahisha waitha ma ghadiboo hum yaghfiroona

# 4310

Waallatheena istajaboo lirabbihim waaqamoo assalata waamruhum shoora baynahum wamimma razaqnahum yunfiqoona

# 4311

Waallatheena itha asabahumu albaghyu hum yantasiroona

# 4312

Wajazao sayyiatin sayyiatun mithluha faman 'afa waaslaha faajruhu 'ala Allahi innahu la yuhibbu aththalimeena

# 4313

Walamani intasara ba'da thulmihi faolaika ma 'alayhim min sabeelin

# 4314

Innama assabeelu 'ala allatheena yathlimoona annasa wayabghoona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi olaika lahum 'athabun aleemun

# 4315

Walaman sabara waghafara inna thalika lamin 'azmi alomoori

# 4316

Waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min waliyyin min ba'dihi watara aththalimeena lamma raawoo al'athaba yaqooloona hal ila maraddin min sabeelin

# 4317

Watarahum yu'radoona 'alayha khashi'eena mina aththulli yanthuroona min tarfin khafiyyin waqala allatheena amanoo inna alkhasireena allatheena khasiroo anfusahum waahleehim yawma alqiyamati ala inna aththalimeena fee 'athabin muqeemin

# 4318

Wama kana lahum min awliyaa yansuroonahum min dooni Allahi waman yudlili Allahu fama lahu min sabeelin

# 4319

Istajeeboo lirabbikum min qabli an yatiya yawmun la maradda lahu mina Allahi ma lakum min maljain yawmaithin wama lakum min nakeerin

# 4320

Fain a'radoo fama arsanaka 'alayhim hafeethan in 'alayka illa albalaghu wainna itha athaqna alinsana minna rahmatan fariha biha wain tusibhum sayyiatun bima qaddamat aydeehim fainna alinsana kafoorun

# 4321

Lillahi mulku assamawati waalardi yakhluqu ma yashao yahabu liman yashao inathan wayahabu liman yashao aththukoora

# 4322

Aw yuzawwijuhum thukranan wainathan wayaj'alu man yashao 'aqeeman innahu 'aleemun qadeerun

# 4323

Wama kana libasharin an yukallimahu Allahu illa wahyan aw min warai hijabin aw yursila rasoolan fayoohiya biithnihi ma yashao innahu 'aliyyun hakeemun

# 4324

Wakathalika awhayna ilayka roohan min amrina ma kunta tadree ma alkitabu wala aleemanu walakin ja'anahu nooran nahdee bihi man nashao min 'ibadina wainnaka latahdee ila siratin mustaqeemin

# 4325

Sirati Allahi allathee lahu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi ala ila Allahi taseeru alomooru

# 4326

Hameem

# 4327

Waalkitabi almubeeni

# 4328

Inna ja'anahu quranan 'arabiyyan la'allakum ta'qiloona

# 4329

Wainnahu fee ommi alkitabi ladayna la'aliyyun hakeemun

# 4330

Afanadribu 'ankumu aththikra safhan an kuntum qawman musrifeena

# 4331

Wakam arsana min nabiyyin fee alawwaleena

# 4332

Wama yateehim min nabiyyin illa kanoo bihi yastahzioona

# 4333

Faahlakna ashadda minhum batshan wamada mathalu alawwaleena

# 4334

Walain saatahum man khalaqa assamawati waalarda layaqoolunna khalaqahunna al'azeezu al'aleemu

# 4335

Allathee ja'ala lakumu alarda mahdan waja'ala lakum feeha subulan la'allakum tahtadoona

# 4336

Waallathee nazzala mina assamai maan biqadarin faansharna bihi badatan maytan kathalika tukhrajoona

# 4337

Waallathee khalaqa alazwaja kullaha waja'ala lakum mina alfulki waalan'ami ma tarkaboona

# 4338

Litastawoo 'ala thuhoorihi thumma tathkuroo ni'mata rabbikum itha istawaytum 'alayhi wataqooloo subhana allathee sakhkhara lana hatha wama kunna lahu muqrineena

# 4339

Wainna ila rabbina lamunqaliboona

# 4340

Waja'aloo lahu min 'ibadihi juzan inna alinsana lakafoorun mubeenun

# 4341

Ami ittakhatha mimma yakhluqu banatin waasfakum bialbaneena

# 4342

Waitha bushshira ahaduhum bima daraba lilrrahmani mathalan thalla wajhuhu muswaddan wahuwa katheemun

# 4343

Awaman yunashshao fee alhilyati wahuwa fee alkhisami ghayru mubeenin

# 4344

Waja'aloo almalaikata allatheena hum 'ibadu arrahmani inathan ashahidoo khalqahum satuktabu shahadatuhum wayusaloona

# 4345

Waqaloo law shaa arrahmanu ma 'abadnahum ma lahum bithalika min 'ilmin in hum illa yakhrusoona

# 4346

Am ataynahum kitaban min qablihi fahum bihi mustamsikoona

# 4347

Bal qaloo inna wajadna abaana 'ala ommatin wainna 'ala atharihim muhtadoona

# 4348

Wakathalika ma arsana min qablika fee qaryatin min natheerin illa qala mutrafooha inna wajadna abaana 'ala ommatin wainna 'ala atharihim muqtadoona

# 4349

Qala awalaw jitukum biahda mimma wajadtum 'alayhi abaakum qaloo inna bima orsiltum bihi kafiroona

# 4350

Faintaqamna minhum faonthur kayfa kana 'aqibatu almukaththibeena

# 4351

Waith qala ibraheemu liabeehi waqawmihi innanee baraon mimma ta'budoona

# 4352

Illa allathee fataranee fainnahu sayahdeeni

# 4353

Waja'alaha kalimatan baqiyatan fee 'aqibihi la'allahum yarji'oona

# 4354

Bal matta'tu haolai waabaahum hatta jaahumu alhaqqu warasoolun mubeenun

# 4355

Walamma jaahumu alhaqqu qaloo hatha sihrun wainna bihi kafiroona

# 4356

Waqaloo lawla nuzzila hatha alquranu 'ala rajulin mina alqaryatayni 'atheemun

# 4357

Ahum yaqsimoona rahmata rabbika nahnu qasamna baynahum ma'eeshatahum fee alhayati addunya warafa'na ba'dahum fawqa ba'din darajatin liyattakhitha ba'duhum ba'dan sukhriyyan warahmatu rabbika khayrun mimma yajma'oona

# 4358

Walawla an yakoona annasu ommatan wahidatan laja'ana liman yakfuru biarrahmani libuyootihim suqufan min fiddatin wama'arija 'alayha yathharoona

# 4359

Walibuyootihim abwaban wasururan 'alayha yattakioona

# 4360

Wazukhrufan wain kullu thalika lamma mata'u alhayati addunya waalakhiratu 'inda rabbika lilmuttaqeena

# 4361

Waman ya'shu 'an thikri arrahmani nuqayyid lahu shaytanan fahuwa lahu qareenun

# 4362

Wainnahum layasuddoonahum 'ani assabeeli wayahsaboona annahum muhtadoona

# 4363

Hatta itha jaana qala ya layta baynee wabaynaka bu'da almashriqayni fabisa alqareenu

# 4364

Walan yanfa'akumu alyawma ith thalamtum annakum fee al'athabi mushtarikoona

# 4365

Afaanta tusmi'u assumma aw tahdee al'umya waman kana fee dalalin mubeenin

# 4366

Faimma nathhabanna bika fainna minhum muntaqimoona

# 4367

Aw nuriyannaka allathee wa'adnahum fainna 'alayhim muqtadiroona

# 4368

Faistamsik biallathee oohiya ilayka innaka 'ala siratin mustaqeemin

# 4369

Wainnahu lathikrun laka waliqawmika wasawfa tusaloona

# 4370

Waisal man arsana min qablika min rusulina aja'ana min dooni arrahmani alihatan yu'badoona

# 4371

Walaqad arsana moosa biayatina ila fir'awna wamalaihi faqala innee rasoolu rabbi al'alameena

# 4372

Falamma jaahum biayatina itha hum minha yadhakoona

# 4373

Wama nureehim min ayatin illa hiya akbaru min okhtiha waakhathnahum bial'athabi la'allahum yarji'oona

# 4374

Waqaloo ya ayyuha asahiru od'u lana rabbaka bima 'ahida 'indaka innana lamuhtadoona

# 4375

Falamma kashafna 'anhumu al'athaba itha hum yankuthoona

# 4376

Wanada fir'awnu fee qawmihi qala ya qawmi alaysa lee mulku misra wahathihi alanharu tajree min tahtee afala tubsiroona

# 4377

Am ana khayrun min hatha allathee huwa maheenun wala yakadu yubeenu

# 4378

Falawla olqiya 'alayhi aswiratun min thahabin aw jaa ma'ahu almalaikatu muqtarineena

# 4379

Faistakhaffa qawmahu faata'oohu innahum kanoo qawman fasiqeena

# 4380

Falamma asafoona intaqamna minhum faaghraqnahum ajma'eena

# 4381

Faja'anahum salafan wamathalan lilakhireena

# 4382

Walamma duriba ibnu maryama mathalan itha qawmuka minhu yasiddoona

# 4383

Waqaloo aalihatuna khayrun am huwa ma daraboohu laka illa jadalan bal hum qawmun khasimoona

# 4384

In huwa illa 'abdun an'amna 'alayhi waja'anahu mathalan libanee israeela

# 4385

Walaw nashao laja'ana minkum malaikatan fee alardi yakhlufoona

# 4386

Wainnahu la'ilmun lilssa'ati fala tamtarunna biha waittabi'ooni hatha siratun mustaqeemun

# 4387

Wala yasuddannakumu ashshaytanu innahu lakum 'aduwwun mubeenun

# 4388

Walamma jaa 'eesa bialbayyinati qala qad jitukum bialhikmati waliobayyina lakum ba'da allathee takhtalifoona feehi faittaqoo Allaha waatee'ooni

# 4389

Inna Allaha huwa rabbee warabbukum fao'budoohu hatha siratun mustaqeemun

# 4390

Faikhtalafa alahzabu min baynihim fawaylun lillatheena thalamoo min 'athabi yawmin aleemin

# 4391

Hal yanthuroona illa assa'ata an tatiyahum baghtatan wahum la yash'uroona

# 4392

Alakhillao yawmaithin ba'duhum liba'din 'aduwwun illa almuttaqeena

# 4393

Ya 'ibadi la khawfun 'alaykumu alyawma wala antum tahzanoona

# 4394

Allatheena amanoo biayatina wakanoo muslimeena

# 4395

Odkhuloo aljannata antum waazwajukum tuhbaroona

# 4396

# 4397

Watilka aljannatu allatee oorithtumooha bima kuntum ta'maloona

# 4398

Lakum feeha fakihatun katheeratun minha takuloona

# 4399

Inna almujrimeena fee 'athabi jahannama khalidoona

# 4400

La yufattaru 'anhum wahum feehi mublisoona

# 4401

Wama thalamnahum walakin kanoo humu aththalimeena

# 4402

Wanadaw ya maliku liyaqdi 'alayna rabbuka qala innakum makithoona

# 4403

Laqad jinakum bialhaqqi walakinna aktharakum lilhaqqi karihoona

# 4404

Am abramoo amran fainna mubrimoona

# 4405

Am yahsaboona anna la nasma'u sirrahum wanajwahum bala warusuluna ladayhim yaktuboona

# 4406

Qul in kana lilrrahmani waladun faana awwalu al'abideena

# 4407

Subhana rabbi assamawati waalardi rabbi al'arshi 'amma yasifoona

# 4408

Fatharhum yakhoodoo wayal'aboo hatta yulaqoo yawmahumu allathee yoo'adoona

# 4409

Wahuwa allathee fee assamai ilahun wafee alardi ilahun wahuwa alhakeemu al'aleemu

# 4410

Watabaraka allathee lahu mulku assamawati waalardi wama baynahuma wa'indahu 'ilmu assa'ati wailayhi turja'oona

# 4411

# 4412

# 4413

# 4420

# 4421

# 4423

# 4424

# 4425

# 4426

# 4427

# 4428

# 4429

# 4430

# 4431

# 4432

# 4433

# 4434

Wainnee 'uthtu birabbee warabbikum an tarjumooni

# 4435

Wain lam tuminoo lee fai'tazilooni

# 4436

# 4437

# 4438

# 4440

# 4441

Wana'matin kanoo feeha fakiheena

# 4442

# 4443

# 4444

# 4446

# 4447

# 4449

# 4450

# 4451

# 4452

# 4459

# 4464

# 4470

# 4471

# 4475

# 4476

Inna fee assamawati waalardi laayatin lilmumineena

# 4477

Wafee khalqikum wama yabuththu min dabbatin ayatun liqawmin yooqinoona

# 4478

Waikhtilafi allayli waannahari wama anzala Allahu mina assamai min rizqin faahya bihi alarda ba'da mawtiha watasreefi arriyahi ayatun liqawmin ya'qiloona

# 4479

Tilka ayatu Allahi natlooha 'alayka bialhaqqi fabiayyi hadeethin ba'da Allahi waayatihi yuminoona

# 4480

Waylun likulli affakin atheemin

# 4481

Yasma'u ayati Allahi tutla 'alayhi thumma yusirru mustakbiran kaan lam yasma'ha fabashshirhu bi'athabin aleemin

# 4482

Waitha 'alima min ayatina shayan ittakhathaha huzuwan olaika lahum 'athabun muheenun

# 4483

Min waraihim jahannamu wala yughnee 'anhum ma kasaboo shayan wala ma ittakhathoo min dooni Allahi awliyaa walahum 'athabun 'atheemun

# 4484

Hatha hudan waallatheena kafaroo biayati rabbihim lahum 'athabun min rijzin aleemin

# 4485

Allahu allathee sakhkhara lakumu albahra litajriya alfulku feehi biamrihi walitabtaghoo min fadlihi wala'allakum tashkuroona

# 4486

Wasakhkhara lakum ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi jamee'an minhu inna fee thalika laayatin liqawmin yatafakkaroona

# 4487

Qul lillatheena amanoo yaghfiroo lillatheena la yarjoona ayyama Allahi liyajziya qawman bima kanoo yaksiboona

# 4488

Man 'amila salihan falinafsihi waman asaa fa'alayha thumma ila rabbikum turja'oona

# 4489

Walaqad atayna banee israeela alkitaba waalhukma waannubuwwata warazaqnahum mina attayyibati wafaddanahum 'ala al'alameena

# 4490

Waataynahum bayyinatin mina alamri fama ikhtalafoo illa min ba'di ma jaahumu al'ilmu baghyan baynahum inna rabbaka yaqdee baynahum yawma alqiyamati feema kanoo feehi yakhtalifoona

# 4491

Thumma ja'anaka 'ala sharee'atin mina alamri faittabi'ha wala tattabi' ahwaa allatheena la ya'lamoona

# 4492

Innahum lan yughnoo 'anka mina Allahi shayan wainna aththalimeena ba'duhum awliyao ba'din waAllahu waliyyu almuttaqeena

# 4493

Hatha basairu lilnnasi wahudan warahmatun liqawmin yooqinoona

# 4494

Am hasiba allatheena ijtarahoo assayyiati an naj'alahum kaallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati sawaan mahyahum wamamatuhum saa ma yahkumoona

# 4495

Wakhalaqa Allahu assamawati waalarda bialhaqqi walitujza kullu nafsin bima kasabat wahum la yuthlamoona

# 4496

Afaraayta mani ittakhatha ilahahu hawahu waadallahu Allahu 'ala 'ilmin wakhatama 'ala sam'ihi waqalbihi waja'ala 'ala basarihi ghishawatan faman yahdeehi min ba'di Allahi afala tathakkaroona

# 4497

Waqaloo ma hiya illa hayatuna addunya namootu wanahya wama yuhlikuna illa addahru wama lahum bithalika min 'ilmin in hum illa yathunnoona

# 4498

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna bayyinatin ma kana hujjatahum illa an qaloo itoo biabaina in kuntum sadiqeena

# 4499

Quli Allahu yuhyeekum thumma yumeetukum thumma yajma'ukum ila yawmi alqiyamati la rayba feehi walakinna akthara annasi la ya'lamoona

# 4500

Walillahi mulku assamawati waalardi wayawma taqoomu assa'atu yawmaithin yakhsaru almubtiloona

# 4501

Watara kulla ommatin jathiyatan kullu ommatin tud'a ila kitabiha alyawma tujzawna ma kuntum ta'maloona

# 4502

Hatha kitabuna yantiqu 'alaykum bialhaqqi inna kunna nastansikhu ma kuntum ta'maloona

# 4503

Faamma allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati fayudkhiluhum rabbuhum fee rahmatihi thalika huwa alfawzu almubeenu

# 4504

Waamma allatheena kafaroo afalam takun ayatee tutla 'alaykum faistakbartum wakuntum qawman mujrimeena

# 4505

Waitha qeela inna wa'da Allahi haqqun waassa'atu la rayba feeha qultum ma nadree ma assa'atu in nathunnu illa thannan wama nahnu bimustayqineena

# 4506

Wabada lahum sayyiatu ma 'amiloo wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioona

# 4507

Waqeela alyawma nansakum kama naseetum liqaa yawmikum hatha wamawakumu annaru wama lakum min nasireena

# 4508

Thalikum biannakumu ittakhathtum ayati Allahi huzuwan wagharratkumu alhayatu addunya faalyawma la yukhrajoona minha wala hum yusta'taboona

# 4509

Falillahi alhamdu rabbi assamawati warabbi alardi rabbi al'alameena

# 4510

Walahu alkibriyao fee assamawati waalardi wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 4511

Hameem

# 4512

Tanzeelu alkitabi mina Allahi al'azeezi alhakeemi

# 4513

Ma khalaqna assamawati waalarda wama baynahuma illa bialhaqqi waajalin musamman waallatheena kafaroo 'amma onthiroo mu'ridoona

# 4514

Qul araaytum ma tad'oona min dooni Allahi aroonee matha khalaqoo mina alardi am lahum shirkun fee assamawati eetoonee bikitabin min qabli hatha aw atharatin min 'ilmin in kuntum sadiqeena

# 4515

Waman adallu mimman yad'oo min dooni Allahi man la yastajeebu lahu ila yawmi alqiyamati wahum 'an du'aihim ghafiloona

# 4516

Waitha hushira annasu kanoo lahum a'daan wakanoo bi'ibadatihim kafireena

# 4517

Waitha tutla 'alayhim ayatuna bayyinatin qala allatheena kafaroo lilhaqqi lamma jaahum hatha sihrun mubeenun

# 4518

Am yaqooloona iftarahu qul ini iftaraytuhu fala tamlikoona lee mina Allahi shayan huwa a'lamu bima tufeedoona feehi kafa bihi shaheedan baynee wabaynakum wahuwa alghafooru arraheemu

# 4519

Qul ma kuntu bid'an mina arrusuli wama adree ma yuf'alu bee wala bikum in attabi'u illa ma yooha ilayya wama ana illa natheerun mubeenun

# 4520

Qul araaytum in kana min 'indi Allahi wakafartum bihi washahida shahidun min banee israeela 'ala mithlihi faamana waistakbartum inna Allaha la yahdee alqawma aththalimeena

# 4521

Waqala allatheena kafaroo lillatheena amanoo law kana khayran ma sabaqoona ilayhi waith lam yahtadoo bihi fasayaqooloona hatha ifkun qadeemun

# 4522

Wamin qablihi kitabu moosa imaman warahmatan wahatha kitabun musaddiqun lisanan 'arabiyyan liyunthira allatheena thalamoo wabushra lilmuhsineena

# 4523

Inna allatheena qaloo rabbuna Allahu thumma istaqamoo fala khawfun 'alayhim wala hum yahzanoona

# 4524

Olaika ashabu aljannati khalideena feeha jazaan bima kanoo ya'maloona

# 4525

Wawassayna alinsana biwalidayhi ihsanan hamalathu ommuhu kurhan wawada'athu kurhan wahamluhu wafisaluhu thalathoona shahran hatta itha balagha ashuddahu wabalagha arba'eena sanatan qala rabbi awzi'nee an ashkura ni'mataka allatee an'amta 'alayya wa'ala walidayya waan a'mala salihan tardahu waaslih lee fee thurriyyatee innee tubtu ilayka wainnee mina almuslimeena

# 4526

Olaika allatheena nataqabbalu 'anhum ahsana ma 'amiloo wanatajawazu 'an sayyiatihim fee ashabi aljannati wa'da assidqi allathee kanoo yoo'adoona

# 4527

Waallathee qala liwalidayhi offin lakuma ata'idaninee an okhraja waqad khalati alquroonu min qablee wahuma yastagheethani Allaha waylaka amin inna wa'da Allahi haqqun fayaqoolu ma hatha illa asateeru alawwaleena

# 4528

Olaika allatheena haqqa 'alayhimu alqawlu fee umamin qad khalat min qablihim mina aljinni waalinsi innahum kanoo khasireena

# 4529

Walikullin darajatun mimma 'amiloo waliyuwaffiyahum a'malahum wahum la yuthlamoona

# 4530

Wayawma yu'radu allatheena kafaroo 'ala annari athhabtum tayyibatikum fee hayatikumu addunya waistamta'tum biha faalyawma tujzawna 'athaba alhooni bima kuntum tastakbiroona fee alardi bighayri alhaqqi wabima kuntum tafsuqoona

# 4531

Waothkur akha 'adin ith anthara qawmahu bialahqafi waqad khalati annuthuru min bayni yadayhi wamin khalfihi alla ta'budoo illa Allaha innee akhafu 'alaykum 'athaba yawmin 'atheemin

# 4532

Qaloo ajitana litafikana 'an alihatina fatina bima ta'iduna in kunta mina assadiqeena

# 4533

Qala innama al'ilmu 'inda Allahi waoballighukum ma orsiltu bihi walakinnee arakum qawman tajhaloona

# 4534

Falamma raawhu 'aridan mustaqbila awdiyatihim qaloo hatha 'aridun mumtiruna bal huwa ma ista'jatum bihi reehun feeha 'athabun aleemun

# 4535

Tudammiru kulla shayin biamri rabbiha faasbahoo la yura illa masakinuhum kathalika najzee alqawma almujrimeena

# 4536

Walaqad makkannahum feema in makkannakum feehi waja'ana lahum sam'an waabsaran waafidatan fama aghna 'anhum sam'uhum wala absaruhum wala afidatuhum min shayin ith kanoo yajhadoona biayati Allahi wahaqa bihim ma kanoo bihi yastahzioona

# 4537

Walaqad ahlakna ma hawlakum mina alqura wasarrafna alayati la'allahum yarji'oona

# 4538

Falawla nasarahumu allatheena ittakhathoo min dooni Allahi qurbanan alihatan bal dalloo 'anhum wathalika ifkuhum wama kanoo yaftaroona

# 4539

Waith sarafna ilayka nafaran mina aljinni yastami'oona alqurana falamma hadaroohu qaloo ansitoo falamma qudiya wallaw ila qawmihim munthireena

# 4540

Qaloo ya qawmana inna sami'na kitaban onzila min ba'di moosa musaddiqan lima bayna yadayhi yahdee ila alhaqqi waila tareeqin mustaqeemin

# 4541

Ya qawmana ajeeboo da'iya Allahi waaminoo bihi yaghfir lakum min thunoobikum wayujirkum min 'athabin aleemin

# 4542

Waman la yujib da'iya Allahi falaysa bimu'jizin fee alardi walaysa lahu min doonihi awliyaa olaika fee dalalin mubeenin

# 4543

Awalam yaraw anna Allaha allathee khalaqa assamawati waalarda walam ya'ya bikhalqihinna biqadirin 'ala an yuhyiya almawta bala innahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 4544

Wayawma yu'radu allatheena kafaroo 'ala annari alaysa hatha bialhaqqi qaloo bala warabbina qala fathooqoo al'athaba bima kuntum takfuroona

# 4545

Faisbir kama sabara oloo al'azmi mina arrusuli wala tasta'jil lahum kaannahum yawma yarawna ma yoo'adoona lam yalbathoo illa sa'atan min naharin balaghun fahal yuhlaku illa alqawmu alfasiqoona

# 4546

Allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi adalla a'malahum

# 4547

Waallatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati waamanoo bima nuzzila 'ala muhammadin wahuwa alhaqqu min rabbihim kaffara 'anhum sayyiatihim waaslaha balahum

# 4548

Thalika bianna allatheena kafaroo ittaba'oo albatila waanna allatheena amanoo ittaba'oo alhaqqa min rabbihim kathalika yadribu Allahu lilnnasi amthalahum

# 4549

Faitha laqeetumu allatheena kafaroo fadarba arriqabi hatta itha athkhantumoohum fashuddoo alwathaqa faimma mannan ba'du waimma fidaan hatta tada'a alharbu awzaraha thalika walaw yashao Allahu laintasara minhum walakin liyabluwa ba'dakum biba'din waallatheena qutiloo fee sabeeli Allahi falan yudilla a'malahum

# 4550

Sayahdeehim wayuslihu balahum

# 4551

Wayudkhiluhumu aljannata 'arrafaha lahum

# 4552

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo in tansuroo Allaha yansurkum wayuthabbit aqdamakum

# 4553

Waallatheena kafaroo fata'san lahum waadalla a'malahum

# 4554

Thalika biannahum karihoo ma anzala Allahu faahbata a'malahum

# 4555

Afalam yaseeroo fee alardi fayanthuroo kayfa kana 'aqibatu allatheena min qablihim dammara Allahu 'alayhim walilkafireena amthaluha

# 4556

Thalika bianna Allaha mawla allatheena amanoo waanna alkafireena la mawla lahum

# 4557

Inna Allaha yudkhilu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu waallatheena kafaroo yatamatta'oona wayakuloona kama takulu alan'amu waannaru mathwan lahum

# 4558

Wakaayyin min qaryatin hiya ashaddu quwwatan min qaryatika allatee akhrajatka ahlaknahum fala nasira lahum

# 4559

Afaman kana 'ala bayyinatin min rabbihi kaman zuyyina lahu sooo 'amalihi waittaba'oo ahwaahum

# 4560

Mathalu aljannati allatee wu'ida almuttaqoona feeha anharun min main ghayri asinin waanharun min labanin lam yataghayyar ta'muhu waanharun min khamrin laththatin lilshsharibeena waanharun min 'asalin musaffan walahum feeha min kulli aththamarati wamaghfiratun min rabbihim kaman huwa khalidun fee annari wasuqoo maan hameeman faqatta'a am'aahum

# 4561

Waminhum man yastami'u ilayka hatta itha kharajoo min 'indika qaloo lillatheena ootoo al'ilma matha qala anifan olaika allatheena taba'a Allahu 'ala quloobihim waittaba'oo ahwaahum

# 4562

Waallatheena ihtadaw zadahum hudan waatahum taqwahum

# 4563

Fahal yanthuroona illa assa'ata an tatiyahum baghtatan faqad jaa ashratuha faanna lahum itha jaathum thikrahum

# 4564

Fai'lam annahu la ilaha illa Allahu waistaghfir lithanbika walilmumineena waalmuminati waAllahu ya'lamu mutaqallabakum wamathwakum

# 4565

Wayaqoolu allatheena amanoo lawla nuzzilat sooratun faitha onzilat sooratun muhkamatun wathukira feeha alqitalu raayta allatheena fee quloobihim maradun yanthuroona ilayka nathara almaghshiyyi 'alayhi mina almawti faawla lahum

# 4566

Ta'atun waqawlun ma'roofun faitha 'azama alamru falaw sadaqoo Allaha lakana khayran lahum

# 4567

Fahal 'asaytum in tawallaytum an tufsidoo fee alardi watuqatti'oo arhamakum

# 4568

Olaika allatheena la'anahumu Allahu faasammahum waa'ma absarahum

# 4569

Afala yatadabbaroona alqurana am 'ala quloobin aqfaluha

# 4570

Inna allatheena irtaddoo 'ala adbarihim min ba'di ma tabayyana lahumu alhuda ashshaytanu sawwala lahum waamla lahum

# 4571

Thalika biannahum qaloo lillatheena karihoo ma nazzala Allahu sanutee'ukum fee ba'di alamri waAllahu ya'lamu israrahum

# 4572

Fakayfa itha tawaffathumu almalaikatu yadriboona wujoohahum waadbarahum

# 4573

Thalika biannahumu ittaba'oo ma askhata Allaha wakarihoo ridwanahu faahbata a'malahum

# 4574

Am hasiba allatheena fee quloobihim maradun an lan yukhrija Allahu adghanahum

# 4575

Walaw nashao laaraynakahum fala'araftahum biseemahum walata'rifannahum fee lahni alqawli waAllahu ya'lamu a'malakum

# 4576

Walanabluwannakum hatta na'lama almujahideena minkum waassabireena wanabluwa akhbarakum

# 4577

Inna allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi washaqqoo arrasoola min ba'di ma tabayyana lahumu alhuda lan yaduroo Allaha shayan wasayuhbitu a'malahum

# 4578

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo atee'oo Allaha waatee'oo arrasoola wala tubtiloo a'malakum

# 4579

Inna allatheena kafaroo wasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi thumma matoo wahum kuffarun falan yaghfira Allahu lahum

# 4580

Fala tahinoo watad'oo ila assalmi waantumu ala'lawna waAllahu ma'akum walan yatirakum a'malakum

# 4581

Innama alhayatu addunya la'ibun walahwun wain tuminoo watattaqoo yutikum ojoorakum wala yasalkum amwalakum

# 4582

In yasalkumooha fayuhfikum tabkhaloo wayukhrij adghanakum

# 4583

Haantum haolai tud'awna litunfiqoo fee sabeeli Allahi faminkum man yabkhalu waman yabkhal fainnama yabkhalu 'an nafsihi waAllahu alghaniyyu waantumu alfuqarao wain tatawallaw yastabdil qawman ghayrakum thumma la yakoonoo amthalakum

# 4584

Inna fatahna laka fathan mubeenan

# 4585

Liyaghfira laka Allahu ma taqaddama min thanbika wama taakhkhara wayutimma ni'matahu 'alayka wayahdiyaka siratan mustaqeeman

# 4586

Wayansuraka Allahu nasran 'azeezan

# 4587

Huwa allathee anzala assakeenata fee quloobi almumineena liyazdadoo eemanan ma'a eemanihim walillahi junoodu assamawati waalardi wakana Allahu 'aleeman hakeeman

# 4588

Liyudkhila almumineena waalmuminati jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha wayukaffira 'anhum sayyiatihim wakana thalika 'inda Allahi fawzan 'atheeman

# 4589

Wayu'aththiba almunafiqeena waalmunafiqati waalmushrikeena waalmushrikati aththanneena biAllahi thanna assawi 'alayhim dairatu assawi waghadiba Allahu 'alayhim wala'anahum waa'adda lahum jahannama wasaat maseeran

# 4590

Walillahi junoodu assamawati waalardi wakana Allahu 'azeezan hakeeman

# 4591

Inna arsanaka shahidan wamubashshiran wanatheeran

# 4592

Lituminoo biAllahi warasoolihi watu'azziroohu watuwaqqiroohu watusabbihoohu bukratan waaseelan

# 4593

Inna allatheena yubayi'oonaka innama yubayi'oona Allaha yadu Allahi fawqa aydeehim faman nakatha fainnama yankuthu 'ala nafsihi waman awfa bima 'ahada 'alayhu Allaha fasayuteehi ajran 'atheeman

# 4594

Sayaqoolu laka almukhallafoona mina ala'rabi shaghalatna amwaluna waahloona faistaghfir lana yaqooloona biasinatihim ma laysa fee quloobihim qul faman yamliku lakum mina Allahi shayan in arada bikum darran aw arada bikum naf'an bal kana Allahu bima ta'maloona khabeeran

# 4595

Bal thanantum an lan yanqaliba arrasoolu waalmuminoona ila ahleehim abadan wazuyyina thalika fee quloobikum wathanantum thanna assawi wakuntum qawman booran

# 4596

Waman lam yumin biAllahi warasoolihi fainna a'tadna lilkafireena sa'eeran

# 4597

Walillahi mulku assamawati waalardi yaghfiru liman yashao wayu'aththibu man yashao wakana Allahu ghafooran raheeman

# 4598

Sayaqoolu almukhallafoona itha intalaqtum ila maghanima litakhuthooha tharoona nattabi'kum yureedoona an yubaddiloo kalama Allahi qul lan tattabi'oona kathalikum qala Allahu min qablu fasayaqooloona bal tahsudoonana bal kanoo la yafqahoona illa qaleelan

# 4599

Qul lilmukhallafeena mina ala'rabi satud'awna ila qawmin olee basin shadeedin tuqatiloonahum aw yuslimoona fain tutee'oo yutikumu Allahu ajran hasanan wain tatawallaw kama tawallaytum min qablu yu'aththibkum 'athaban aleeman

# 4600

Laysa 'ala ala'ma harajun wala 'ala ala'raji harajun wala 'ala almareedi harajun waman yuti'i Allaha warasoolahu yudkhilhu jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu waman yatawalla yu'aththibhu 'athaban aleeman

# 4601

Laqad radiya Allahu 'ani almumineena ith yubayi'oonaka tahta ashshajarati fa'alima ma fee quloobihim faanzala asakeenata 'alayhim waathabahum fathan qareeban

# 4602

Wamaghanima katheeratan yakhuthoonaha wakana Allahu 'azeezan hakeeman

# 4603

Wa'adakumu Allahu maghanima katheeratan takhuthoonaha fa'ajjala lakum hathihi wakaffa aydiya annasi 'ankum walitakoona ayatan lilmumineena wayahdiyakum siratan mustaqeeman

# 4604

Waokhra lam taqdiroo 'alayha qad ahata Allahu biha wakana Allahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeeran

# 4605

Walaw qatalakumu allatheena kafaroo lawallawoo aladbara thumma la yajidoona waliyyan wala naseeran

# 4606

Sunnata Allahi allatee qad khalat min qablu walan tajida lisunnati Allahi tabdeelan

# 4607

Wahuwa allathee kaffa aydiyahum 'ankum waaydiyakum 'anhum bibatni makkata min ba'di an athfarakum 'alayhim wakana Allahu bima ta'maloona baseeran

# 4608

Humu allatheena kafaroo wasaddookum 'ani almasjidi alharami waalhadya ma'koofan an yablugha mahillahu walawla rijalun muminoona wanisaon muminatun lam ta'lamoohum an tataoohum fatuseebakum minhum ma'arratun bighayri 'ilmin liyudkhila Allahu fee rahmatihi man yashao law tazayyaloo la'aththabna allatheena kafaroo minhum 'athaban aleeman

# 4609

Ith ja'ala allatheena kafaroo fee quloobihimu alhamiyyata hamiyyata aljahiliyyati faanzala Allahu sakeenatahu 'ala rasoolihi wa'ala almumineena waazamahum kalimata attaqwa wakanoo ahaqqa biha waahlaha wakana Allahu bikulli shayin 'aleeman

# 4610

Laqad sadaqa Allahu rasoolahu arruya bialhaqqi latadkhulunna almasjida alharama in shaa Allahu amineena muhalliqeena ruoosakum wamuqassireena la takhafoona fa'alima ma lam ta'lamoo faja'ala min dooni thalika fathan qareeban

# 4611

Huwa allathee arsala rasoolahu bialhuda wadeeni alhaqqi liyuthhirahu 'ala addeeni kullihi wakafa biAllahi shaheedan

# 4612

Muhammadun rasoolu Allahi waallatheena ma'ahu ashiddao 'ala alkuffari ruhamao baynahum tarahum rukka'an sujjadan yabtaghoona fadlan mina Allahi waridwanan seemahum fee wujoohihim min athari assujoodi thalika mathaluhum fee attawrati wamathaluhum fee alinjeeli kazar'in akhraja shatahu faazarahu faistaghlatha faistawa 'ala sooqihi yu'jibu azzurra'a liyagheetha bihimu alkuffara wa'ada Allahu allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati minhum maghfiratan waajran 'atheeman

# 4613

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tuqaddimoo bayna yadayi Allahi warasoolihi waittaqoo Allaha inna Allaha samee'un 'aleemun

# 4614

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tarfa'oo aswatakum fawqa sawti annabiyyi wala tajharoo lahu bialqawli kajahri ba'dikum liba'din an tahbata a'malukum waantum la tash'uroona

# 4615

Inna allatheena yaghuddoona aswatahum 'inda rasooli Allahi olaika allatheena imtahana Allahu quloobahum lilttaqwa lahum maghfiratun waajrun 'atheemun

# 4616

Inna allatheena yunadoonaka min warai alhujurati aktharuhum la ya'qiloona

# 4617

Walaw annahum sabaroo hatta takhruja ilayhim lakana khayran lahum waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun

# 4618

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo in jaakum fasiqun binabain fatabayyanoo an tuseeboo qawman bijahalatin fatusbihoo 'ala ma fa'atum nadimeena

# 4619

Wai'lamoo anna feekum rasoola Allahi law yutee'ukum fee katheerin mina alamri la'anittum walakinna Allaha habbaba ilaykumu aleemana wazayyanahu fee quloobikum wakarraha ilaykumu alkufra waalfusooqa waal'isyana olaika humu arrashidoona

# 4620

Fadlan mina Allahi wani'matan waAllahu 'aleemun hakeemun

# 4621

Wain taifatani mina almumineena iqtataloo faaslihoo baynahuma fain baghat ihdahuma 'ala alokhra faqatiloo allatee tabghee hatta tafeea ila amri Allahi fain faat faaslihoo baynahuma bial'adli waaqsitoo inna Allaha yuhibbu almuqsiteena

# 4622

Innama almuminoona ikhwatun faaslihoo bayna akhawaykum waittaqoo Allaha la'allakum turhamoona

# 4623

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la yaskhar qawmun min qawmin 'asa an yakoonoo khayran minhum wala nisaon min nisain 'asa an yakunna khayran minhunna wala talmizoo anfusakum wala tanabazoo bialalqabi bisa alismu alfusooqu ba'da aleemani waman lam yatub faolaika humu aththalimoona

# 4624

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ijtaniboo katheeran mina aththanni inna ba'da aththanni ithmun wala tajassasoo wala yaghtab ba'dukum ba'dan ayuhibbu ahadukum an yakula lahma akheehi maytan fakarihtumoohu waittaqoo Allaha inna Allaha tawwabun raheemun

# 4625

Ya ayyuha annasu inna khalaqnakum min thakarin waontha waja'anakum shu'ooban waqabaila lita'arafoo inna akramakum 'inda Allahi atqakum inna Allaha 'aleemun khabeerun

# 4626

Qalati ala'rabu amanna qul lam tuminoo walakin qooloo aslamna walamma yadkhuli aleemanu fee quloobikum wain tutee'oo Allaha warasoolahu la yalitkum min a'malikum shayan inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun

# 4627

Innama almuminoona allatheena amanoo biAllahi warasoolihi thumma lam yartaboo wajahadoo biamwalihim waanfusihim fee sabeeli Allahi olaika humu assadiqoona

# 4628

Qul atu'allimoona Allaha bideenikum waAllahu ya'lamu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi waAllahu bikulli shayin 'aleemun

# 4629

Yamunnoona 'alayka an aslamoo qul la tamunnoo 'alayya islamakum bali Allahu yamunnu 'alaykum an hadakum lileemani in kuntum sadiqeena

# 4630

Inna Allaha ya'lamu ghayba assamawati waalardi waAllahu baseerun bima ta'maloona

# 4631

Qaf waalqurani almajeedi

# 4632

Bal 'ajiboo an jaahum munthirun minhum faqala alkafiroona hatha shayon 'ajeebun

# 4633

Aitha mitna wakunna turaban thalika raj'un ba'eedun

# 4634

Qad 'alimna ma tanqusu alardu minhum wa'indana kitabun hafeethun

# 4635

Bal kaththaboo bialhaqqi lamma jaahum fahum fee amrin mareejin

# 4636

Afalam yanthuroo ila assamai fawqahum kayfa banaynaha wazayyannaha wama laha min furoojin

# 4637

Waalarda madadnaha waalqayna feeha rawasiya waanbatna feeha min kulli zawjin baheejin

# 4638

Tabsiratan wathikra likulli 'abdin muneebin

# 4639

Wanazzana mina assamai maan mubarakan faanbatna bihi jannatin wahabba alhaseedi

# 4640

Waannakhla basiqatin laha tal'un nadeedun

# 4641

Rizqan lil'ibadi waahyayna bihi badatan maytan kathalika alkhurooju

# 4642

Kaththabat qablahum qawmu noohin waashabu arrassi wathamoodu

# 4643

Wa'adun wafir'awnu waikhwanu lootin

# 4644

Waashabu alaykati waqawmu tubba'in kullun kaththaba arrusula fahaqqa wa'eedi

# 4645

Afa'ayeena bialkhalqi alawwali bal hum fee labsin min khalqin jadeedin

# 4646

Walaqad khalaqna alinsana wana'lamu ma tuwaswisu bihi nafsuhu wanahnu aqrabu ilayhi min habli alwareedi

# 4647

Ith yatalaqqa almutalaqqiyani 'ani alyameeni wa'ani ashshimali qa'eedun

# 4648

Ma yalfithu min qawlin illa ladayhi raqeebun 'ateedun

# 4649

Wajaat sakratu almawti bialhaqqi thalika ma kunta minhu taheedu

# 4650

Wanufikha fee assoori thalika yawmu alwa'eedi

# 4651

Wajaat kullu nafsin ma'aha saiqun washaheedun

# 4652

Laqad kunta fee ghaflatin min hatha fakashafna 'anka ghitaaka fabasaruka alyawma hadeedun

# 4653

Waqala qareenuhu hatha ma ladayya 'ateedun

# 4654

Alqiya fee jahannama kulla kaffarin 'aneedin

# 4655

Manna'in lilkhayri mu'tadin mureebin

# 4656

Allathee ja'ala ma'a Allahi ilahan akhara faalqiyahu fee al'athabi ashshadeedi

# 4657

Qala qareenuhu rabbana ma atghaytuhu walakin kana fee dalalin ba'eedin

# 4658

Qala la takhtasimoo ladayya waqad qaddamtu ilaykum bialwa'eedi

# 4659

Ma yubaddalu alqawlu ladayya wama ana bithallamin lil'abeedi

# 4660

Yawma naqoolu lijahannama hali imtalati wataqoolu hal min mazeedin

# 4661

Waozlifati aljannatu lilmuttaqeena ghayra ba'eedin

# 4662

Hatha ma too'adoona likulli awwabin hafeethin

# 4663

Man khashiya arrahmana bialghaybi wajaa biqalbin muneebin

# 4664

Odkhulooha bisalamin thalika yawmu alkhuloodi

# 4665

Lahum ma yashaoona feeha waladayna mazeedun

# 4666

Wakam ahlakna qablahum min qarnin hum ashaddu minhum batshan fanaqqaboo fee albiladi hal min maheesin

# 4667

Inna fee thalika lathikra liman kana lahu qalbun aw alqa assam'a wahuwa shaheedun

# 4668

Walaqad khalaqna assamawati waalarda wama baynahuma fee sittati ayyamin wama massana min lughoobin

# 4669

Faisbir 'ala ma yaqooloona wasabbih bihamdi rabbika qabla tuloo'i ashshamsi waqabla alghuroobi

# 4670

Wamina allayli fasabbihhu waadbara assujoodi

# 4671

Waistami' yawma yunadi almunadi min makanin qareebin

# 4672

Yawma yasma'oona assayhata bialhaqqi thalika yawmu alkhurooji

# 4673

Inna nahnu nuhyee wanumeetu wailayna almaseeru

# 4674

Yawma tashaqqaqu alardu 'anhum sira'an thalika hashrun 'alayna yaseerun

# 4675

Nahnu a'lamu bima yaqooloona wama anta 'alayhim bijabbarin fathakkir bialqurani man yakhafu wa'eedi

# 4676

Waaththariyati tharwan

# 4677

Faalhamilati wiqran

# 4678

Faaljariyati yusran

# 4679

# 4680

# 4681

Wainna addeena lawaqi'un

# 4682

Waassamai thati alhubuki

# 4683

Innakum lafee qawlin mukhtalifin

# 4684

Yufaku 'anhu man ofika

# 4685

Qutila alkharrasoona

# 4686

Allatheena hum fee ghamratin sahoona

# 4687

Yasaloona ayyana yawmu addeeni

# 4688

Yawma hum 'ala annari yuftanoona

# 4689

Thooqoo fitnatakum hatha allathee kuntum bihi tasta'jiloona

# 4690

Inna almuttaqeena fee jannatin wa'uyoonin

# 4691

Akhitheena ma atahum rabbuhum innahum kanoo qabla thalika muhsineena

# 4692

Kanoo qaleelan mina allayli ma yahja'oona

# 4693

Wabialashari hum yastaghfiroona

# 4694

Wafee amwalihim haqqun lilssaili waalmahroomi

# 4695

Wafee alardi ayatun lilmooqineena

# 4696

Wafee anfusikum afala tubsiroona

# 4697

Wafee assamai rizqukum wama too'adoona

# 4698

Fawarabbi assamai waalardi innahu lahaqqun mithla ma annakum tantiqoona

# 4699

Hal ataka hadeethu dayfi ibraheema almukrameena

# 4700

Ith dakhaloo 'alayhi faqaloo salaman qala salamun qawmun munkaroona

# 4701

Faragha ila ahlihi fajaa bi'ijlin sameenin
