Hatha nuzuluhum yawma addeeni

# 5036

Nahnu khalaqnakum falawla tusaddiqoona

# 5037

Afaraaytum ma tumnoona

# 5038

Aantum takhluqoonahu am nahnu alkhaliqoona

# 5039

Nahnu qaddarna baynakumu almawta wama nahnu bimasbooqeena

# 5040

'ala an nubaddila amthalakum wanunshiakum fee ma la ta'lamoona

# 5041

Walaqad 'alimtumu annashata aloola falawla tathakkaroona

# 5042

Afaraaytum ma tahruthoona

# 5043

Aantum tazra'oonahu am nahnu azzari'oona

# 5044

Law nashao laja'anahu hutaman fathatum tafakkahoona

# 5045

Inna lamughramoona

# 5046

Bal nahnu mahroomoona

# 5047

Afaraaytumu almaa allathee tashraboona

# 5048

Aantum anzatumoohu mina almuzni am nahnu almunziloona

# 5049

Law nashao ja'anahu ojajan falawla tashkuroona

# 5050

Afaraaytumu annara allatee tooroona

# 5051

Aantum anshatum shajarataha am nahnu almunshioona

# 5052

Nahnu ja'anaha tathkiratan wamata'an lilmuqweena

# 5053

Fasabbih biismi rabbika al'atheemi

# 5054

Fala oqsimu bimawaqi'i annujoomi

# 5055

Wainnahu laqasamun law ta'lamoona 'atheemun

# 5056

Innahu laquranun kareemun

# 5057

Fee kitabin maknoonin

# 5058

La yamassuhu illa almutahharoona

# 5059

Tanzeelun min rabbi al'alameena

# 5060

Afabihatha alhadeethi antum mudhinoona

# 5061

Wataj'aloona rizqakum annakum tukaththiboona

# 5062

Falawla itha balaghati alhulqooma

# 5063

Waantum heenaithin tanthuroona

# 5064

Wanahnu aqrabu ilayhi minkum walakin la tubsiroona

# 5065

Falawla in kuntum ghayra madeeneena

# 5066

Tarji'oonaha in kuntum sadiqeena

# 5067

Faamma in kana mina almuqarrabeena

# 5068

Farawhun warayhanun wajannatu na'eemin

# 5069

Waamma in kana min ashabi alyameeni

# 5070

Fasalamun laka min ashabi alyameeni

# 5071

Waamma in kana mina almukaththibeena addalleena

# 5072

Fanuzulun min hameemin

# 5073

Watasliyatu jaheemin

# 5074

Inna hatha lahuwa haqqu alyaqeeni

# 5075

Fasabbih biismi rabbika al'atheemi

# 5076

Sabbaha lillahi ma fee assamawati waalardi wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 5077

Lahu mulku assamawati waalardi yuhyee wayumeetu wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 5078

Huwa alawwalu waalakhiru waaththahiru waalbatinu wahuwa bikulli shayin 'aleemun

# 5079

Huwa allathee khalaqa assamawati waalarda fee sittati ayyamin thumma istawa 'ala al'arshi ya'lamu ma yaliju fee alardi wama yakhruju minha wama yanzilu mina assamai wama ya'ruju feeha wahuwa ma'akum ayna ma kuntum waAllahu bima ta'maloona baseerun

# 5080

Lahu mulku assamawati waalardi waila Allahi turja'u alomooru

# 5081

Yooliju allayla fee annahari wayooliju annahara fee allayi wahuwa 'aleemun bithati assudoori

# 5082

Aminoo biAllahi warasoolihi waanfiqoo mimma ja'alakum mustakhlafeena feehi faallatheena amanoo minkum waanfaqoo lahum ajrun kabeerun

# 5083

Wama lakum la tuminoona biAllahi waarrasoolu yad'ookum lituminoo birabbikum waqad akhatha meethaqakum in kuntum mumineena

# 5084

Huwa allathee yunazzilu 'ala 'abdihi ayatin bayyinatin liyukhrijakum mina aththulumati ila annoori wainna Allaha bikum laraoofun raheemun

# 5085

Wama lakum alla tunfiqoo fee sabeeli Allahi walillahi meerathu assamawati waalardi la yastawee minkum man anfaqa min qabli alfathi waqatala olaika a'thamu darajatan mina allatheena anfaqoo min ba'du waqataloo wakullan wa'ada Allahu alhusna waAllahu bima ta'maloona khabeerun

# 5086

Man tha allathee yuqridu Allaha qardan hasanan fayuda'ifahu lahu walahu ajrun kareemun

# 5087

Yawma tara almumineena waalmuminati yas'a nooruhum bayna aydeehim wabiaymanihim bushrakumu alyawma jannatun tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha thalika huwa alfawzu al'atheemu

# 5088

Yawma yaqoolu almunafiqoona waalmunafiqatu lillatheena amanoo onthuroona naqtabis min noorikum qeela irji'oo waraakum failtamisoo nooran faduriba baynahum bisoorin lahu babun batinuhu feehi arrahmatu wathahiruhu min qibalihi al'athabu

# 5089

Yunadoonahum alam nakun ma'akum qaloo bala walakinnakum fatantum anfusakum watarabbastum wairtabtum wagharratkumu alamaniyyu hatta jaa amru Allahi wagharrakum biAllahi algharooru

# 5090

Faalyawma la yukhathu minkum fidyatun wala mina allatheena kafaroo mawakumu annaru hiya mawlakum wabisa almaseeru

# 5091

Alam yani lillatheena amanoo an takhsha'a quloobuhum lithikri Allahi wama nazala mina alhaqqi wala yakoonoo kaallatheena ootoo alkitaba min qablu fatala 'alayhimu alamadu faqasat quloobuhum wakatheerun minhum fasiqoona

# 5092

I'lamoo anna Allaha yuhyee alarda ba'da mawtiha qad bayyanna lakumu alayati la'allakum ta'qiloona

# 5093

Inna almussaddiqeena waalmussaddiqati waaqradoo Allaha qardan hasanan yuda'afu lahum walahum ajrun kareemun

# 5094

Waallatheena amanoo biAllahi warusulihi olaika humu assiddeeqoona waashshuhadao 'inda rabbihim lahum ajruhum wanooruhum waallatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina olaika ashabu aljaheemi

# 5095

I'lamoo annama alhayatu addunya la'ibun walahwun wazeenatun watafakhurun baynakum watakathurun fee alamwali waalawladi kamathali ghaythin a'jaba alkuffara nabatuhu thumma yaheeju fatarahu musfarran thumma yakoonu hutaman wafee alakhirati 'athabun shadeedun wamaghfiratun mina Allahi waridwanun wama alhayatu addunya illa mata'u alghuroori

# 5096

Sabiqoo ila maghfiratin min rabbikum wajannatin 'arduha ka'ardi assamai waalardi o'iddat lillatheena amanoo biAllahi warusulihi thalika fadlu Allahi yuteehi man yashao waAllahu thoo alfadli al'atheemi

# 5097

Ma asaba min museebatin fee alardi wala fee anfusikum illa fee kitabin min qabli an nabraaha inna thalika 'ala Allahi yaseerun

# 5098

Likayla tasaw 'ala ma fatakum wala tafrahoo bima atakum waAllahu la yuhibbu kulla mukhtalin fakhoorin

# 5099

Allatheena yabkhaloona wayamuroona annasa bialbukhli waman yatawalla fainna Allaha huwa alghaniyyu alhameedu

# 5100

Laqad arsana rusulana bialbayyinati waanzana ma'ahumu alkitaba waalmeezana liyaqooma annasu bialqisti waanzana alhadeeda feehi basun shadeedun wamanafi'u lilnnasi waliya'lama Allahu man yansuruhu warusulahu bialghaybi inna Allaha qawiyyun 'azeezun

# 5101

Walaqad arsana noohan waibraheema waja'ana fee thurriyyatihima annubuwwata waalkitaba faminhum muhtadin wakatheerun minhum fasiqoona

# 5102

Thumma qaffayna 'ala atharihim birusulina waqaffayna bi'eesa ibni maryama waataynahu alinjeela waja'ana fee quloobi allatheena ittaba'oohu rafatan warahmatan warahbaniyyatan ibtada'ooha ma katabnaha 'alayhim illa ibtighaa ridwani Allahi fama ra'awha haqqa ri'ayatiha faatayna allatheena amanoo minhum ajrahum wakatheerun minhum fasiqoona

# 5103

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha waaminoo birasoolihi yutikum kiflayni min rahmatihi wayaj'al lakum nooran tamshoona bihi wayaghfir lakum waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun

# 5104

Lialla ya'lama ahlu alkitabi alla yaqdiroona 'ala shayin min fadli Allahi waanna alfadla biyadi Allahi yuteehi man yashao waAllahu thoo alfadli al'atheemi

# 5105

Qad sami'a Allahu qawla allatee tujadiluka fee zawjiha watashtakee ila Allahi waAllahu yasma'u tahawurakuma inna Allaha samee'un baseerun

# 5106

Allatheena yuthahiroona minkum min nisaihim ma hunna ommahatihim in ommahatuhum illa allaee waladnahum wainnahum layaqooloona munkaran mina alqawli wazooran wainna Allaha la'afuwwun ghafoorun

# 5107

Waallatheena yuthahiroona min nisaihim thumma ya'oodoona lima qaloo fatahreeru raqabatin min qabli an yatamassa thalikum too'athoona bihi waAllahu bima ta'maloona khabeerun

# 5108

Faman lam yajid fasiyamu shahrayni mutatabi'ayni min qabli an yatamassa faman lam yastati' fait'amu sitteena miskeenan thalika lituminoo biAllahi warasoolihi watilka hudoodu Allahi walilkafireena 'athabun aleemun

# 5109

Inna allatheena yuhaddoona Allaha warasoolahu kubitoo kama kubita allatheena min qablihim waqad anzana ayatin bayyinatin walilkafireena 'athabun muheenun

# 5110

Yawma yab'athuhumu Allahu jamee'an fayunabbiohum bima 'amiloo ahsahu Allahu wanasoohu waAllahu 'ala kulli shayin shaheedun

# 5111

Alam tara anna Allaha ya'lamu ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi ma yakoonu min najwa thalathatin illa huwa rabi'uhum wala khamsatin illa huwa sadisuhum wala adna min thalika wala akthara illa huwa ma'ahum ayna ma kanoo thumma yunabbiohum bima 'amiloo yawma alqiyamati inna Allaha bikulli shayin 'aleemun

# 5112

Alam tara ila allatheena nuhoo 'ani annajwa thumma ya'oodoona lima nuhoo 'anhu wayatanajawna bialithmi waal'udwani wama'siyati arrasooli waitha jaooka hayyawka bima lam yuhayyika bihi Allahu wayaqooloona fee anfusihim lawla yu'aththibuna Allahu bima naqoolu hasbuhum jahannamu yaslawnaha fabisa almaseeru

# 5113

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha tanajaytum fala tatanajaw bialithmi waal'udwani wama'siyati arrasooli watanajaw bialbirri waattaqwa waittaqoo Allaha allathee ilayhi tuhsharoona

# 5114

Innama annajwa mina ashshaytani liyahzuna allatheena amanoo walaysa bidarrihim shayan illa biithni Allahi wa'ala Allahi falyatawakkali almuminoona

# 5115

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha qeela lakum tafassahoo fee almajalisi faifsahoo yafsahi Allahu lakum waitha qeela onshuzoo faonshuzoo yarfa'i Allahu allatheena amanoo minkum waallatheena ootoo al'ilma darajatin waAllahu bima ta'maloona khabeerun

# 5116

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha najaytumu arrasoola faqaddimoo bayna yaday najwakum sadaqatan thalika khayrun lakum waatharu fain lam tajidoo fainna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun

# 5117

Aashfaqtum an tuqaddimoo bayna yaday najwakum sadaqatin faith lam taf'aloo wataba Allahu 'alaykum faaqeemoo assalata waatoo azzakata waatee'oo Allaha warasoolahu waAllahu khabeerun bima ta'maloona

# 5118

Alam tara ila allatheena tawallaw qawman ghadiba Allahu 'alayhim ma hum minkum wala minhum wayahlifoona 'ala alkathibi wahum ya'lamoona

# 5119

a'adda Allahu lahum 'athaban shadeedan innahum saa ma kanoo ya'maloona

# 5120

Ittakhathoo aymanahum junnatan fasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi falahum 'athabun muheenun

# 5121

Lan tughniya 'anhum amwaluhum wala awladuhum mina Allahi shayan olaika ashabu annari hum feeha khalidoona

# 5122

Yawma yab'athuhumu Allahu jamee'an fayahlifoona lahu kama yahlifoona lakum wayahsaboona annahum 'ala shayin ala innahum humu alkathiboona

# 5123

Istahwatha 'alayhimu ashshaytanu faansahum thikra Allahi olaika hizbu ashshaytani ala inna hizba ashshaytani humu alkhasiroona

# 5124

Inna allatheena yuhaddoona Allaha warasoolahu olaika fee alathalleena

# 5125

Kataba Allahu laaghlibanna ana warusulee inna Allaha qawiyyun 'azeezun

# 5126

La tajidu qawman yuminoona biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri yuwaddoona man hadda Allaha warasoolahu walaw kanoo abaahum aw abnaahum aw ikhwanahum aw 'asheeratahum olaika kataba fee quloobihimu aleemana waayyadahum biroohin minhu wayudkhiluhum jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha radiya Allahu 'anhum waradoo 'anhu olaika hizbu Allahi ala inna hizba Allahi humu almuflihoona

# 5127

Sabbaha lillahi ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 5128

Huwa allathee akhraja allatheena kafaroo min ahli alkitabi min diyarihim liawwali alhashri ma thanantum an yakhrujoo wathannoo annahum mani'atuhum husoonuhum mina Allahi faatahumu Allahu min haythu lam yahtasiboo waqathafa fee quloobihimu arru'ba yukhriboona buyootahum biaydeehim waaydee almumineena fai'tabiroo ya olee alabsari

# 5129

Walawla an kataba Allahu 'alayhimu aljalaa la'aththabahum fee addunya walahum fee alakhirati 'athabu annari

# 5130

Thalika biannahum shaqqoo Allaha warasoolahu waman yushaqqi Allaha fainna Allaha shadeedu al'iqabi

# 5131

Ma qata'tum min leenatin aw taraktumooha qaimatan 'ala osooliha fabiithni Allahi waliyukhziya alfasiqeena

# 5132

Wama afaa Allahu 'ala rasoolihi minhum fama awjaftum 'alayhi min khaylin wala rikabin walakinna Allaha yusallitu rusulahu 'ala man yashao waAllahu 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 5133

Ma afaa Allahu 'ala rasoolihi min ahli alqura falillahi walilrrasooli walithee alqurba waalyatama waalmasakeeni waibni assabeeli kay la yakoona doolatan bayna alaghniyai minkum wama atakumu arrasoolu fakhuthoohu wama nahakum 'anhu faintahoo waittaqoo Allaha inna Allaha shadeedu al'iqabi

# 5134

Lilfuqarai almuhajireena allatheena okhrijoo min diyarihim waamwalihim yabtaghoona fadlan mina Allahi waridwanan wayansuroona Allaha warasoolahu olaika humu assadiqoona

# 5135

Waallatheena tabawwaoo addara waaleemana min qablihim yuhibboona man hajara ilayhim wala yajidoona fee sudoorihim hajatan mimma ootoo wayuthiroona 'ala anfusihim walaw kana bihim khasasatun waman yooqa shuhha nafsihi faolaika humu almuflihoona

# 5136

Waallatheena jaoo min ba'dihim yaqooloona rabbana ighfir lana waliikhwanina allatheena sabaqoona bialeemani wala taj'al fee quloobina ghillan lillatheena amanoo rabbana innaka raoofun raheemun

# 5137

Alam tara ila allatheena nafaqoo yaqooloona liikhwanihimu allatheena kafaroo min ahli alkitabi lain okhrijtum lanakhrujanna ma'akum wala nutee'u feekum ahadan abadan wain qootiltum lanansurannakum waAllahu yashhadu innahum lakathiboona

# 5138

Lain okhrijoo la yakhrujoona ma'ahum walain qootiloo la yansuroonahum walain nasaroohum layuwallunna aladbara thumma la yunsaroona

# 5139

Laantum ashaddu rahbatan fee sudoorihim mina Allahi thalika biannahum qawmun la yafqahoona

# 5140

La yuqatiloonakum jamee'an illa fee quran muhassanatin aw min warai judurin basuhum baynahum shadeedun tahsabuhum jamee'an waquloobuhum shatta thalika biannahum qawmun la ya'qiloona

# 5141

Kamathali allatheena min qablihim qareeban thaqoo wabala amrihim walahum 'athabun aleemun

# 5142

Kamathali ashshaytani ith qala lilinsani okfur falamma kafara qala innee bareeon minka innee akhafu Allaha rabba al'alameena

# 5143

Fakana 'aqibatahuma annahuma fee annari khalidayni feeha wathalika jazao aththalimeena

# 5144

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo ittaqoo Allaha watanthur nafsun ma qaddamat lighadin waittaqoo Allaha inna Allaha khabeerun bima ta'maloona

# 5145

Wala takoonoo kaallatheena nasoo Allaha faansahum anfusahum olaika humu alfasiqoona

# 5146

La yastawee ashabu annari waashabu aljannati ashabu aljannati humu alfaizoona

# 5147

Law anzana hatha alqurana 'ala jabalin laraaytahu khashi'an mutasaddi'an min khashyati Allahi watilka alamthalu nadribuha lilnnasi la'allahum yatafakkaroona

# 5148

Huwa Allahu allathee la ilaha illa huwa 'alimu alghaybi waashshahadati huwa arrahmanu arraheemu

# 5149

Huwa Allahu allathee la ilaha illa huwa almaliku alquddoosu assalamu almuminu almuhayminu al'azeezu aljabbaru almutakabbiru subhana Allahi 'amma yushrikoona

# 5150

Huwa Allahu alkhaliqu albario almusawwiru lahu alasmao alhusna yusabbihu lahu ma fee assamawati waalardi wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 5151

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tattakhithoo 'aduwwee wa'aduwwakum awliyaa tulqoona ilayhim bialmawaddati waqad kafaroo bima jaakum mina alhaqqi yukhrijoona arrasoola waiyyakum an tuminoo biAllahi rabbikum in kuntum kharajtum jihadan fee sabeelee waibtighaa mardatee tusirroona ilayhim bialmawaddati waana a'lamu bima akhfaytum wama a'lantum waman yaf'alhu minkum faqad dalla sawaa assabeeli

# 5152

In yathqafookum yakoonoo lakam a'daan wayabsutoo ilaykum aydiyahum waasinatahum biassooi wawaddoo law takfuroona

# 5153

Lan tanfa'akum arhamukum wala awladukum yawma alqiyamati yafsilu baynakum waAllahu bima ta'maloona baseerun

# 5154

Qad kanat lakum oswatun hasanatun fee ibraheema waallatheena ma'ahu ith qaloo liqawmihim inna buraao minkum wamimma ta'budoona min dooni Allahi kafarna bikum wabada baynana wabaynakumu al'adawatu waalbaghdao abadan hatta tuminoo biAllahi wahdahu illa qawla ibraheema liabeehi laastaghfiranna laka wama amliku laka mina Allahi min shayin rabbana 'alayka tawakkana wailayka anabna wailayka almaseeru

# 5155

Rabbana la taj'ana fitnatan lillatheena kafaroo waighfir lana rabbana innaka anta al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 5156

Laqad kana lakum feehim oswatun hasanatun liman kana yarjoo Allaha waalyawma alakhira waman yatawalla fainna Allaha huwa alghanniyyu alhameedu

# 5157

'asa Allahu an yaj'ala baynakum wabayna allatheena 'adaytum minhum mawaddatan waAllahu qadeerun waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun

# 5158

La yanhakumu Allahu 'ani allatheena lam yuqatilookum fee addeeni walam yukhrijookum min diyarikum an tabarroohum watuqsitoo ilayhim inna Allaha yuhibbu almuqsiteena

# 5159

Innama yanhakumu Allahu 'ani allatheena qatalookum fee addeeni waakhrajookum min diyarikum wathaharoo 'ala ikhrajikum an tawallawhum waman yatawallahum faolaika humu aththalimoona

# 5160

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha jaakumu almuminatu muhajiratin faimtahinoohunna Allahu a'lamu bieemanihinna fain 'alimtumoohunna muminatin fala tarji'oohunna ila alkuffari la hunna hillun lahum wala hum yahilloona lahunna waatoohum ma anfaqoo wala junaha 'alaykum an tankihoohunna itha ataytumoohunna ojoorahunna wala tumsikoo bi'isami alkawafiri waisaloo ma anfaqtum walyasaloo ma anfaqoo thalikum hukmu Allahi yahkumu baynakum waAllahu 'aleemun hakeemun

# 5161

Wain fatakum shayon min azwajikum ila alkuffari fa'aqabtum faatoo allatheena thahabat azwajuhum mithla ma anfaqoo waittaqoo Allaha allathee antum bihi muminoona

# 5162

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu itha jaaka almuminatu yubayi'naka 'ala an la yushrikna biAllahi shayan wala yasriqna wala yazneena wala yaqtulna awladahunna wala yateena bibuhtanin yaftareenahu bayna aydeehinna waarjulihinna wala ya'seenaka fee ma'roofin fabayi'hunna waistaghfir lahunna Allaha inna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun

# 5163

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tatawallaw qawman ghadiba Allahu 'alayhim qad yaisoo mina alakhirati kama yaisa alkuffaru min ashabi alquboori

# 5164

Sabbaha lillahi ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 5165

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo lima taqooloona ma la taf'aloona

# 5166

Kabura maqtan 'inda Allahi an taqooloo ma la taf'aloona

# 5167

Inna Allaha yuhibbu allatheena yuqatiloona fee sabeelihi saffan kaannahum bunyanun marsoosun

# 5168

Waith qala moosa liqawmihi ya qawmi lima tuthoonanee waqad ta'lamoona annee rasoolu Allahi ilaykum falamma zaghoo azagha Allahu quloobahum waAllahu la yahdee alqawma alfasiqeena

# 5169

Waith qala 'eesa ibnu maryama ya banee israeela innee rasoolu Allahi ilaykum musaddiqan lima bayna yadayya mina attawrati wamubashshiran birasoolin yatee min ba'dee ismuhu ahmadu falamma jaahum bialbayyinati qaloo hatha sihrun mubeenun

# 5170

Waman athlamu mimmani iftara 'ala Allahi alkathiba wahuwa yud'a ila alislami waAllahu la yahdee alqawma aththalimeena

# 5171

Yureedoona liyutfioo noora Allahi biafwahihim waAllahu mutimmu noorihi walaw kariha alkafiroona

# 5172

Huwa allathee arsala rasoolahu bialhuda wadeeni alhaqqi liyuthhirahu 'ala addeeni kullihi walaw kariha almushrikoona

# 5173

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo hal adullukum 'ala tijaratin tunjeekum min 'athabin aleemin

# 5174

Tuminoona biAllahi warasoolihi watujahidoona fee sabeeli Allahi biamwalikum waanfusikum thalikum khayrun lakum in kuntum ta'lamoona

# 5175

Yaghfir lakum thunoobakum wayudkhilkum jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu wamasakina tayyibatan fee jannati 'adnin thalika alfawzu al'atheemu

# 5176

Waokhra tuhibboonaha nasrun mina Allahi wafathun qarreebun wabashshiri almumineena

# 5177

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo koonoo ansara Allahi kama qala 'eesa ibnu maryama lilhawariyyeena man ansaree ila Allahi qala alhawariyyoona nahnu ansaru Allahi faamanat taifatun min banee israeela wakafarat taifatun faayyadna allatheena amanoo 'ala 'aduwwihim faasbahoo thahireena

# 5178

Yusabbihu lillahi ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi almaliki alquddoosi al'azeezi alhakeemi

# 5179

Huwa allathee ba'atha fee alommiyyeena rasoolan minhum yatloo 'alayhim ayatihi wayuzakkeehim wayu'allimuhumu alkitaba waalhikmata wain kanoo min qablu lafee dalalin mubeenin

# 5180

Waakhareena minhum lamma yalhaqoo bihim wahuwa al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 5181

Thalika fadlu Allahi yuteehi man yashao waAllahu thoo alfadli al'atheemi

# 5182

Mathalu allatheena hummiloo attawrata thumma lam yahmilooha kamathali alhimari yahmilu asfaran bisa mathalu alqawmi allatheena kaththaboo biayati Allahi waAllahu la yahdee alqawma aththalimeena

# 5183

Qul ya ayyuha allatheena hadoo in za'amtum annakum awliyao lillahi min dooni annasi fatamannawoo almawta in kuntum sadiqeena

# 5184

Wala yatamannawnahu abadan bima qaddamat aydeehim waAllahu 'aleemun biaththalimeena

# 5185

Qul inna almawta allathee tafirroona minhu fainnahu mulaqeekum thumma turaddoona ila 'alimi alghaybi waashshahadati fayunabbiokum bima kuntum ta'maloona

# 5186

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo itha noodiya lilssalati min yawmi aljumu'ati fais'aw ila thikri Allahi watharoo albay'a thalikum khayrun lakum in kuntum ta'lamoona

# 5187

Faitha qudiyati assalatu faintashiroo fee alardi waibtaghoo min fadli Allahi waothkuroo Allaha katheeran la'allakum tuflihoona

# 5188

Waitha raaw tijaratan aw lahwan infaddoo ilayha watarakooka qaiman qul ma 'inda Allahi khayrun mina allahwi wamina attijarati waAllahu khayru arraziqeena

# 5189

Itha jaaka almunafiqoona qaloo nashhadu innaka larasoolu Allahi waAllahu ya'lamu innaka larasooluhu waAllahu yashhadu inna almunafiqeena lakathiboona

# 5190

Ittakhathoo aymanahum junnatan fasaddoo 'an sabeeli Allahi innahum saa ma kanoo ya'maloona

# 5191

Thalika biannahum amanoo thumma kafaroo fatubi'a 'ala quloobihim fahum la yafqahoona

# 5192

Waitha raaytahum tu'jibuka ajsamuhum wain yaqooloo tasma' liqawlihim kaannahum khushubun musannadatun yahsaboona kulla sayhatin 'alayhim humu al'aduwwu faihtharhum qatalahumu Allahu anna yufakoona

# 5193

Waitha qeela lahum ta'alaw yastaghfir lakum rasoolu Allahi lawwaw ruoosahum waraaytahum yasuddoona wahum mustakbiroona

# 5194

Sawaon 'alayhim astaghfarta lahum am lam tastaghfir lahum lan yaghfira Allahu lahum inna Allaha la yahdee alqawma alfasiqeena

# 5195

Humu allatheena yaqooloona la tunfiqoo 'ala man 'inda rasooli Allahi hatta yanfaddoo walillahi khazainu assamawati waalardi walakinna almunafiqeena la yafqahoona

# 5196

Yaqooloona lain raja'na ila almadeenati layukhrijanna ala'azzu minha alathalla walillahi al'izzatu walirasoolihi walilmumineena walakinna almunafiqeena la ya'lamoona

# 5197

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo la tulhikum amwalukum wala awladukum 'an thikri Allahi waman yaf'al thalika faolaika humu alkhasiroona

# 5198

Waanfiqoo min ma razaqnakum min qabli an yatiya ahadakumu almawtu fayaqoola rabbi lawla akhkhartanee ila ajalin qareebin faassaddaqa waakun mina assaliheena

# 5199

Walan yuakhkhira Allahu nafsan itha jaa ajaluha waAllahu khabeerun bima ta'maloona

# 5200

Yusabbihu lillahi ma fee assamawati wama fee alardi lahu almulku walahu alhamdu wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 5201

Huwa allathee khalaqakum faminkum kafirun waminkum muminun waAllahu bima ta'maloona baseerun

# 5202

Khalaqa assamawati waalarda bialhaqqi wasawwarakum faahsana suwarakum wailayhi almaseeru

# 5203

Ya'lamu ma fee assamawati waalardi waya'lamu ma tusirroona wama tu'linoona waAllahu 'aleemun bithati assudoori

# 5204

Alam yatikum nabao allatheena kafaroo min qablu fathaqoo wabala amrihim walahum 'athabun aleemun

# 5205

Thalika biannahu kanat tateehim rusuluhum bialbayyinati faqaloo abasharun yahdoonana fakafaroo watawallaw waistaghna Allahu waAllahu ghaniyyun hameedun

# 5206

Za'ama allatheena kafaroo an lan yub'athoo qul bala warabbee latub'athunna thumma latunabbaonna bima 'amiltum wathalika 'ala Allahi yaseerun

# 5207

Faaminoo biAllahi warasoolihi waannoori allathee anzana waAllahu bima ta'maloona khabeerun

# 5208

Yawma yajma'ukum liyawmi aljam'i thalika yawmu attaghabuni waman yumin biAllahi waya'mal salihan yukaffir 'anhu sayyiatihi wayudkhilhu jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha abadan thalika alfawzu al'atheemu

# 5209

Waallatheena kafaroo wakaththaboo biayatina olaika ashabu annari khalideena feeha wabisa almaseeru

# 5210

Ma asaba min museebatin illa biithni Allahi waman yumin biAllahi yahdi qalbahu waAllahu bikulli shayin 'aleemun

# 5211

Waatee'oo Allaha waatee'oo arrasoola fain tawallaytum fainnama 'ala rasoolina albalaghu almubeenu

# 5212

Allahu la ilaha illa huwa wa'ala Allahi falyatawakkali almuminoona

# 5213

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo inna min azwajikum waawladikum 'aduwwan lakum faihtharoohum wain ta'foo watasfahoo wataghfiroo fainna Allaha ghafoorun raheemun

# 5214

Innama amwalukum waawladukum fitnatun waAllahu 'indahu ajrun 'atheemun

# 5215

Faittaqoo Allaha ma istata'tum waisma'oo waatee'oo waanfiqoo khayran lianfusikum waman yooqa shuhha nafsihi faolaika humu almuflihoona

# 5216

In tuqridoo Allaha qardan hasanan yuda'ifhu lakum wayaghfir lakum waAllahu shakoorun haleemun

# 5217

'alimu alghaybi waashshahadati al'azeezu alhakeemu

# 5218

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu itha tallaqtumu annisaa fatalliqoohunna li'iddatihinna waahsoo al'iddata waittaqoo Allaha rabbakum la tukhrijoohunna min buyootihinna wala yakhrujna illa an yateena bifahishatin mubayyinatin watilka hudoodu Allahi waman yata'adda hudooda Allahi faqad thalama nafsahu la tadree la'alla Allaha yuhdithu ba'da thalika amran

# 5219

Faitha balaghna ajalahunna faamsikoohunna bima'roofin aw fariqoohunna bima'roofin waashhidoo thaway 'adlin minkum waaqeemoo ashshahadata lillahi thalikum yoo'athu bihi man kana yuminu biAllahi waalyawmi alakhiri waman yattaqi Allaha yaj'al lahu makhrajan

# 5220

Wayarzuqhu min haythu la yahtasibu waman yatawakkal 'ala Allahi fahuwa hasbuhu inna Allaha balighu amrihi qad ja'ala Allahu likulli shayin qadran

# 5221

Waallaee yaisna mina almaheedi min nisaikum ini irtabtum fa'iddatuhunna thalathatu ashhurin waallaee lam yahidna waolatu alahmali ajaluhunna an yada'na hamlahunna waman yattaqi Allaha yaj'al lahu min amrihi yusran

# 5222

Thalika amru Allahi anzalahu ilaykum waman yattaqi Allaha yukaffir 'anhu sayyiatihi wayu'thim lahu ajran

# 5223

Askinoohunna min haythu sakantum min wujdikum wala tudarroohunna litudayyiqoo 'alayhinna wain kunna olati hamlin faanfiqoo 'alayhinna hatta yada'na hamlahunna fain arda'na lakum faatoohunna ojoorahunna watamiroo baynakum bima'roofin wain ta'asartum fasaturdi'u lahu okhra

# 5224

Liyunfiq thoo sa'atin min sa'atihi waman qudira 'alayhi rizquhu falyunfiq mimma atahu Allahu la yukallifu Allahu nafsan illa ma ataha sayaj'alu Allahu ba'da 'usrin yusran

# 5225

Wakaayyin min qaryatin 'atat 'an amri rabbiha warusulihi fahasabnaha hisaban shadeedan wa'aththabnaha 'athaban nukran

# 5226

Fathaqat wabala amriha wakana 'aqibatu amriha khusran

# 5227

a'adda Allahu lahum 'athaban shadeedan faittaqoo Allaha ya olee alalbabi allatheena amanoo qad anzala Allahu ilaykum thikran

# 5228

Rasoolan yatloo 'alaykum ayati Allahi mubayyinatin liyukhrija allatheena amanoo wa'amiloo assalihati mina aththulumati ila annoori waman yumin biAllahi waya'mal salihan yudkhilhu jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu khalideena feeha abadan qad ahsana Allahu lahu rizqan

# 5229

Allahu allathee khalaqa sab'a samawatin wamina alardi mithlahunna yatanazzalu alamru baynahunna lita'lamoo anna Allaha 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun waanna Allaha qad ahata bikulli shayin 'ilman

# 5230

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu lima tuharrimu ma ahalla Allahu laka tabtaghee mardata azwajika waAllahu ghafoorun raheemun

# 5231

Qad farada Allahu lakum tahillata aymanikum waAllahu mawlakum wahuwa al'aleemu alhakeemu

# 5232

Waith asarra annabiyyu ila ba'di azwajihi hadeethan falamma nabbaat bihi waathharahu Allahu 'alayhi 'arrafa ba'dahu waa'rada 'an ba'din falamma nabbaaha bihi qalat man anbaaka hatha qala nabbaaniya al'aleemu alkhabeeru

# 5233

In tatooba ila Allahi faqad saghat quloobukuma wain tathahara 'alayhi fainna Allaha huwa mawlahu wajibreelu wasalihu almumineena waalmalaikatu ba'da thalika thaheerun

# 5234

'asa rabbuhu in tallaqakunna an yubdilahu azwajan khayran minkunna muslimatin muminatin qanitatin taibatin 'abidatin saihatin thayyibatin waabkaran

# 5235

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo qoo anfusakum waahleekum naran waqooduha annasu waalhijaratu 'alayha malaikatun ghilathun shidadun la ya'soona Allaha ma amarahum wayaf'aloona ma yumaroona

# 5236

Ya ayyuha allatheena kafaroo la ta'tathiroo alyawma innama tujzawna ma kuntum ta'maloona

# 5237

Ya ayyuha allatheena amanoo tooboo ila Allahi tawbatan nasoohan 'asa rabbukum an yukaffira 'ankum sayyiatikum wayudkhilakum jannatin tajree min tahtiha alanharu yawma la yukhzee Allahu annabiyya waallatheena amanoo ma'ahu nooruhum yas'a bayna aydeehim wabiaymanihim yaqooloona rabbana atmim lana noorana waighfir lana innaka 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 5238

Ya ayyuha annabiyyu jahidi alkuffara waalmunafiqeena waoghluth 'alayhim wamawahum jahannamu wabisa almaseeru

# 5239

Daraba Allahu mathalan lillatheena kafaroo imraata noohin waimraata lootin kanata tahta 'abdayni min 'ibadina salihayni fakhanatahuma falam yughniya 'anhuma mina Allahi shayan waqeela odkhula annara ma'a addakhileena

# 5240

Wadaraba Allahu mathalan lillatheena amanoo imraata fir'awna ith qalat rabbi ibni lee 'indaka baytan fee aljannati wanajjinee min fir'awna wa'amalihi wanajjinee mina alqawmi aththalimeena

# 5241

Wamaryama ibnata 'imrana allatee ahsanat farjaha fanafakhna feehi min roohina wasaddaqat bikalimati rabbiha wakutubihi wakanat mina alqaniteena

# 5242

Tabaraka allathee biyadihi almulku wahuwa 'ala kulli shayin qadeerun

# 5243

Allathee khalaqa almawta waalhayata liyabluwakum ayyukum ahsanu 'amalan wahuwa al'azeezu alghafooru

# 5244

Allathee khalaqa sab'a samawatin tibaqan ma tara fee khalqi arrahmani min tafawutin fairji'i albasara hal tara min futoorin

# 5245

Thumma irji'i albasara karratayni yanqalib ilayka albasaru khasian wahuwa haseerun

# 5246

Walaqad zayyanna assamaa addunya bimasabeeha waja'anaha rujooman lilshshayateeni waa'tadna lahum 'athaba assa'eeri

# 5247

Walillatheena kafaroo birabbihim 'athabu jahannama wabisa almaseeru

# 5248

Itha olqoo feeha sami'oo laha shaheeqan wahiya tafooru

# 5249

Takadu tamayyazu mina alghaythi kullama olqiya feeha fawjun saalahum khazanatuha alam yatikum natheerun

# 5250

Qaloo bala qad jaana natheerun fakaththabna waqulna ma nazzala Allahu min shayin in antum illa fee dalalin kabeerin

# 5251

Waqaloo law kunna nasma'u aw na'qilu ma kunna fee ashabi assa'eeri

# 5252

Fai'tarafoo bithanbihim fasuhqan liashabi assa'eeri

# 5253

Inna allatheena yakhshawna rabbahum bialghaybi lahum maghfiratun waajrun kabeerun

# 5254

Waasirroo qawlakum awi ijharoo bihi innahu 'aleemun bithati assudoori

# 5255

Ala ya'lamu man khalaqa wahuwa allateefu alkhabeeru

# 5256

Huwa allathee ja'ala lakumu alarda thaloolan faimshoo fee manakibiha wakuloo min rizqihi wailayhi annushooru

# 5257

Aamintum man fee assamai an yakhsifa bikumu alarda faitha hiya tamooru

# 5258

Am amintum man fee assamai an yursila 'alaykum hasiban fasata'lamoona kayfa natheeri

# 5259

Walaqad kaththaba allatheena min qablihim fakayfa kana nakeeri

# 5260

Awalam yaraw ila attayri fawqahum saffatin wayaqbidna ma yumsikuhunna illa arrahmanu innahu bikulli shayin baseerun

# 5261

Amman hatha allathee huwa jundun lakum yansurukum min dooni arrahmani ini alkafiroona illa fee ghuroorin

# 5262

Amman hatha allathee yarzuqukum in amsaka rizqahu bal lajjoo fee 'utuwwin wanufoorin

# 5263

Afaman yamshee mukibban 'ala wajhihi ahda amman yamshee sawiyyan 'ala siratin mustaqeemin

# 5264

Qul huwa allathee anshaakum waja'ala lakumu assam'a waalabsara waalafidata qaleelan ma tashkuroona

# 5265

Qul huwa allathee tharaakum fee alardi wailayhi tuhsharoona

# 5266

Wayaqooloona mata hatha alwa'du in kuntum sadiqeena

# 5267

Qul innama al'ilmu 'inda Allahi wainnama ana natheerun mubeenun

# 5268

Falamma raawhu zulfatan seeat wujoohu allatheena kafaroo waqeela hatha allathee kuntum bihi tadda'oona

# 5269

Qul araaytum in ahlakaniya Allahu waman ma'iya aw rahimana faman yujeeru alkafireena min 'athabin aleemin

# 5270

Qul huwa arrahmanu amanna bihi wa'alayhi tawakkana fasata'lamoona man huwa fee dalalin mubeenin

# 5271

Qul araaytum in asbaha maokum ghawran faman yateekum bimain ma'eenin

# 5272

Noon waalqalami wama yasturoona

# 5273

Ma anta bini'mati rabbika bimajnoonin

# 5274

Wainna laka laajran ghayra mamnoonin

# 5275

Wainnaka la'ala khuluqin 'atheemin

# 5276

Fasatubsiru wayubsiroona

# 5277

Biayyikumu almaftoonu

# 5278

Inna rabbaka huwa a'lamu biman dalla 'an sabeelihi wahuwa a'lamu bialmuhtadeena

# 5279

Fala tuti'i almukaththibeena

# 5280

Waddoo law tudhinu fayudhinoona

# 5281

Wala tuti' kulla hallafin maheenin

# 5282

Hammazin mashshain binameemin

# 5283

Manna'in lilkhayri mu'tadin atheemin

# 5284

'utullin ba'da thalika zaneemin

# 5285

An kana tha malin wabaneena

# 5286

Itha tutla 'alayhi ayatuna qala asateeru alawwaleena

# 5287

Sanasimuhu 'ala alkhurtoomi

# 5288

Inna balawnahum kama balawna ashaba aljannati ith aqsamoo layasrimunnaha musbiheena

# 5289

Wala yastathnoona

# 5290

Fatafa 'alayha taifun min rabbika wahum naimoona

# 5291

Faasbahat kaassareemi

# 5292

Fatanadaw musbiheena

# 5293

Ani ighdoo 'ala harthikum in kuntum sarimeena

# 5294

Faintalaqoo wahum yatakhafatoona

# 5295

An la yadkhulannaha alyawma 'alaykum miskeenun

# 5296

Waghadaw 'ala hardin qadireena

# 5297

Falamma raawha qaloo inna ladalloona

# 5298

Bal nahnu mahroomoona

# 5299

Qala awsatuhum alam aqul lakum lawla tusabbihoona

# 5300

Qaloo subhana rabbina inna kunna thalimeena

# 5301

Faaqbala ba'duhum 'ala ba'din yatalawamoona

# 5302

Qaloo ya waylana inna kunna tagheena

# 5303

'asa rabbuna an yubdilana khayran minha inna ila rabbina raghiboona

# 5304

Kathalika al'athabu wala'athabu alakhirati akbaru law kanoo ya'lamoona

# 5305

Inna lilmuttaqeena 'inda rabbihim jannati anna'eemi

# 5306

Afanaj'alu almuslimeena kaalmujrimeena

# 5307

Ma lakum kayfa tahkumoona

# 5308

Am lakum kitabun feehi tadrusoona

# 5309

Inna lakum feehi lama takhayyaroona

# 5310

Am lakum aymanun 'alayna balighatun ila yawmi alqiyamati inna lakum lama tahkumoona

# 5311

Salhum ayyuhum bithalika za'eemun

# 5312

Am lahum shurakao falyatoo bishurakaihim in kanoo sadiqeena

# 5313

Yawma yukshafu 'an saqin wayud'awna ila assujoodi fala yastatee'oona

# 5314

Khashi'atan absaruhum tarhaquhum thillatun waqad kanoo yud'awna ila assujoodi wahum salimoona

# 5315

Fatharnee waman yukaththibu bihatha alhadeethi sanastadrijuhum min haythu la ya'lamoona

# 5316

Waomlee lahum inna kaydee mateenun

# 5317

Am tasaluhum ajran fahum min maghramin muthqaloona

# 5318

Am 'indahumu alghaybu fahum yaktuboona

# 5319

Faisbir lihukmi rabbika wala takun kasahibi alhooti ith nada wahuwa makthoomun

# 5320

Lawla an tadarakahu ni'matun min rabbihi lanubitha bial'arai wahuwa mathmoomun

# 5321

Faijtabahu rabbuhu faja'alahu mina assaliheena

# 5322

Wain yakadu allatheena kafaroo layuzliqoonaka biabsarihim lamma sami'oo aththikra wayaqooloona innahu lamajnoonun

# 5323

Wama huwa illa thikrun lil'alameena

# 5324

Alhaqqatu

# 5325

Ma alhaqqatu

# 5326

Wama adraka ma alhaqqatu

# 5327

Kaththabat thamoodu wa'adun bialqari'ati

# 5328

Faamma thamoodu faohlikoo biattaghiyati

# 5329

Waamma 'adun faohlikoo bireehin sarsarin 'atiyatin

# 5330

Sakhkharaha 'alayhim sab'a layalin wathamaniyata ayyamin husooman fatara alqawma feeha sar'a kaannahum a'jazu nakhlin khawiyatun

# 5331

Fahal tara lahum min baqiyatin

# 5332

Wajaa fir'awnu waman qablahu waalmutafikatu bialkhatiati

# 5333

Fa'asaw rasoola rabbihim faakhathahum akhthatan rabiyatan

# 5334

Inna lamma tagha almao hamanakum fee aljariyati

# 5335

Linaj'alaha lakum tathkiratan wata'iyaha othunun wa'iyatun

# 5336

Faitha nufikha fee assoori nafkhatun wahidatun

# 5337

Wahumilati alardu waaljibalu fadukkata dakkatan wahidatan

# 5338

Fayawmaithin waqa'ati alwaqi'atu

# 5339

Wainshaqqati assamao fahiya yawmaithin wahiyatun

# 5340

Waalmalaku 'ala arjaiha wayahmilu 'arsha rabbika fawqahum yawmaithin thamaniyatun

# 5341

Yawmaithin tu'radoona la takhfa minkum khafiyatun

# 5342

Faamma man ootiya kitabahu biyameenihi fayaqoolu haomu iqraoo kitabiyah

# 5343

Innee thanantu annee mulaqin hisabiyah

# 5344

Fahuwa fee 'eeshatin radiyatin

# 5345

Fee jannatin 'aliyatin

# 5346

Qutoofuha daniyatun

# 5347

Kuloo waishraboo haneean bima aslaftum fee alayyami alkhaliyati

# 5348

Waamma man ootiya kitabahu bishimalihi fayaqoolu ya laytanee lam oota kitabiyah

# 5349

Walam adri ma hisabiyah

# 5350

Ya laytaha kanati alqadiyatu

# 5351

Ma aghna 'annee maliyah

# 5352

Halaka 'annee sultaniyah

# 5353

Khuthoohu faghulloohu

# 5354

Thumma aljaheema salloohu

# 5355

Thumma fee silsilatin thar'uha sab'oona thira'an faoslukoohu

# 5356

Innahu kana la yuminu biAllahi al'atheemi

# 5357

Wala yahuddu 'ala ta'ami almiskeeni

# 5358

Falaysa lahu alyawma hahuna hameemun

# 5359

Wala ta'amun illa min ghisleenin

# 5360

La yakuluhu illa alkhatioona

# 5361

Fala oqsimu bima tubsiroona

# 5362

Wama la tubsiroona

# 5363

Innahu laqawlu rasoolin kareemin

# 5364

Wama huwa biqawli sha'irin qaleelan ma tuminoona

# 5365

Wala biqawli kahinin qaleelan ma tathakkaroona

# 5366

Tanzeelun min rabbi al'alameena

# 5367

Walaw taqawwala 'alayna ba'da alaqaweeli

# 5368

Laakhathna minhu bialyameeni

# 5369

Thumma laqata'na minhu alwateena

# 5370

Fama minkum min ahadin 'anhu hajizeena

# 5371

Wainnahu latathkiratun lilmuttaqeena

# 5372

Wainna lana'lamu anna minkum mukaththibeena

# 5373

Wainnahu lahasratun 'ala alkafireena

# 5374

Wainnahu lahaqqu alyaqeeni

# 5375

Fasabbih biismi rabbika al'atheemi

# 5376

Saala sailun bi'athabin waqi'in

# 5377

Lilkafireena laysa lahu dafi'un

# 5378
